#  696 – Preparations for the Return of the City of Chaos

With just that gentle touch, it felt as though Vera 1’s very soul was trembling. Her whole body was soaring, immersed in sheer bliss.

What kind of foot was this? Braised pig trotter? A tender, slow-stewed lamb shank? No… none of those. This was the foot of a beautiful girl; fragrant, divine, and utterly irresistible.

**PERO! PERO! PERO!** [1](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-696-preparations-for-the-return-of-the-city-of-chaos/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-110501)　

At that moment, completely captivated by that flawless leg, Vera 1 seemed to awaken a rather dangerous obsession. She began licking it uncontrollably as if savoring every trace of that divine sensation.

Above her, Yae-hime’s eye twitched slightly. She suddenly realized, she had chosen the wrong method. These two little perverts were beyond saving, they were full-blown foot fetishists!

“Ahh, this leg… so smooth, so tender, and it smells amazing… Master, can I rub my face on it?” Vera 1 asked in a daze, totally intoxicated. Dignity? Shame? Toss it. Throw it all away!

‘I want nothing—nothing but this beautiful leg!’

“No.” Seeing the sickly obsession in Vera 1’s eyes, Yae-hime hurriedly pulled her foot back, a little unnerved.

“Pity,” Vera 1 said with regret as she withdrew her hands. Then, her expression shifted as she respectfully declared, “Vera 1 swears absolute loyalty to Master!”

“No need to repeat yourselves. Just get along with each other from now on.” With that, Yae-hime handed her one of the roasted chickens from the platter.

Vera 1 inhaled the aroma, took it slowly, and immediately began tearing into it without restraint. Her eating habits were no different from Vera 3’s. She had been far too hungry. Once she entered food mode, she lost all sense of composure. Even making a fool of herself in front of her glorious master didn’t matter in the slightest.

After the two girls finished their roasted chicken, Yae-hime personally purified their bodies. Then, together, they headed to the newly renovated living room to enjoy a delicious midnight snack.

The little ones ate with great joy. Whatever distance had lingered between them melted away at the dinner table, leaving only warmth and laughter.

Yae-hime stepped outside alone to enjoy the breeze. The night sky wasn’t particularly beautiful, the moonlight was hidden behind thick clouds, without a single star in sight.

“Master, you’re not eating?” Little Blue suddenly popped out beside her. In one hand, she held a roasted chicken leg; in the other, a jumbo shrimp. It was unclear if she’d brought them for Yae-hime or intended to eat them herself.

“I’ll pass,” Yae-hime said with a gentle shake of her head. She had already eaten some shrimp noodles made by Layna in-game earlier. Her taste buds had been satisfied. There was no need to eat more. After all, whether she ate or not didn’t make a difference to her body. Eating food was merely a way to satisfy the desire of the palate.

“Ohh, then I won’t hold back!” Hearing her master say she wasn’t eating, Little Blue immediately scarfed down both items. She ate so fast it was almost frightening.

“No one’s stealing it from you,” Yae-hime grumbled. If she didn’t keep this little one in check, her table manners would grow more and more outrageous.

“Ahahaha~ I’ll be more careful next time,” Little Blue said, her cheeks a little flushed.

Yae-hime purified her hands and lips with a touch of spiritual energy.

“Hehe, squeaky clean! Hug me, Master!” Seeing her hands spotless, Little Blue latched onto Yae-hime’s neck without hesitation.

Yae-hime gave her cheek a gentle pinch and asked, “How’s the situation with the City of Chaos?”

“It’s going great, because someone has been handling it!” Little Blue replied proudly.

“Don’t give me that,” Yae-hime pinched her nose. “It’s obviously Kinkara managing it for you.”

Kinkara wasn’t some strange entity, just one of Alicia’s distant ancestors. Since their real name had long been forgotten, Yae-hime had casually made one up. In the end, she really had just made up that name on the spot.

“Hehe, you saw through it! Master is amazing!” Little Blue grinned mischievously.

“By the way, is Kinkara still unable to come outside?” Yae-hime asked.

Little Blue nodded. “He’s still in recovery and can’t wander around. Also, the mana density here is a bit thin, nowhere near what it is inside the City of Chaos.”

“A shut-in, huh,” Yae-hime chuckled.  

“Pretty much,” Little Blue laughed as well.  

“Anyway, in a few days, I’ll be sending the City of Chaos back into the game for repairs.”

Her ring held a massive stockpile of repair materials, ready to be used as soon as the city re-entered the game world.

“Whoa! Really!?” At that, Little Blue practically exploded with excitement. She was deeply attached to that scrappy little city, as much as if it were her own second body. Hearing it would be repaired filled her with uncontrollable joy.

“You think I’d joke about that?” Yae-hime patted her head. “I don’t know the exact day yet. Just make sure you’re ready.”

“Mhm!” Little Blue nodded, then suddenly remembered the other little cuties at home. “What about Vera and the others? That world’s pretty special, there’s a good chance they won’t be able to come with us.”

“Yeah, finding a place for them is a bit tricky.” Yae-hime pursed her lips slightly. Two potential locations came to mind: Jade Flower Garden and the stairwell at the top of the unfinished building.

“Which do you think is safer, Little Blue; Jade Flower Garden, or the stairwell at the top of the ruin?”

“I’d say the unfinished building. After all, Vera’s main body already knows about Jade Flower Garden,” Little Blue replied.

“True… but the stairwell isn’t exactly the best place to live.” Yae-hime clearly didn’t like the idea of her precious girls staying somewhere so run-down.

“That’s easy! I’ll just send some puppets to renovate it!” Little Blue beamed.

“Oh right! I almost forgot about the puppets we have at home.” Yae-hime tapped her palm. “Alright, I’ll leave it to you.”

“Got it! I’ll take care of it right now!” Little Blue nodded quickly. Her bright blue eyes flashed, summoning three humanoid puppets.

“There’s a storage room in that stairwell, open it up and turn it into one big room. As for the stairs, I’ve already destroyed them, so just seal the whole area off. Make it as comfortable as possible.” Yae-hime gave her instructions.

“Understood!” Little Blue snapped her fingers, and the three puppets vanished in a flash of white light.

“Can we bring household appliances and furniture into the game world?” Yae-hime suddenly asked.

Little Blue shook her head. “Not directly, but we can store them inside the void here. Once we return, we can instantly restore everything.”

“That’s way more convenient,” Yae-hime said with satisfaction. She hated moving. Even if she didn’t have to do it herself, just the thought of it felt like a hassle. Returning everything to its original place with a single swish, now that was efficiency.

“It’s convenient, sure…but the storage time can’t be too long,” Little Blue reminded her.  

“How long are we talking?”  

“Three days. Technically, seventy-two hours. Any longer than that, and the supporting power from the City of Chaos will vanish.” Little Blue explained patiently.  

“Seventy-two hours is more than enough.”

Yae-hime had two goals for sending the City of Chaos back. First, to repair some of its functions. Second, to serve as a backup for Alicia’s rebellion. Because who knew what unexpected events might arise during that mission?

And remembering Alicia’s habit of fumbling right at the finish line only made her worry even more.

+++

# 697 – Berserk Drug Acquired

As night deepened, the work below continued in an orderly fashion. The dilapidated stairwell, after extensive renovation by the three humanoid puppets, was now nearly complete. With just some fine-tuning left, it would be ready for occupancy.

“Mm, not bad at all,” Yae-hime said, surveying the interior with a satisfied nod.  

“Of course! These are my most prized puppets!” Little Blue lifted her chin proudly.  

Yae-hime gave her a playful pat on the backside. “Alright, alright, I get it, you’re amazing.”  

“Ow!” Little Blue yelped theatrically, pretending it hurt. As if she’d truly been struck hard.  

“Okay, enough fooling around,” Yae-hime said, stepping out of the stairwell.

The little ones quickly followed after her.

By this time, the clouds had dispersed, revealing a crescent moon in the night sky, casting a faint silver glow over the earth.

“Has Lucky begun moving?” Yae-hime asked, gazing up at the moon above. Though the opponent wasn’t especially strong, she still had to stay alert to anything that might happen off the battlefield, just in case.

“Let me take a look.” Little Blue tapped into the void and pulled up a stream of information. “Master, Lucky and a bunch of his men have already chartered a plane from the United States and are en route to Okinawa.”

At the mention of Okinawa, Yae-hime’s expression shifted slightly. She suddenly recalled a closed beta player: Honda Yu.

“That Avenger-class player might actually pose a bigger threat to me than Mira does.”  

“Master?” Little Blue tilted her adorable head, not quite understanding.  

“Little Blue, look into Honda Yu for me,” Yae-hime said softly, brushing aside a few strands of hair tossed about by the night breeze.  

“Okay! I’ll get on it right away!” Without asking further, Little Blue dove into the search.

It didn’t take long before she brought the results back to Yae-hime. It was mostly what Yae-hime already suspected. Honda Yu had completely disappeared after that incident.

“She’s probably holed up somewhere playing the game,” she said. Thinking back to how that witch had gone on a killing spree against foreign players in-game, Yae-hime could vaguely guess what kind of situation she was in now.

Probably not much better than her own had been before.

“She’s a ruthless one. I’ll have to be extra careful if we cross paths again.” Then, changing the subject, Yae-hime asked, “So, is Lucky planning to sail from Okinawa to Baiding Island?”

“That’s still unclear,” Little Blue replied with a shake of her head.  

“Keep an eye on it for me.”  

“Got it!”  

“Let’s head up.” Yae-hime looked up toward the void.

Little Blue nodded. Her eyes flashed with a soft blue glow. In the next moment, the two of them vanished into beams of white light.

Meanwhile, inside the game—

“Taurus, 98% of our core members have reached level 20,” S.K.Y. reported after checking the guild stats.

“Very good!” Taurus slapped the table, grinning with delight. He’d already slapped the table so many times that day that the surface was covered in palm marks.

The constant banging drew annoyed glances from nearby non-guild players. But once they saw the powerful Death of Love guild members surrounding him, their expressions changed instantly.

Some were frustrated, some resentful, others fearful. In the end, they could only mutter complaints under their breath or stomp their feet on the ground to show their displeasure.

Taurus caught their reactions from the corner of his eye, and his lips curled into a sneer of contempt.

“By 6 a.m., every core member will definitely be above level 20,” S.K.Y. continued.

“Mm, not bad at all.” Taurus withdrew his hand and tapped his forehead lightly. “Did the military side agree to provide that item for us?”

At that, S.K.Y. nodded. “They did. It’ll be ready to deploy by early tomorrow morning. As long as that black-hearted princess shows up, she won’t escape us.”

“It’s a bit of a waste to use such a treasure… but we’ve got no other choice.” A cold, vicious glint flashed in Taurus’ eyes, alongside an undisguised greed. As long as things went according to plan tomorrow and the black-hearted princess fell into their trap, he could wipe her out completely.

‘Your equipment’s top-tier. Too bad it’s about to become mine!’ Clenching his fists, he couldn’t suppress the smug grin forming on his handsome face.

S.K.Y. gave him a quick glance, then slowly lowered his head again. ‘Looks like I can’t stay in Huadu any longer.’

The moment Taurus succeeded would be the moment of his total defeat. Everything S.K.Y. had worked for would become someone else’s glory. How could he possibly accept such an outcome?

‘Once I log out, I’ll head back to my hometown. No one knows about that place. As long as I stockpile enough food, I can hide out for a long time.’ With that thought, S.K.Y.’s pupils turned completely blood-red. ‘No matter what happens, I’ll claim everything that’s rightfully mine!’

“S.K.Y., keep up the good work. After tomorrow’s battle, I’ve got a big gift for you!” Taurus looked over at him and smiled.

Hearing this, S.K.Y. closed his eyes. When he reopened them, his gaze had returned to normal. “Thank you, Young Master Taurus,” he said with a polite smile.

The two locked eyes for a moment. A strange tension slowly filled the air between them.

---

Time flew by. In the blink of an eye, morning arrived. After having breakfast with her little cuties, Yae-hime returned to her room and logged into the game.

In the guest room of Layna’s home, a flash of white light revealed her elegant figure.

“I wonder if the berserk drug is finished.” She stepped out of the room and headed toward Layna’s workshop.

The air carried a faint medicinal scent. Standing at the door, Yae-hime gently knocked. After a few seconds, the workshop door slowly opened, revealing a pale and visibly exhausted girl… It was Layna.

“Princess, it’s done!” she said, giving a thumbs-up with a tired smile.  

“Thank you,” Yae-hime replied as she conjured a green needle, swiftly pricking it into Layna and injecting a surge of dense life energy.

Layna’s long-deprived body absorbed the life energy greedily, like parched soil drinking in spring rain. Perhaps the infusion was too intense, her entire body trembled as a faint blush bloomed across her face.

Even her brain felt like it was vibrating. As though she might ascend to heaven at any moment. The joy she felt was beyond words.

By the time Layna recovered, Yae-hime had already prepared breakfast and placed it neatly on the table, “Here you go.”  

Seeing only one portion, Layna blinked in confusion. “You’re not eating?”  

“I’ve already eaten,” Yae-hime replied with a faint smile.  

“Well then, I won’t hold back.” It was Layna’s first time tasting Yae-hime’s cooking, and she was full of anticipation.

However, once she took a bite… the best she could say was: it was average. Truly, painfully average. Compared to her own culinary skills, there was an obvious gap. Still, she ate it with great enjoyment.

After the meal—

“Princess, there are ten finished bottles in total. Originally, there were eleven, but I messed one up by accident.” Layna spoke a bit apologetically.

“No worries. Ten bottles is already fantastic.” Yae-hime picked one up. Looking at the clear vial of crimson liquid, a joyful smile spread across her face.

In past battles against strong opponents, she had always been suppressed for a while at the start, taking unnecessary damage. But now, with these berserk drugs, she could skip that phase entirely and start at full power from the get-go!

+++

# 698 – OMG, it’s a Hidden Boss!

After leaving Layna’s house, Yae-hime hurried back to Aoma Village at full speed. By that time, Angelica had already eaten breakfast with her father.

“Princess, you’re back!” The moment she saw Yae-hime, she beamed brightly, radiating the charm of a gentle, caring woman.

“Mm, I just came back from visiting my apothecary friend,” Yae-hime replied.  

“Have you had breakfast yet?” Angelica asked.  

Yae-hime nodded, then got straight to the point. “Did the church build the production line as I requested?”

To improve the efficiency of bottling holy water, she had previously suggested to Micha that a simple production line be set up. Though called a “production line,” it was really just a basic setup. All it required was a water supply pipe, a reservoir, and a water channel.

“Yeah, it was completed overnight,” Angelica replied.  

“No time to waste, let’s go check it out.”

They shut the door behind them and quickly headed toward the church.

The early morning breeze was a bit chilly, and the area around the church was quiet and mostly empty. The massive palm print still remained on the ground outside. According to Angelica, the church had decided not to repair it, choosing instead to leave it as a memorial.

Although Yae-hime felt it was a bit unsightly and spoiled the town’s appearance, if the locals liked it, she saw no reason to object.

The clergy at the church were early risers. As soon as they reached the entrance, they saw two clerics already sweeping the grounds.

“Greetings, Lord Angel!”

When they saw Yae-hime, wearing a white mask and black robes, they immediately stopped what they were doing and bowed respectfully.

“I’m here to see Micha,” Yae-hime said, speaking in a slightly altered voice. It sounded a bit strange, deliberately disguised.

Hearing this, one of the clerics quickly stepped forward to lead the way. Before long, they arrived at the church’s warehouse.

The area had been renovated: a tall reservoir had been installed, with a pipe equipped with a switch valve hanging above it. Near the bottom of the reservoir, a sealed, sloped water channel extended into the room next door.

Even without seeing it, Yae-hime knew that channel ended in ten faucet-like devices for filling bottles.

“Ten workstations…for now, this will do,” she murmured, inspecting the rough production line.

Angelica was just about to speak when Micha arrived first.

“Lord Angel!”

Yae-hime gave the smiling priest a polite nod.

“We’ve completed the task as ordered!” Micha said, bowing respectfully.  

“Thank you for your hard work,” Yae-hime replied, then turned to the large water tank. “Can we begin?”  

“Ready anytime, Lord Angel,” Micha said, standing upright.

By this point, the support teams were already in place, one group drawing water from the well using water magic, another handling the bottling next door, and a third managing logistics and transport. All stood at the ready.

“Then let’s begin. No one is allowed to enter without my permission, except for Angelica,” Yae-hime instructed.  

“Yes, Lord Angel. I’ll station Holy Knights outside to guard the entrance,” Micha replied solemnly.  

“Good. Off you go,” Yae-hime said with a wave of her hand.

Micha quietly exited the warehouse, and Angelica walked over to lock the door behind him.

“Angelica, find a place to sit. I’ll call you if I need help.” Yae-hime walked toward the ladder leading up to the water tank as she spoke.  

“Okay, Princess,” Angelica answered. She pulled over a stool and sat by the door, her gaze following Yae-hime closely.

Yae-hime leapt lightly onto the work platform attached to the reservoir. Looking down at the clear water inside, her pupils suddenly shifted to a vivid emerald green. Green fire wrapped around both hands.

As she placed her hands into the tank, the crystal-clear water quickly transformed into a deep green hue.

‘Aureole Town is a fair distance from here. Transporting the holy water will take time…better enhance it a little.’

Considering the possibility that Micha might run into trouble at the town’s church, or waste time boasting, Yae-hime decided to go the extra mile and infuse the water with more life energy, extending its shelf life.

Fifteen minutes passed. The water in the tank now glowed with a vibrant emerald sheen. Yae-hime withdrew her hands. A pulse of energy flung off the excess liquid, and she gave a gentle tug on a red cord beside the reservoir.

A bell suddenly rang in the room next door.

The staff there froze for a moment before quickly realizing what it meant. They immediately sprang into action. Minute by minute, the process moved along. Yae-hime continued calmly channeling her energy, while the workers labored in a bustling, coordinated rhythm.

Before long, all the bottles were filled. The first batch of Holy Water was complete and ready for delivery. Early that morning, Micha and a group of clerics set off with the holy water, bound for Aureole Town.

The outbreak over there was only a matter of time before it got resolved. Yae-hime had nothing to worry about. As long as Micha built a reputation, the surrounding towns would eventually come asking for help.

‘By then, there’ll be people willing to pay for those pricey crystal bottles. But before that, I need to stay alert for the Apostles. Three of them have died here already, no doubt that organization will send stronger forces to deal with me.’ With that thought, Yae-hime took out three Holy Spirit Shards.

Two of them emitted an ominous black aura; the third was dull and lifeless.

‘Though returning to Jade City now is a bit risky, the Apostles will likely attack again. I need to double up on safety measures.’ Clutching the shards, Yae-hime decided to head back immediately.

“Angelica, arrange a beast carriage for me.”

With her current strength, going up against stronger Apostles would be extremely dangerous.

“Yes, Princess,” Angelica replied, nodding and quickly leaving the warehouse.

‘Now that I’ve escaped, the city’s internal search effort will definitely weaken. Besides, Richard isn’t the type to personally lead the hunt every day.’ After a quick analysis, Yae-hime concluded that sneaking back into Jade City was feasible.

“There’s definitely risk, but it’s worth a try.”

After all, sometimes the most dangerous place was the safest one. Who would expect someone who had just escaped by the skin of their teeth to return so soon?

After a brief wait, Angelica had the beast carriage ready. It was the fastest and best in the village, and the coachman was a devout believer who held deep reverence for the Lord Angel.

Once she got in, the carriage set off immediately.

Inside, the ride was bumpy. After all, it wasn’t built for comfort, it wasn’t a luxury passenger model. Still, it was far faster than most high-end beast carriages. That meant less time spent on the road.

With nothing else to do, Yae-hime opened the forums and browsed trending topics. The first post that caught her eye had a familiar air about it: «Shocking! Hidden Boss Possibly Spotted in the Mangrove Forest!»

She clicked it open. At the top of the post was a blurry image. The location: a mangrove forest roughly ten kilometers from the Wastelands. In the picture, a massive black shadow could be seen amidst the trees, along with a pair of glowing green eyes.

The original poster had used exaggerated language to describe what they’d seen. The comment section was filled with astonishment and curiosity.

“Something seems off.” Yae-hime narrowed her eyes, noticing some details others missed.

She closed that thread and looked at the second hot post. It was a thread from the Death of Love guild. The content was full of stern warnings.

“So Taurus and S.K.Y. are targeting the so-called hidden boss in the Mangrove Forest?” she murmured. “Interesting.”

Making such a grand show of it, what a clumsy misdirection. Yae-hime clearly smelled a setup.

“Heh… interesting, very interesting.” By now, the fattened crops were ripe for harvesting. Time to collect. With that thought, an exquisite smile bloomed on her face, one that could topple cities.

At that very moment, a massive crowd of players had gathered outside the Mangrove Forest. Most of them were members of Death of Love. But neither S.K.Y. nor Taurus were among them.

The rest were unaffiliated onlookers hoping to get lucky or grab a piece of loot. As for other guild players, there were only a few scattered here and there. Likely scouts sent to gather intel.

Many of the unaffiliated players had already started livestreams, broadcasting the event inside and outside the game.

Some more laid-back players had even paused what they were doing just to watch the show unfold via the virtual screens. Even the outside world was paying attention, waiting for what could become a major boss fight.

Time ticked by. Two hours passed, and the towering trees of the Mangrove Forest remained still. Spectators grew restless, and the livestream audience grew impatient as well.

They couldn’t figure out why such a massive guild hadn’t entered the forest to lure the hidden boss out. Were they just going to stand around waiting for the boss to come out and die on its own?

The livestream chat was filled with complaints. But the Death of Love guild stayed calm and unmoved, completely ignoring the noise from the outside world.

Elsewhere, under the same sky, a beast carriage raced at full speed from Aoma Village and began slowing down as it neared Jade City. Eventually, it came to a stop two or three kilometers from the city.

Yae-hime stepped out and handed the coachman a few gold coins. He refused at first, but she tossed the money into the carriage and walked away without a word. Now he had no choice but to accept it.

With gratitude in his heart, the coachman cheerfully turned the carriage around and headed back to the village.

Yae-hime, in the blink of an eye, reached the city’s moat. After sensing no danger, she leapt into the water and dashed across the surface like a martial arts master.

Not a single drop clung to her feet.

Reaching the base of the city wall, she carefully surveyed her surroundings, then sprang upward like a phantom. Using the wall’s crevices, double-jumping, and her danger sense, Yae-hime dodged several hidden traps and swiftly scaled the wall.

Then she leapt down in one smooth motion. Her figure vanished into the shadows beneath the wall. It was a flawless infiltration, enough to leave anyone awestruck.

Under the same night sky, in a room within the church… Irene lay in bed, bored out of her mind. She wore a thin nightgown and stared blankly at the ceiling. “So boring… I want to read a novel.”

Ever since a sense of foreboding crept into her heart yesterday, she hadn’t left her room. Even her meals had been delivered by others. Many within the church were now talking about Irene’s condition. Some were even considering calling in a doctor to examine her. But that idea had quickly been shut down by the high priest.

The reason? “A saintess cannot fall ill.” Everyone who heard it nodded in agreement. If word got out that a divinely blessed saintess was sick, it would do more harm than good to the church’s reputation.

“So boring. So, so boring!” Irene suddenly sat up in frustration, muttering to herself.

**Click!**

At that very moment, a sharp sound came from the direction of the door.

+++

# 699 – It Really Was Just a Tiny Matter

Irene snapped to full alert and sprang up from the bed with a sharp whoosh, conjuring a Holy Spirit Hammer in her hand, ready to strike.

At that moment, the door opened, and a figure darted inside, casually shutting the door behind them.

Irene’s eyes narrowed as she gripped the glowing golden hammer tightly. Her small hand raised, one foot stepped forward, and her petite frame leaned in preparation to launch forward.

But then, a familiar voice rang out.

“What, is this how you greet people now?”

Her body froze mid-motion. Irene forcibly halted herself, her wide, adorable eyes staring ahead.

As expected, it was that familiar, beautiful figure.

“Princess!” Delight and surprise flashed across her face. The Holy Spirit Hammer in her hand instantly dispersed into golden particles, and she lunged forward with all her might. “My novel! Hurry, hand it over!”

At this moment, Irene looked just like a poor creature suffering withdrawal, finally spotting her long-awaited medicine. She was absolutely desperate. Yae-hime tilted her body aside, dodging Irene’s flying tackle with ease.

Irene landed face-first on the floor and let out a pitiful cry. “Wuuu… why didn’t you catch me?!” She pouted, complaining.

“With the way you came at me, I’d have broken a few bones,” Yae-hime replied seriously.

Irene thought about it and found the statement not entirely unreasonable. Unlike ordinary clerics, she possessed considerable strength. If she crashed into someone at full force, she really might end up hurting them.

“You want to read the lewd novel, huh?” Yae-hime’s expression shifted into a dazzlingly stunning smile.

That smile alone sent shivers down Irene’s spine, an ominous feeling surging in her heart. She clearly remembered, whenever Yae-hime smiled like this, it never ended well!

“Oh? You don’t want to read it after all?” Yae-hime retracted her smile and turned to leave.  

“Wait—no! I do! I want to read it!” Irene scrambled up from the floor and clung tightly to Yae-hime’s elegant leg.  

“Oho, so you do want to read it.” Yae-hime lowered her head with a grin. That smile carried an unmistakably devious edge.  

“Wh-What are you planning?” Irene asked nervously.

“Nothing much. Just a little something I need your help with,” Yae-hime replied with a calm smile.  

“Is it really something small?” Irene still felt uneasy.  

“Of course. When have I ever lied to you?”  

“Ugh… fine, I’ll help!” Whether it was out of a desperate desire to read the novel or a bit of trust in Yae-hime, Irene hesitated briefly before nodding in agreement.  

“You’re really doing me a big favor.” Yae-hime lifted her up and gently set her down on the bed.

“So what is it? Just say it, I’ll smack it twice and get it done!” Irene said as she sat on the bed, her tone tinged with impatience. That latest lewd novel by Alicia, she had only read part of it last time. Ever since, she had been constantly preoccupied with what came next, unable to eat or sleep in peace.

“Purify these two shards for me. After that, all three need to be fully recharged.” Yae-hime nonchalantly took out three Holy Spirit Shards from her ring.

Irene stared at the shards in Yae-hime’s palm, momentarily dumbfounded and dazed. Then, like a threatened kitten, she suddenly jumped up and roared, “I don’t know where you got these shards from, but asking me to purify and recharge them all…that’s just too much! Are you some kind of demon?!”

If not for the room’s excellent soundproofing, her voice would’ve echoed through the entire church.

“You’re noisy,” Yae-hime said, furrowing her delicate brow as she grabbed Irene’s small hand and placed the shards into her palm. “You’re a saintess. You promised to help, remember? You can’t go back on your word.” With that, she gave Irene an innocent, harmless smile.

“You really are a devil!” Irene looked like she was about to cry.  

“Alright, get to work. There’ll be a reward afterward.” Yae-hime patted her head.  

“Wuu… you meanie!” Irene stretched out her pretty little leg and kicked Yae-hime away slightly.  

“I’ll be back later.” Yae-hime walked toward the door.  

“Don’t come back!” Irene hurled a pillow at her.

But Yae-hime had already slipped out. The pillow hit the door and slid to the floor.

“Meanie!” Irene jumped off the bed and retrieved the pillow. “Wait a sec… isn’t that troublemaker wanted? How does she still dare to come back here?” Staring at the closed door, Irene murmured with a confused expression.

Leaving the church, Yae-hime quietly made her way into the commoners’ district.

“I wonder how Princess is doing these days…” a crisp, bell-like voice rang out in a shabby little hut.  

“Don’t worry, Princess will be fine,” a man’s voice replied. Rough, yet tinged with a gentle warmth.  

“Big brother… is there any way we can help Princess?”  

“I don’t know. We don’t even know where she is.”  

“Sigh… Princess, oh Princess, I hope you’re safe.”

“Mhm, safe and sound indeed.” Suddenly, a sweet voice echoed in the room, startling the sibling pair.

They turned with alarm to see a breathtakingly beautiful figure standing before them. It was none other than Yae-hime.

“Prin—” Aurora exclaimed excitedly, but quickly clamped her hands over her mouth and lowered her voice. “Princess.”

The soundproofing in this run-down house wasn’t great. If someone overheard them, it could cause serious trouble.

“Princess, why are you still in the city?” her brother Fiat asked in surprise. He also kept his voice low.

“I didn’t stay, I just snuck back in,” Yae-hime replied with a smile.

Hearing that, the two siblings were briefly stunned, but quickly regained their composure. After all, they knew full well, things like this were par for the course when it came to Princess. Only she would dare to do something so bold.

Of course, that boldness came from her sheer capability.

“No one’s been bothering you lately, right?” Yae-hime walked over and asked softly. Her tone carried a distinct trace of concern.

Hearing that, Aurora felt a wave of warmth rise in her chest. Even when Princess’ own situation was in such dire straits, she still took the time to worry about them. So gentle. So thoughtful.

“No, on the contrary, people seem to be keeping their distance from us,” Fiat said with a helpless chuckle.  

“That’s normal. In their eyes, your status has changed…you’re far above the rest of the people around here.” Yae-hime explained.

When everyone’s on the same level, and someone suddenly rises above the rest, it naturally breeds envy and petty targeting. But once you’re far beyond them, they start to keep their distance, treating you like you’re from another world.

Yae-hime had come to understand this more deeply herself as of late.

“Princess, what have you been up to lately?” Aurora asked curiously.  

“Well, that’s a bit of a long story, but I’ll keep it short…”

Since the siblings were people she could trust, Yae-hime gave them a quick rundown of recent events. After hearing everything, the two siblings couldn’t help but gasp in shock. They never imagined Princess’ escape from Jade City had been so perilous.

And to think she encountered such terrifying foes afterward…it was thrilling, but also incredibly dangerous.

“You’ve really been through a lot, Princess…” Aurora looked up at Yae-hime, her face tinged with concern.  

“Princess is someone destined for great things. Of course it won’t be easy,” said Fiat.  

“Enough about that. I actually came to ask you for a favor, do you two have time?” Yae-hime waved her hand lightly, shifting the topic.

+++

# 700 – Yae-hime’s Arrangements, Lili’s Whereabouts

“Yes!” Aurora answered immediately. Even if she didn’t have time, as long as Princess asked, she would find a way, no matter what.

Fiat nodded, indicating he felt the same as his sister.

“Excellent.” Yae-hime smiled calmly. “What I’m asking of you is actually quite simple. I’ve already mentioned the epidemic issue earlier. I’d like Aurora to help with some inscription work on the containers. As for you, Fiat, your job is to protect Aurora and the related personnel. Is that alright?”

The siblings quickly processed her request and nodded almost in unison.

“Very good. Later, head to Aoma Village and find the village chief’s daughter, Angelica. She’ll make the arrangements for you.”

“Got it, Princess!” Aurora replied cheerfully. She hadn’t expected to be useful so soon, her heart was filled with joy.

“Understood! I will not disappoint you!!” Fiat had always wanted to repay his debt. Now that he finally had the chance to do something for his benefactor, he was filled with energy.

After chatting with the siblings for a while, Yae-hime left the commoners’ district.

Beneath the same sky, within the Imperial Magic Academy’s Sage Tower…

“Lady Allie doesn’t seem to be in a good mood lately.”  

“Yeah, maybe it’s because of that Black-hearted Princess business.”  

“Now that you mention it, what exactly did the Black-hearted Princess do to become a national fugitive?”  

“No idea, but it couldn’t have been anything good.”

Two beautiful receptionists chatted as they stepped onto a circular stone platform. One of them pressed her foot onto a gem on the left side, used to activate upward movement.

The next moment, the platform began to rise steadily.

Just then, the space around them started to ripple unnaturally. Yet neither of them noticed a thing.

When the platform reached the designated floor, they stopped it and stepped off toward the reception desk. Throughout the whole ride, neither had noticed the subtle distortions in their surroundings.

Inside the research lab… Allie sat on her bed, her mood rather sour. Though, compared to yesterday, she was in slightly better spirits.

“That b̲a̲s̲t̲a̲r̲d̲ Richard seriously needs a beating.” Clenching her fist lightly, Allie stared coldly ahead. If her strength had recovered, she would’ve stormed the palace by now. “If anything happens to my Princess, I’ll make you pay!”

While Richard was conducting a search in the outer district, Allie had remained unaware. It wasn’t until later that she sensed some residual spiritual fluctuations. And then came the news: Princess was now wanted across the entire city. Only then did she piece everything together.

**Clink clink!**

Suddenly, a crisp chime echoed inside the room. It was the doorbell she had set up.

“Who’s there?” Allie looked toward the stone door and asked. But there was no response. After a few seconds, the bell rang again.

“Heh. Trying to provoke me at a time like this?” With a cold sneer, Allie stepped down from the bed and blinked to the doorway. She had already decided to give whoever was outside a brutal beating to vent her anger.

The stone door slowly opened. Subtle ripples distorted the space around her. Such changes could never escape Allie’s perception. She slammed the stone door shut and unleashed a terrifying aura from within.

‘Using magic right in front of me? Courting death!’

Crackling lightning surged in Allie’s left hand, gathering with lethal intensity as she prepared to strike the source of the spatial disturbance.

“Is this how you always greet people?” Before the words even finished, a beautiful figure stepped out from the void.

The moment Allie got a clear look, she froze, stunned and disbelieving. Then, the lightning in her hand slowly dissipated.

“Why are you still in the city?” she asked at last.  

“I snuck back in,” Yae-hime replied with a smile.  

“Have you lost your mind? Do you even understand how dangerous your situation is?” Allie scolded her with a stern expression.

“I know,” Yae-hime nodded. “But I had to come back.”

Hearing this, Allie’s heart instantly raced, her face flushing slightly as she asked, “You came back… for me?”

Yae-hime felt there was some ambiguity in those words, but it was true that one of her reasons for returning was to treat Allie’s illness.

“Mm.” After a brief pause, she nodded.

“That’s really dangerous, you know. You’re impossible sometimes.” Despite saying that, Allie’s heart brimmed with sweetness.

“Has anything changed in the city lately?” Yae-hime, unaware of Allie’s inner thoughts, quickly moved to the matter that concerned her most.

“Things are more or less the same as usual. As for the palace… I don’t really know.” Allie shook her head. Her intelligence network only covered the outer districts and parts of the inner district. The palace was outside her reach.

“I see.” Yae-hime lightly pressed her cherry lips together, as though she had expected that answer.

“Yeah, I don’t have a dedicated intel network, so it’s hard to get anything from there. Sorry I couldn’t be of more help,” Allie said with a tinge of guilt.

“It’s fine.” Yae-hime shook her head. “It’s just that I’ve been short on useful information lately. That aside, has Lili come to see you?”

Compared to intel about the palace, she was more interested in Lili’s whereabouts. There were two reasons for this. First, she wanted to know how things were progressing with Alicia. Second, if possible, she wanted to meet Alicia in person and see if there was anything she could help with.

Right now, only Lili knew where Alicia was.

Allie shook her head gently. “No, we haven’t seen each other in a while.”  

“Is that so…” Yae-hime sounded a little disappointed.  

“When I see Lili next, I’ll tell her to find you,” Allie said.  

“Mm, I’ll leave it to you.”  

“It’s getting late, let’s begin.” Allie naturally began to take off her clothes.

Seeing this, Yae-hime was momentarily caught off guard.

‘You’re seriously just stripping like that!?’

While it was true that her purpose here was to treat Allie’s illness, she hadn’t even brought up the subject yet, and the other party was already undressing… It really felt like she wasn’t being treated like an outsider at all.

Within seconds, Allie looked like a newborn, her silvery hair cascading down like a waterfall, covering the forbidden curves of her chest. In that state, she was undoubtedly more alluring than being completely nude! Even Yae-hime found herself briefly dazed.

“Do you like what you see?” Allie asked with a smile. A deep flush tinted her face, but it didn’t feel like it came from embarrassment.

If Yae-hime had to guess, she’d never believe that expression was born of shyness.

“You’re beautiful. Let’s get started,” Yae-hime replied, pretending not to notice anything as she walked to the bedside. In her heart, she silently vowed, ‘Once the treatment’s done, I’m out of here!’

Allie lay obediently on the bed, her crimson eyes staring intently at Yae-hime. It felt as though she were trying to see through her completely.

Yae-hime chose to ignore the gaze. Her pupils suddenly turned emerald green, and a glowing green needle appeared in her hand. Then, the needles rained down like a storm, striking the vital points on Allie’s body with perfect precision.

She sealed away the virus and the mutating energy within her, drawing them out bit by bit.

“Next part’s going to hurt. Brace yourself.” Soon after, Yae-hime finished the needlework. She pressed one hand against Allie’s flat lower abdomen, her eyes glowing green once more.

At the same time, Allie felt a surge of indescribable pain shoot through her entire body. It was as if tens of thousands of ants were biting her all at once, or like she was being gnawed at by an uncountable swarm of poisonous insects and venomous snakes. The sensation was utterly unbearable!

+++

# 701 – Unimaginable Benefits

Seeing the pained expression on Allie’s face, Yae-hime still didn’t stop her hand. She understood clearly, this was the backlash of that mutated energy.

‘It’s nothing more than a dying struggle!’

With green flames flickering in her palm, she immediately injected more life energy into Allie’s body. In that instant, two potent energies clashed within her, creating an even more excruciating torment.

Yet Allie gritted her teeth and endured in silence. Beads of sweat covered her skin, her face pale as paper, and her tightly clenched lips had even begun to bleed.

Yae-hime could no longer afford to hold back. She continued pouring life energy into Allie’s body in an unending stream. She was determined to suppress the mutated energy and virus in the shortest time possible.

Second by second, time ticked by.

At this point, not only was Allie suffering, Yae-hime was struggling as well. Her life energy wasn’t infinite. The more she used it, the more it felt like her body was being utterly drained.

Fortunately, the battle inside was nearing its end. With her abundant life force, she managed to encircle half of the mutated energy and virus completely. As for the other half, it had vanished, hiding who knew where.

This outcome was more or less what Yae-hime had anticipated. Just one more attempt, and she would be able to wipe them all out.

“Checkmate,” she murmured, the corners of her lips curling into a victor’s smile. With that, she raised her slender hand and pulled out a green orb, about the size of a tennis ball, from Allie’s lower abdomen.

The orb was densely packed with compressed mutated energy and virus.

Lying on the bed, Allie looked utterly spent, as if she had just gone through childbirth, her body nearly collapsing from exhaustion. The battle earlier had taken that heavy a toll on her.

Yae-hime shifted her gaze away from Allie and looked at the green orb in her hand.

“That was seriously exhausting… Let’s hope this brings me something in return.” As she spoke, she suddenly pressed the orb against her chest. The mutated energy and virus began to slowly merge into her body.

The moment they were fully absorbed, Yae-hime lifted the seal on the orb. The next instant, the mutated energy, infused with spatial turbulence, exploded violently within her, rampaging like a storm.

“Ugh!” Yae-hime’s expression changed, and she couldn’t help letting out a cry of pain. At that moment, it felt like she was being torn apart by a thousand blades, so agonizing she wanted to die.

But no matter how unbearable, she had to endure it. Because the rewards were tremendous!

Soon enough, the system’s notifications began ringing in her ears one after another. Yae-hime’s spatial attribute was rising at an astonishing pace. At last, as it reached its peak, she underwent a complete metamorphosis.

At the same time, the system chimed again.

Ding! You have acquired: Basic Spatial Resistance.

Ding! Your skill “Void Walk” has evolved into Basic “Void Crossing”.

Ding! Your perception of space has increased to Beginner level. You have obtained: Basic “Spatial Awareness”.

Ding! Your control over space has increased to Beginner level. You have obtained: Basic “Spatial Manipulation”.

After hearing the system announcements, Yae-hime was simply overjoyed. This reward had far exceeded her expectations. It was an absolute windfall.

Sensing her surroundings carefully, she immediately noticed that her awareness of space had grown much clearer. Not only that, she felt an illusion, like she could stand upon the void itself.

When she lifted her foot and stepped forward, ripples faintly spread through the surrounding space.

“No way…” Sensing the anomaly, Yae-hime’s pupils contracted, and a wave of shock washed over her. She could clearly feel that she was standing on solid ground!

To confirm it wasn’t just her imagination… She stepped down with more force, but her foot never touched the floor!

“Incredible…” Placing her other foot into the thin air as well, Yae-hime’s entire figure remained suspended in midair. She could confirm with certainty, she wasn’t using any flashy technique or auxiliary tool at all.

“I’m really standing in midair!” She spoke with a hint of excitement.

Given the height of the Sage Tower, standing on the void was no different from hovering in midair.

“I wonder if I can actually walk like this?”

Yae-hime felt eager to try. Actually, scratch that, she had already taken the first step. And the result…? It was undoubtedly possible. She was still stepping on thin air. Even her previous skill, Void Walk, hadn’t allowed for something like this!

“Hehe, being able to do this without relying on any tools, this is amazing!” Yae-hime laughed as she walked back and forth through the air, as gleeful as a child with a new toy.

Before long, she was walking through the sky as naturally as if she were on solid ground. She even managed to break into a sprint. However, after the dash, she suddenly felt dizzy and drained of strength.

“The consumption is too much…” After checking her mana, she couldn’t help but twitch at the corner of her eye.

Aside from what she had used to treat Allie, the remaining mana was nearly depleted!

“Not even ten minutes, and this much mana’s already gone?” She had originally planned to use this skill for travel, but now she had to give up on that idea. At least for the time being, it wasn’t feasible.

“Still, it should be fine for use in battle.” Although there was still much she hadn’t figured out, this skill, when combined with her double jump, greatly enhanced her mobility. In combat, it would make her movements even more unpredictable.

“This Void Crossing seems to be a higher-tier version of Void Walk. The sky is no longer a limit for me.”

As long as she had enough mana, that is.

Clenching her fist lightly, Yae-hime couldn’t help but smile in delight.

“Ah, I nearly forgot.” She suddenly turned her head toward the bed and saw that the exhausted Allie was already fast asleep. “I got a little carried away,” she said with a wry smile.

Walking to the bedside, Yae-hime gave Allie an injection. Since she didn’t intend to wake her, the injection was extremely gentle, barely noticeable to a normal person.

Under normal circumstances, Allie would have definitely felt it. Unfortunately, her condition now was far removed from normal.

“Sweet dreams.” Yae-hime had no intention of waking her. After saying that, she quietly slipped out of the lab.

“Did someone go down just now?” the receptionist at the front desk blinked and suddenly asked.

Another receptionist followed her gaze, only to see the platform, which had been there moments ago, already gone.

“Maybe Lady Allie went down?”  

“Quite possibly.”

On the first floor of the Sage Tower, the receptionists glanced at the descending, empty lift with a hint of confusion on their faces. But that expression vanished quickly. This sort of situation happened from time to time, and they had long since grown used to it.

Five minutes later—

In a certain room of the church, a girl’s anguished cries echoed.

“Help! I’m going to be drained dry… Ahhhhh~ Nooo! There’s really not a single drop left!”

**Click.**

At the same time, the door let out a crisp sound. Then, it opened and quickly shut. During this entire process, Irene didn’t notice a thing. More like, she didn’t even have the energy to pay attention to what was happening on that side.

“Uuuu… I’m being completely drained dry, help me~”

Looking at the three shards stuck to her palms, constantly siphoning her holy power, Irene muttered with tearful despair. She wanted to stop, but found she simply couldn’t. Her divine energy was being drained at an alarming rate.

“You’ve worked hard.” Just then, a familiar voice suddenly rang out behind her. Immediately after, Irene felt a faint prick of pain at her neck.

+++

# 702 – Aaaah! The Goddess Above!

“You jerk, you finally came back!” Feeling the familiar energy surging into her, Irene was both delighted and furious.

“You seem full of spirit. Looks like you don’t need my help after all.” Yae-hime chuckled behind her.

“Don’t say that, I’m about to be drained dry!” At those words, Irene panicked immediately.

“Charging three shards at once, you’re really something.” Yae-hime glanced at her palm and couldn’t help but laugh.

This little one had clearly gotten greedy and tried to charge all three shards at once, only to end up losing control.

“Ugh, it’s your fault!” Irene spun around and shot Yae-hime a fierce glare. She already looked more energetic than before.

“My fault? How?” Yae-hime blinked in confusion.  

“You told me to finish it quickly!” Pouting, Irene puffed up her cheeks adorably.  

“But I never said to do all three at once.” Yae-hime reached out and gently patted her head.  

“I don’t care, it’s all your fault!” Irene huffed with righteous indignation.  

“Alright, alright, it’s all my fault.” Yae-hime spoke as if pacifying a child, her face overflowing with indulgence.

That look nearly made Irene explode on the spot. However, the three shards chose this moment to act up again, making her abort her tantrum. She cried out in urgency, “You jerk, help me already!”

Without hesitation, Yae-hime placed a hand on her chest and poured more life energy into her. At the same time, her eyes glowed green as she used clairvoyant sight to observe the internal changes, offering precise support.

Her own life energy was running low, so she had to use it sparingly.

“H-Hey! Where are you touching?!” Irene’s face turned bright red as she cried out.  

“Quiet. Focus on the conversion.” Yae-hime replied calmly, unfazed. Such trivial matters didn’t concern her in the slightest.

“Mmm…” Irene wanted to retort, but as she felt the continuous influx of life energy, she obediently focused on the conversion process, allowing the fragments to absorb it. Only when they were full could she finally be free. As for how she would deal with this shameless rascal afterward… she’d figure it out then.

With Irene fully cooperating, Yae-hime found the process much smoother. The two of them worked in perfect sync, one injecting energy, the other converting it.

Yae-hime had to replenish a good amount of mana during the process, but at last, after fifteen minutes, the three fragments were finally fully charged.

“Ugh, I’m exhausted…” Irene tossed the golden-glowing fragments aside, collapsed onto the bed, and groaned weakly.

Yae-hime also sat on the bed, her pretty face slightly pale and clearly fatigued. Charging three Holy Spirit Shards had drained both of them significantly.

“We’ll have to use them sparingly.”

“If you don’t, I’ll bite you to death… rawr!” Irene crawled over and bit Yae-hime’s hand with her tiny mouth.

“Don’t worry, I won’t use them recklessly.” Yae-hime chuckled as she carefully stored the shards away.

“Hmph!” Irene released her bite with a huff. “Where’s the reward you promised me?”  

Hearing that, Yae-hime hesitated. “Right now?”  

“Of course! I want it now!” She had worked so hard to charge those shards, she deserved a great reward!

Irene pushed herself up halfway and leaned against Yae-hime.

“So you’re saying… you agree?” Yae-hime blinked, smiling as she asked.  

“Agree—wait, agree to what? Waaah! What are you doing?!”

Suddenly, just as she was rising, Yae-hime pushed her down onto the bed. Then, with practiced ease, her clothes were removed.

“Your reward.” Yae-hime loomed over her with a mischievous smile.

“S-Stop! I don’t want this kind of reward!” Irene’s cheeks were burning red as she flailed in a panic. She never imagined the reward would be the kind of forbidden scenes described in those lewd novels!

“Relax, it’ll be over quickly.” Yae-hime grinned.

“O-Over quickly?!” Scenes from those novels instantly flashed through Irene’s mind. They always said “quick,” but the battle went on for three whole days and nights! “No, this isn’t okay! Princess, there are gods watching from above!”

She definitely didn’t want her first time to be that kind of intense, soul-consuming showdown. Desperately, she begged for mercy.

“It won’t hurt, I promise. Now let me take a look.” Yae-hime swiftly undid the last bit of clothing covering Irene’s form.

“Princess, nooo!” The poor girl was now utterly drained of strength. No matter how she struggled, it was futile. In the blink of an eye, she had become like a newborn.

“Hmm, still in pretty good shape. Not much that needs adjusting.” Yae-hime scrutinized Irene’s body with a professional gaze.

The latter blushed furiously, her skin flushing a soft pink, delicate and breathtaking.

“N-No… You can’t…” Her voice had become barely audible, filled with anxiety and anticipation. ‘Father in heaven… Today, Irene is going to become a woman!’ With that thought, she shut her eyes tightly, whispering faint protests while bracing herself nervously.

“Here we go.” At that moment, Yae-hime formed a glowing green needle in her hand and swiftly plunged it down.

“No—wait—Goddess above—aaah! That hurts!” Before she could finish her cry, a sudden sharp pain struck her lower body. She opened her eyes and saw a verdant green needle stuck into the area just above her abdomen.

“You jerk! Why are you stabbing me with a needle?!” She cried out in frustration.

“Just doing a few adjustments. A full-body beauty treatment.” Yae-hime replied nonchalantly.

Hearing that, Irene was completely dumbfounded. ‘Full-body beauty treatment? Wait… wasn’t this supposed to be about ascending to heaven?!’ At that moment, she finally realized she had gravely misunderstood. No—horribly misunderstood!

She had even mentally prepared herself for a fierce and passionate battle. ‘Waaah, I’m so embarrassed I could die!’ Right now, all Irene wanted was to crawl into a hole and disappear.

“Were you imagining something naughty?” Seeing her expression, Yae-hime suddenly broke into a mischievous grin.

“You’re the worst! I hate you!” Flushed as red as a cherry, Irene scrambled for a pillow and threw it at Yae-hime. Unfortunately, it was instantly swatted back, right into her face.

“Ow!”

At the same time, green flames ignited in both of Yae-hime’s hands, and her eyes turned a bright emerald hue. “Alright, don’t squirm.” With that, she placed her glowing hands on Irene’s body and began the meticulous full-body beauty treatment.

Irene immediately let out a string of mortified and indignant screams. Even though it wasn’t the intimate scene she had feared, being touched all over like this was still embarrassing beyond belief!

No—she would rather have gone through a passionate clash than be subjected to this kind of treatment!

‘I wanna die… Just let me die…’

In less than two minutes, all resistance melted away. Irene gave up completely and lay there like a limp doll, letting Yae-hime do as she pleased.

Twenty minutes later, Yae-hime finally withdrew her hands and let out a soft breath. Although there hadn’t been many parts of Irene’s body that needed adjusting, perfecting all the details still took considerable effort.

“All done.” She declared.

On the bed, Irene lay motionless like a salted fish, showing no signs of life. Clearly, she had emotionally shut down. Seeing her unresponsive, Yae-hime gently tucked her in with a blanket, then quietly left the church on her own.

“Ugh… I’ll never get married now… never…” After a long while, Irene finally stirred, her face filled with despair. “No, I won’t let that jerk get away with this. She’s going to take responsibility!”

But as soon as she said that, a wave of exhaustion washed over her, and she couldn’t help but close her eyes and slowly drift into sleep.

+++

# 703 – Grandmaster Lucky

Outside Jade City, a black shadow skimmed across the water’s surface and landed on the shore. Under the sunlight, a beautiful figure appeared. It was none other than Yae-hime.

Although it didn’t seem particularly dangerous inside the city, she still played it safe by coming outside. This way, even if Richard had another sudden impulse to raise the city’s barrier, she wouldn’t end up in a bind like last time.

Ding!

Suddenly, the system’s notification chimed.

Upon listening closely, she realized it was an update to Irene’s affection level. Just like with Layna and the others, it had instantly maxed out to triple question marks.

Now it was Yae-hime’s turn to have question marks floating above her head. She was utterly baffled by how affection levels worked in this game. No matter how she thought about it, she just couldn’t figure it out.

In her past life, these NPCs were impossible to conquer even through blood, sweat, and tears. Yet in this life, they seemed to be flinging themselves at her!

Shaking her head, she decided not to think too hard about it. It wasn’t worth dwelling on. After all, it only benefited her and didn’t bring any harm.

“I wonder what’s going on at the Mangrove Forest.” Murmuring softly to herself, Yae-hime leapt up into a roadside tree and concealed her presence, then opened the forum to check the latest news.

《War Breaks Out: Hidden Boss vs. Death of Love Guild》

This trending post was the first thing she saw.

With a light tap, a video began playing automatically. On screen, the Death of Love guild was locked in fierce battle with a one-eyed monster shrouded in black mist, its appearance completely obscured.

“What the heck is that? I’ve never seen it before.” Yae-hime stared at the monster for a while, but nothing came to mind. ‘Could it be a hidden boss, or perhaps…’ At that thought, the corners of her lips curled upward, revealing a smile full of intrigue and amusement.

“Guess I’ll play with you guys for a bit, and harvest a nice batch of leeks while I’m at it.” Even before she finished speaking, the tree branches quivered, and Yae-hime’s figure vanished in an instant.

At the same moment, in the real world, Okinawa.

Lucky stepped out of the airport with his entourage, his overwhelming presence so intense that even ordinary bystanders could feel it.

Actually, what they felt was actually the suffocating pressure exuded by the tall, broad-shouldered men in black suits trailing behind him.

As for Lucky himself, he looked more like an ordinary, well-off middle-aged man in a traditional Chinese jacket.

“Grandmaster Hong!” Not far off, a middle-aged man in a white Taoist robe with a black belt called out with delight.

Behind him stood more than a dozen other men in Taoist robes, though their belts came in a variety of vibrant colors. They were all dark-skinned and powerfully built, their expressions stern and vaguely exuding murderous intent. One look and you could tell they weren’t people to mess with.

“Grandmaster Ota, it’s been too long. I hope you’ll forgive my lack of greetings.” Lucky walked up and cupped his hands respectfully.

“Come now, we’re like brothers. You make us sound like strangers with talk like that.” The man known as Grandmaster Ota patted Lucky on the shoulder with a grin.

“That’s true. Even after more than a decade, you haven’t changed… you’re still just as warm and commanding as ever.” Lucky returned the shoulder pat, his face blooming with a radiant smile like a chrysanthemum in full bloom.

“You, on the other hand, have grown even more impressive over the years!” Ota clapped his shoulder even harder. The very air rippled from the impact.

Not to be outdone, Lucky responded with even greater force. A series of _thud thud thud_ echoed through the scene.

Both entourages tensed instantly, the atmosphere thickening with pressure, making it hard to breathe.

“Ota, I think that’s enough for a test. Let’s not scare the juniors.” Lucky withdrew his hand with a calm smile, as if completely unfazed by the exchange.

“Hahaha! Lucky, your strength is truly formidable. Please forgive my offense.” Grandmaster Ota laughed heartily. He, too, was an Intermediate Grandmaster, only a month ahead of Lucky in reaching that realm.

“Your strength is just as impressive,” Lucky replied, subtly hiding his slightly reddened hand behind his back.

“Hahaha, we’re evenly matched.” Ota clenched his fist, his entire arm trembling faintly. It was clear both men had taken some damage from their little test.

Fortunately, injuries at that level would heal quickly and wouldn’t affect the duel scheduled for the evening. Both had exercised good judgment in controlling their strength.

“I’ve already prepared a banquet at my dojo. Been waiting for your arrival.” Ota smiled warmly, looking as harmless as a friendly neighbor, which only made the savage aura of the men behind him stand out even more.

“Then I’ll gladly accept your hospitality,” Lucky replied, still smiling like a blooming chrysanthemum.

The two groups made their way to the parking lot together. There, more than a dozen business vehicles and a few large motorcycles were parked.

Lucky and Grandmaster Ota shared one car. When the fleet of vehicles and motorcycles rolled out together, the sight was more than a little impressive. Anyone unaware might’ve mistaken it for the motorcade of a visiting head of state from a small nation.

“Ota, have the ships to Baiding Island been arranged?” Inside the car, Lucky leaned back in his seat and asked in a low voice.

“Already taken care of,” Ota replied with a casual air.

“I really owe you for this one,” Lucky said with a slight frown. “The local branch has been completely unreliable.”

Originally, members of the local branch were supposed to pick him up from the airport and take him to Ota’s dojo together. But the entire branch had come down with food poisoning, all half-dead and bedridden, forcing Ota to come fetch him personally.

Naturally, Lucky was far from pleased. Those branch members had completely embarrassed him.

“Mass incidents like that are truly disastrous.” Ota shook his head lightly before continuing, “By the way, Lucky…Grandmaster Kim from Korea has already arrived at my dojo. Before long, experts from the surrounding countries will gather as well. Your influence really is something to behold.”

“Hehehe, they’re just doing me a favor, that’s all.” Receiving such lavish praise, Lucky grinned from ear to ear, clearly pleased.

“Favor or not, influence comes from power. The fact they’re willing to come proves that your strength is widely recognized.” At that, Ota changed the subject with a hint of curiosity, “By the way, how confident are you about this duel? To be honest, I’m planning to place a big bet on your victory.”

Lucky had initially felt a flare of irritation from that question, but hearing the latter half, his mood instantly improved. With a smile, he replied, “I wouldn’t dare say one hundred percent, but I’d wager ninety-nine percent odds.”

His words were filled with utter confidence.

“Good!” Ota clapped his hands. “That’s the Lucky I know! Such confidence, such presence! Just like a Northern War God, unstoppable!”

“Haha, you flatter me,” Lucky said, rubbing his nose. “It’s just a kid who’s newly stepped into the Grandmaster realm, nothing to be concerned about. To be frank, this so-called Princess is merely the first sacrificial offering in my counterattack against Cathay’s martial world. I will make her a blood sacrifice, and let the entire world know— that I, Lucky, have returned as a king!”

As he recalled the humiliation of being driven out of Cathay in the past, Lucky’s heart trembled with rage.

“All that I lost that day…I’ll reclaim it, with interest!”

Beside him, Grandmaster Ota watched Lucky grow increasingly agitated. After a brief hesitation, he discreetly pulled out his phone and placed a five million bet on Princess.

Not out of loyalty or sympathy, but simply, just in case.

+++

# 704 – The Blackhearted Princess’ Mercy

In the game, outside the Mangrove Forest.

“Roar!”

A massive, mysterious beast wreathed in dark energy let out a thunderous roar. Its long tail whipped out like a lash, sending the surrounding players flying. However, there were simply too many players. No matter how hard the beast tried to retaliate, the players swarmed in like an endless tide of ants, relentlessly charging forward.

Further away, a few solo players and hidden scouts stood by, merely spectating.

At the same time, both in and out of the game, the livestream rooms were bustling with activity. The chat barrage was firing off like a machine gun.

To watch the livestream, even many foreign players still in-game were cursing the company for being greedy, while obediently paying the fee to access the cross-server stream.

In that moment, the Linhnan server once again became the center of attention.

“That’s odd. This boss doesn’t seem to hit very hard. It’s been going on for so long and no one’s died yet.” A player in the outer crowd spoke with confusion.

“Now that you mention it, that big guy does look fierce, swinging with all his might, but it’s been ages and not a single death.”  

“Yeah, yeah. This is the weakest boss I’ve ever seen.”  

“I don’t think it’s that strange. This is a hidden boss, after all. It’s bound to be different from the usual ones.”  

“That makes sense. This one must be a defense-type boss. Look, with so many people beating on it, its HP barely drops. The defense is seriously impressive.”  

“Shame its attack is so weak though.”

The crowd buzzed with speculation and commentary. While regular players didn’t think much of it, scouts from other guilds couldn’t shake the feeling that something wasn’t quite right.

Far away in the American server, Dorado, Mira was also watching the livestream. Her brow furrowed slightly, her face full of suspicion.

“This whole fight looks like a farce…” With plenty of boss battle experience under her belt, Mira could tell this wasn’t a real boss fight. If anything, it looked more like a clumsy performance.

“This boss must be some kind of special summon. And they’re putting so much effort into staging this farce…” At that moment, a stunning figure suddenly flashed through Mira’s mind. “So that’s what this is. Of course. It’s all for her, isn’t it? Hehehe… things are getting interesting.”

Very few people realized it was all an act. The vast majority were still in the dark. They genuinely believed it was just an unconventional boss battle.

Inside the Mangrove Forest, S.K.Y. and Taurus stared intently at the stream, their faces filled with tension and anticipation. Behind them stood a dense crowd of players. These were all elite members of the Death of Love guild.

They were waiting here for the main character…no, they were waiting for the arrival of that walking treasure trove in human form.

“It’s been twelve hours since that shadow creature was summoned. The cooldown’s already passed and it still hasn’t disappeared.” Taurus suddenly spoke.

“Looks like once this shadow creature is summoned, it won’t vanish unless it’s killed.” S.K.Y. replied.

“Heh, we hit the jackpot. I thought we’d end up wasting a usage.” Taurus chuckled as he looked at the [Shadow Horn] in his hand. As it turned out, that strange boss outside had been summoned using this horn, which they had obtained earlier in the underground labyrinth.

Just as Mira had guessed, the whole event was a setup, crafted with one particular person in mind.

“It’s been half a day. Why hasn’t the Blackhearted Princess shown up yet?” Taurus put away the horn and looked to S.K.Y.

With a calm expression, S.K.Y. said, “She’s a wanted criminal in the Empire. She’ll have fled somewhere remote. Getting back here isn’t going to be quick. Calm down for now, Master Zhang.”

“I’m just worried she won’t dare to show up,” Taurus said.  

“She will. The Blackhearted Princess will definitely come,” S.K.Y. declared with certainty.  

Taurus raised a brow and asked, “Why are you so sure?”

S.K.Y. brushed his bangs aside and replied confidently, “Because I know her. That Blackhearted Princess is greedy to her core. From the Beginner Village to Jade City, everything she’s done reeks of greed. Last time she ‘stole a chicken’ and reaped huge rewards. This time, she’ll try to steal a chicken again. And in the end, she’ll pay the ultimate price for her greed!”

Hearing that, Taurus recalled the time he had been tricked by the Blackhearted Princess and found the statement all too true.

“Greed leads only to ruin.” He, too, pushed back his hair, his handsome face gleaming with a sinister glint. “Why don’t people ever learn?”[1](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-704-the-blackhearted-princess-mercy/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-110536)　

“Indeed,” S.K.Y. nodded, a faint red gleam flashing through his eyes. The night before, he had already left Huadu in secret. By now, no one knew where he was. ‘Once this succeeds, my true rise will begin.’

At that thought, the corners of S.K.Y.’s mouth curled up into a cruel smile.

Just then, the magic array map in his hand suddenly vibrated. A green dot lit up on it.

It was a regional detection magic device they had borrowed from a direct army unit. As long as detection tools were set up in the area, the device could identify targets within a specified level range.

Their target level was set to 30. Whenever a level 30 player or NPC entered the vicinity of the Mangrove Forest, the square-shaped array map would trigger an alert and lock onto the target’s position.

“A green dot, that’s the Blackhearted Princess!” S.K.Y. exclaimed excitedly.

Targets that entered detection range were color-coded: blue for NPCs, green for players. Currently, there was only one level 30 player. Clearly, that wretched Blackhearted Princess had stepped right into their trap!

“She finally came!” Taurus clenched his fists tightly, his face overflowing with wild delight.  

“Yes, and she thinks we don’t know. She’s probably out there watching the show,” S.K.Y. said, overjoyed.  

“Have the outside players scatter and begin encircling her… Wait! Make it look real, don’t scare her off!” Taurus spoke with mounting excitement. He had never felt this thrilled in his life, as if injected with pure adrenaline.

‘After today, I’ll be nʌmbər wʌn[2](https://re-library.com/translations/reborn-as-a-transcendent/volume-3/chapter-704-the-blackhearted-princess-mercy/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-110536) in this game!’ Just imagining all the treasures the Blackhearted Princess carried ending up in his possession sent a wave of exhilaration through him.

“Got it!” S.K.Y., struggling to contain his excitement, quickly relayed Taurus’ orders to the outside forces.

Soon enough, the players within the Mangrove Forest began responding. While pretending to fight, they slowly pulled back, tightening the encirclement toward the outskirts.

The players watching the show still had no idea what was happening. It wasn’t until a swarm of Death of Love members closed in that they realized something was wrong, and fled in a panic.

Unfortunately, it was already too late. That entire area had been completely sealed off by Death of Love guild members!

At that moment, the colossal shadow beast came charging in. The players at the front were instantly torn to shreds, and those with slightly lower levels were crushed into dust. Only the players above level 20 barely clung to life. Even so, they were gravely wounded.

The shadow beast rampaged like an out-of-control dump truck, flinging players into the air like bowling pins. The air filled with relentless screams of agony.

That ferocity, it was a world apart from before. The runaway dump truck—no, rampaging shadow beast—charged straight ahead with unstoppable momentum. At this rate, it looked like the slaughter would be completely one-sided.

However, just as everyone thought so, a pale, jade-like hand suddenly appeared and gently pressed against the shadow beast. In the next instant, the rampaging beast was forcibly halted in its tracks. The force of its charge exploded outward.

Players nearby were blown off their feet, tumbling about in a pitiful mess.

“Now that’s interesting.” The one who had stopped the shadow beast dead in its tracks was none other than Yae-hime, who had been quietly watching from the crowd.

“It’s the Blackhearted Princess! She’s here!” One of the players who hadn’t been caught in the shockwave immediately recognized her and shouted excitedly.

“She’s here too?!”  

“Why did she suddenly step in to help?”  

“No, that beast was clearly charging at her! We were just caught in the crossfire!”  

“A setup, this was all a setup!”

Realization began to dawn on the players present, and cries of alarm echoed through the crowd. At that moment, both in-game and in real-world livestreams, the screens were flooded with barrage comments. Shock and disbelief spilled through the chat like a wave.

No one could have guessed that this so-called boss fight was actually a trap set specifically for the Blackhearted Princess! What stunned them even more was that the jet-black beast wasn’t a boss at all, but a monster under someone’s control!

In that moment, countless players were left in disbelief at the Linhnan server’s stunning level of innovation, along with a flood of jealousy and envy they couldn’t conceal.

“Are we even playing the same game?” Many players echoed the same sentiment in unison.

“Just as I thought.” Mira gazed at the stunning girl on the screen, a smile of confirmation spreading across her face. “Now let’s see how you plan to deal with this crisis.”

Outside the Mangrove Forest, the atmosphere grew tense and deadly. All the members of Death of Love had their eyes locked onto Yae-hime, awaiting the signal to launch an all-out assault.

“I’ll give you two seconds to log out. Anyone still here after that…dies.” Suddenly, Yae-hime spoke. Her voice wasn’t loud. But everyone present, and all those watching the livestream, heard her loud and clear.

A flood of question marks popped up above everyone’s heads. Was the Blackhearted Princess out of her mind? She was the one in an absolutely disadvantageous position. And yet she had the audacity to make such a bold threat? It was utterly laughable!

From their perspective, surrounded by nearly ten thousand players and a boss-tier beast, the Blackhearted Princess had zero chance of survival.

“One.” That graceful voice rang out again. Yet no one reacted. Neither Death of Love’s players nor the spectators from other guilds or solo players made a move. They simply waited for the battle to begin.

“Two!” As her countdown ended, the shadow beast under her pale hand suddenly flew backward. A terrifying force burst forth from its body, carving a deep trench into the earth and sending soil flying into the air.

On the other side, a sword wreathed in flames materialized in Yae-hime’s hand. Her slender, snow-white fingers gripped the tip of its hilt as she softly spoke four words, “Ancient Celestial Sword Formation.”

Then, with a light release of her fingers, the [Dragonsorch] sword dropped straight down.

+++

# 705 – The Might of the Sword Formation

At that moment, everyone present felt an incredibly sharp aura. It was as if their entire nervous system had been pricked by needles, bringing a rush of exquisite, tingling pain.

Though the attack had yet to be unleashed, the terrifying prelude alone filled the crowd with dread and terror. Yet what came next was even more horrifying. The surrounding scenery distorted the instant the sword fell, as ripples spread outward at incredible speed. The entire world seemed to warp and twist!

Whether it was the players outside the Mangrove Forest or the viewers watching the livestream, they were all overwhelmed by an indescribable shock.

The sword landed with a sound. It was like striking something solid, yet to some, it looked as if the sword had plunged into water, sinking into the ground. At the same time, the sharp sword aura carved an enormous circle into the earth around it.

Within the circle, golden light flickered as formation patterns rapidly emerged. That piercing aura intensified, like countless sharp blades slashing viciously across everyone’s skin.

Pain. An indescribable pain. There were no visible wounds, yet it felt worse than being torn apart.

Before this phantom pain had even faded, a clap of thunder rang out, shaking their ears. The skies changed color! Ferocious winds swept across the battlefield, lightning cracked, thunder roared, and the ground trembled, like the end of the world had arrived!

It was the first time the livestream audience had witnessed such a terrifying ultimate move. Their scalps tingled as they trembled with excitement.

But no—this was only the prelude!

The viewers were stunned. The players on-site, however, were seized with fear. The chilling dread of imminent death! Run. They had to run immediately. Staying here meant certain death!

Some players attempted to log out of the game. Unfortunately, it was already too late. A terrifying divine force suddenly enveloped the entire area, pinning everyone down, including the rampaging shadow beast, rendering them completely immobile.

The scent of death quietly filled the air.

“Activate!” Within the formation, Yae-hime let out a soft command. In that instant, the formation was fully activated, unleashing a surge of metallic essence and ancient power.

The next moment, the golden energy transformed into countless blades, wildly rampaging within the array.

Even through the virtual screen, S.K.Y. and Taurus could feel that bone-chilling aura of ultimate slaughter.
