『Her Job should also be sorcery-oriented, but her being bad with magic is likely not easy to resolve. Having stamina wouldn’t be a waste no matter what field you’ll be working in, so I don’t think joining this course is a bad idea at all.』

I’d love to just continue chatting with Ciel, but Palra and Belltina positioned themselves on the opposite sides of Ciel, hiding behind Ciel while peeping at each other. What is this situation?  

They’re doing this with the smallest being between them, so it must look comical to an outsider.

『What should we do about this?』  

『Hmm… It could be a good idea to introduce them to each other.』

While it’s a bit interesting just observing them as is, since Ciel is troubled being sandwiched between them, I presented a solution. Rather, normally they should be introduced to each other by now, right?  

Ideally, it would be nice if Palra asked who the mystery girl is, but that’s probably impossible. Meanwhile, there’s even less of a chance Belltina would do that. After all, even though she was able to speak to Ailneige around lunchtime—perhaps because Palra wasn’t there—she’s staying completely silent now.

At my suggestion, Ciel turned around, only for Belltina to hurriedly shift out of her line of sight. However, Ciel turned too quickly, catching the full extent of Belltina’s clumsy attempt to hide.  

Ciel already knew that Belltina was around, and she might have also noticed Belltina trying to avoid her line of sight, so she didn’t comment about her timid hiding.

「Belltina, you’re here.」  

「B-Bell really was found out!」

From her words and tone, she must have noticed our detection ability.  

She has quite the good eyes; it’s a shame that she’s not making the best out of it.  

With Ciel confronting Belltina, Palra appears to have gained the confidence to ask about her: 「Ailneige, who is she?」  

With the ideal situation suddenly set, Ciel provided a brief introduction.

「This is Belltina, my seatmate during Magic Circle Studies. And this here is Palra, my seatmate in Class A.」

That wasn’t a lot of information, but knowing each other’s names should be enough for a first meeting.  

Beyond this, I hope the two of them will do their best to get along. After all, whether it be about Palra or Belltina, Ailneige probably won’t be able to provide more information.

「N-nice to meet you. My name is Palra.」  

「Nice…to meet…」

How do I say this? That introduction sounded quite reluctant, as if she only spoke out of obligation.  

However, it seems like Belltina truly is the shyest between them, as she not only hid behind Ail, but she also couldn’t even respond with her name.  

The reason why Palra was able to communicate somewhat decently might be partly due to how small Belltina is.

I was prepared for awkward silence after this, but surprisingly, Palra initiated a conversation.

「Belltina, are you aspiring to be a hunter too?」  

「For Bell… Not really. But Bell thinks that if things don’t go well, Bell might have to become a hunter.」  

「I see. For me, I only had becoming a hunter in my mind and nothing else… You’re amazing, Belltina.」  

「Bell, amazing?」  

「Yup. But then we might not be able to be hunters together; that makes me feel a bit sad.」

『They seem to be hitting it off.』  

『They get over their shyness fast… perhaps they’re just on the same wavelength.』  

『Like Ain and I?』  

『I don’t think they’re at our level. Our time together is incomparable to theirs, after all.』  

『Yes, yes! That’s right, absolutely right!』  

『At any rate, it would be a lot easier for us if the two of them became friends.』

They’ll probably continue staying with Ailneige in the future.  

I’ve said a lot of things about them up until now, but having a friendly conversation like this is honestly difficult for us, so I really hope the two of them can have it between themselves.

『Will it really?』  

『I’m sure that we’ll need to form a party at some point in this course, and grouping with them would be a safe bet.』  

『Good point. It’ll be much better compared to having strangers.』

Hunters don’t typically go solo. Being able to divvy up roles is important, and most people don’t have the luxury of owning a magic pouch, so in most cases, it’s more profitable to act in groups.  

There are even requests that can only be accepted by a party of multiple people. That’s why I believe that we’re going to have to move as a party in the near future.  

It is possible that we’ll be grouped randomly, but I don’t think they’ll do that this early on.

As Belltina was starting to be convinced that maybe being a hunter could be a good choice, our teacher Ishparht made his appearance. Today, there are other adults around too: the spearman we’ve met before, a sorcerer-looking lady, and another lady wearing nimble-looking clothes.  

Considering their balance, perhaps they’re a four-man party who accepted a request to teach?  

Since Ailneige is only interested in swordsmanship, we probably won’t have much interaction with the teachers outside of Ishparht.

They also brought a cart loaded with a large variety of weapons. These are likely for training use.

「Today, we’ll start with 15 laps as well.」

The class started with Ishparht’s announcement, which was met with boos.

To be more exact, part of the students groaned with disappointment, while the others were mad and asked why.

「And once you’re done, you can proceed to weapons handling, so decide on your weapon before then.」  

「Teacher!」  

「What is it?」  

「If we can’t finish 15 laps within the class period, are we just going to run for the entirety of this course?」

Hearing Ishparht’s words, a sorcerer-ish student posed a question.  

Most enrolled in this course to learn combat, so they’re probably concerned that it’ll only end in stamina training.

「We’ll gradually decrease the running time and distance, so no need to worry about that.」  

「…Understood. Thank you very much.」

I can understand being dissatisfied by Ishparht’s answer, but this is probably arranged so that they can instruct each student based on their progression.  

Only those with a good physical foundation－with sufficient stamina－can proceed to the next step, because swinging around a weapon you can’t properly handle is dangerous.

Several other students still weren’t convinced, but Ishparht paid no heed and simply cut off their questions.  

That seems a bit forceful, but if he answers each and every one of them, this period might end with only that, so no complaints from me.

「Now then, begin.」

With Ishparht’s signal, the students started running.  

This time, everyone went all at once, and Palra didn’t have a late start like before.

「U-umm… Ailneige…」  

「I’ll be running at full speed today, so I believe it’ll be best you don’t try to keep up.」  

「O-okay. Do your best.」  

「You too. And Belltina, please don’t overextend yourself.」  

「The truth is, Bell is thinking that this might already be too much for Bell…」

As Belltina shared her thoughts, Ciel upped her pace, not staying to listen.

『I can use physical reinforcement today, right?』  

『We didn’t enroll on this course to run, after all, and you already have enough in terms of stamina.  

But we are acting the part of an E-rank hunter, so it’ll be best to hold back a bit…』  

『Yup, I’m taking that into consideration. But we’ll end up standing out, right?』  

『An active E-rank hunter standing out in a basic-level course isn’t strange at all, so it should be fine.』

We’re basically one step away from being able to graduate anyway, and it’s not like Ailneige is concealing the fact that she’s E-rank. The only problem is that we don’t know how fast an average E-rank hunter is, but we can make up excuses for that problem.  

And so we finished the 15 laps, but there’s still around half of the period remaining. No one was able to keep up with Ciel, but I believe Rynaetra could do so if she wanted to.  

Among the fast ones are Princess Leshimiiya (with Rynaetra) and Palra. There should be others who can keep up with them, but many wore themselves out trying to match Ciel’s pace.

As for Belltina, she appears to have retired early on, as she’s curled up by the oval’s edge right now.

「I’m finished.」  

「Again, you’re pretty fast.」  

「Despite appearances, I am an E-rank hunter.」

As Ciel informed Ishparht that she’s done with the laps, he didn’t show any surprise at all.  

Since he knows that Ailneige is a hunter, this was probably within his estimations. From his respose, it seems like Ciel ran at a speed adequate for an E-rank hunter. In that case, we could try going a bit faster next time. Though by we, I mean Ciel.

「So, you want to learn how to use a rapier, was it?」  

「Yes. Since I have no proper knowledge of the basics.」  

「Ever wielded one before?」  

「I’ve brandished one a few times in the past.」  

「Then let’s assess your current level for now.」

Saying so, he picked out one sword from the pile of weapons and handed it to us.  

What Ciel received was a simple, unadorned rapier. It’s light enough for Ciel to swing with one hand with the aid of physical reinforcement and doesn’t seem to have a sharp edge.

Ciel swung the sword in an ∞ pattern to test it out, creating a pleasant whistling sound.

「I’ll stay on defensive, so could you trying hitting me for a bit?」  

『What should I do?』

In other words, she’s asking if we can use Sword Dancer-esque—Dance Princess’ capabilities.  

We are currently in the center part of the oval. The students running on the outer edge won’t be disrupted by us, but it’s a conspicuous position. Moreover, since Ailneige finished first, we’ve already attracted considerable attention.

『It should be fine not to worry too much. After all, you’ve never swung a sword without Job assistance.』  

『Understood.』  

『But just to be sure, it might be better to inform him that you’ll be doing it your own way.』  

「I’ll be utilizing my Job’s capabilities.」  

「Have you normally used a sword before?」  

「Never.」  

「I see. Then try attacking me the best you can.」

Ishparht pulled out a one-handed sword and took on a battle stance.  

Ciel also took a battle stance, but their stances are completely different. With her body leaning forward onto one leg and her arms lowered, I’m not even sure it qualifies as a proper stance.

「Here I go.」

And since this is training, Ciel called out before making her move.

◇◇◇

「Okay, I’ve got a clearer gist of it now.」  

「I’m glad to hear that.」  

「Your sword-handling’s pretty lacking compared to your movements.」  

「Figures, I was completely reliant on my Job.」  

「But in my opinion, your movements itself wasn’t bad at all.」

As the striking test finished, Ishparht gave his assessment of Ciel’s Job-reliant sword swings.  

The Dance Princess is considered worse than a low-tier Job on its own, so it wasn’t surprising. The praise about Ciel’s movements probably speaks more about her dance proficiency than her sword skill.

「For now, I guess we’ll start from the basic slashes.」  

「I’m in your care.」  

「Now, I’m going to show how it’s done, so try mimicking me.」

Ishparht changed his weapon to a rapier and took on a fighting stance.  

He put his left hand behind his back, stepped forward with one foot, and swung the sword downwards.  

For me, it only looked like a normal slow swing downwards, but Ciel seemed to have gleaned something from it, as she asked with a serious expression, 「Could you do it one more time?」

After seeing Ishparht’s exemplar swing several more times, Ciel’s following practice swing immediately received passing marks.

+++

# 167: Sorceric Tools and God

It’s the third day of our campus life. For today, we have a course in Sorceric Tool Studies. The academy seems to put great importance on this subject, as it’s held in a large room capable of receiving a considerable number of students.  

Though perhaps it was just assigned a large room due to the sheer number of enrollees.  

With its size, it looks less like a school classroom and more like a university lecture hall.

By the time I entered the room, around half of the seats were already occupied, and many gazes were immediately directed to me upon entry. While we have been attracting eyes even in other classrooms, here I feel the most amount of stares yet.  

This must be because there are overwhelmingly more male students here. It’s not like there aren’t any girls, but boys probably consist of around 80% of the students.

As such, we sat down some distance away from the male crowd.  

Almost immediately after, we were approached by a familiar girl who asked, 「Can I sit next to you?」 By no means did she leave a good impression on our previous meeting, so did she approach us aware of that, or did she completely forget what happened?

While she didn’t leave a good impression, she was just annoyingly aggressive; as long as she can control herself, it’s all good.

「Feel free to do as you wish, Tietta.」  

「Then if you’d excuse me.」

With that, Palra’s roommate Tietta sat next to me.  

Let’s just say that this is better than having an unknown male student next to me. Still, what do I do if a boy tries to sit next to us in the future?  

I can’t really think of any convincing reason to stop them from sitting down, but on the other hand, they might annoyingly try to initiate conversations; I already feel miserable imagining it. Well, I’ll think about it when it happens.

「I’m surprised you’re here, Ailneige. If I recall, weren’t you already an active hunter?」  

「I’m just here out of curiosity. And I might be able to use what I learn here for my hunter work. Still, Tietta, you don’t specialize in sorceric tools either, do you?」  

「Yeah. I want to focus on armor, or rather outfits. However, if I use accessory-styled sorceric tools to supplement protection, don’t you think it can provide more leeway for design freedom?」  

「Perhaps it could.」

When speaking of sorceric tools hunters use, the magic pouch is the first to come to mind, but it’s not actually that accessible in reality. You can’t even acquire one without being a high-ranked hunter, so it’s only natural.  

While accessory-type sorceric tools do exist, they’re apparently also quite expensive, so they probably aren’t really common to find among hunters either.

Still, we barely had the opportunity to be in a party, and joining one isn’t necessary for us, so my knowledge is only based on hearsay.  

However, if there is a sorceric tool that can deploy a barrier, I believe it’ll probably be somewhat popular.  

In that form, a barrier can be deployed immediately, and even people who can’t use sorcery can utilize it. The rear support can use it to guard against stray attacks and debris, while front-liners can hold one as an emergency precaution.

And if the barrier can remain active for a long time, then the user could probably go as far as to work in their pajamas. No, I guess that’ll depend on the potency of the barrier spell.

「So, Ailneige, you’re a hunter, right?」  

「An E-rank hunter, but a hunter nonetheless.」  

「Then do you use leather chest armor? A thick cloak? Hunters tend not to use heavy armor, right?」  

「My equipment isn’t much different from the standard sorcerer hunter gear.」

Since we requested it to be designed that way.

「I guess it really is function over form, huh… Mobility and defense can’t really be neglected, but if you focus on those, your outfit will inevitably end up looking rough…」

In our case, we could probably do our hunter work in a fashionable dress, but I understand that this isn’t normal.  

What we need from our equipment is not protective capability, but ease of movement… Well, that’s also important, but what we actually need the most is equipment that makes us look like a nondescript hunter. If anything ever bypasses my barrier, what we’re wearing probably wouldn’t make any difference anyway.  

In a sense, we do value fashion like Tietta does, but we’re aiming in a completely different direction. Though if hunters had a status entry specifically for assessing fashion, we’d probably be fashionable just to fit in.

「Using powerful monster materials results in sturdy but light equipment, though.」  

「That’d go against my purpose. Most importantly, I can’t handle those materials.」  

「I’ve heard that you can wear chain mail under your clothes, so perhaps you could focus on adding protection where it can’t be seen?」  

「That’s one way around it, huh. Then you might be able to wear fashionable clothes on top of it.」

That said, other people have probably already come up with the same idea. Chainmail specifically made for sorcerers has already been developed.  

Still, it seems like something about this idea stood out to Tietta, as she’s currently groaning in deep contemplation.

「Don’t you ever wish you could style up more?」  

「It’s hard to say; I prioritize survival, after all.」  

『I do wish that you’d be more stylish, though.』  

『Oh, but I am stylish when it comes to getting Ain adorable outfits, aren’t I? Besides, I also have more adorable clothes these days.』  

『We did get dressed in a lot of clothes back at the manor.』

As I chatted with Ciel while keeping the mumbling Tietta in the corner of my eye, someone was approaching from the seat next to me, opposite of Tietta. Glancing that way, I see Belltina timidly sitting down, so I lightly wave my hand her way.

She got along with Palra, but Belltina probably has terrible compatibility with Tietta. Belltina’s eyes went wide open in surprise before she responded with a conservative wave.

While this transpired, the Sorceric Tool Studies teacher arrived.

The name of our Sorceric Tool Studies teacher is Liens Coltraw.  

He’s a former court sorcerer who was enamored with sorceric tools, leading to him quitting and becoming an academy teacher, or so they say. His name wasn’t mentioned in the Princess’ excellent individuals list, so he must not have left many achievements during his court sorcerer days. Perhaps it’s because he couldn’t achieve much as a court sorcerer that he walked the sorceric tools path instead.  

Well, it’s all just groundless speculation on my part, and even if it turns out to be true, then that doesn’t really change anything.

Liens is a man in his forties with salt-and-pepper hair and glasses; he appears to have a cheerful, or rather laid-back, demeanor.

「As today is our first meeting, our discussion will start from the very basics of Sorceric Tool Studies. But first, does anyone here know the difference between an artificer without an Artificer Job and those that do?」

Liens gave the students a question, which was followed by several hands raised in the air.  

I don’t know the answer, so I stayed a spectator. Though I probably wouldn’t raise my hand even if I did.

「First is that if you don’t have the Job, a special sorceric tool is needed when crafting a sorceric tool. Another is that there are sorceric tools that can only be made by those with the Job.」

The teacher nodded to the nameless student’s answer.

「Broadly speaking, those two are the most significant. A prominent example of an item only those with the Job can create is the magic pouch. While it also depends on the size, it’s said that only skilled artificers can craft them.  

The sorceric tool protecting the royal throne can only be created by Artificer Job as well.」  

『A sorceric tool being able to inhibit the use of sorcery is awfully weird, after all.』  

『That’s true.』  

『By the way, it sounds like Ain can’t make a magic pouch; is that alright?』

Ciel asked with a teasing tone. It might sound like sarcasm depending on how you take it, but I know that Ciel isn’t being malicious.  

We’ve already considered the possibility; she’s asking me with confidence that I can probably make a magic pouch.  

The faith she has in me feels quite heavy, but even if I can’t make one, I’m sure Ciel won’t mind it. Be that as it may, I already have some speculation about how it can be done. But I don’t even know how to craft a sorceric tool normally, so that’s where I’ll have to start.

『The discussion is about what can and can’t be done with the Job, so I think that there are ways around it.』  

『You won’t tell me how?』  

『It’ll be embarrassing if I end up being wrong.』  

『Oh, but I want to see Ain embarrassed, though?』  

『I don’t want to be embarrassed with this.』  

『_With this_, huh.』

Ciel was somewhat chipper, but I know what she’s implying. It was as if I admitted that it’s fine to embarrass me through other things.  

Still, if that can make Ciel happy, then I can endure a little embarrassment. Not that I plan on ever feigning embarrassment.  

Nonetheless, embarrassing things are embarrassing, so I would appreciate it if Ciel refrained from such acts.

「For those that don’t have the Artificer Job, you will need to use this sorceric quill pen.」

He then presented what, at first glance, appears to be a completely normal quill pen. If I have to comment on it, the quill it’s crafted from is bizarrely high quality.  

But this object is special. So special that I don’t even know if it’s right to call such a thing a sorceric tool.

「When utilizing this sorceric tool, it automatically absorbs your magic power and changes it into ink. And without a magic circle written by this ink, you can’t craft a sorceric tool. Normally, you would need to purchase this from a temple or the church, but you will be lent one while you are here in this academy, so you don’t need to worry about not owning one. You will have to return it by the end of our course, so make sure not to damage or lose it.」  

『It can be bought from the church?』  

『It’s probably made using some connection to the divine, you see.』  

『Oh, is that so?』  

『That’s how it feels, at least.』

While I can’t really give a proper explanation, it has some indescribable divine-ish quality to it.  

Considering this world’s structure, defeating monsters and expending many magic cores is most preferable, so I’m confident that the Creator God actively endorses the production and use of sorceric tools, the very symbol of magic core consumption.

「I don’t have the Artificer Job, you see. This pen has served me very well and has been a beacon of inspiration for me. In my first attempts at making sorceric tools, I didn’t know of this pen’s existence.  

I tried to learn by imitation, but I couldn’t figure out what was wrong with my handiwork. After thorough research and experiments, I finally came to know of this pen, but by then, I was cast as a failure of a court sorcerer. Those dunces who can’t understand the wonders of sorceric tools—」  

「Teacher! Can we return to the main topic first?」

As Liens started speaking faster and faster, a student from the front called his attention.  

I assumed he had a laid-back personality, but it appears that he’s a complete sorceric tool geek. He’s not even an Artificer, yet he’s so obsessed to the point that he apparently got fired from being a court sorcerer; he could probably exhaust a whole hour just talking about sorceric tools if prompted.  

He’s so passionate about it, I suspect that he could probably match or outlast Carol and Mia’s sorcery tangents.  

Also, during his speed-rambling, he vaguely gave off mad scientist vibes.

_Why is someone like him a teacher?_ I thought, but perhaps there simply aren’t many teachers who can teach about sorceric tools.

Seemingly coming to his senses, Liens forced out a cough and then started writing on the board.

「In this basic-level course, I will require all of you to craft and present any one simple sorceric tool, so while it’s still early, please start thinking about what you would like to create. Once you’ve decided on that, inform me what you would like to submit so—」

And so, with the occasional derailment from Liens, the Sorceric Tool class was able to reach its end.

+++

# 168: Puppet Sorcery and Idle Chat

「It’s finally here!」  

『Time for the Puppet Sorcery course.』

Four days since opening; it’s finally the day for Ciel’s most awaited Puppet Sorcery course.  

Ciel has been in high spirits since early morning, so combined with how boring yesterday’s Hunter Studies was, Ciel’s anticipation is through the roof.  

Even without the class, the opportunity to be able to talk with Munyechka should be a good thing. She’s the first active S-rank hunter we’ve ever met, so we might be able to hear some interesting stories as well.

「You seem to be in a jovial mood.」  

「Today is the Puppet Sorcery course day.」  

「That’s quite exciting.」

Seeing Ciel’s excitement, Mia responded with a gentle tone.  

And then, as if realizing something, she continued.

「In that case, would you be making a doll of Lady Ainsel?」  

「I’m not so sure. But we should, I think?」  

「If that’s the case, then may I be bold to ask for a puppet of you two?」  

「Alright, but why is that?」  

「I want them to adorn the room.」

The sudden suggestion had Ciel tilt her head, puzzled. I’m confused about it as well.  

However, if you ask me if I want a Ciel puppet, I’m completely on board, so I can understand the sentiment. But a puppet of me is unnecessary.  

Some might think, _‘Well, the only difference is the color’_, but that’s not the case. Ciel is Ciel; I am me.

Ciel appeared to have finally digested Mia’s words, promising her, 「Eventually.」

「But it would certainly be nice to have an Ain puppet somewhere I can always see.」  

『I don’t think that’s really necessary.』  

「Unlike Ain, I don’t have many chances to see you in person, you know? Could I at least have a puppet to look at?」

Having a puppet of yourself on display would be genuinely embarrassing, so I firmly refused; however, I couldn’t think of any argument against Ciel’s request. Whenever I’m not in control, I can move freely to some extent, but that doesn’t seem to be the case for Ciel, so the only time she can see me in flesh is through the mirror.

If I were in her shoes, I’d at least want a puppet of Ciel, and I probably wouldn’t have been able to keep my motivation up back at the Rispelgia mansion in the first place.  

That’s why I gave up, telling Ciel, 『I understand. I’ll allow it,』 which she—with a blooming smile—replied, 「Thank you.」

『But first, it’s time to head to the academy.』  

「It’s already that time? In that case, we’ll be leaving now.」  

「Of course. Please take care.」

Sent off by Mia, we headed to the academy building.

◇◇◇

When heading out in the morning, we bump into Belltina.  

So in the end, the residents of this floor should be us, Belltina, Rulinia, Rynaetra, and Munyechka, I believe?  

Rulinia and Rynaetra are probably here for the princess, and Munyechka is part of the academy staff. Meanwhile we are who we are, so the only proper student here is probably Belltina. Though from Belltina’s words, she seriously doesn’t want to study, apparently.

After meeting with Belltina, we have small exchanges on the way to the academy, but since our classrooms are different, we quickly part ways.  

The miserable expression she showed before parting must be due to her not having any friends in her class. Stay strong.

There were no particular announcements today; we only had attendance checking, so we decided to head straight to the Puppet Sorcery classroom.  

I’m usually the one in control in the morning, but since today’s Puppet Sorcery is a morning class, Ciel is the one active. We only have Combat Training in the afternoon, so Ciel will be active the whole day today.  

While Ciel was against it, there really isn’t much that can be done since it’s our class schedule. Though depending on how many students are enrolled in Puppet Sorcery, it might be alright for us to switch out as we like.

Now, the Puppet Sorcery classroom is located deep inside the Sorcery Department building. We passed by several students on the way, but as we drew near to the classroom, there was no more human presence. There were no more voices or footsteps that could be heard.  

It looks like Puppet Sorcery is really unpopular. This probably reflects the public’s opinion on it. Recalling our conversation with Munyechka, there are even times when they don’t open the course to begin with.

「There you are.」

As we entered the Puppet Sorcery classroom, a girl’s high-pitched voice greeted us.  

The classroom was devoid of people except for Munyechka. Feeling around a bit, it seems like there are no other puppets today.  

She could at least have Semiette present, but perhaps it’s bothersome to have two of herself around.

「Nice to meet you. My name is Cielmer.」  

「You must be the host personality. I believe you already know me, but I’m Munyechka.」

I wondered how Ciel planned to present herself, but with her introducing herself as Cielmer, it seems like she’s going to act normally. While Ciel was a bit lacking in etiquette, since Munyechka doesn’t seem to be bothered, I’ll deem it acceptable.  

More importantly, Munyechka’s remark seems to have somewhat upset Ciel.

「No, no, that’s wrong. There’s no host or something between us. This body is my body, and also Ain’s body.」  

「I see, you seem to have a rare sort of relationship. My bad.」  

「As long as you understand. It is true that Ain came to me, after all.」  

「Uh-huh. Then once again, welcome, Cielmer.」  

「I’ll be in your care from today on, Munyechka.」

After exchanging greetings once again, Ciel sat down among the excess of chairs, and Munyechka sat next to her.

『Are we the only students enrolled in this course?』  

「Are there no other people coming?」  

「Yup. There aren’t that many people eccentric enough to take Puppet Sorcery, you see.」  

「Is that so? I believe I’m just living normally, though.」  

「Having the gall to say that despite the abilities you have makes you plenty eccentric.」

Ciel tilted her head, puzzled, but I can’t deny Munyechka’s claim. Though in our case, it’s more precise to say that it’s me and not Ciel who’s the actual eccentric. I’m the one sleeplessly researching sorcery nonstop, after all.  

Nonetheless, even without me, no one among Ciel’s peers can equal her in strength, so that does make her eccentric in a way.

「Well then, I suppose it’s time for class.」  

「That’s somewhat sudden.」  

「No one else is coming, you see? Frankly, there’s actually not much to teach you; having a chat would probably be more productive, if you ask me.」  

「But I want to learn Puppet Sorcery.」  

「You should be able to use Puppet Sorcery within the day, I think.」

Saying so, Munyechka retrieved a doll small enough to sit on her lap.

「Now, this is a doll for Puppet Sorcery; can you figure out how it’s used?」  

「Mnn… Can I touch it?」  

「Sure, since it’s teaching material. Touch as much as you like. I didn’t make it for myself, so it’s simple in construction.」

Receiving permission, Ciel began touching the doll. I was startled by its smooth texture, but it’s probably made of wood. It has a similar texture to well-polished wood… I think.  

It wore a very indigo dress, which Ciel stripped without any hesitation. Probably because she can’t examine it closely with the clothes on the way.  

Besides, Munyechka didn’t interject, so it should be alright.

Taking the dress off, it even has proper underwear, but now a magic circle drawn on its back can be seen.  

Other than that, it seems to use a magic core as well, so it must be a type of sorceric tool, categorically speaking.  

In that case, I just have to decipher the magic circle—and now I understand how it’s to be used. It has two magic circles, though, so that might be troublesome.

「I see. I need to do this, right?」

Ciel also understood quickly and immediately activated the magic circle. It doesn’t seem to use the magic power conductive ink from the other day, so Ciel circulated her magic power as she normally does.  

As for the doll’s mechanism, you must first activate the magic circle that operates separately from its sorceric tool functionality. After doing so, the magic circle that makes it function as a sorceric tool will automatically activate, resulting in magic power threads extending from the doll. Together with the first magic circle, this will allow the user to puppet the doll like a marionette.

Unlike an actual marionette, you don’t need to pull on the threads to make it move; you can control it with pure magic power, but it’s apparently easier to move it in tandem with your fingers until you get used to it. Like making it wink when you bend your right index finger, for example.

However, Ciel can already manipulate it with only her magic power, to a certain extent. It’s a bit clumsy, but Ciel is making the doll dance around and around the way she usually does.

「See? We’re pretty much half done with the course.」  

「Isn’t that too simple?」  

「Normal students aren’t capable of manipulating a doll purely through magic power alone, you know? Most wouldn’t be able to operate this doll’s magic circle to begin with.  

Skilled ones would only be able to activate it at most.」  

「Is this really enough for a course?」  

「Originally, students would be provided dolls to start with, on which they’d need to write a magic circle on. The first lessons would be learning the sort of magic circles and ink required for its functions.」  

「Is that ink different from normal ink? We don’t know much about it.」

Not only have we been using normal ink up until now; we’ve even drawn magic circles on the ground with only our shoes, so we honestly don’t know the difference.  

Munyechka responded, 「I expected as much,」 showing no sign of surprise.

「 Would I be correct to assume that you two didn’t even know of its existence before your enrollment here?」  

「Yes. Ain noticed when activating a magic circle during one class that it was so easy; she conversely had a hard time with it.」  

「Activating a magic circle for you two—particularly Ain—is probably as easy as breathing, isn’t it? That magic circle must have been made using general-purpose magic ink.」  

「There are other types?」  

「It’s basically differentiated by the medium you’ll be writing on. General-purpose ink isn’t particularly choosy. To be exact, it functions even on non-paper mediums, but it wouldn’t be as effective. Say that its efficacy is 10 on paper, it would only be 7 on other mediums.  

The other types of ink are made to suit specific mediums. For example, when writing on this doll, you’d use an ink specialized for wood. That one would have the efficacy of 8 on wood, but only has the efficacy of 2 on other mediums.」

「The general-purpose one seems to be the safest choice.」  

「Right. That’s why there’s normally no need to know this much. After all, it just becomes a little less conductive when not used on paper.  

The inks used for making sorceric tools are also special, which are apparently only taught in detail in Puppet Sorcery and Golemancy.」

I see. I understand, but honestly I don’t think we’d find much use for it. We haven’t had any difficulty with magic circles up to this point, so unless Ciel wants to try it, we probably won’t bother with these inks.

「Well, we probably won’t use it.」  

「You probably won’t. There’s a risk of becoming negligent with magic power control if you get too used to it, and it practically only helps in writing. Well, only a few think that way. People normally use aiding catalysts like staves and ink.  

Now then, back to the main topic, this course’s objective is for the students to be able to freely move a doll to some extent, so the only remaining thing to teach you is where to procure dolls.」  

「Couldn’t we craft one?」  

「I can, but it isn’t something any ordinary student can make. First, teaching how to craft sorceric tools is necessary, and at that point, there won’t be time to fulfill the actual course objective; frankly, it’ll be a different course altogether.」  

「That’s why this class isn’t popular, is it?」

Hearing Ciel’s blunt comment, Munyechka laughed before nodding.

+++

# 169: Doll, Condition, and Divine Punishment

「To be more exact, despite how technically and financially demanding it is, the dolls aren’t really that strong, or that useful, on their own—that’s likely the main cause of Puppet Sorcery’s unpopularity. Have you thought of what you could actually do with Puppet Sorcery?」  

「I’m just hoping that we could use it for Ain’s body, I guess?」  

「Right, you might have that goal in your case, but there aren’t many people like you. Having two souls inhabiting one body is a rarity among rarities.」  

「You say that, but I’ve been together with Ain since I was born.」

To be precise, Ciel’s birth should have happened first, so I haven’t exactly been with her since birth, but pointing it out would be pedantic, so forget about it.  

Talking about the happenings at Rispelgia isn’t exactly pleasant either.

「That honestly piques my interest, but let’s leave that for another day. Puppet Sorcery makes use of expensive sorceric tools in the form of dolls, which are not suited for straightforward combat. At best, it’s typically used to entertain children.」  

「That’s a very niche usage.」  

「It certainly is. And even people who can use it for play don’t really need it to entertain anyway.」

Saying so, 「Ogua, Mohmora, Palfor[1](https://re-library.com/translations/two-as-one-princesses/volume-6/chapter-169-doll-condition-and-divine-punishment-part-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-111110),」 Munyechka casts a spell, creating a mass of water. The water then turned into the shape of the bird and began flying inside the classroom.  

What was one bird of water eventually split into many, and, within a few minutes, there were several hundred small birds blanketing the entire ceiling.  

The clarity of her magic power’s flow was one of, if not the most beautiful I’ve ever seen, and if I had to do the same, I’m not confident that I could achieve the same.

Ciel, fully powered and with my support, could probably do something similar, not out of precise magic power manipulation, but through the use of a large amount of magic power, so it’s not exactly the same.

Side note, the sight of the innumerable water birds delighted the small spirits.

「This kind of play would delight an audience more, you see.」  

「Amazing. I don’t think I can do that at all.」  

「Ainsel can probably do it, can’t she?」  

「Really?」  

『I’m not really confident. I’ve spent most of my time only practicing barrier and detection, after all.』  

「She’s not really confident.」  

「Is that so? I figure she should be able to do it with her capabilities.」  

「She said it’s because she spent her time only on specific things.」  

「Hmnh….」

Munyechka stared with a meaningful gaze. Her gaze feels like it’s going through Ciel and is directly focused on me, but I really hope it’s just my imagination.  

Fearing any potential inquiries, I subtly guided Ciel to wonder why Munyecka thought of mastering Puppet Sorcery.  

With no signs of knowing my true intent, Ciel inquired Munyechka with pure curiosity in her eyes.

「Munyechka, why did you choose to learn Puppet Sorcery?」  

「Hm? It’s because I love dolls.」  

「Is that so?」  

「I’ve loved dolls since I was little, see. Due to that, my Job was also related to dolls, and after making and playing with dolls all the time, I grew capable of using Puppet Sorcery.」  

「And eventually achieved Puppet Magic, right?」  

「So it was the same case for you, then?」

Sharply reacting to Ciel’s words, Munyechka responded with her own question.  

Considering that response, I suppose we can be almost certain that Munyechka has also achieved magic.  

Now, normally this question should be answered with either confirmation or misdirection, but since Ciel was unfortunately not the one who had achieved magic, she couldn’t answer immediately.

『Can I?』  

『I don’t mind.』  

「Not me, but Ain. I can’t use magic.」  

「Uh-huh, I see.」

Once again, Munyechka stares with a meaningful gaze. As someone attuned to sorcery and magic, Ciel—or rather, my—existence must be quite the curiosity. Two souls sharing one body, each independently capable of using sorcery. Ciel might even gain magic eventually. And while we haven’t told Munyechka, we have different Jobs as well.  

Consequently, from an outside observer, Ciel may appear to possess two Jobs and even exhibit signs of magic usage. The fact that the soul houses both one’s magic power and Job could very well be a groundbreaking discovery. For an individual of Munyechka’s caliber, she might be able to glean a lot from just this information.

「For now, you’re actually Munyechka, right?」  

「Ah, so you… or rather Ainsel knows that I’m a doll, does she? I am the real, genuine Munyechka. I suppose it’s fine to tell you this, but in exchange for gaining magic, I lost my human body and gained this puppet body. And I’m not sure if it’s because of that, but I consequently no longer have what’s known as a life span. I’ve been alive for a couple hundred of years, although I don’t know if “alive” is the proper word for it.」  

「So you’re long-lived. Then do you know about Fii’s past?」  

「I can’t clearly recall when we first met, but objectively speaking, it should be a long time ago. Though, it probably doesn’t feel that long ago from Fiiya’s perspective.」  

「What kind of person was Fii back then?」  

「She shouldn’t have changed that much, I think? She was otherworldly yet easygoing, but tended to take extreme measures against hostilities. Ah, but I have heard that she was more rowdy in the past.」  

「She did say that she captured Tur.」

As Ciel chuckled to herself, Munyechka tilted her head in confusion.  

I don’t think many know of Tur’s existence, and those that do probably haven’t been to the den since Khyturi was given a name, so it’s normal for her to not know.  

Still, I’m surprised Munyechka casually shared that her sacrifice is the loss of her body. While I don’t think she has any reason to lie, she might be withholding an important portion of information.

Let’s set aside the speculation for now and focus on the conversation between Ciel and Munyechka.

「Who is Tur?」  

「The white dragon at the den’s lowest stratum, you know?」  

「You must be describing a true dragon, then. Thinking about it, that doesn’t sound implausible… To begin with, dens actually have a lowest stratum, huh.」  

「She apparently caught Tur from somewhere and dragged Tur into the den.」  

「That’s hard to believe, but I can’t deny that it’s possible with Fiiya.」  

「Tur is the only dragon I know, but are there others around?」

Dragons are touted for their great strength, but it’s true that we only know Tur. Wyverns are considered dragonkin, but they are also said to be far weaker than true dragons. Dragons are considered S-rank, so I think they should be around the strength of strata 80-90 monsters.  

But if beings of that level are roaming on the surface, wouldn’t every country be in constant high alert?

「There are, but the remaining dragons don’t leave their territory. The ones that used to wander were hunted down long ago, you see. Every so often, stray dragons will appear out of nowhere… but I’ve only seen two dragons in my lifetime.」  

「Then it’s probably hard to find them normally.」  

「That reminds me, another dragon has been defeated recently, reducing their numbers further.」  

「Oh, defeated, huh?」  

「Though I said recently, it was around several odd decades ago deep in the southern mountains.」  

「In other words, there’s a person who can defeat a dragon in the south?」  

「I suppose that would be the case. They’re probably still alive, I think?」

If they’re alive, that likely means that the experience of defeating the dragon must have increased their magic power capacity. In that case, I’d rather not deal with someone like that. We’ll probably go to the south eventually, so I’ll keep that in mind.

「That aside, could we go back to the topic of dolls?」  

「I thought I’d already explained enough about Puppet Sorcery, but is there anything else you want to know?」  

「It’s just a hunch, but Iena and the others are different from the dolls for Puppet Sorcery, aren’t they?」  

「They certainly are. Iena and Semiette are made with Puppet Magic.」  

「In that case, I’d like one of those.」

Since it’s meant to be my body, then a doll similar to the one used for Iena certainly would be better.  

I don’t really know how to move the standard sorceric dolls. Iena appears to be moving through a portion of Munyechka’s soul, so a doll like that might be more convenient for me to use.

「While I’m probably the only one who can make dolls like them, I can’t really just give one away that easily.」  

「Well, fair enough. Do you have some sort of bargaining point?」  

「I’m glad you’re quick on the uptake. Could you acquire several dolls’ worth of materials for me? I want to make new ones too, but material gathering is honestly such a chore. Also, I want to know the sacrifice you paid for your magic.」  

『What do you think?』  

『It would depend on the materials themselves, but for the sacrifice, I don’t really mind telling her.』

This is honestly something that probably should be kept secret, but if it’s to achieve Ciel’s wishes, then it’s negotiable. Since I’m always with Ciel, the sacrifice’s demerit doesn’t really matter anyway. In that sense, Munyechka’s demerit shouldn’t really affect her in combat either.  

Anyhow, it’s not a big problem. Just as Munyechka must have something else in her sleeve, I do as well.

「That won’t be a problem. What materials do you need?」  

「I’ll talk about it eventually. We’ll start the actual gathering after we finish the entire Puppet Sorcery course content.」  

「Oh, that’s a shame.」  

「This is a proper class, after all. If we don’t go through the proper procedures, Katrina is going to get mad at Semiette.」

Katrina… Ah, the headmistress. Katrina Lorbeim. From the rumors we’ve heard from Princess Leshimiiya, she is someone with the potential to be an S-rank hunter.  

One of the prime suspects for the taboo attempt. Speaking of suspects, Munyechka would be one of them, so I suppose we should check just to be sure.

『Ciel, could we switch for a moment?』  

『Sure, of course.』

With this quick exchange, Ciel and I switched. As we did, Munyechka seemed to have noticed it, as she had a meaningful look on her face.

「Hello. It appears that you can tell when we switch places.」  

「Right, hello, Ainsel. Just vaguely, though. I’m glad to hear that my hunch was right. So, what brought you out here?」  

「There is one thing I really want to ask about, Ms. Munyechka.」  

「One thing, eh.」  

「Ms. Munyechka, are you attempting to commit a taboo?」

I don’t think she is, which is why I asked directly, and she heartily laughed at me. Still, I know that she’s not being sarcastic, and her laugh was quite pretty, so I can’t really feel mad.  

Besides, with her laughing this much, it should be safe to assume that she isn’t involved.

「Nope, absolutely not. I don’t want to get hit with a divine punishment and all that.」  

「I suspected as much, which is why I asked the way I did, but do you perhaps know of someone who was hit with a divine punishment?」  

「A long, long time ago. If I recall, the punishment back then was the confiscation of their Job.」  

「That’s quite dreadful.」  

「Oh, but you don’t sound too concerned.」

Munyechka responded with a slight surprise, but in my case, losing my Job won’t really be a problem. I can protect Ciel even without Song Princess; it’s mostly an added convenience.  

Frankly, I’ve had more problems due to having Song Princess. Excluding the events at Rispelgia, we’ve only been in mortal danger during our first battle against an Artificial Divine Messenger, and now I have proper countermeasures.

「Well, there were cases where people were instantly killed, or even had their very souls erased, among various other methods, so I swore to myself that I would never commit a taboo.」  

「I’d rather not get killed myself, so I’ll make sure to be careful as well.」

If there are various forms of divine punishment, then maybe we can ask the Creator God about it when we have the chance.  

But in that case, I guess we’ll have to go to a temple. A temple, huh… We’ll think of how to go about this later.

+++

# 170: Free Time, Munyechka, and the Headmistress

The next day after the Puppet Sorcery class, we had no courses in the morning, only Field Training in the afternoon. While Combat Training is similarly done outdoors, Field Training entails more practical training activities, not just bodybuilding and combat.  

The practical part apparently involves training in the mountains located within the academy grounds.

While we could do hunter work in our free time this morning, we decided to work on our task and find Munyechka. We tried going to her room earlier, but she wasn’t there, so after the morning homeroom, we’ll try visiting the Puppet Sorcery classroom.  

We’ve been seeing our classmates every day, but since it’s only been a few days, everyone is still just beginning to settle into their own groups. With me only having small talk with Palra, Ailneige hasn’t attracted attention yet… I think. Well, Princess Leshimiiya is also in this class, and lightning sorcerer Alcrei frequently snaps at hero Juerd who he seems to hate the sight of, so the attention will probably stay with them until they calm down.

The princess actually seems to be interacting with every single one of our classmates, since even Palra mentioned Princess Leshimiiya during our conversations, which caught me by surprise. How do I say this? I’m impressed that Palra managed to hold a conversation with the princess.  

Well, she did say that she was so nervous that she can barely remember what they were talking about, so maybe it’s wrong to say that Palra managed.  

But since it’s the princess, she probably won’t get angry even with a little discourtesy.

Today, as with any other day, I’m talking with Palra at a healthy distance away from the rest of the class. To be more exact, I’m listening to Palra talking.

「Ailneige, did you take Field Training?」  

「I did.」  

「Thank goodness… I was starting to worry about what I’d do if I didn’t know anyone there…」  

「Do you have classes where you don’t know anyone?」

To my inquiry, Palra stared at the far horizon and muttered, 「I have… yeah.」 Noticing the sadness in her expression, I stopped asking further questions and returned to the topic of Field Training.

「Belltina should also have Field Training, I believe.」  

「Are you sure? Bell doesn’t seem to be the active type from what I see.」  

「She likely wants to have as many options for the future, you see. That’s why I think she must have taken courses necessary for becoming a hunter.」  

「That does sound plausible. After all, she’s always present for Combat Training, despite having a hard time from not having enough stamina.」

Belltina always says that she doesn’t want to work, but she does seem to understand what getting cut off from her family entails and also understands how becoming a hunter can serve as a safety net.  

As long as you haven’t committed a crime, anyone is welcome to be a hunter. However, there is no assurance that you will be able to survive the lifestyle. Frankly, if we consider a ruler’s thought process, they’d probably prefer people dying as hunters than running to a life of crime. On the Hunter Guild’s end, they’ll certainly prefer their hunters to stay alive, but they can’t really afford to support each and every hunter. To begin with, many people become hunters for the freedom it offers, which makes it difficult to provide overly systematic support.

So if you want to survive in that environment, you need to be prepared for it. For hunters, mistakes can cost one’s life, but here in the academy, a mistake will only cost you a scolding at worst, so you can blunder as much as you like. Being able to safely accumulate experience is a valuable opportunity.

「That reminds me, Ailneige, have you ever gone to the mountains or forests for hunter work?」  

「I have. Palra, you should be familiar with them as well, correct?」  

「I was just following my father around, frantically trying to do whatever he said, so I honestly want some pointers for navigating through a mountain; do you have any?」  

「At any rate, you should be good as long as you keep vigilant against threats. Getting ambushed by monsters is most terrifying, you see.」

In my old world, your footwork and stamina management might be the first priority, but in this world, it’s this. The people of this world have high physicality in general, so most are probably capable of crossing a mountain if we’re strictly speaking of physical capability. On the other hand, there are more dangers to look out for. While there are also threats like wild bears and boars in my old world, it’s not like there aren’t preventative measures against them, and they do avoid noises that could come from people. In this world, however, monsters are creatures that actively seek to attack people, so the noises will instead attract them.

「Keep vigilant… how do I do that?」  

「I have my barrier, so I really can’t say. Goblins can’t kill me no matter how many there are, and even with D-rank monsters, I can handle them to a certain extent.」  

「That’s amazing! But I don’t think I can mimic that.」  

「You took this course precisely so you could learn, didn’t you?」  

「That’s true; I just don’t have the confidence… I can understand the actual lecture, and, in hindsight, there’s a lot that somewhat reminds me of what my father and I were doing during our hunts, but…」

Normal students don’t really have any previous experience to draw on like her, and she’s free to practice her learnings in the upcoming classes, so there really isn’t much need to worry. Besides, while keeping vigilant is important, strong monsters don’t really appear in areas close to the royal capital, so being overly conscious might even be counterproductive.

「Well, what’s most important is to not die.」  

「I see. I’ll make sure to remember.」  

「Please do.」

I’d feel awful if Palra ends up dying, so I’d rather she stay alive if possible. Though I can’t really see this timid Palra jumping headfirst into danger.  

As I replied, Ms. Claura arrived. There wasn’t any special announcement today.

With homeroom over, we headed to the Puppet Sorcery classroom.

『Will she be there in the Puppet Sorcery classroom?』  

『We’ll find out either way, but I have a hunch she’s the type who would be there. She probably considers that to be her place of belonging, you see.』

I think she’s like those students who are always in their club rooms or researchers who sleep over in their laboratories. Carol is probably the same, and Mia would likely be similar had she been born in a different family, in my opinion.

『So in my case, by Ain’s side.』  

『We’re always together though.』  

『Oh, but there was a time when you were away without a word, you know?』  

『I’m sorry about that.』

The Creator God practically kidnapped me when we met, but me not being able to be with Ciel for 3 whole days was partially the consequence of me neglecting myself.  

I honestly feel guilty about it, so the apology naturally left my lips. Ciel replied, 『It’s alright,』 in her usual tone, but I seriously want to make sure something like that never happens again.

Walking through the ever-empty halls, we reached the Puppet Sorcery classroom where we were met by Munyechka, who clearly looked like she was just in the middle of a task.

「Good morning, Ms. Munyechka.」  

「Ainsel, is it? Hm, morning. What brought you to my sanctuary? If you came with no particular reason at all, then I might have to consider using extreme methods to remove you.」  

「My apologies for having interrupted your work. There was something I wanted to inquire about, but Ms. Munyechka, were you always that kind of character?」  

「Hm, oh. Sorry. I don’t have much of a proper personality to begin with. Iena and Semiette are unquestionably still me.」  

「Good point. Do you perhaps have a different persona in a previous version or something similar?」  

「Hmmm, for that, I suppose I’ll leave it as a yes.」

That’s quite a suggestive answer… So, in short, it’s not that there’s a main doll that can house her soul; any suitably made doll is capable of housing her soul.  

The perquisites are unknown, but that implies that she can have as many “spare lives” as she needs. If her doll’s functionality is improved, will it directly strengthen Munyechka herself?  

If you hope to defeat Munyechka, you might have to, at worst, destroy every single one of her dolls first. If she has one hidden, then she can survive. Is she some kind of action game character or what?

Perhaps this is exactly the reason why Munyechka is an S-rank hunter.  

No matter how unknown an area is, she can explore it without any risk of dying; if she “dies,” she’ll just return with information, and the usefulness of that is immeasurable.

「Now then, what business do you h—two have with me?」  

「We wanted to ask what kind of person the headmistress is.」  

「You mean Katrina?」  

「Ms. Munyechka, you are in a position to speak casually with the headmistress, aren’t you?」

I don’t know about the other faculty members, but since she’s a hunter undertaking a request, it shouldn’t be unusual for her to be seeing the headmistress.  

Even if that’s not the case, she’s likely interacted with the headmistress as Semiette. After all, she did previously say something about being scolded.

「Well, that’s right. Katrina is one of my apprentices, so we do speak in casual terms.」  

「So she was your apprentice. With you as a master, the headmistress having the potential to be S-rank does sound convincing now.」  

「I do recall her being described that way. But S-rank is impossible for Katrina in my opinion.」  

「Is that so?」  

「Even with a lifetime spent on learning sorcery, normal people can’t really reach the realm of magic, you see. And the only way I can think of to reach S-rank without magic is by defeating a dragon in a life-or-death struggle.」

Defeating a dragon, huh. Well, doesn’t that sound awfully familiar? This is making my head hurt a bit.  

I guess if one can defeat a dragon without it being a mortal struggle, then that means they should already be S-rank. Fighting a dragon-class opponent is not as straightforward as it sounds. It should be difficult enough to search for them, and if you exhaust yourself before reaching one, you’ll most likely just die. Now I understand just how large the gap between A and S-rank is.  

In short, one would need an experience as intense as fighting a dragon in a battle to the death; there isn’t really any need to hyperfocus on the dragon part itself. For example, defeating monsters of the 90th stratum should be enough. That said, reaching that stratum might actually be more difficult than finding a dragon.

「Capabilities aside for now, could you tell me what kind of person she is?」  

「To start off innocuously, she loves to take care of people. She previously took the initiative to take care of me, you see, and now she’s even the head of this academy. Currently, she seems to enjoy teaching people more than improving her own sorcery skills.」  

「Does she have any interest in sorceric tools?」  

「Being my apprentice, I’ve had her try Puppet Sorcery, but she wasn’t interested at all. She’s not particularly disinterested in sorceric tools as a whole, but she’s not the type that wants to create sorceric tools or daydream new ones.」  

「Thank you very much. That’s good to hear.」  

「Glad to be of help.」

As I thought, it seems that the headmistress is also unlikely to be the one. Still, it’s a bit risky to make a final judgment from secondhand information, so it might be best to personally approach—no, that sounds bothersome, but I also can’t ignore a task entrusted to me, so…

「What should I do if I want to meet with the headmistress?」  

「You can just have Semiette bring you there. Being fellow teachers, that should allow the meeting to be somewhat organic. Katarina knows Semiette, and she shouldn’t have any reason to turn you down.」  

「Can we ask that of you?」  

「It’s perfect for showing that Semiette is doing her duties, so I’ll take on your request. Semiette will leave immediately after guiding you, so feel free to take your time.」  

「Thank you very much.」

Immediately after giving my gratitude, I reconsidered and spoke to Ciel.

『Can I give her some of our magic pouch’s excess monster materials?』  

『I don’t really mind. We don’t really have any use for them anyway.』  

『Thank you.』

Receiving her permission, I think I’ll give away the horn of a den stratum 70 monster.  

Being one of the many monsters Ciel defeated, it was a bull that had gem-like horns. If properly processed, it may potentially end up more beautiful than any regular gems. There were other bull monsters of the same type with different colored horns, so there are many colors to choose from.  

We should have stored all the horns we broke in battle, so this should be alright.

I want to organize the contents of our magic pouch, but it’ll likely cause a ruckus if we do it at a Hunter’s Guild, and I’m not really sure if there’s anyone who can dismantle monsters at Mother Fii’s manor. I would leave them the task if there was one, though.  

Anyway, for now, I handed Munyechka the horn.

「This may not be much, but please accept it.」  

「This is… you’ve brought quite a rare item. This should be from a monster in the lower strata. Oh right, you two have gone to the lowest stratum.」  

「We still have more, so please use it as you please. You can even sell it.」  

「I can’t sell this. If I tried, no one would purchase it for an adequate price. Still, I have my own uses, so I’ll gladly accept. Well then, I’ll have Semiette lead you to Katrina’s place.」

Semiette began moving like a living human and instructed us to follow her. I was getting ready to leave, but recalling something, I decided to ask for Munyechka’s opinion first.

「That reminds me, I felt the headmistress looking at me during the freshmen welcome party; do you have any idea why it could be?」  

「Katrina loves promising individuals, so it must be that.」  

「I see, thank you very much.」

Now then, I wonder how Ailneige is in the headmistress’ eyes. I just hope this won’t lead to anything bothersome.

+++

# 171: Headmistress and Preferred Type

「Headmistress, please open the door.」

In front of the door with the sign “Office of the Academy Head,” Semiette spoke with a superficially polite tone. Semiette is technically part of the teaching staff, so wouldn’t it be prudent to be a bit more careful with her attitude?  

Maybe she’s projecting a bit of her “master” persona because there aren’t any people around at present. After all, Semiette should also know that there’s only one presence inside the office.

The individual within lethargically approached the door and begrudgingly opened it.

「What’s it this time, master? Don’t you usually prefer to be left alone all the time?」  

「Today I’ve brought someone who wanted to meet you, so you’d best sharpen your act.」  

「Wanted to meet me?」

The robed lady beyond the door looked around left and right before finally looking down and noticing me.  

Seeing her face, considering her position as a headmistress, she looks younger than I’d expected. I wouldn’t be surprised if she’s in her twenties, but I also wouldn’t disagree even if she turned out to be in her forties.  

Since her ears aren’t pointed, she probably isn’t an elf. In that case, it might be easy to know what kind of hunter she was with some investigation. Actually, if we ask Grandmaster Rhavelt, he might probably tell us the people’s general perception of the headmaster during his time.

「Pleased to meet you, I am—」  

「I know, Ailneige, correct?」  

「You know of me?」  

「I am the academy headmistress, after all—is what I’d like to say, but it isn’t as if I actually remember the names of all the students.」  

「Well, I suppose so.」

The headmistress already recognizes Ailneige, so I assume that she probably had at least researched the students she’s interested in. She did previous look at us and seems to know enough about us that my half-hearted response didn’t elicit a displeased reaction.  

Then, as if to confirm something, she turned to Semiette.

「Master, why are you with her?—Just so you know, I am aware that she’s the sole student of the Puppet Sorcery course. But I don’t believe that this is enough for you to favor someone. Well, it’s easy to see that this isn’t the only factor.」  

「She’s an acquaintance’s kin.」  

「Why do you always act like this whenever you’re Semiette?」  

「It’s because you’re the headmistress and I’m but a teacher. Doesn’t Vyfia show you the same respect as well?」  

「It’s questionable if such a surface-level act can even be considered a show of respect, but oh well. Am I correct to assume that she’s a relative of Master Munyechka’s friend?」  

「That’s exactly the case. As such, I’ll be taking my leave. Please take care of her for me.」  

「What did you even come here for… master…」  

「I came here to show that I’m working. As a teacher of this academy, I brought a student wanting to meet our dear headmistress.」

Semiette said with an indifferent tone, to which the headmistress responded with an exhausted sigh. It appears that trouble comes with her as a master. In our case, the most “master-like” person we know is probably Carol. It’s a bit hard to say if she was troublesome or not. But she isn’t really our sorcery master to begin with, so I guess there’s no use comparing.  

Rather, from our relationship with Perla, we’re more of a master-ish character, but I wonder if she saw us that way. I hope she’s doing well these days.

As I was lost in my thoughts, it seemed like Semiette and the headmaster had finished their conversation, as Semiette announced, 「Now, I’ll be taking my leave,」 and left.  

While rubbing her temple, the headmistress turned to me.

「Sorry to make you wait. I’m told that you need something of me, but could you first come inside?」  

「Understood.」

I suppose it’s not good to hold a conversation in front of the office. With the headmistress being famous, a first-year having a one-on-one conversation with her would be conspicuous, so I gladly complied.  

The headmistress’ office doesn’t look that much different from the principal’s offices I know. It’s not particularly unusual, nor does it seem to have any strange equipment or hidden rooms.

「Welcome to my office. This is the first time I’ve had a student within the first days of the academy opening, but make yourself comfortable.」  

「Thank you very much. It might be weird for me to ask this myself, but do students actually come to the headmistress’ office frequently?」  

「Despite appearances, I am famous, so there is a subset of people who visit out of curiosity, but excluding special events, it’s not very common. It’s generally only students chosen to represent in inter-academy competitions, students with outstanding achievements, or those with particularly excellent grades.」  

「Inter-academy competitions?」  

「It’s rare to find students who enrolled without knowing this, but to put it simply, we hold contests with the first academy for students to test their abilities. I believe it should be easier to understand this way.」  

「I see.」  

「You don’t sound interested.」  

「Yes, I’m not.」

The first academy is where _that_ prince is, and we don’t want to stand out. In that sense, it’s not that I’m not interested, but I would never want to participate in that.  

Even if good performance is recognized and may result in a secure employment as a knight or court sorcerer, I’d rather not. Honestly, those aren’t really a plus for us at all. It’s unlikely to result in us getting better treatment, and any attempt to take us in would risk becoming an international problem.

The headmistress responded to my immediate reply with silent musing but then she spoke with a serious expression.

「I heard that you wanted to see me, but would you mind telling me about yourself first?」  

「Don’t you already know enough about me?」  

「Your name is Ailneige; you’re an E-rank hunter who is usually in a two-man party. You are not a local and most probably hail from Central. Considering your extraordinary finances, you are either from a major merchant family or a noble, but from your magic power assessment, you are more likely to be of noble blood. Your fighting style is mainly defensive through the use of barriers, which you proactively leverage to complete herb gathering requests.  

This is the all information I have on hand, but it is possible that these were intentionally leaked. After all, your capabilities are surely well beyond that; I don’t even know if I can win against you.」

『So apparently she doesn’t know, but is that true?』  

『From what I can sense, we wouldn’t lose, so I suppose we can win against her. To begin with, if she wasn’t hiding her strength when she was active and she didn’t reach S-rank, then we can probably win.』

It’s a different story if the headmistress was actually concealing her strength, resulting in her remaining at A-rank, but I don’t think she has any reason to do that. If she was like us, who simply remained in A-rank because S-rank would be troublesome, there should be rumors about her being actually S-rank in strength despite her rank. Moreover, Munyechka, her own master, proclaimed that she can’t reach S-rank, so we can probably win.  

If what Princess Leshimiiya told us was true, then the headmistress should not be able to perfectly perceive my power. Even so, she can probably still sense it somewhat, which is probably why she looked our way during the welcome party.

『Can I talk about us being Mother Fii’s daughter?』  

『Isn’t it fine? It shouldn’t really cause us any problems. Besides, if it does, then we can just run. When that happens, can we go play by the ocean?』  

『That sounds nice. Let’s find one we can swim at next.』  

『Could you teach me how to swim, Ain?』  

『If you’re fine with my way of swimming.』  

『I’m looking forward to it.』

While discussing with Ciel, the headmistress was puzzled by the silence, so I continued as if nothing happened.

「About myself, was it? I don’t intend on putting on airs, so I wouldn’t mind sharing. But headmistress, do you truly want to know who I am? There are such things better left unknown, you know?」  

「So you’ll actually give a proper answer?」  

「It’s not really a problem as long as I choose who to share it with, after all. Even if I don’t, it’ll only be troublesome, not fatal.」

If we were just a princess of another nation, then I’d probably have to be prudent about various cross-national matters my actions could influence. However, we are the family of Central’s Mistress Fiiyanamia. Mother Fii rules Central not through economic prowess nor through political might, but through violence. It’s not an exaggeration to say that overwhelming violence is the source of her authority.  

What Mother wants to protect is strictly the very land of Central; the people living there are none of her concern. In that sense, Mother Fii is like a dragon, and we’re similar in that regard.

If humanity’s rules happen to put Ciel in danger, I can easily crush those rules.  

When that happens, Mother Fii would probably be the only one capable of stopping me. Because of that, exposing our secret would not be fatal for us, but for our opposition. There is a slim chance that we may encounter beings close to my level, which is why I never neglect improving myself.

「Had you chosen to remain an ordinary student, there would be no need, but at this point, I cannot afford to not know. Despite appearances, I am an academy head.」  

「I see. My name is Cielmer. Regarding my status, I am Fiiyanamia’s adopted daughter.」  

「…—Yup, I’ve considered the possibility, but still… 」

The headmistress’ face was difficult to describe. Mother Fii adopting a child is a major incident that she probably has kept in the corner of her mind, so I can understand her disbelief of that said child being here.  

Perhaps she initially denied the possibility out of how much she’d rather not handle the responsibility. Having Fiiyanamia’s daughter graduate from your academy would surely bring great prestige, but that is hardly necessary for an already prestigious academy. If you’d ask me, the anxiety of such an important individual possibly getting into trouble under your tenure would probably be a greater concern.

「Would I be correct to assume that you’re as young as you appear?」  

「I’m 13 years old, so I should be older than I appear, I believe?」

I mused for a moment, but since I don’t intend to share about Ainsel, I decided to speak from Ciel’s perspective. I don’t even know how to count my age to begin with. While I technically have more than 30 years of life experience, since I did die and was supposed to reincarnate properly, you could say that I was “born” when I was sent to Ciel, or since I wasn’t actually reincarnated, you could also consider my age of death as my proper age.

「—To think there are beings like you around. The world truly is large. As an educator, it makes me feel equal parts joyful and sad.」  

「Was this enough to satisfy you?」  

「More than enough. While that certainly was information I, as a headmistress, would rather not know, it’s terrifying to think of what could happen had I remained uninformed. And as you said, with your capabilities and Mistress Fiiyanamia behind you, it wouldn’t be an issue for you even if you were exposed.」  

「I believe you should already understand, but please keep this between us.」  

「Of course. I would never antagonize you if I had the choice.」

With our conversation having reached a good pause, I asked, 「Shall we continue?」 The headmistress replied, 「Sorry, of course,」 and so I proceeded without hesitation.

「Headmistress, do you have any interest in crafting sorceric tools?」  

「Nope. I love seeing people who do their best to make better sorceric tools, but I wouldn’t make one myself. Well, I simply love cheering on individuals giving their best effort.」

As I thought, the headmistress appears to be uninvolved. While I can’t be fully certain, since sorceric tools use magic cores, people who don’t have interest in sorceric tools are unlikely to develop an alternative energy to replace magic cores. Besides, even if I try to lead her with questions hinting about the taboo, she probably won’t give a straightforward answer. Anyway, that should be enough for today, but it’d be dull to just end things here, so I decided to continue the conversation for a bit.

「Is that why you became an academy head?」  

「This isn’t a position you can reach by simply wanting to be one, but that was the reason why I accepted the offer, yes. The more someone stakes their life on achieving their goals, the more I just want to cheer them on.」  

「… Even if that said goal is revenge?」  

「I would at least try to persuade against it for reasons of morality, and I would intervene if it’s unjustified; but depending on the circumstances, I’d cheer them on. Even if their motivation is revenge, I find people working towards their goals likable. For that reason, I find you likable as well. After all, to have gained such power at such a young age, you must have had experiences I can’t even fathom.」

I know fully well that I’m not the one to criticize, but it sounds like the headmistress has a quite peculiar sense of morality.

+++

# 172: Field Training and Party

After our exchange with the headmistress, we first returned to Munyeckha’s place to give our thanks.  

We’ll likely need her help again in the future, and her cooperation is absolutely necessary for the creation of Ciel’s doll, so it should be fine to show a level of consideration.

『So the headmistress is good, right?』  

『If I had to say, she’s unrelated. Her not having interest in creating sorceric tools is probably true, and I couldn’t feel much ambition for greatness from her. Even with a talent like Cielmer before her, there wasn’t any major change in her expression.』

For people with the ambition to reach S-rank or achieve other great deeds, Cielmer’s existence should be extremely eye-catching. An A-rank hunter at 13 years old, with the greatest patron by the name of Fiiyanamia behind her. Objectively speaking, she is an unmistakable genius, a target of envy for those aiming for greater heights. Even for individuals in different fields of expertise, I wouldn’t be surprised if they had something to say about her background.  

Despite this, I didn’t feel anything of that sort from the headmistress. Perhaps I just couldn’t read through her, but if that’s the case, only my inexperience is to blame, so I’ll just apologize to Mother.

Mother personally seems fine with us failing this task, though. Even if someone does manage to commit a taboo, they’ll just receive divine punishment in the end. Mother said that the greatest problem with this would be the loss of a gifted individual, but she probably doesn’t mind if humanity goes extinct anyway.  

Personally, I don’t find humanity’s extinction to be a good thing.

『Fufu, Ain calling me by Cielmer feels somewhat interesting.』  

『If you want, I can always call you Cielmer, you know?』  

『That’s not fair.』

Hearing Ciel’s seemingly pouty tone, I apologized with a smile, 『I’m sorry about that.』  

While it sounds that way, I’m sure she’s not actually sulking. Rather, there might even be a chance that she’s acting that way to trouble me a bit, I believe?  

I was able to notice it this time, so I could respond with composure, but I’d probably be flustered otherwise.

『Today’s Ain is such a tease,』 Ciel’s voice echoing in my mind was so hopelessly cute, I couldn’t hide a smile.

◇◇◇

Today’s course is Field Training. We’ll be holding our class outdoors, so Ciel will be mainly in charge. Depending on the situation, I might have to participate as well, but since this is our first class, Ciel is out. We are to assemble in front of the entrance of the forest within the academy premises.  

After changing and arriving at the assembly area, Palra quickly saw Ail and drew near. Come to think of it, we did chat earlier this morning, discussing our predictions of how Field Training will be, I think? Palra also asked for hints about how to keep vigilant, but my method isn’t really mimickable, so please learn it through our lessons. I was the one who spoke with her earlier, but this time it’s Ciel, so there’s no telling whether Ail will remember this morning’s conversation properly.

「Ailneige!」  

「You came quite early.」  

「I had nothing to do for my free time…」  

「Is that so?」

Ciel casually brushes off Palra’s self-pitying remark. What did I do during my free periods in the past again? I’m sure I also talk to my friends, but I think I generally find being alone comfortable, so I spend my free time by myself. Also, I just felt a presence silently approaching. How do I say this? While not as good as a professional assassin, this is quite the impressive stealth action.  

The weaving between the crowds is done well, and even after going somewhere without any people at all, the focus on us is not lost.

I’ve thought about this before, but Belltina seems to be quite skillful in using her Magic Eyes. Her way of using it might be considerably misguided, though. Maybe I should master more of the Song Princess’ abilities as well? Though I don’t really think it will change much for me in the end.  

Unlike Ciel, who regularly uses her Dance Princess abilities in battle, I only use Song Princess for support against monsters of A-rank and above. It’s more of a trump card, not something we can really flaunt.
