Because of that, my side as a magic user is stronger than my side as a Song Princess, to the point where barriers are what I consider to be my specialty. I do love singing, so I sing frequently, but I don’t use the Song Princess’ powers that much. And I don’t plan on using it in the academy unless Ciel is required to display a certain level of strength.

That aside, I kept Belltina’s approach a secret from Ciel and simply observed.

「U-um…」  

「Belltina, so you also enrolled for Field Training.」  

「Y-Yes! Bell didn’t really want to, but it might be necessary if the worst comes to pass…」  

「That’s true.」

I’m not sure whether Ciel noticed her in advance, but given her complete lack of surprise at Belltina’s sudden appearance, she must have.  

As of present, Belltina excels at avoiding people and is skilled in sensing presences, but she doesn’t actually have much in the way of stealth capability. In other words, she’s similar to us. Against people who can use detection, her presence is easy to discern. To put it differently, she’s currently only performing on pure talent without actual polished skill.

In our case, the very nature of our Jobs makes us stand out, so we’re just fundamentally unsuited for stealth and spy work.

「Ah, Belltina, are you doing good?」  

「Bell isn’t doing that good. Now that Bell has come here, Bell feels terrible.」  

「I guess you’re only here to be a hunter?」  

「Bell isn’t particularly aspiring to be one, you know? But if Bell had been a bit more capable, Bell might not have ended up in this course.」

『What does she mean by that?』  

『Perhaps she tried various courses but couldn’t find any she could comfortably keep up with?』  

『But Belltina’s Magic Eyes are excellent, aren’t they?』  

『Maybe no one simply knows how truly capable Belltina’s Magic Eyes are? Perhaps Belltina even actively lives in a way to prevent other people from noticing it.』  

『It sounds bothersome if it gets revealed. But then wouldn’t that limit Belltina’s capabilities?』  

『Which is likely why she was told that they’ll only care for her up until her graduation.』

Having such a rare Job, Belltina’s family is surely at least keeping an eye on her, but her act of hiding its utility is probably why she was disowned.  

Is the reason why Belltina keeps it secret even after being disowned because she doesn’t think her parents will find it useful, because she doesn’t realize its possible applications herself, or because of some other reason?  

If she can avoid aiming for quick success while still being willing to take a certain level of risk, then I believe that Belltina should be able to make a decent living as a hunter. Though if I had to say, if she pairs with Palra, then they might be able to have a reasonably consistent rate of success.

As the class period approaches, I look around and observe that there might be more people than during Combat Training. No, there actually is more.  

Certain troublemakers—Alcrei and Juerd—that weren’t present during Combat Training were around, so I immediately realized it. Unlike Combat Training, which can be done even in the privacy of your home, Field Training requires the students to enter a forest, so people generally can’t skip it. Everyone starts from basic-level. The necessary aptitude for this can’t really be assessed during the entrance exam, so it does make sense.

Well, we were actually granted an exemption for this as well. After all, we already have a track record of venturing into forests for hunter-related work. Even among people our age, being E-rank is rare. This academy does have a number of students whose combat abilities or physical prowess might surpass E-rank standards in certain respects—like in rule-bound duels or in sheer agility—but to be officially recognized as an E-rank hunter, you also need camping and survival skills… Or so I think. In our case, though, camping simply means putting up a barrier and sleeping anywhere. And since I stay awake, I can immediately respond if anything happens.

Now, regarding Alcrei, I don’t know if he just doesn’t care to pay attention to his surroundings or if he deems the people in this class unworthy of attention, but he has not noticed Belltina’s presence. I don’t really mind, since we might get roped into trouble if he does. Also, Belltina seems to know that Alcrei is present, as she is hiding behind Palra’s silhouette.

「Seems like everyone’s here. Alright, gather around.」

It looks like Ishparht’s party is also in charge of this course, as evidenced by the familiar—though still unnamed—teachers present.  

However, perhaps because there are more students this time, another party has joined them, and there are now around 10-odd teachers.　

「Now, for Field Training, we will have everyone here right now group themselves in parties of 3-6 people. Once you’ve decided on your party, inform any of us teachers who your members are, and from then on, if there are any further changes in your party composition, make sure to similarly update us about it. In particular, if one of your members are to leave or be replaced, we’ll need to confirm that the majority of your party members are in agreement with it. Otherwise, we will only give permission for special circumstances.」

What I’ve feared has come to fruition. Still, I’ve considered this possibility and have already marked candidates for our party.  

Still, isn’t this quite sudden? Are they telling us that we should befriend other people within the allotted time or that we need to be able to work with anyone to some extent?  

Them making it difficult to change parties might also be to discourage the students from just grouping randomly with whoever is left.

「Once you’ve formed your party, your task today is to climb to the summit of the mountain and bring back one of the tokens we’ve placed there. Let me make this clear: failing to collect a token today will not affect your grade, so don’t rush; take your time deciding who to partner with. This is primarily a task for those who formed their parties quickly and are currently unoccupied. That said, all students are required to enter the forest at least once during this course, so make sure to finalize your party before the end of this period. If you haven’t chosen your party members by then, we’ll assign the remaining students into groups ourselves, just so you’re aware.」

As Ishparht finished explaining, the students immediately moved.  

The majority appear to have formed parties with the people they usually socialize with, since Alcrei grouped with his cohorts and quickly left for the mountain, while Juerd is with his usual lineup. The only difference from the usual is that Rulinia isn’t with them.  

Speaking of Rulinia, she seems to have joined the princess’ party, which consists of the princess, Rulinia, Rynaetra, and one unfamiliar student. Not only is the student unfamiliar, but he? is probably one of Munyechka’s dolls. The doll appears to be a boy equipped with a shield and a one-handed sword. He’s short but has the vibe of a protagonist with a strong sense of justice.

Princess Leshimiiya doesn’t seem to have realized this, but he’s sure to be a top-class bodyguard. I have no idea how they met, but I suspect that it could be through the headmistress.

『So we really have to form a party, huh?』  

『Right, but fortunately, we have people we can comfortably team up with, don’t we?』  

『Well, just as you said, Ain. Far better than grouping with random strangers.』

「Shall we form a party with the three of us?」  

「I’m fine with that. Honestly, thanks. I really don’t think I could team up with anyone other than you two, so I’m really glad.」  

「Bell can’t think of other people as well!」

Hearing their blatantly relieved replies, I couldn’t help but think about how helplessly weak they are in terms of communication skills.

+++

# 173: Observation, Chat, and Stray Shots

Our party was decided quickly, but we decided to stay put and observe the situation for now. I didn’t think we’d stand out, but since there have been people stealing glances at us—or rather Ciel—I had Ciel do her best to have an enjoyable conversation with Palra and Belltina. Hard to tell if she succeeded, but still.

How do I say this? Since I’ve been focused on avoiding the more particularly troublesome-looking individuals, I haven’t been as vigilant with other people. At this point, maybe we’d be better off joining Princess Leshimiiya’s party, but that would be too conspicuous, and Palra would probably faint out of anxiety.  

In any case, thanks to Ciel’s efforts, Ailneige no longer looks free in other people’s eyes, and while there were still some who tried to invite us, they easily backed down when refused.

The reason we have yet to make a move is because we’re waiting for Mr. Hero and Mr. Lightning Sorcerer to leave. Particularly with Alcrei, he seems to be conscious of Ailneige as someone of the opposite sex, so he might coerce us to join his party; meanwhile, Juerd knows that we are an E-rank hunter, so he might come and bother us from that front.

Back to Alcrei, he seems to have some friction with Belltina as well, so I don’t want to risk getting his attention. Fortunately, both of them grouped with their usual companions—Juerd’s members are all girls with Rulinia absent, while Alcrei has his cohorts—so we didn’t have to wait for too long. Alcrei did start a quibble due to Juerd’s harem party, but the teachers immediately quelled the situation, and he left for the mountain to escape.  

Juerd’s party left a few minutes after, but now that they’re both gone, we can finally move.

『They’re gone now.』  

『Really? That was somewhat tiring.』  

『Good work. Shall we switch?』  

『No, I’m fine the way it is. Talking with Palra can be exhausting, but it’s not unpleasant.』  

『True, Palra seems to have a keen sense of how much distance to maintain.』

I’ve already noticed it before, but while Palra’s tendency to talk about herself may turn some people off, she never oversteps other people’s personal boundaries.  

Actually, the reason why Palra talks a lot about herself might be so that she doesn’t carelessly ask uninvited questions. She’s doing her best since she doesn’t want to accidentally touch on sensitive topics. If I think of it that way, this awkwardness just makes her endearing.

As if to support that idea, Palra has recently started asking us more questions. Through our brief interactions, it seems she’s developed a good understanding of our boundaries; her questions have become more meaningful, but she remains cautious. Figuratively speaking, she always keeps herself two or three steps away from the edge of what we’re comfortable discussing.

Because of that, she has a decent affinity for people like Ciel, who naturally find talking to people—with some exceptions, like me—bothersome. The same goes with people like Belltina, who barely joins the conversation outside of the occasional nodding.

「Well, shall we go to the teacher now?」  

「Uh… Yeah, let’s go, let’s go!」

This is a good example. Palra energetically responded, but I’m sure that she must have been wondering why we only chatted here without reporting to a teacher until now, yet she doesn’t ask why. Some might say that there’s no need to keep secrets between party members, but I think it’s fine to have one or two secrets even with close friends.  

In our case, we carry more secrets that would likely trouble those trying to pry them out of us; I’m honestly more concerned about whether they’re truly ready to hear them.

Still, being secretive to the point of getting into trouble is even a common story trope, so finding a good balance is important.

『Once we enter the mountain and there aren’t any people around, let’s explain our reasoning.』  

『Yeah, let’s do that.』

While we may share an unspoken consensus of not wanting to get involved with conspicuous people, there’s no need to keep this unspoken.  

Or so I mused, when suddenly, 「So you formed a three-person party,」 the most conspicuous student of all spoke to me. Palra and Belltina immediately froze, likely out of nervousness. I can’t really blame them. After all, it was the princess of their own kingdom who had just spoken. Perhaps understanding that this is unavoidable, Ciel responded to her.

「I’d rather not group with unfamiliar strangers.」  

「Certainly, you do often chat with Palra, Mi—no, Ailneige.」

Yup, calling us Miss Ailneige isn’t really good in public. Though only Palra and Belltina should have heard it, so it should be alright.

「However, I am surprised to see Miss Chilandia with you.」  

「Chilandia… You mean Belltina?」

After Ciel muttered as if to confirm, Princess Leshimiiya turned to Belltina. Seemingly overwhelmed by her gaze, Belltina nodded.

「The Chilandia family is a typical Earl house. Belltina, I believe, is the third daughter of the family.」  

「Is that so?」

While this isn’t really something to discuss right in front of her, this is likely information one can easily gather with little research. Besides, the princess making eye contact with Belltina was probably to ask for her permission. Though Belltina couldn’t really decline in her position, her permission was probably still important.

Besides, there are likely other rumors circulating about Belltina, so the princess was probably only providing the bare minimum information. Perhaps she even knows that Belltina is to be cut off upon graduation? I feel like she does, but refrained from saying it out of consideration.

Consideration for both Fiiyanamia’s daughter and Belltina.  

She informs us of what kind of individual we are associating with, while still maintaining Belltina’s dignity. Well, we’re already aware of her circumstances, but the princess doesn’t know.

While Ciel and Princess Leshimiiya continued talking, Belltina was behind us desperately trying to explain her situation to Palra.  

This was because Palra, despite probably having some suspicions prior, was greatly shaken after hearing that Belltina is a noble—much less one from an Earl house.

「B-B-Bell is, when Bell graduates… Actually, Bell has probably been already disowned by the family. That’s why Bell is not exactly a noble anymore… Bell is a failure, called Chilandia’s dead weight…. That’s why, Bell is nothing at all!」

Belltina said, trying to soothe her, but that’s a bit too much. On the other hand, Palra was barely able to respond properly, 「Umm, uhh… I… see.」 She seems to be still conflicted about whether it would be better for her to be more courteous or stay unchanged.

「So Bell would be happy if you continued treating me the same.」  

「Umm, then, Belltina, is it really fine to treat you like before?」  

「If it wasn’t, then Bell would have said it from the start… maybe…」

I’ll ignore how she muttered the last part under her breath. In reality, if Belltina truly found Palra’s way of speaking disrespectful, she likely would have given a warning at their first meeting. As long as they don’t have a twisted personality, most nobles would probably do the same. Those who get offended by commoners speaking to them casually, at least.

「Will your party be fine with only back-liners?」  

「I’ll be on the frontline.」  

「…Right, of course, Ailneige is capable of working solo.」

Turning my attention back to Ciel, they appear to be discussing party balance.  

At first glance, Ailneige is a sorcerer, while Palra has a bow, making them both back liners. Meanwhile, the small Belltina doesn’t look like a front-liner at all.  

And with Ailneige being smaller than Belltina, it does sound weird for her to be a front liner, but fortunately, Ailneige has a background of being an E-rank hunter, and the princess knows our identity as well. That’s probably why she didn’t really have much more to say.

Besides, the princess’ party is not any less imbalanced, as it consists of only four: Princess Leshimiiya, Rulinia, Rynaetra, and Munyechka’s doll, whom I have yet to know. They might gain more members, though.  

Still, just judging by their appearance, none of the four really look like frontline combatants. That said, Rynaetra and Munyechka (Temp) can probably perform well in front. Since we’ll inevitably attract attention if we talk for too long, I was starting to think of how to end this when Rynaetra advised, 「Princess, it’s about time.」

「In that case, we’ll be heading out first.」  

「We’ll be leaving after a bit. Take care.」  

「Yes, take care as well.」

As the princess’ party left, we moved out as well.  

While he’s a bit farther away, reporting to Ishparht would probably make the discussion end quickly.

◇◇◇

「So three people, then?」  

「If I focus on being on the frontline, with my lack of experience, it should result in a good balance.」  

「Opportunities to build up experience on that front are hard to come by, so I can understand the sentiment. Besides, with your ability, you all should be able to come home safely even when encountering goblins, right?」  

「I can even repel a wolf, as long as it’s not a whole pack.」

As we reported our party composition to Ishparht, despite how our party appeared, he quickly deemed us acceptable. While the other teachers might also be aware of Ailneige’s background, Ishparht has actually faced Ail in direct combat, so he’s thankfully easy to talk to.  

The durability of Ail’s barrier should be able to last for some time even against a pack of wolves, but it would be difficult if we simultaneously had to protect the backline members. Enveloping the two with barriers would be preferably left as a last resort, so Ailneige will necessarily have to kite the enemy around in general. And that would be impossible against a pack.

「U-um, will goblins appear?… Sir?」  

「Let’s see. There are generally no monsters around, but you might happen to come across a stray goblin once.」

Palra inquired with her best attempt at polite speech, which Ishparht replied to with an ominous answer. I guess we’ll encounter at least one goblin on the way and back.  

While I felt bad seeing Palra with a fearful look upon hearing this, the name of a certain Job popped into the corner of my mind. However, leaving that aside for now, I had Ciel ask Ishparht something I was curious about.

「Is there only a single route?」  

「There are several routes, but one is more obvious than the others.」  

「Understood. Now then, we’ll be taking our leave… Are you two fine with that?」

Ciel turned to Palra and Belltina for confirmation—after I advised her. Palra took the initiative to ask a question earlier, so she might have other questions in her mind.  

Fortunately, the two of them nodded in agreement, but rather than it being because they have no other questions, it felt more like they’re just too anxious to ask further.

+++

# 174: Party, Discussion, and Formation

「First off, let me explain why we took so much time, Palra.」  

「Is that something I’m allowed to hear?」  

「It’s connected to Belltina’s circumstances, so it would be better for you to know.」

Saying so, Ciel gazes at Belltina. The sudden attention had her quivering for a moment before softly nodding. Palra audibly gulped; she had a serious expression, as if she was about to hear very important information.  

It may seem like a very tense scene, but with us being in a tranquil forest with gentle sunlight peeking through the leaves, we only look like three girls playing around. It probably only seems like a pleasant time to the adults watching from afar, like that teacher over there who’s discreetly observing us. We’ve likely been under watch ever since we deviated from the obvious route Mr. Ishparht mentioned, right after the first fork near the entrance.

From this point onward, we’ll need to move in proper formation—which I plan to have Ciel suggest—but before that, it’s best to share information with the rest of the party. That’s why we chose a spot that’s hard for the other students to find.

「I didn’t want to bump into Alc… Um, Tweyezel? and Juerd.」  

「Our classmates?」  

「Palra, do you want to be close to them?」

That reminds me, Alcrei’s family name was Tweisel, wasn’t it? I’m impressed that Ciel remembered it, even if not completely, but I guess it’ll be more problematic if she doesn’t. He is the son of an Earl, after all; calling him by some weird nickname would be scary, and it’ll be annoying if people think we’re close if we call him by his first name, so remembering a noble’s name is important.  

Now then, after hearing the names of Tweisel’s third son and Mr. Hero, and Ciel’s inquiry, Palra frantically shook her head in response. While it might be different for those who actively seek the favor of high-ranking nobles or royalty, for people like us who prefer a peaceful and quiet life, getting involved with such conspicuous individuals is the last thing we want. Besides, there’s always the risk that we simply won’t get along with them. Juerd, in particular, has a mindset that’s fundamentally incompatible with ours.

「Besides that… can I tell her what’s going on between you and Tweisel?」  

「Ah, um, Bell will explain. It’s about Bell, after all…」

I’m honestly grateful that Belltina is going to explain it herself. The most we know is that she isn’t on good terms with Alcrei, or rather that Alcrei doesn’t think highly of Belltina.  

Whether their friction is due to a personal issue or a family issue, I don’t know. And while I don’t know if Belltina is willing to share that much, we’ll still get a clearer picture of her situation.

「I see, Bell was also a noble…」  

「Bell has been kicked out of home, so that’s no longer the case…」

While I can’t be sure when exactly the family will completely cut her off, I feel like she might still be technically a part of House Chilandia. Since they might find some utility for her during the course of her academic stay, I believe they’re still keeping a metaphorical leash on her. But for Belltina, she probably thinks that the family has already cut ties with her.  

Still, if the Chilandia were to ever welcome Belltina back, it might only be when she gains the highest honors in the academy, isn’t it? That’ll depend on the Chilandia family’s standards, so I can only speculate.

「Bell’s Chilandia House and the Tweisel House are of Earl status and of the same faction, but House Tweisel has a higher standing within the faction. Because of that, I think, he always comes to Bell on sight and bullies Bell for being a failure. So if possible, I don’t want to meet him again. Since Bell will no longer be a noble from here on, Bell will have no choice but to bear with whatever he’d do to me.」  

「Being a noble seems tough…」

Palra muttered with a difficult expression, but I wonder how much she could actually comprehend? Anyway, Belltina’s statements were honestly enlightening on my part, so I’m contemplating what to do next.  

One thing I can say is that if Belltina graduates in her current state, it’ll be the start of a life of hiding from Alcrei. Alcrei is the son of a relatively high-status noble. Belltina would be a regular commoner. At worst, her getting killed wouldn’t be a major incident, so unless Alcrei forgets about her, she might end up being his plaything. The most realistic methods of avoiding this future would be to either run away to where he can’t reach her or to be valued enough that he can no longer lay a hand on her.

To put it simply, she needs to have a powerful backer, but wouldn’t that require Belltina herself to proactively find people that would help her? Fortunately, there are high aristocrats and even royalty here in the academy, both far greater than the Tweisel House, so she might be able to ask for help from them.  

The problem then is that I don’t think Belltina is capable of doing so. Also, this has a high chance of worsening her relationship with her family, but since their relationship has already reached the point of disowning, it probably won’t get any better. Still, this would result in her having to evade both Houses Tweisel and Chilandia, so that might be complicated.

I can only hope that Belltina does her best, or, at worst, that she manages to escape to Central. In any case, I’ll leave that decision for later. The most important information for me is that Belltina’s Chilandia family and Alcrei’s Tweisel family are both a part of the same faction. With Tweisel being anti-Central, that would mean that the Chilandia family is also anti-Central.  

Just because they’re anti-Central doesn’t necessarily mean that we need to take action against them, but with their standing, her family might come into conflict with us.

「Come to think of it, Ailneige, you already knew that Bell was a noble beforehand, right?」  

「I’ve known about it, yes.」  

「Were you surprised when you first knew?」  

「She practically revealed it during our first meeting, so not particularly.」

We didn’t know her family name, but it was certain that she came from a prestigious family, and Belltina didn’t appear to be hiding it as well. Still, what drove her to ask such a question? And why isn’t she delving deeper?  

For the latter, it’s likely because she feels like it would cross the line. As for the former, perhaps she’s curious why Ailneige doesn’t behave differently around nobles and why even Princess Leshimiiya showed some concern for us. While it might not be obvious to most, Palra may have picked up on the attitude difference from our time together so far.

「Incidentally, Palra, if you would like to know what I am, I can tell you. It wouldn’t be a problem for me even if I did, you see.」  

「Umm, uhhh…」

Palra seems to be wavering… I think. Ciel and I have already agreed that it’s fine to eventually tell Palra about our identity as Mother Fii’s daughter. However, since Palra might not be able to understand it if we reveal too much at once, we’ve decided that it’s better to reveal the truth gradually and only when Palra herself expresses the desire to know. In other words, we’re not opposed to telling her, but we’re not particularly eager to do so either. It’s not necessarily a matter of trust. Rather, it’s that Palra likely doesn’t have the means to spread such information easily. After all, I’ve never seen her interact with any classmates aside from Ail or Belltina unless absolutely necessary.

「Ailneige, if you were in my position, would you rather ask or not?」  

「I might.」  

『No matter what it is, Ain will protect me, after all.』  

『I’d protect you as much as I can, but if we were just a regular commoner and Palra turned out to be Mother Fii’s daughter, I’d run away as far as possible, you know?』  

『Dealing with Fii sounds difficult, right?』

While Ciel and I were talking, it seems like Palra has found her answer: 「This sounds scary, so I won’t ask.」 I think that’s the correct choice. I’m sure she’ll be more troubled than she already was with Belltina.

「Now, shall we depart then? What should we do about our formation?」  

「I don’t really know much about this, so I honestly want to leave the decision-making to you…」  

「Bell feels the same.」

A forfeit of responsibility—that’s what I’d like to call it. But they’re not wrong in candidly for deferring to the most experienced member present. It’s a common tale: someone insists that their judgment is the correct one, only to end up causing what should be an easily avoidable accident. However, while we normally stay safe by using detection magic to monitor our surroundings or ambush monsters while keeping track of our direction, I don’t think that level of vigilance is necessary here. Besides, if these two get too used to our way of doing things, it might cause issues later on. So, I’ll continue using detection on my own, without offering much instruction.

「Palra and Belltina shall walk in front, and I will be following from behind.」  

「Umm, you’re going to be the front liner, right? So why…」  

「It’s so the two of you can watch out for monsters as we proceed. Additionally, since Belltina has the least stamina among us, you will lead in front and dictate our overall pace.」  

「Uhh… That’s a heavy responsibility, isn’t it?」

Hearing Ciel’s response, Belltina let out a frightened shriek. She will be in charge of controlling the party’s overall movement speed, so it certainly sounds like a heavy responsibility, but this should be normal protocol for mountain climbing even in my old world. Not only is it great for pace management, but it also allows the people behind to immediately notice if those with lesser stamina are forcing themselves. Once, there was an experienced mountain climber who led the trail and got carried away, resulting in the beginners barely being able to keep up and too tired to complain. That was certainly a field trip experience of all time.  

While having a beginner lead might cause us to take a wrong turn, we can just step in and correct her before that happens. In fact, even if we get lost, I can still detect the general direction of the academy, so there’s no chance of us not being able to return.

「Don’t mind us and simply walk at your own pace, is what I meant. Becoming unable to move due to exhaustion would be the most dangerous outcome, so if you start to feel even slightly exhausted, please slow down to a more comfortable pace. I’ll be completely frank, but you speeding up in consideration of us would only lead to trouble.」  

「O-okay, understood.」

Perhaps overwhelmed by Ciel’s uncharacteristically lengthy explanation, Belltina nervously nodded. Being stern here would be the best not only for Ailneige but also for Belltina’s sake, so I have nothing to comment.

「Umm, we’ll have to keep vigilant against monsters, right?」  

「I’ll keep a lookout as well, and if a monster actually draws near, I’ll step forward before we bump into it.」

This is still just practice, after all. If they can’t manage it on their own, we’ll simply pick up the slack. Both Ciel and I are keeping an eye out for enemies as well. It might sound arrogant to say, but there’s probably no safer training environment than this. Honestly, if we really wanted to, we could probably escort these two all the way to the middle strata of the den. But that would be complete overkill in this context. Well, in the end, I just have to do for them what I already do for Ciel on a daily basis.

Belltina, who had some understanding of Ciel’s—or rather, our—true capabilities, immediately looked visibly relieved upon hearing this. As for Palra, she wore a pensive expression, but perhaps recalling that Ail was an active hunter, she eventually nodded and replied, 「Understood.」

「Now then, please walk in front. I’ll be right behind you.」

Ciel’s words seemingly caused them to jump out of nervousness, their bodies stiff to the point I can even imagine their joints creaking as they turned their heads to face each other.  

It didn’t take a minute to predict that we’ll likely turn back midway through this excursion.

+++

# 175: Rest, Job, and Approaching Figure

With a quick scan of the mountain area, I got a rough estimation of where creatures of a certain size are located. Because I stretched my detection thin to cover a wider area, I can’t distinguish between humans and monsters, so I’m just generalizing them as creatures for now.  

Recalling our teacher’s words, the ones acting alone are probably goblins. The students seem to be following the obvious beaten path, as I currently don’t see any other party straying from that path like we are. The beaten path is sure to be the quicker and most reliable way to go, so we’ll probably be seen as irregulars. Among the teachers, we might even be considered more problematic than Alcrei’s party.

『Still, goblins acting alone should be quite rare, right?』  

『That’s right. While one goblin might occasionally stray from their group, having multiple strays in an area is unnatural.』  

『In that case, is there perhaps a Monster Tamer among the teachers back?』  

『Very likely.』

We only have surface-level knowledge regarding the Monster Tamer Job. Monster Tamers are a familiar presence in games and stories. In those examples, tamers capture a monster to bond with as an irreplaceable partner, but that shouldn’t be the case in this world.  

After all, monsters are born of miasma, it’s questionable if they even have free will and emotions. And even if they do, they probably can’t bond with humans anyway. It might be possible to attempt communication and bond with beings on Tur’s level, but former monsters are not common, and if it’s possible to tame them, you’d undoubtedly become one of the world’s greatest.

And so what I wanted to say is that it should be alright to defeat the goblins roaming in this mountain. While it may be a bad way to describe it, these goblins are probably compelled throwaway pawns.  

And while they may wound you in battle, they probably can’t kill you. Considering that they’re used for this class, they’re likely ordered not to kill anyone.

Incidentally, I wonder what the Creator God thinks of controlling monsters when they should be defeated instead? There’s probably some conditions regarding this, but I guess it’s not something to contemplate now.  

For the time being, since they’re still safe and I probably won’t be needed until later, I had Ciel ask Belltina a question. Actually, the two in front are too tense, they might tire themselves out too soon.

「Belltina, may we speak about your Job?」  

「Ah, um… Yes.」  

「Let’s have a short break while we’re at it.」

I don’t know if it’s just good timing, but Belltina has started to show exhaustion, so Ciel urged the group to rest. Noticing her name mentioned, Belltina was a bit startled; perhaps she was so focused to the point of not feeling her own exhaustion. I’ve concentrated to the point of ignoring exhaustion before, so I can relate. You think it’s still alright since you can still breathe normally, but then you’ve actually pushed yourself dangerously exhausted. It brings me back to that marathon I’ve run before. I was fine the whole time I was running, but the moment I stopped, it became painful to breathe and I lost strength in my legs, leading to them going numb. It’s surprisingly hard to be aware of when you’re straining yourself.  

Ciel has stamina, so she rarely reaches the point of complete exhaustion, and I’ve always made her rest whenever she starts to feel tired when we’re working out of town, so Ciel doesn’t have much resistance to taking a break.

「Palra, are you alright?」  

「I’m completely… No, I think I’m feeling a bit tired.」  

「In that case, let’s take a break here. Once we finish resting, we’ll need to head back.」  

「We’re going back?」  

「Considering the time, the class period should be ending soon.」

Ciel glanced at the watch we had kept in our magic pouch and I saw that we should be able to return right before the end of the period. This is probably why she decided to inform them, but then Palra showed a look of surprise.

「Ailneige, you know the time? Could you tell from the sun’s position, or so?」  

「I simply looked at my timepiece.」  

「A timepiece… you have one?」

Watches are sorceric tools, so they’re quite pricey. While sorceric tools are cheaper in Ausente, maybe she just didn’t expect us to bring one along. Even among hunters, it’s not common to own one, since you can roughly estimate the time using the sun. For example, you start making camp as it gets dark and begin working as the sun peeks out.  

Besides, you might be hesitant to move around too much in fear of damaging the watch, and there’s no point getting one if it just breaks.

「I have a magic pouch, you see.」  

「Eh!」  

「I received a small one from an acquaintance. Besides, since I work solo—although I’ve had a partner recently—I also have various other sorceric tools.」  

「It must be tough being alone.」  

「It’s not exa—… No, that’s correct.」

While it’s not particularly tough in our case, it’s hard to describe us as working alone. Our situation is uniquely different from regular people, so I’ve taught Ciel about what’s generally difficult to do normally. That must be why Ciel corrected herself.  

I can feel Ciel’s growth in how conversations like these can now be left to her, but since there’s something I need doing that is probably still difficult for her right now, I asked to switch out for a short moment.

As for what it is, it’s to suggestively smile at Belltina. Putting aside whether I managed to do well, there was a need to apply silent pressure on Belltina, since she might have noticed that Ailneige doesn’t really have a lot of sorceric tools on her. We immediately switched back and continued the conversation.

「Now then, Belltina, is it alright if I share what your Job is?」  

「Umm, yes.」  

「Palra, I want you to remember this: Belltina is a Magic Eye Holder.」  

「Magic Eye Holder?」  

「It’s an extremely rare Job. In Belltina’s case, I believe it allows her to see magic power, correct?」  

「Yes, Bell is able to see magic power.」  

「Can see magic power…?」

Yup, Palra doesn’t understand the value of being able to see magic power. Honestly, it probably isn’t known to the common people. I suspect this is because people who can see magic power are limited. Thanks to that, the value of magic power concealment is also barely known, which is helpful for us.

「Just to confirm, Belltina, you can see magic power even with objects obstructing your view, correct?」  

「Ah, umm, how do you know that much?」  

「When you previously found Tweisel, he was still a considerable distance away when you reacted.」  

「Ughh… Bell only managed to do it after working hard to notice when father was coming to Bell’s room.」

So that’s the reason? It’s because Belltina was hiding from her father that he was unable to recognize her true value. I can’t say whether it’s for better or for worse, but I personally think it’s for the better. Belltina’s family is apparently of the anti-Central faction, after all. Even if it’s not her intention, her parents may command her to be our opposition.

「If you can perceive magic power, you can apparently also detect the presence of monsters, so I had Belltina on the lookout. After all, it can be used to locate humans too.」  

「Woah～…」

Hearing Ciel’s explanation, Belltina let out a faint cheer. She sounds somewhat amazed, but maybe she’s just overwhelmed by the unexpected information. Monsters hold magic power since they are part of the miasma purification process, and the magic cores obtained from defeating them also hold magic power. Still, her reaction is understandable since not many can see magic power.  

Actually, the people who can immediately respond to surprise attacks from behind may be sensing magic power instinctively.

「As for why I also had Palra on lookout duty, it’s so that the two of you can work solo to some extent in the future.」  

「Me too?」  

「Bell hasn’t really decided to be a hunter yet…」  

「If you’re able to locate monsters, it could give you an advantage in joining parties. As for Belltina, I believe it would be best if you are at least capable of the bare minimum, just as a lifeline.」

Particularly with Palra’s case, since we’ve been using her to keep people away, I won’t be able to rest well if she suddenly dropped dead, so I want to train her up to a certain level. I don’t intend to go hardcore with the training, so they shouldn’t stand out in class.  

And so, Ciel’s explanation was finished, and now Palra and Belltina began talking to each other.

「Bell, your Job was actually amazing.」  

「It might be a rare Job, but that’s not true. Bell has never heard anyone call it amazing.」  

「From what Ailneige said, I don’t think that’s the case… but since it’s not fair that only your Job is exposed, I’ll tell you mine too. I’m an Advanced Huntsman.」  

「Having an Advanced Job is much more amazing, you know!」  

「But because of this, I was told that I had to go to the academy… Even though it’s so far from home and I don’t have any acquaintances here…」  

「That’s tough…」

The two seem to be resonating with each other. Belltina prefers to seclude herself and avoid human interaction, meanwhile Palra finds satisfaction in remaining in the small world of her village.  

They’re similar yet different, but they can probably find a lot in common between themselves. On this occasion, for example, instead of being concerned about how their Job may determine their life in the future, they’re saying that they’d rather return to the peace they had before. Palra would have rather remained in her village despite the inconveniences instead of being sent out to find a better life with her Job; Belltina, meanwhile, doesn’t really care about her Job and just wants to be a shut-in. Still, most people would probably be livid if they overheard their conversation.

『From the flow of the conversation, it might be best if we tell them about Ail’s job as well.』  

『Should I declare our Job as Sword Dancer?』  

『That should be fine, but would you prefer it to be more open-ended?』  

『It’s best to avoid telling lies, right?』  

『In that case, sharing that barrier sorcery is your specialty but you can also sword dance should be enough. The rest can be left to their imagination.』  

『Let’s do that.』

Ciel shouldn’t be the type to particularly detest lying, so the fact that she is showing some reluctance probably means that she sees the two a bit differently from other people. While I don’t know if she’ll eventually reach the point of considering them friends, this isn’t a bad thing at all. Anyhow, once she feels like she can divulge the name Cielmer without any political reason, I guess they’ll be considered friends?  

We’ve lied about many things in the past, but we’ve also been particularly picky with whom to divulge our Job to. Perhaps that’s why she is hesitant in lying about her Job. Though in the meantime, we can’t really tell them the truth yet.

「I believe you should already know, but I’m proficient in barrier sorcery. A D-rank monster shouldn’t be able to break through my defense; but against a C-rank monster, a hit or two could break it, so make sure we don’t encounter one; if we do, please run.」  

「So that’s how Ailneige is able to act solo as an E-rank hunter.」  

「You don’t necessarily need to go to dangerous places for simple herb collection, you see. The most I’d encounter are wolves or orcs, I think.」

There’s no harm in having a weapon, but since we generally avoid combat, herb collection avoids weapon damage and should be easy to do even for them. Especially since Belltina has Magic Eyes and Palra should be able to lay traps and secure the surrounding area after locating a collection point.  

As for the barrier thing, Ciel explained Ailneige’s limits as rehearsed, so I need to make sure to remember that as well.

「Also, I can sword dance.」  

「I saw you use a sword in our other class, but that explains it.」  

「It is in line with the nature of my Job. I can’t say how useful it will be, but I can probably handle E-rank monsters.」

Regarding the sword dance, she’s technically not lying. After all, we genuinely don’t know how useful Ciel’s sword attacks are when powered solely by Dance Princess. Ciel is skilled with sorcery on her own, so we can’t use that as a reference, but when swinging a sword, she is dependent on the full capabilities of Dance Princess. Additionally, we typically empower it with Song Princess as well. So when it’s just sword dancing, we don’t know how effective it would be.  

Ciel probably can’t trade blows with Juerd, at least.

With this, it should be about time for us to return, but there was a child-sized creature slowly lumbering towards our direction.

+++

# 176: Palra, Belltina, and the First Battle

『Ain, what should I do about this?』  

『It’s still a fair distance away; let’s observe if the two can notice it for now. If they still don’t by the time it gets too close, you can step forward and use it as a practice dummy for your rapier.』  

『And if they do?』  

『If there is still time to give instructions, let’s have the two of them defeat it while you stall for time. If they take too long, I’ll leave the final decision to you.』  

『Understood. Still, Palra aside, can Belltina even attack properly?』  

『It’s also to see if she can, if I have to say. Once we know this, we can assign party roles.』

While I was somewhat ominous about it, the approaching creature was just a stray wind goblin, so it’s no trouble. If it’s only goblins—even if we take Ailneige’s capabilities into consideration—I should be able to protect the two even from a hundred of them.  

So it isn’t an issue, and I’m honestly more afraid of taking friendly fire from the two when they attack from behind us. Those are still blockable, though. While they may have high-tier Jobs, Ailneige can easily defend against attacks from people with no combat experience. That reminds me, how do bow-using Jobs take down high-ranked monsters?

With close combat weapons like swords and spears, the blades can be sharpened by coating them—consciously or subconsciously—with magic power, or rather the power of one’s Job. From observing the Fool’s Gathering, even non-combat Jobs can do something similar, so I shouldn’t be mistaken. Still, it isn’t as effective as when done with a combat Job, so maybe they’re compensating with pure competency?  

Now with bow and arrows, enhancing the bow itself is easy, but enhancing arrows to be fired is different. Close-quarters weapons are enhanced through direct contact, while arrows are apparently a different story. I’m not really familiar with the details since I can’t use any attack imbued with magic power.

However, I have a hunch that enhancing an arrow might be within the realm of sorcery, which could explain why only people with particular Jobs—like Bowman and Huntsman—are able to pull it off. Even a normal arrow can take down a wolf, so I guess we’ll just have to hope that Palra is able to achieve this enhancement before encountering a stronger monster. Since we probably won’t be using a bow in the future.  

Heck, Ciel probably won’t be using the sword much after we leave the academy. After all, she’s undoubtedly much better off using sorcery.

While I was musing to myself, the goblin continued to draw nearer, and as it reached close enough that the two should be able to sense it, Belltina began acting restlessly. She turned to Ciel and Palra as if wanting to say something.  

Noticing this, Palra asked, 「Bell, what’s wrong?」 to which Belltina reacted with joy before remembering the situation and hurriedly explaining. While this went on, Ciel had retrieved her rapier.

「T-there’s a small—a small person-like thing coming towards us…!」  

「It’s seems like you’ve noticed it.」  

「Eh? Eh? …Ah!」

Palra could not immediately understand the situation from Belltina’s words alone, so by the time she realized what was going on, the goblin was just around the corner. However, since it was still apparently possible to give simple instructions, Ciel said, 「I’ll keep it occupied, so please stay back and bring it down.」  

It would have been impressive if the two immediately prepared for combat, but they seem to be far from that level yet, as they were overwhelmed and frozen in place. As this happened, a small green humanoid—the goblin appeared.  

_Ghgyagyagya!_—With a grating cry, it ran towards Ciel as it saw our group. In its hand was a thick piece of wood that served as a simple club, and as it approached us with moderately fast steps, it then swung the club down.

Ciel meets the swung club with her rapier before smoothly pulling back, successfully parrying it. It’s interesting how it appeared as if the club was pulled aside by Ciel’s sword. There was barely any impact felt, and the fact that she can achieve this even without access to the full power of the Dance Princess is impressive.  

As its club slammed to the ground, the goblin was dumbfounded and couldn’t understand what just occurred for a moment, but it soon realized what happened, resulting in it wildly swinging its club enraged. Ciel avoided it with a single step while making distance from the two at the back.

The two seem to have finally processed the situation and began preparing to attack.  

It felt like they were bewitched by Ciel’s movements for a moment, but let’s just ignore that. Perhaps, with Ciel’s beauty, it was simply unavoidable.  

While she wasn’t making a full effort, the two were lucky enough to see Ciel’s beautiful gestures, so I guess I’ll go with that reasoning.

As though dancing with the goblin, Ciel light-footedly dodged, parried, and occasionally countered its attacks without any difficulty. She can be left on her own, since even in the unlikely event that the goblin hits her, the damage still won’t reach her.  

On the other hand, the two back-liners don’t share the same composure; Palra has her bow drawn yet is unable to take a good aim at the moving goblin, while Belltina is slow with her spellcasting, and so far, every spell she’d launched had flown off into the distant horizon without any sign of hitting its mark. And honestly, her spells have low attack power, so even if it connects, it might not be able to defeat the goblin. After observing for a while, I don’t see this ending anytime soon, so I decided to call to Ciel.

『Ciel, could you limit the goblin’s movements a bit more?』  

『I can, but… It’s hard to aim, I see.』

After a quick glance behind, Ciel understood the situation and altered her behavior. Earlier, she was focused on evasion, but now she’s being more aggressive to keep the enemy in place. Hitting the raised club before it was swung, slashing at the ground ahead when the goblin attempts to move; while it may only be effective due to the enemy being a goblin, she successfully minimized the enemy’s movement.

This level of control is probably only possible with Ciel’s good grasp of the goblin’s movement, or rather, its rhythm. According to Ciel, everyone has their own attack rhythm, and by moving to its flow, you can deal with most anything. Breaking the enemy’s rhythm can also allow you to stop their movement. Though I can’t help but think that this feat is only possible for a Dance Princess with abundant combat experience like her.

Now then, the battle has taken a turn for the better, with the two finally landing their hits; the goblin is almost torturously wounded little by little, but as the end of the period was quickly approaching, Ciel eventually took it out of its misery with one last strike.

The now dead goblin’s body has abrasions, burns, and shallow cuts all over the place. Meanwhile, the two torturers were breathing heavily and anxiously stared at Ciel as if to ask if it’s finally over. Ignoring the two dazed girls, Ciel retrieved the goblin’s magic core and burned its body. By the time Ciel finished the usual routine and returned to the two, they had finally regained composure.

「Good work.」  

「Thanks, good work.」  

「Good workkk—…」

The apologetic Palra and the exhausted Belltina both seem to be unhappy with their performance. Considering that this is their first battle, I personally think they did well enough, but it looks like they don’t see it that way.

『That was a struggle, but it reminded me of Ain in the past; very adorable.』  

『You were so cool, Ciel.』  

『In that case, I’m happy. But this was only possible because I trust that Ain is protecting me, you know?』  

『Glad to be of strength.』

I couldn’t help but respond somewhat curtly from embarrassment. Had I been in control, my cheeks would have surely been bright red. Ciel’s understanding expression shows that she easily saw through my veneer of curtness, which only makes it more embarrassing.  

Seeing the two being gloomy, an idea appeared to have popped into Ciel’s mind, as she suddenly called out to them.

「You might have some dissatisfaction with your performance, but you’ll gradually get the hang of it.」  

「That might be true, but still…」  

「To celebrate our victory and safety, I’ll give you this.」

Saying so, Ciel handed over the recently acquired goblin magic core to Palra. She stared at the magic core for a while but then shook her head in refusal.

「I can’t accept this; you should be the one to keep it, Ailneige.」  

「In that case, I’ll hand this over for now, so you can repay me after you manage to defeat a goblin during our stay in the academy.」

Despite the twists and turns, that is the magic core of the first monster we party defeated. It should make for a perfect memento. We don’t need it ourselves, but it may end up having sentimental value to Palra.  

With Ciel being so adamant, Palra folded and was about to reach for it when the two of them noticed Belltina staring with envy. Upon realization, Palra quickly turned away.

『Is it possible to make alterations to a magic core?』  

『Magic cores used for sorceric tools are characteristically small, so it should be possible.』  

『Understood.』  

「Alright, then I shall keep this in the meantime. Once I find a way to cut and process it, I will return the magic core to you two, so pay it back eventually.」

After saying that, Ciel asserted, 「If we don’t leave now, we won’t make it in time,」 then turned around and walked off without waiting for their reactions. While watching over the two hurriedly chasing after her, I posed Ciel a question.

『Why are you so adamant about giving it to them?』  

『I suddenly remembered.』  

『Remembered what?』  

『See, when we became a hunter and were choosing requests, Ain said that the first request should be herb collection, right?』  

『I did. It was the first thing that came to mind about hunters.』

It’s actually more so about the adventurers in the stories in my old world, but I remember wanting to do those kinds of tasks since hunters were kind of similar.

『It made me think about how important a first experience is. Looking back, every first experience I had with Ain has become an important memory for me.』  

『That’s certainly a fair point. Let’s experience many more things in the future then, shall we?』  

『As long as Ain is with me, I don’t really mind if it’s not the first time, you know?』

_Wouldn’t that be boring, though?_ I thought at first, but if that day, that one day, were to continue on forever, I couldn’t help but find it to be a very tempting prospect.

◇◇◇

「Tomorrow will be your first rest day since the academy opening.」

As the day ended, we returned to the class A homeroom, where Ms. Claura spoke of tomorrow’s rest day. After defeating the goblin, we managed to return at a decently good time. We then split up with Belltina, whose face was overflowing with sadness, and this was enough to understand her situation in her own class, making me feel a bit bad. Live strong.

「I’m sure there are many of you looking forward to it, already making plans on what to do or how to unwind, but please take caution on how you spend your days. You are all allowed to leave the academy premises, but make sure to behave in ways befitting of a second academy student.  

Students who are planning on doing hunter work, in particular. While there’s nothing wrong with that, do avoid causing problems. If trouble is unavoidable, please make sure to protect yourselves, but do not be the one to start trouble! Alright?」

Based on how much emphasis is made, there must be a consistent number of students causing problems every year, or someone who has caused a major issue in the past years. I can’t deny that there are potential troublemakers in this class. There are already some names in my mind, and I’m sure the name Ailneige is also counted among these problem children.  

In the sense of getting dragged into trouble, we’ve already been involved with trouble since the announcement of enrollment passers. And in situations like this, both sides usually end up being treated as troublemakers.  

Honestly, I can’t confidently say that we won’t get into further trouble. After all, there are already at least two people who could rope us into trouble within the academy.

After reminding us to be on time the day after our rest day, the class was dismissed.

+++

# nterlude: Belltina’s Past and Academy Life -  ※Belltina POV

I—Belltina—was suddenly told by my father to leave the house that day. Things might have gone differently if we had had a proper conversation, but while part of Bell was anxious upon hearing that, there was also great relief.

◇◇◇

When I was born, my parents were apparently happy at first. Being a proud noble, father believed that a noble should have abundant magic power befitting their status, so he was happy that Bell had the foundations for abundant magic power. I can recall how he angrily told Bell this.  

Everything changed after Bell’s sorcery lessons began. Bell’s magic power gradually increased to the point of surpassing the standard for nobles, but after seeing how my sorcery wouldn’t improve no matter how hard I tried, father had since started yelling at me. Before I knew it, there were no more sorcery lessons, and mother wouldn’t look at Bell anymore.

Since then, Bell shut herself in her own room and would constantly try to watch out for father’s presence, because father would yell at me if we ended up crossing paths. If not, he would still have an annoyed and displeased face. I was so scared, so afraid, that whenever it felt like father was coming near my room, I would immediately hide under my bed. I didn’t even want to eat with them, so Bell ate alone in her room.  

But since I don’t really get to eat food properly that way, one day I got the courage to sneak to the kitchen, and since then I would ask for a portion of food there. With me leaving my room now, Bell became more vigilant of father’s presence, and on the occasion that Bell bumped into him, she would get yelled at and run crying back to the bedroom.

As Bell’s days continued like this, the day when Bell was bestowed her Job came. In other words, it was Bell’s 10th birthday, and Bell was now seeing things she’d never seen before. At first I didn’t notice, but when I searched for father’s presence as I do daily, I saw bluish-white stuff stuck to all sorts of things. This color was thinner in the air and thicker near sorcery tools, and after seeing the bluish-white stuff inside Bell through the mirror, I had a clue what it was.  

Remembering my original intention, I hurriedly checked to see if father was nearby and saw the bluish-white stuff from beyond the walls. I finally realized that this was magic power when I noticed a particularly intense presence of the bluish-white stuff approaching quickly. Knowing that this presence was father’s and what I was seeing was his magic power, I hid in a dark corner of my room.

Several seconds after, the door was violently opened, and father yelled, 「Belltina, show yourself!」 Normally, he would only scan the room and leave, but this time he directly called for Bell, so despite being afraid—since I thought that he might get scarier if I stayed quiet―I showed myself and responded, 「What might it be, father?」  

Seeing me come out, father scanned me from head to toe before scoffing and handing me a piece of paper.

「You are at least capable of imbuing this with magic power, aren’t you?」  

「Y-yeshh…」  

「Stop dawdling!」

Being yelled at by my irate father, I reflexively imbued it with magic power. Even with how bad Bell is at control, I can at least do this much. After all, I can operate magic circles, albeit badly. It may take Bell a long time to activate and only result in substandard effects, but being able to activate it does mean that I can imbue things with magic power.  

Looking at the paper, it had 【Belltina Chilandia Job: Magic Eye Holder】 written on it. I’ve never heard of the Job Magic Eye Holder before, but I immediately understood what it does. It must be because of this Magic Eye that Bell became capable of seeing magic power since this morning.

Father snatched the sheet of paper from Bell’s hands and muttered, 「Magic Eye Holder?」 with a puzzled look. It seems like father doesn’t know about this Job either.

「Has there been anything different since today?」

Father asked, but Bell didn’t respond. More precisely, Bell couldn’t respond. Judging that this meant that nothing was different, father lost interest in Bell and left the room.  

It felt like a storm had just passed, and now I’m alone in my room again. While badmouthing father in my mind, I repeatedly punched the nearest pillow.

◇◇◇

After learning about my Job, father stopped coming to my room. I learned this later while sneaking out of my room for food―I was able to move around the house more easily thanks to my Job―but it seems like father is concerned about my condition. Apparently, he’s trying to find if there’s any use for this unfamiliar Magic Eye Holder Job.  

Upon knowing this, Bell was convinced that my choice back then wasn’t a mistake. After all, if father had known what the Magic Eye Holder Job could do, Bell might have had to meet with father even more. If possible, Bell would rather live quietly without seeing father ever again.

Since then, I was able to have a peaceful, secluded life for a while. During this time, I learned that the reason why Bell is bad with sorcery is because her magic circuits are shorter than other people’s. While father and other people have their circuits extending up until their fingertips, Bell’s aren’t as long and extensive. Recalling what my tutor said before, shorter circuits limit the amount of magic power you can use at once, making it difficult to do sorcery. And that’s why Bell can’t do it well. Knowing this doesn’t really change anything, though.

Bell’s situation changed two years after father mostly lost interest in me, when it was time for Bell to enroll in an academy. I’d completely forgotten about it until then, but father suddenly came to me and said, 「You carrying the name of Chilandia is an embarrassment in itself. As a show of mercy, I’ll permit you to enroll in the second academy; see this as a final chance in freedom and leave the Chilandia House.」 It wasn’t just a verbal stipulation; father even provided a magic contract, so he seriously wants Bell to leave the house.

Having been here since birth and having secluded myself for a good portion of my life, the idea of leaving the house is very dreadful and worrying, but just the thought of never having to see father again gave Bell a great sense of comfort.  

The thought of never having to see father brought me a feeling of liberation I’ve never felt before; I felt like I could do anything, and I was able to read the content of the magic contract with a clear mind.

The contract says Bell will be forbidden to name herself as a member of the Chilandia house and will cut ties with the family. In exchange, Bell will be enrolled in the second academy and will be ensured the freedom to live as she likes with the expenses shouldered by the Chilandia family. Upon reaching the end of this contract via graduating, dropping out, or long-term non-attendance, Bell will be removed from the Chilandia family.

Bell had a lot of free time while in self-seclusion, so I actually studied a lot of things. To be more precise, Bell secretly borrowed books to read to kill time. Among those books is one that describes the second academy, so I have an idea of what kind of place it is. That’s why, seeing its name and father’s sign already on the contract, Bell spoke to father with confidence that I could do anything.

「Does this mean Bell is free to do whatever in the academy?」  

「See it as a final act of mercy.」  

「In other words, Bell is free to be reclusive and get the best dorm room, right?」  

「Hold on—」  

「If Bell recalls correctly, it’s probably not possible to stay cooped up in the other rooms. At the very least, Bell would need to go to the cafeteria to get food. If father can live without eating food, then Bell won’t force it.」  

「…Alright, but don’t you get carried away.」

After seeing father leave with a soured expression, I suddenly became afraid of what I dared to do a moment ago, but since the contract is sealed, father will have to enroll Bell no matter what. Otherwise, the magic contract’s recoil will take effect.

And a while after, Bell’s second academy enrollment plan was made official.

◇◇◇

Once my enrollment was confirmed and Bell could move into the dorm, Bell was immediately sent out with the minimum things needed for my free lifestyle. Bell normally enrolled and passed with her own abilities, but father used his connections so we could see the results early, which is how Bell was able to move in earlier than the others. Since Bell was really scared when encountering many unfamiliar people during the enrollment, this honestly saved Bell, so Bell stayed silent and obeyed. No, honestly, I just couldn’t say anything. I don’t want father to yell at me again.

When Bell moved into the dorm, father said, 「The moment you exit the academy, you are no longer a daughter of mine,」 which filled me with a strange sense of liberation and, at the same time, released a heavy weight from my stomach.

As Bell’s dorm life began, it was time for Bell to practice living her own. Bell’s room, the second best after the one for royalty, has the necessary equipment needed for independent living. Here, you can cook, wash clothes, and take a bath. Groceries aren’t an issue either. Bell just needs to tell the people here what I need, and they will deliver it to my front door the next day. These purchases will be paid for by the Chilandia house, so while Bell doesn’t plan on buying anything luxurious, I won’t hesitate on buying necessities.

Bell brought a lot of long-lasting food when moving in, so it should be alright for a while, but unlike at home, Bell doesn’t have any servants around. Considering how Bell will need to do everything by herself after leaving the academy, practicing this early on isn’t a bad idea. Food will eventually run out if you don’t know how to cook, but fortunately, since I’ve been sneaking into the kitchen for food, I’m somewhat familiar with the equipment.  

At first, Bell failed several times, wounding herself, and the food wasn’t delicious at all, but after several days of practicing 3 times a day, Bell could now make relatively edible food. And since Bell preferred to stay secluded, I also managed to learn how to clean, wash clothes, and take a bath on my own.[1](https://re-library.com/translations/two-as-one-princesses/volume-6/interlude-belltinas-past-and-academy-life-first-half-part-2-%e2%80%bbbelltina-pov/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-111807)　

And before I noticed it, the academy opening was fast approaching, meaning I have to leave my room soon. Bell has finally gotten used to life by herself and was thinking how it would be nice to just continue living like this, but that isn’t possible.  

There was a provided document explaining academy opening, so Bell panickedly looked for it and read the contents. I already know about how the classes are done beforehand, and it’s good that I now know where my homeroom is, but it says here that they’ll be holding a party. While Bell does have a dress—I brought one that doesn’t stand out—I never thought I’d have to wear it ever again.

Moreover, isn’t the academy a place where Bell will have to spend a long time with strangers to begin with?  

Bell was enjoying her life alone so much that she forgot this. Do I have to speak to people I don’t know? Can’t I stay in seclusion? If I drop out, I won’t be able to continue this lifestyle, so Bell can’t have that happen.

Thinking ahead, Bell also needs to consider her life after leaving the academy. Suddenly, Bell couldn’t help but feel anxious. Let me just stay inside my room for today.

◇◇◇

It’s so over. Unbeknownst to Bell, everything was so over. Bell just decided to go home right after the opening homeroom, and now everyone in class seemed to be friendly with each other; Bell was left in the dust, silently waiting for the party to get over at a quiet corner.  

And then, at this party, I happened to see Alcrei. Being Chilandia’s shame, Bell rarely leaves the house, but I have been brought to different events every now and then. One of these events included gatherings for children close in age, and there, for some reason, Alcrei knew Bell was a failure and constantly bullied Bell for it. Moreover, since Alcrei’s Tweisel family was of greater status, father never came to my rescue—he probably would have if the Tweisel were lower status but would still yell at me at home afterwards―and Alcrei would pick on me every time we met until he felt satisfied.

Because of that, Bell’s heart nearly stopped when I saw him, and Bell desperately ran around to avoid being discovered by him.

After that day, the classes began, and while everyone else was enjoying each other’s company, Bell was all by her lonesome. At first, it didn’t really bother me, but since I was constantly surrounded by happy people, it felt uncomfortable being there. Since everyone was chatting with their neighbors, Bell felt bad for the people next to me; everyone is so big and scary, and I can’t help but twitch when I hear a loud voice.  

Still, thinking about the future, I can’t just be absent from my classes; whenever I return to my room, I feel almost glad to be alone by myself.

In the midst of this, two days after the opening, during the Magic Circle Studies course I took for some reason, I happened upon a person who would change my life.

+++

# Interlude: Belltina’s Past and Academy Life (Second Half) ※Belltina POV

My first encounter with her is… very hard to describe. It was the first day of Magic Circle studies; around me were all unfamiliar people, and the seats were mostly occupied—at that time, Bell even considered going back to her room rather than having to sit next to someone. This particular course is also available for upperclassmen to enroll in, so there were a lot of large people around, and Bell really wanted to go home. Still, thinking of the future, becoming an artificer seemed like a good option, so it would be best for Bell to attend this class.  

As an artificer, Bell could seclude herself and simply make sorceric tools. Bell might have to become a hunter if left with no other options, so I also took hunter courses, but the ideal would be work I could do while being reclusive. Bell doesn’t want work that needs interacting with people.

Just as Bell was about to be overwhelmed by the feeling of wanting to go home and the anxieties of the future, I found her.  

It was a girl who didn’t look scary and was smaller than Bell. With only that information, Bell sat down next to her without even seeing her face. Bell then got curious about what kind of person she was and reflexively stared at her.  

While not on full power, I constantly have my magic eyes turned on. This is so I can quickly run when I see a scary person—just like how I run the moment I notice father back at home—and I’ve worked hard to be able to use it at all times other than when asleep. However, if I actually focus on using it, I get exhausted from seeing too much magic power, so I generally have it on low power.

This backfired on me—though in hindsight, this was for the best—because I was only able to notice it after getting so close: the girl next to me has a lot more magic power than father. So much magic power; Bell has never seen that much before. And yet Bell didn’t notice until sitting next to her. Bell has no idea why this was; all Bell knows is that this girl is so much better at controlling magic power than anyone she knows.  

While it seems like the girl isn’t using sorcery, she actually had a barrier up the whole time. Moreover, it’s not the commonly seen round barrier; it matches the shape of her body, as if she’s wearing an extra layer of clothes. Seeing this, Bell realized—

This girl is very talented, Bell is sure of it.  

However, Bell noticed one more thing. While the girl’s sorcery is obviously amazing, despite this, Bell didn’t feel scared of her at all. Being smaller than Bell, she isn’t really intimidating. And, how do I describe this? …Her gaze when she noticed Bell was like those of the adults that don’t think badly of Bell. People who are mean or eventually end up bullying Bell have a different kind of expression when looking at her.

Eventually, the class began, and Bell finally noticed just how long she was staring at the girl, but since the girl didn’t say anything, she really isn’t a scary person after all.

◇◇◇

When the Magic Circle Studies class ended, Bell decided to take a certain action.  

I was thinking of going to the academy cafeteria, a place I’ve never been to before.  

Up until now, I would either return to my room to eat or bring a simple lunch to eat somewhere with no people, but I didn’t bring lunch this time. Bell could just return to the dorm instead, but in case of future emergencies, I want to know how the cafeteria works.[1](https://re-library.com/translations/two-as-one-princesses/volume-6/interlude-belltinas-past-and-academy-life-second-half-part-1-%e2%80%bbbelltina-pov/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-111809)　  

As for why this came to mind, it’s because there’s a person nearby who probably won’t get angry even if I secretly followed. If the girl is also heading to the cafeteria, Bell will secretly follow her and see how the cafeteria system works.

And so, Bell is about to eat her first cafeteria food since arriving here. Being able to get food without needing to speak much to the cafeteria person, Bell was touched by how amazing this cafeteria is.  

The limited number of open seats because there are so many people around is an issue, though. Next time, I’ll try coming when there are fewer people. Fortunately for Bell, my Magic Eyes allow me to see where there are less people, but there are barely any seats with no people around at this time. It’s impossible for Bell to eat next to unfamiliar people, so I desperately searched and saw an open seat nearby a person I do know, so I decided on that one.

While she might not be scary, it’s still impossible for Bell to talk to her, so I sat near her while making sure she didn’t notice before focusing my attention on the meal. The cafeteria’s food is probably delicious, but since there are so many people around, I couldn’t remember much of the taste. Incidentally, I just noticed now since there are other people eating, but Bell seems to be a slow eater.  

Because of that, instead of savoring the taste, Bell was desperately trying her best to eat faster. Thinking about it now, Bell didn’t really need to hurry since she wasn’t really pressed for time.

As I was focused on the food, the girl in front of me suddenly stood up, told me a troublesome person was on the way, and left. I was startled since I didn’t expect her to talk to me, but the ‘troublesome person’ part sounded concerning, so I focused on my Magic Eyes and stared at the cafeteria entrance. Among the different clumps of magic power, I saw one from a person I could never forget.  

Someone Bell would rather not see, only second to father… Honestly, Bell might rather see father instead of him. Before I noticed, my body was already preparing to escape. I don’t want to meet him to the point that I didn’t hesitate to leave my food unfinished.

Thanking the girl for telling me, I headed to the exit, but Bell couldn’t move fast enough because there were so many people.  

And so, Bell ended up crossing paths with him, with Alcrei. Fortunately, he left after a few words, but had we met while I was sitting down, there’s no telling what he would’ve done to Bell.  

After this, I found the girl who helped me, and seeing how skillfully she weaved through the waves of people, Bell decided to follow behind her. Besides, Bell also wanted to thank her.

As I was following behind, still unsure about how to talk to her, we eventually got into the dorm’s floor traversal apparatus without me noticing it.  

Being all alone with her in an enclosed room, Bell completely blanked out, but as she was about to leave for her room, I finally gathered the courage to call for her. Rather, after coming this far, not talking to her is no longer an option. After all, there’s no one else around. She surely noticed that Bell has been following her.

「What’s wrong?」 Seeing that she doesn’t seem to think badly of Bell, I mustered my strength and introduced myself.

◇◇◇

The girl’s name was Ailneige, she said. Ailneige lives on the same floor as Bell—meaning she could afford it—and she apparently noticed Bell following her the whole time. Actually, once we were alone, Bell noticed that Ailneige had another spell that was constantly up other than her barrier. This is probably detection sorcery. If my eyes aren’t mistaken, then she seems to be using it throughout this whole floor. Bell knew she had a lot of magic power, but it seems like she had even more magic power than I thought.

Right there, I then explained why I was following her, incidentally also explaining how Bell was given up on, and I honestly don’t remember what else Bell said, but even after everything, she didn’t seem to think badly of Bell.

Since then, we’ve had several classes together, and I was able to approach, get noticed, and talk to her; I even got into talking terms with Palra—a commoner who aspires to become a hunter—things that would have been unthinkable for the lonesome old Bell.  

However, the two of them are in a different homeroom class, so Bell couldn’t be with them all the time… Still, I’m now a bit excited about going to the academy. Even the Combat Training I hate feels just a bit bearable with the two of them there. And while we don’t meet during homeroom, at least one of them is present in most of Bell’s courses, so I even want to just skip over homeroom and get to the classes ASAP.

Palra, in particular, always gestures to me whenever she sees me, so Bell can rest assured and sit next to her, and she also talks with me a lot, so I kind of feel like we’re really close. Ailneige is… It’s weird to say when Bell is the one pursuing her, but she’s a bit hard to approach, so—

「Palra, what do you think of Ailneige?」  

「Of Ailneige?」

—One day, since Bell had the chance to talk privately with Palra, Bell asked for her thoughts. Bell has been curious about how Palra sees Ailneige since they’ve been together longer, and I also wanted to hear other people’s impressions of her.

「Let’s see… It’s just a hunch of mine, but she’s probably a noble, isn’t she?」  

「Bell thinks so as well.」  

「But she doesn’t seem to be concerned about status and stuff, though it’ll probably be scary to get on her bad side either way.」  

「Is it because she’s that strong?」  

「All I know is that she’s likely far stronger than me—」  

「Is that so? Understood. Thank you very much.」  

「Oh, but you know, I want to get much closer to Ailneige.」  

「Bell… Bell would like to become closer with her too.」

As I thought, normal people can’t seem to tell just how strong Ailneige is. Which is probably why she’s not getting talked about. After all, she’s the strongest among everyone Bell has ever seen, and that includes the principal. Bell even wonders why she’s in the academy.  

Still, since she’s here, Bell wants her to stay in the academy until graduation, but Bell also thinks that the slight distance is fine. Bell just needs to be careful not to make her mad.

◇◇◇

It’s finally come: the Field Training course. Dragging my feet there, Bell was then sentenced to grouping with other people. If Bell ever joins a party with strangers, Bell would surely be ignored. That would be the best case; Bell might just get straight up bullied.
