You see, after forming the party, we’ll be going into a mountain. Since the teachers’ eyes won’t always be present there, if Bell gets bullied, Bell might just die.  

But very, very, very, very, very fortunately for Bell, she miraculously has acquaintances. Just as Bell had decided to turn around and run if the three of us didn’t end up in the same party, 「Shall we form a party with the three of us?」 Ailneige made a proposal.

If Bell misses this chance, there might be no other chances left, so I immediately nodded my head.

And with that, our formed party went inside the mountain, where—while it was already obvious before—Bell learned that only she has no stamina. Before that, Bell had to tell Palra that she was a noble, but Palra accepted Bell, which was really a weight off the shoulders, so that was nice. Now, with no need to keep secrets, Bell feels like we’ve gotten a bit more closer.  

Bell was really surprised when Ailneige asked Palra if she wanted to know Ailneige’s true identity, but it seems like talking about it won’t really inconvenience Ailneige. In that case, then she must be a very high-status person. People occasionally get killed for knowing a high noble’s secrets, so Bell is of the opinion that Palra’s cautious judgment was correct.

If you needlessly poke your nose in other people’s business, you’ll only get dragged into trouble. Just like father’s bad tempers.

That aside, back to my stamina issue. I already knew it during Combat Training, but both Ailneige and Palra have plenty of stamina. But they’re also kind of reversed? For some reason, Ailneige, who’s a sorcerer, has even more stamina than Palra, who lived in the mountain her whole childhood.  

Meanwhile, Bell gets tired after just a short walk on the mountain trail, and we had to rest because of that. If Bell had to make an excuse, keeping alert while walking made me tired much easier. But Palra, who was doing the same, seemed completely fine, so Bell probably just doesn’t have stamina.

The two of them didn’t get angry at all, and after the break we took, we ended up encountering our first monster—a goblin.  

Ailneige stood in front so we only had to attack, but we were overwhelmed with this first fight with a monster, so we couldn’t move for a while even after getting instructions.  

Moreover, while we were in the middle of battle, we couldn’t keep our eyes off of Ailneige’s movements. The way Ailneige fought with her rapier was, as the namesake Sword Dancing describes, smooth and almost rehearsed; it looked as if she was really dancing. When we finally remembered our current situation, we quickly returned to attacking, but in the end, Ailneige practically defeated it alone. If she were alone, she would have probably ended the fight faster.

It’s not like Bell wants to become a hunter, but Bell hates being a burden like this even more. Ailneige said that we’d eventually get used to it, but it felt as though Bell was told that she was useless, which I can’t necessarily deny.

No. That’s not it. Bell is scared of being abandoned by Ailneige. Bell is scared of being left behind, of no longer being able to experience this now-fun academy life.

That’s why Bell secretly asked Palra if we can train a bit together during our free time so that Bell can fight even just a bit better.

+++

# 177: Princess Leshimiiya and Munyechka’s Doll

「Please forgive me for the sudden call.」  

「I don’t mind. To begin with, it was simply an invitation for tea; there’s no need for apologies.」  

「That’s… right…」

On the other side of the table lined with a tea set and snacks, Princess Leshimiiya answered with an awkward smile. I don’t intend to comment on it, so I took my cup of black tea to my lips. As the nation’s princess, she probably wanted to know how Cielmer has been doing at the academy so far.

As for what led to this, since tomorrow is our first holiday, Princess Leshimiiya took the opportunity to invite us for tea. We were already contemplating whether we should play with the spirits on the roof today, so with no reason to refuse, we came.  

Since I’m going to be playing with the spirits after this anyway—which was the pretext Ciel used—I’m the one currently active. Because the princess generally treats me as one of higher status, interacting with her isn’t exhausting, but there’s no telling what her servants’ opinions are, so I can’t help but feel for her complicated position. If it were Ciel, she probably wouldn’t be bothered by trivial things like that.

In any case, since it seems like the princess is having difficulty initiating the conversation, I’ll start with a random topic. The cookies they prepared to pair with the tea should be a decent launching point. It is pretty delicious, as one would expect from a tea snack of royalty. It’s far more delicious than any department store cookies in my old world—I’ve never tasted fancy cookies, so I can’t use it for comparison—and even in this world, I’ve only tasted snacks of around this level at our manor in Central.

「This cookie is delicious; where does this come from?」  

「These were sourced from my mother’s personal purveyor. I’m delighted to hear that you enjoy it.」  

「As expected of one personally recognized by the queen. I’d love to buy from them sometime.」  

「Would you like me to provide you an introduction?」  

「I likely wouldn’t be able to purchase anything if I go alone, so please do so if the opportunity arises.」

_We_ could probably buy a whole store’s worth of it, but _Ailneige’s_ budget can only afford these as a once-a-year treat at best. I don’t know if she understands the exact nuance of my words, but Princess Leshimiiya most likely knows that I, a student who can afford living in the highest dorm floor a regular student can avail, am not saying the truth at all.  

As if to prove my point, Princess Leshimiyiia giggled before answering, 「Alright. I look forward to that day arriving.」

「Were the snacks from our previous meetings also purchased from that purveyor?」  

「That’s right. While we do have several favorites, we’ve been partial to that particular shop recently.」  

「Is it currently trending in Ausente?」  

「If I have to admit; I’m hoping to make it a fad in the near future.」  

「I see. Forgive my embarrassing lack of research. My manners and etiquette are also different from that of Ausente’s, so if you notice me behaving unsightly, please be frank with me about it.」  

「I’m not going to nitpick on trivial errors in private, you know. Besides, your conduct and gestures are always enchantingly beautiful, Miss Ailneige.」  

「I feel honored to hear that, but I still have a long way to go.」

No matter how you cut it, Ciel’s conduct and gestures are much more beautiful. I know it’s just polite niceties, but if _my_ movements are enchanting, then Ciel’s would be hypnotic, wouldn’t they? Her movements, filled with intent from her body to her fingertips, will likely look more impressive the more knowledgeable the viewer is.  

Just as I reached for my teacup, Ciel called out to me.

『Is it time for talking practice?』  

『So you’ve noticed… We might be invited to tea parties in the future, so I was thinking that it would be best if we’re equipped to safely handle it.』  

『That sounds bothersome.』  

『I feel the same way.』

Nonetheless, we already had a party as soon as the academy opened, so there’s nothing to lose in practicing. Still, it’d be nice if I only had to talk to Ciel forever—let’s stop with that thought.  

Now then, it should be about time to broach the main subject, and it seems like the princess has managed to pull herself together.

「Incidentally, Miss Ailneige, how has the academy been?」  

『So, how has it been?』  

『Hard to say. There are boring times, but there have also been a lot of fun and stimulating things so far… I suppose? I want to chat with Munyechka more, at least. Also, watching Palra and Belltina is… interesting?… I guess? For some reason, I don’t really get tired of them.』  

『That’s great to hear.』

For me, it’s like I’m attending school with Ciel, which makes me feel a bit of happy nostalgia. Or so I wanted to respond, but since I’ve been quiet in front of the princess for a short while, I gave up on that.  

Still, so that is Ciel’s opinion of the two girls? I hope this progress continues and they eventually become friends, but this does make me feel a bit lonely; it’s complicated to describe. That aside, I’m more curious about how Ciel couldn’t properly define her relationship with Palra and Belltina. Is it because she’s never been with children close to her age for a long time?—Anyway, I want Ciel to feel more of these positive emotions in the future. Etching that in my mind, I respond to the princess’ question with Ciel’s answer in consideration.

「Some classes do leave me unsatisfied, but that’s simply the result of my course choices, so I suppose it can’t be helped. Other than that, I’ve been enjoying my time.」  

「That’s good to hear. Regarding the classes, I can’t say that I disagree with your assessment, but it is the result of my personal course choices as well.」  

「Rather, Princess Leshimiiya, shouldn’t you be already educated enough to be eligible for graduation?」  

「Well, who knows? All I can say is that I didn’t necessarily enroll in the academy strictly to learn. Besides, Miss Ailneige, aren’t you active enough as a hunter to fulfill the graduation requirements as well?」  

「Who’s to say? It’s a bit special in my case. My sorcery is primarily self-studied, and, most importantly, my weapon handling is amateurish at best.」

It’s such a hollow conversation, but I suppose this is just how nobles gather information. I’m sure our conversation is mostly like this because there are other people around, but it’s not like we can always be alone with Princess Leshimiiya. She’s a nation’s princess, while we’re hiding our identity. We would probably be allowed to be alone together if I revealed it, but considering the troublesome consequences, I guess this is still better.

「You were doing practice swings during class, I recall.」  

「Princess Leshimiiya, do you plan on specializing in sorcery?」  

「I have learned swordsmanship for self-defense, but the moment I’m required to take up the sword, that practically means that we’ve already lost the war…」  

「You are a princess, after all.」

I answered in jest, and she shot me with a slightly exasperated gaze. It’s not like I don’t understand her feelings, but we and the princess have different roles, or rather what’s required of us is different, so please stop with those eyes. To begin with, we aren’t really required to do anything, nor do we have responsibilities.

「Speaking of class, there was an unfamiliar face among your party members, wasn’t there?」  

「Unfamiliar face… do you mean Fithuille?」  

「Most likely.」  

「She is… How do I describe her…」  

「I don’t mind if you can’t share about her.」

I know that she’s one of Munyechka’s dolls. Knowing her name is good enough. In fact, I could even just ask Munyechka directly. That’s why I really don’t mind, but I suppose the princess just wants to be accommodating.

「It’s not that. The truth is, I mostly don’t know much about her either. All I can say for sure is that she’s basically a bodyguard…」  

「Isn’t that dangerous?」  

「I’m at least certain that she’s not dangerous. After all, his Majesty and the headmistress have guaranteed her background.」  

「In that case, you probably can’t refuse even if you want to.」

Hearing my words, the princess shows a wry smile. Her refusal would mean that she doesn’t trust the king and the headmistress’ judgment. There are things she can’t refuse even if she wanted to. As to be expected from a hierarchical-aristocratic system. In the princess’ case, the king being her actual father probably made it hard to refuse as well. Personally, I see it as her father cherishing her to the point of having an S-rank hunter—even one only at 1/10 strength—guard her. But this probably isn’t something that she should hear from my mouth, so I’ll keep quiet.

「From my personal impression of her, I feel that Fithuille is somewhat similar to you, Miss Ailnege.」  

「In what way?」

While impressed by her sharp observation, I inquired. Princess Leshimiiya moved her head a bit as though to flip through her memories before giving her answer.

「The way she is attending the academy whilst hiding her true strength, if I had to say? I believe that both of you are capable enough to not need enrollment in this academy in the first place. Regarding Fithuille, she is likely to be around high-level hunter in terms of strength. Moreover, I suspect that she might be far older than us… possibly even an adult.」  

「She doesn’t appear that way, though…」

Actually several centuries old on the inside, but judging only from her appearance, it’d be impossible to guess. I personally think that guessing that she’s a doll would be easier than guessing her actual age, but that might not be the case for other people.

「Her capability as a bodyguard was acknowledged by father and the headmistress, so she must be fairly strong. There is a possibility that she had another noble’s recommendation, but there was nothing I could find about her background. If a family wanted to have the honor of raising a royal’s bodyguard, they should have boldly announced their name. Since that wasn’t the case, it’s highly possible that she was chosen for her capability, and had there been anyone of her strength among our peers, there would be many rumors about her by now.」  

「And that’s why you suspect she’s an adult.」  

「That’s what I believe, at least…」

After saying that, Princess Leshimiiya shot me a meaningful glance. With Ailneige—or rather Cielmer—existing as a precedent, there is a chance of having another highly capable individual close in her age with their identity kept a secret from the public.  

It doesn’t apply to me, since I am technically older than I appear, but Ciel’s appearance matches her age—though she’s relatively small—and she’s already around B-rank in strength even without my assistance, so I can’t deny the possibility.

「However, I doubt Rynaetra found you getting a new bodyguard all that amusing, did she?」  

「That’s… right. In fact, Rynaetra looks at her with an antagonistic glare, among various other things. Fithuille was able to deal with her well, so things fortunately never escalated into incidents. Fithuille’s composure is also part of why I suspect that she may actually be an adult.」  

「So when your party encountered the goblin in the mountain, did Fithuille take the initiative to lead?」  

「No, she only observed and gave words of advice. That aside, would I be right to assume that your party also encountered a goblin?」  

「It seems like it was arranged that every party would encounter one. In our case, I took the opportunity to test my two party members’ current combat abilities.」

Considering that she works as a teacher through Semiette, Fithuille is likely skilled at coaching too. With that topic finished, it was now time to talk about my party.

+++

# 178: The Princess, Fithuille, and About the Party

「That reminds me, Miss Ailneige, you previously said that you would be the party vanguard, but was that alright?」  

「In terms of swordsmanship, I can’t say for sure if I’m sufficiently combat ready, but as for sorcery, I’m capable enough to be a qualified hunter. As a solo E-rank hunter, my barrier can defend against goblin attacks without as much as a scratch.」

『If there’s something that can break through Ain’s barrier, we’d be in big trouble.』  

『But before that, the land around us would apparently be in bigger trouble. However, there may be ways of overcoming my barrier without needing to break it, so I’m not letting my guard down.』  

『Yes, I’m always counting on you.』

Putting aside my barrier’s durability for now, my barrier should be able to make it look like we’re capable of close-quarters combat against monsters. Rather, Ciel could probably do it on her own. The problem is that her attacks are light, so it’ll completely devolve into a battle of attrition, but Ciel should be able to avoid all attacks, I think?  

While my barriers are crazy, I feel like Ciel when she focuses on dodging is basically on the same level of crazy. If you want to hit Ciel when she has my support, the best option would likely be to deny her any space to evade with a wide-area attack. But with the force spread out, the impact will never breach my barrier, so it would be hell for the enemy.

Hard and difficult to hit. That sounds familiar.

「For reference, may I ask up until monsters of what rank are you able to handle?」  

「I’d run if I bumped into a C-rank monster. While my barrier won’t break in one hit, it wouldn’t last for long either. With D-rank monsters, I’m fine even with a few of them. After all, even when I was surrounded by a pack of wolves in the past, I was able to return safely.」

If Princess Leshimiiya wasn’t the one asking this question, I probably wouldn’t have answered. Since the princess knows that Ailneige is Cielmer, she should know that my answer doesn’t actually mean anything, hence why I’m telling her. If I kept too many secrets in front of a royal, the people surrounding her might find it odd. I also think the princess posed this question with the understanding that it’s something that I might be willing to answer. For that reason, I’m intentionally playing along.

「It would be appreciated if you kept this a secret between us, Princess Leshimiiya.」  

「Yes, of course. I am not so ignorant as to thoughtlessly mention the abilities of another nation’s hunter.」  

「My bad.」

It’s a truly hollow conversation, but it’s probably necessary, so I’ll follow suit.  

I’ve been using this as an opportunity to practice, after all, so this much isn’t any trouble.

「So how did your party members fare?」  

「They still have much to work on. It was apparently their first time fighting a monster as well.」  

「It must have been dreadful for them. I can still remember the fear I felt during my first confrontation with a monster despite having bodyguards by my side.」  

「Me as well; during my first monster encounter, I was so scared that I couldn’t move.」  

「You as well, Miss Ailneige?」  

「It was several years back. It’s not as if I’ve been able to use barriers since I was born, you know?」

『Oh, is that so? Ain was already using a barrier as early as I can remember, I think.』  

『Regarding that, it took nearly a year from your birth—or rather from the time I was sent to your side—until I was able to use barriers. Though back then, there was no way to keep track of time, so I don’t actually know the exact days it took.』  

『Besides that, Ain didn’t need any sleep, right?』

While Ciel and I were chatting, Princess Leshimiiya had a slightly surprised expression. While she does know Ailneige’s true identity, what does she actually think we are?  

We’re just about the same age—well, technically, I’m a year older than her. But honestly, her reaction is understandable. That reminds me… I wonder how many of our classmates actually know that I am—or rather, Ciel is—a year older than most of them. Come to think of it, there probably aren’t many who know Ciel’s real age in general. The Hunter Guild might know, but I don’t know how many currently have access to that information, and Mother Fii isn’t really the type to be concerned about age. Actually, Ciel herself doesn’t seem to care about her own age either.

「I genuinely thought that you were already proficient with sorcery in the far past, Miss Ailneige.」  

「I’m still far from proficient even now, you know? I’m just a humble E-rank hunter. While bumping into a D-rank monster wouldn’t be a problem, whether I can defeat them is another story.」  

「…Y-Yes, that’s true. But from our eyes, that’s already more than what the average is capable of.」  

「In my case, I concentrated all my effort in a single specialization, you see. If the princess were to do the same, you may even surpass me with ease.」  

「Is that so?」  

「From what I saw during the entrance exam, you should have more magic power than I do… However, with your status, honing only a single skill may prove to be difficult.」

She surely has royal duties to attend to, and, honestly, there’s no need for her to go that far to master sorcery. After all, she’s the princess of a nation. While it would be better for her to be able to defend herself, it’s ultimately fine even if she’s completely incapable of self-defense. After all, she has guards to compensate for that.

「Forgive me for somewhat forcefully returning to the previous topic, but from your perspective, how was your party members’ performance? As citizens of Ausente, I want to keep informed about their competency.」

In other words, unlike with Ailneige, she wants all available information. Despite her courteous tone, it’s practically an order. While I’m sure refusing wouldn’t count as lese majeste, if she continues asking afterwards, it’ll be difficult to dodge the question without making my identity public here. Both Palra and Belltina are actually this nation’s citizens, so Princess Leshimiiya’s words take precedence over mine, even as Central’s princess-like figure. But let me turn her down one time.

「I’m not really one to divulge others’ personal information…」  

「Could you make an exception just this once?」

And with that, I’ll stop dodging the question. This brings no harm to Ailneige on its own anyway, and, I believe, the princess is adamant about this because she wants to know whether the two party members have done anything that could possibly upset or harm Ailneige.  

Belltina, in particular, is also from an anti-Central family, so the princess must also have some concerns.

「Understood. However, I’d prefer to keep the number of people overhearing as little as possible—」

As I was speaking, I could easily feel the people around us turn their gazes towards me.  

They must be concerned about us being left alone. Well, I’m not backing down on my demands, though.

「I would appreciate it if you could limit it to one female bodyguard. I don’t mind if you even request for someone stronger than me.」

Hoping that the princess takes the hint, she nodded and responded, 「That won’t be an issue.」  

After that, she commanded a nearby attendant to bring Fithuille here and turned to me as if to confirm. As I nodded, Princess Leshimiiya smiled with relief.  

Before long, Fithuille arrived, and the princess then ordered everyone but her to leave. There were several who appeared hesitant, but I confirmed through detection that everyone left the room.

「Princess, you called?」  

「I need you to serve as my bodyguard right now. The reason I only called for you is because I want to limit the people hearing the contents of our conversation.」  

「Understood. But is Thuille really needed?」

Fithuille gave off an unsociable impression, but when I think about how she’s still Munyechka on the inside, it’s just amusing. On that note, Iena and Semiette are also technically Munyechka. Rather than being a good actress, I probably just haven’t seen the _real_ Munyechka yet. It’s possible that the main body’s personality is also an act.  

However, I think all of them share a general thought process, so it’s not like I can’t trust her.

「That’s…」

Princess Leshimiiya looks my way with a troubled expression. Well, I was the one who requested Fithuille, so that’s only natural.  

Following the princess’ gaze, Fithuille turned to me and, with barely any change in expression, opened her eyes wide.

「Correction. If security is actually needed, then Thuille alone is not enough. Is there a different reason?」  

「—You can tell her true power, then?」  

「I can.」

Hearing Fithuille’s confident response, Princess Leshimiiya showed a contemplative expression. She must be adjusting her personal assessment. After all, she just learned that Fithuille is a talent capable of seeing through Ailneige’s true strength. While it may be partly true that she saw through my power, the reason she reacted like that was probably because she personally knows about us. Munyechka must have informed her, after all, and I don’t think the dolls don’t share information with each other.

「Back to the previous topic, I am not expecting you to fight Miss Ailneige. If things ever escalate to that point, there’s no telling what Ausente’s fate would be.」  

「Thuille was only called so the princess can talk in private?」  

「Yes, it was so we can be alone with the least amount of people.」  

「Besides, I’m familiar with how nobles tend to react.」

Since the princess seemed curious about my reasoning, I offered a plausible-sounding explanation. The truth, however, is that I know Fithuille is actually Munyechka, and I’m certain she holds no ulterior motives toward Palra and Belltina.  

Apparently, this fabricated reason was convincing enough, as the princess nodded with satisfaction. Still, I suspect her expression of understanding was partly intentional. According to her earlier explanation, Fithuille has the endorsement of both King Ausente and the headmistress. While I can’t speak for the king with certainty, I highly doubt either of them would personally harbor any malicious intent toward Palra or Belltina.

「Now then, we were talking about my impression of my party members, weren’t we? First, let me say in advance that the princess’ worry is unneeded.」

In other words, her worries about them having upset Ailneige and of them possibly weighing me down in the future.

「Though as I said earlier, the two still have much to work on—particularly with Belltina; she’s sure to have a difficult time in the future.」  

「Is that perhaps… in relation to her family?」  

「No, it’s in relation to her personal difficulties with sorcery. If she wishes to be able to mainly fight with sorcery, then it would likely require great effort on her part.」

Hearing my answer, the princess had a complicated smile; is it because she’s worried that Belltina is going to be a burden for me?  

Well, that isn’t all Belltina has to offer, so while being careful about how much to say, I continued my report to Princess Leshimiiya.

+++

# 179: Princess Leshimiiya and About Belltina

「Before elaborating on Belltina, I want to reaffirm the common perception of her. Princess Leshimiiya, how much do you know about Belltina?」  

「Umm, that’s…」  

「That despite having a large magic power reserve, she is hopelessly terrible with sorcery, if I have to guess?」  

「—It’s as you say.」  

「Is this a well-known fact among the Ausente nobility?」

I personally want to know more about Belltina’s circumstances, so I tried asking Princess Leshimiiya’s objective opinion. If it’s already a well-known fact, it will likely affect her future activities, so it might be better to give the princess some information. Also, I simply want to know the intrinsic risks of being with Belltina.

「About Miss Chilandia—there is not that much information about her that has come to the surface. I believe the Chilandia family has been hiding her on purpose. However, there are rumors saying that the daughter of Chilandia can’t use sorcery. It may be more correct to say that not many people have made the connection between the rumors and Miss Belltina herself.」  

「So in general, Belltina shouldn’t have any problem as long as she doesn’t associate with the Chilandia name, yes?」  

「That should be the case, at least.」

The princess showed a troubled smile, likely because of Alcrei’s existence. I know I asked to begin with, but I’m really impressed by how clearly and confidently the princess answered. Not only did she have information, but she also understood how widely known it was to the public, something likely impossible to learn unintentionally.

「And another thing, do you know of the party called the Fool’s Gathering?」  

「Hmm—I seem to recall hearing that name somewhere…」  

「It’s a hunter party that is mainly active in Central. One of their members, a female sorcerer, is the daughter of a considerably influential family in Central. Is the name Amyulute familiar to you?」  

「I remember now. It’s the party Lady Viviana is affiliated with, correct? If I’m not wrong, it’s been said that Lady Viviana’s way of sorcery is quite peculiar, but—」  

「I sure wonder why Viviana, a lady of the Amyulute family, is earning a living as a hunter.」

With this much information, the princess should get the idea. She could probably understand even with fewer hints, but the faster this conversation goes, the better.

「Does Lady Viviana also have a similar difficulty in sorcery as Miss Belltina?」  

「Both of them are bad with sorcery for nearly the same reason. But half-hearted effort simply isn’t enough to become someone like Viviana.」

In reality, Viviana’s issue is already resolved, but I don’t need to tell her about that, so I’m keeping quiet.  

I have no idea how hard Viviana worked to climb to the level of B-rank, and I don’t know what kind of training she went through, so I have no baseline for how much struggle Belltina will go through as a hunter. Though if it’s just being a hunter, she can technically become one even now.

「—So, is it… umm, alright?」

I wonder how much meaning there is hidden behind her hesitant ‘alright.’ I don’t plan on puzzling all of this out, so I’ll just say the information I want to relay.

「While Belltina may have a significant handicap combat-wise, she has an ability that easily compensates for it. The Chilandia family is most likely unaware of it, however. After all, she’s uncharacteristically undertaking hunter courses here in the second academy.」  

「May I ask you to teach me about that said ability?」  

「Is there an obligation to inform the royalty about one’s abilities here in Ausente?」  

「No, that isn’t the case, but…」

Unless you’re a knight in direct service to the country, they probably don’t require that. Individuals who will become hunters, in particular, are actually under Central’s jurisdiction, so demanding their information is difficult. Though this does depend on the relationship between the local Hunter Guild and the country, so I can’t say for sure. Still, the princess will likely continue feeling anxious unless she gains enough information, so I’ll give a vague rundown.

「Belltina is a talent specialized in detection and enemy search. Solely judging by her specialty, she’s capable enough to contend with me.」  

「To that extent!?」

Perhaps due to her inadvertently showing an unfiltered response, the shocked princess shyly said, 「Apologies,」 while lowering her head. I feel like she was most shocked about the _‘capable enough to contend with me’_ part. Well, Belltina’s abilities being underestimated does help me, so I don’t particularly care. Maybe there’s also a sense of relief, since detection alone shouldn’t be able to do significant harm. If it was her combat ability that’s around our level, Ausente would need to be cautious with her as well.

「At the very least, she’s capable enough to perceive the barrier I’m currently using.」  

「You’re currently using? Fithuille, can you see it?」  

「I know it’s there. But I can’t see it clearly. How to possibly break through it is even more unclear.」

As I thought, Munyechka’s dolls can perceive it, but she seems to be telling the truth about not knowing how to break through, so I’ll take that as good news.  

The princess not being able to sense it is normal; I’ll be troubled otherwise. Unlike pure magic power, barriers are normally visible unless tampered with, so depending on her capability, she might be able to see it. However, with this barrier being imperceptible even for Ciel, there’s no way the princess can perceive it.  

After hearing Fithuille’s words, Princess Leshimiiya nodded with conviction before letting out an astonished sigh.

「The Chilandias have lost quite the precious talent, it seems.」  

「They did indeed, but please keep this a secret. She would rather not be brought back into the Chilandia family, and it would be troublesome if she were eyed by other nobles. That may consequently encroach on my peace.」  

「Of course. I swear that this will not be divulged from my lips.」  

「I would greatly appreciate that.」

Princess Leshimiiya nodded in response to my light threat, so I guess we can end the topic of Belltina here. Her specifically saying _‘from my lips’_ is probably to account for people who already know about Belltina. Like Alcrei.

「As for Palra, there’s nothing particularly of note. She has a promising Job, but she doesn’t have the experience to fully take advantage of it yet.」  

「If I recall, hers is Advanced Huntsman, is it? It’s quite an uncommon Job.」  

「Do you know about Belltina’s Job?」  

「I only know the Jobs of those who have publicized theirs during the entrance exam. For that reason, I am not aware of your Job either, Miss Ailneige. There are rumors of it being either Sword Dancer or something similar, however…」  

「Who can say?」

From an outsider’s perspective, perhaps it looks similar enough? We are currently acting the part of Sword Dancer, so it’s as anticipated. Still, the princess doesn’t sound convinced by the rumors. We generally use sorcery—and magic—so she must think that we have a sorcerer-type Job, and those without it normally need a magic circle or a chant to perform sorcery.  

If Princess Leshimiiya intends to question us about our Job, I’ll need to consider our next move, but she kept silent, as if to show that she had no intention of pursuing the topic.

「Is the Huntsman Job really that uncommon? 」  

「It is. There are more Archers than there are Huntsmen, you see.」  

「When you put it that way, that does seem to be the case. While Archers are better when it comes to pure archery, Huntsmen are also capable of utilizing traps, among other things.」

There are Jobs like the Huntsman that are a composite of multiple traits, with one example being the Warrior Job. Warriors have a level of mastery when using weapons of various forms, but in exchange, they are less skilled compared to, let’s say, Swordsmen and Spearmen with their specialized weapons. It’s similar to how Sorcerers are generally skilled in various forms of sorcery, but they fall short in flame sorcery when compared to Flame Sorcerers.  

Song Princess and Dance Princess also have multiple traits of their Job line, but instead of being a master of none, these two come with a major demerit, making them slightly different from the previous examples.

「That’s about everything regarding the two. For Palra, I would appreciate it if you also avoid unwarranted intervention with her.」  

「Of course. Both of them will likely find work here in Ausente, and that’s more than enough.」  

「Ausente probably consumes a large amount of magic cores, after all.」  

「That’s right. In terms of sorceric tool development and implementation, I’m confident that ours do not fall behind Central’s. In that sense, our nation values hunters more than the average nation.」

It’s precisely why the academy accepts commoners and why we were able to sneak in. Sorceric tools are vital to this country, and so are their energy sources, the magic cores. As a result, hunters, individuals that harvest magic cores, are also equally vital. I’m sure that Ausente would love to have their own den if they could. I wonder if the magic cores harvested in Central are exported to Ausente?  

Besides that, the magic pouch we have would be a treasure trove for them. Then again, a pouch crammed with A-rank and higher monster materials would be a treasure for anyone. Speaking of which, I wonder if we can find a use for those herbs we found along with the hairpin-turned-spirit rest stop? At this rate, they might just end up as fertilizer.

「That reminds me, is there anyone connected to the Elbert family you’ve previously mentioned in this academy?」  

「Marquis Elbert should not have any kin of academy age, and I haven’t heard of their family enrolling in the academy either. However, if it’s people under their umbrella, there are a few. You can technically consider Miss Belltina as one of them.」  

「Well, the Chilandia family is anti-Central, after all.」

I don’t know about Belltina’s personal opinion, but the Chilandia family is undoubtedly anti-Central.  

With nobles, the parents’—or rather the family head’s—authority is generally absolute, so you can’t go against their orders. Though Belltina gives me the impression that she’ll disobey one way or another.

「Other than her, Tweisel is likely to be suspicious.」  

「The Tweisels are also anti-Central, huh.」

Hearing my words, the then princess had an apologetic expression. At first, I wondered why, but then I realized it was likely because of our affiliation with Central. More than that, we hold a status akin to that of a princess.  

It makes sense. Anyone in her position, having to inform an individual of that standing that certain families or factions of her own nation bear hostility toward their homeland, would naturally wear such a conflicted expression.  

It doesn’t really bother me, though. After all, the ‘antis’ of the anti-Central faction are most likely not focused on Mother Fii but on the freeloaders that constitute the gathering called Central. Still, perhaps there are some families that actually want to pick a fight with Mother Fii.

「Does the anti-Central faction believe they can win against Mistress Fiiyanamia?」  

「Surely they believe they stand a fighting chance, at least.」  

「To begin with, what exactly is the anti-Central faction actually against?」  

「The queen, Mistress Fiiyanamia… I suppose? The truth of the matter aside, it’s a cause that has quite the impact.」  

「That certainly is the case.」  

「They probably don’t truly stand in opposition to her; either they have something to gain in taking this stance, or they want to use this as a pretext to overthrow the current monarchy and rule for themselves, at least in my opinion.」  

「Is it really alright to share that much?」  

「It’s because you are the only other person here, Miss Ailneige. It’s not like you would do anything with this information, and if, hypothetically, you made this public, there isn’t anyone who can rebuke you, is there?」

It was somewhat of a deep topic, which almost seemed like mild grumbling midway, but it sounds like she really was just venting. I suppose that Ailneige is the only one she can confide in with things like these. Though rather than it being because I’m Fiiyanamia’s daughter, it’s probably because of Ailneige’s—Cielmer’s—general temperament.  

If we ever make this information public, punishment will likely fall to the princess, but she must have shared it partly to show just how much trust she has in us. I am self-aware of how much I’m leaving the princess to deal with, so I’m willing to handle at least this much mental aftercare. I’m just lending an ear, after all, so it’s not like I need to do anything special.

I will need to discuss this with Ciel, but at worst, we can just pick a fight with Ausente and return to Central.  

After that, we had a short exchange with Princess Leshimiiya before heading to the rooftop.

++++

# Levelmaker - Chapter 520 - # Rir’s Strange Behavior (Shuu)

“The hell are ya doin’!?”

I hurriedly stepped behind Rir and held down her arms. Then, while pinning them down so she couldn’t move them, I slowly peeled her hands off the statue’s neck.  

_…It kinda feels like she’s usin’ a lot more power than normal._

A few minutes later, I had managed to get her off the statue.

“Oy, Rir!!”

This wasn’t something she would normally do, and even supposing it was part of the prayer, she should’ve said something when I tried to stop her. More importantly, even after peeling her off, she didn’t move at all.

“Rir, what’s wrong?”

I peered at her face. Her eyes were empty, as if there was no one in there. Her expression was blank, save for some slight dread. Her cuteness and rich expressiveness were nowhere to be found.

Right now, it was as if she was staring into empty space with eyes like those of a dead fish. She didn’t even blink.

“Rir… Rir!”

I tried shaking her shoulders to get her out of this trance. I hoped that this might change something, that a strong enough impulse would fix it.

“Woof!”

Ten seconds later, Rir produced the same doglike bark she always used.  

_…Good, looks like that snapped her outta it._

“Rir, are you alright?”  

“I’m… alright. Why do you have tears in your eyes, Shuu?”

_Good… that’s really good. I was afraid I’d lost her again._  

_I just had that gut feelin’._

“Rir… earlier, you acted weird.”  

“Eh… what?”  

“You don’t remember?”

_Is her memory still hazy?_  

For now, I told her what she had done and how she had acted afterwards.

“…I did that?”  

“Yes.”

She looked at me with an expression of disbelief. Still, she gradually started to frown, as if she was remembering something.

“N-Now that you mention it, I feel like my consciousness grew dim while I was praying. I don’t remember anything after that.”  

“I see.”

I was curious what happened there, but… for the time being, I was glad that she was fine.

“At any rate, can you even remove the head of a Jizou statue?”

To that simple question, there was one clear answer in my memories.

“Yep, you can. We once saw it with its head off. This statue, I mean.”

That happen quite a long time ago… before Ayumu shielded Mika from the glass shards. When Ayumu, Mika, and I were in the neighborhood, we discovered that, for some reason, the statue’s head was lying next to it.

It obviously scared me. But Ayumu just said, “we can’t leave it like this,” so the three of us lifted the extremely heavy head and placed it back on the statue.

Since a long time ago, there were always weird rumors about that statue, so I was scared we’d end up cursed if we left it like that. Though Ayumu probably just felt sorry for it and Mika went along with him.

Thinking about it now, this might be part of the reason Lord Jizou revived the two of them in Anazumu. It might also be the reason Kanata, Sakura, and I luckily ended over there.

“Woof~, to think something like that would happen…”

When I told her about my memories, Rir looked at me in understanding.

“Yep… more importantly, are you fine now?”

In reaction to my question, she touched her body in several places and tried repeatedly opening and closing her hands.

“It looks like I am.”  

“Hah… that’s good.”

_What a relief._

_Maybe – assumin’ Lord Jizou is one of Anazumu’s gods – there was a reaction with Rir, since she’s originally from the same place. And then she ended up actin’ weird. Does that make sense?_

_…Right now, it doesn’t matter._

“Let’s go home for the day,” I said while standing up and holding out my hand to her.

_We can start investigatin’ it from tomorrow on in Anazumu. Let’s ask Kanata for help and find out what happened._

Normally, Ayumu was the most experienced traveler in all things Anazumu, but he would be busy organizing the wedding of his acquaintances.

“You’re… right.” Rir didn’t take my hand and instead pulled me into a strong embrace. In this position, she rubbed her cheeks against me. “You were so worried, there were tears in your eyes. I love you, Shuu!”  

“Eh, well, uhm. I didn’t wanna lose you again.”  

“Awoo! Should we go to one of these hotels, after all? I want to offer you my body and soul.”

I avoided her crazy impulse with a “we can do that tomorrow without any rush.”  

_These hotels are seriously dangerous. I am… also in the mood to cut loose, but Anazumu is better suited for that._

“…Anyway, let’s go home.”  

“…Woof~.”

Holding each other’s hand tightly so we wouldn’t get separated, we walked towards our home. For now, we decided to discuss it with everyone and keep Rir away from the statue.

+++

# 521 – After the Weekend

After spending practically the whole day with Mika, our first date on Earth had come to an end. It was obvious that, compared to her 13-year-old version, a date with the more adult 16-year-old Mika would feel different. The biggest differences were those caused by growth.

And during said first date, we also had our first time… In such a well-equipped establishment.

To be honest, it would be accurate to say that I yielded to my desires. I went about it with as much caution as possible, but Mika seemed to be satisfied.  

That might be obvious, but differences in figure and age changed the experience. The main difference between her 13- and 16-year-old versions was… well, I won’t tell.

In any case, in that establishment, about one hour before the end of our date, I heard her say the words “I am yours, and you are mine” for the first time in quite some time. Just a short while ago, I’d have said that these words were exaggerated, but now I completely agreed with her. There was no longer any way to deny it.

“Sorry ’bout that, but could you all hear me out?”

When I opened my eyes, the six of us were gathered in the usual room of the mansion. And in the middle of this, Shuu drew our attention.

“Is something wrong?” I asked him with my head inclined.

He looked more serious than usual.

“Yep… when Rir got close to that Jizou statue on Earth, she started actin’ strange.”

_Huh… she seems normal enough now. Is there anything off about her?_

“Woof, that said, Shuu fixed it already,” she hurriedly added.

Well, that tracked. If something to that account happened, Shuu would likely have us return to Anazumu in a rush.

“You said she acted weird…?”  

“Yep, in fact, I brought her to the statue as part of our date, and then-”

According to him, the moment Rir offered a prayer in the manner you would for gods of Anazumu, she tried to take off the statue’s head, as if something was possessing her. On top of that, she apparently couldn’t remember anything from that time.

“So, another weird thing happened,” I mused.  

“Yup. There might be somethin’ ’bout that statue, after all. Related to this world.”

I had previously told Shuu to some extent that Lord Jizou might be connected to Anazumu. It was about six minutes from his house to the statue, plus the only thing nearby were Mika’s and my homes, so I thought he only went there rarely, but he ended up visiting it to offer thanks for meeting Rir, anyway.

On that note, Mika and I visited the place every day without fail, either on our way to school or back. Lord Jizou was the reason we were so happy now… so it was really important to stop there. To thank him from the bottom of our hearts.

“I dunno why she was tryin’ to take off its head, though.”  

“Oh, now that you mention it, we did touch that statue’s head before, haven’t we?” Mika commented nostalgically.

She was right, when we were in third year of elementary school or so, on our way back from school after the three of us decided to play at my house, we discovered that the statue’s head had been removed. This might sound obvious, but we put it back in its original place.

_How nostalgic… I remember it being fairly heavy._

Come to think of it, in his explanation when I came to Anazumu, Lord Jizou wrote that I was kind to him, so he sent me here. Something about cleaning up bird feces, but the head affair might’ve been included in that, too. Or rather, it was weird that he had bigger issued with bird poop than his head being removed.

“With what happened, wouldn’t it be better to keep Rir away from the Jizou statue on Earth for a while?” Mika asked.  

“Yep, that’s true,” Shuu replied.

In the end, these kinds of things made me curious. They appealed to my adventurous spirit. But what we needed for the rest of our lives was stability, so we could spend our time happily with our loved ones. If we went and messed around with it, an evil god or something similar might appear, and I absolutely didn’t want to go through grief like when I lost Mika… or Shuu lost Rir, again[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-521-after-the-weekend/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-101209).

You could argue that Amritas solved these issues, but back with Surtr, it only worked out since Shuu was coincidentally carrying around Rir’s body parts, like someone with a weird fetish. There might be another close call like that.

Mika and I were tied together by a divine grade item that made it so we wouldn’t get separated, no matter what, but the other two couples didn’t have that.

“Well, that’s all I wanted to tell you. Let’s go with what Ayumu said and keep Rir away from the statue.”  

“Yep, that should work. Then, let’s split up, everyone!”

When I said that, Kanata and Sakura left while somehow acting cold towards each other. Shuu and Rir were whispering, apparently discussing something, before both blushing and leaving the room while acting somewhat suspiciously.

“Now, there are things for us to do,” Mika announced.  

“Yep. From today on, the preparations start in earnest. There’s only little time left until the planned day.”

Mika and I decided to advance the plans for Uruto and Parasuna’s wedding.

#### Footnotes:

1. Someone is starting to get genre savvy.

+++

# 522 – Progress Update

On the day after coming back to Anazumu, I was on my way to the “Hikari” inn. The original plan was to make my report concerning the wedding cake, but that wasn’t all I had. I would also present them with ideas for the decorations used for the ceremony and the food that would be served.

“Welcome, Alim, thanks for coming today.”  

“It’s no trouble, Mr. Uruto.”

He was standing in front of the inn’s door to welcome me. We then went to the usual room, where Parasuna was obviously already waiting. For now, I sat down in the offered chair.

“Today, I will present you the design for the wedding cake.”  

“Right.”  

“As a matter of fact, I have also finished deliberating about the decorations of the venue and the food that will be served, so is it alright with you, if I address these, too?”  

“Yes, of course!”

_In that case, let’s start with the cake._  

I had created a model of the cake with Dark Matter, after pondering the design for the whole week on Earth.

“What do you think?”

It was a three-layered cake with a design that looked cool and mature at first, but also had cute elements. On the top, there were long pieces of white chocolate resembling rabbit ears, and a small hut made of marzipan.

The rabbit ears symbolized Parasuna, while the hut was Uruto. This way, they were both on the cake.

“This is me… and that’s Uruto?”  

“Exactly. The rabbit ears and the small hut together… that’s you two.”

At that explanation, they looked at each other and smiled.

“We do not have any complaints.”  

“So… should I go with this design?”  

“Yes, please do.”

_Alright, great. I had several alternatives in case they didn’t like it, but this was still the one I put the most work into. I’m glad they’re happy with it._

“Then, that’s it for the cake. Next will be the decorations.”  

“Oh, you don’t need to show those to us. It’ll be more fun if we only see them on the very day,” Uruto replied.  

“Everything you make is wonderful, Alim,” Parasuna added, “so I’m sure no matter what you pick, it will exceed our expectations.”  

“I see, making things fun is important, huh,” I mused.

Indeed, creating a situation, where not only the guests but also the bride and groom were excited, was important. Definitely.

_Then what about the food?_

“In that case, I’ll make my own decisions on the decor… alright? What about the food?”  

“Right… we don’t have any special requests for that.”  

“The royals from this country will be here, obviously… and so will those from other countries, who’ll apparently come here on some business, so there should be a solid and appropriate spread. That’s about it.”

_Ugh, so there will also be royals from other countries? Here for some business… I hope nothing weird happens again. I really don’t want to get in a war with another country of have to fight another evil god._

_Well, I’ll just make the food. It’s a good opportunity to use up some of the stores of ingredients in my magic bag._

“Understood… that was everything from my side. For this meeting, I mean. Please look forward to the day of the wedding.”  

“We will… thank you so much,” Uruto said.  

“Thank you for everything you’ve done for us, Alim,” Parasuna followed suit.

The two of them stood up and offered a handshake, which I accepted. This was a joyous event that only happened once in your life, so I’d go all out. Well, from now on, it was just preparing stuff with Dark Matter and getting the food ready.

“I’ll be off, then. I wish you both all the best.”  

“Yes…! You keep at it with Mika, too, Alim.”  

“G-Gender doesn’t matter for love!” Parasuna exclaimed. “We got over many hurdles ourselves, so there’ll be a solution for you, too!”

Dang, apparently, they were worried about Mika’s and my relationship. Not that there was any reason, seeing I was actually male. Neither getting married nor having children should be an issue. But I shouldn’t make light of their worries.

“Yes… thank you for saying that. Soon, I will try to build a machine that allows me to turn into a man.”  

“Ha-ha-ha, you turning into a man, Alim. I can’t imagine that.”

Well, I wouldn’t have breasts, and some parts here and there would look slightly more masculine, but it would be barely any different from my current appearance. This might be cause for worry, but at this point, I had accepted my own body for what it was. There would come a day when I’d reveal to the people close to us like these two, that I had turned male.

_I’m sure it’ll happen… though when? Three years for now at the shortest, probably. How will we be in three years…? I can only see us still being all lovey-dovey._

Leaving these ponderings aside, I had to go home.

“See you.”

I left the “Hikari” inn. Then, I immediately returned to the mansion, to make out with Mika.

“Mika, I’m mostly done with my bigger jobs.”  

“You worked hard.” Right after telling her that, she gave me a kiss on the cheek. “Would you like to have a meal? Or a bath? Or me?”  

“It’s only noon. Let’s go with the meal.”

_…I wonder, does Mr. Uruto say things like that to Miss Parasuna?_

+++

# 523 – Visitor from Another Country

“Was lunch good?”  

“Yep, I could taste all the delicious love you put in.”  

“Eh-heh-heh-heh-heh,” Mika giggled joyfully.

Earlier, I had seen Uruto and Parasuna make similar expressions… they were probably happy… and I likely also radiated joy right now.

Incidentally, these days, I started using magic beast materials for cooking as much as possible. It would be a waste to just let this stuff sit in the magic bag forever. I was also thinking of using the other materials to create some divine grade devices. But only after Uruto and Parasuna’s wedding was over.

“Ayumu~, what will you do later?”  

“Hm? I don’t have any other big plans today, so after prepping the cooking materials, I’m free.”  

“Gotcha.”

After we were done eating dinner and had put the tableware away, Mika came to my side.

“Now, the meal is over, so next will be ‘me’, right?”  

“Eh?”  

“And afterwards the bath! Come on, Ayumu… you know what I’m saying, don’t you?”

I knew. I did, but that wasn’t part of the joke.  

_Well, there are days like these…_

It wasn’t like I was particularly averse, so I picked her up in a princess carry, brought her to the bed in our bedroom, where I carefully set her down. Then, I immediately dove onto the bed, too.

When I got close, I could see that she was blushing ever so slightly. Thinking about what we were about to do, I likely also turned red. Recently, I often felt like this. Naturally… I didn’t mind it at all. On the contrary, it made me happy.

“So, shall we start? Though it’s still the middle of the day.”  

“Yeah.”

I pushed her down, so she lay prone on the bed, and then took off the clothing on her upper body. This was how it always went, I gazed at her body, which was as beautiful as her face, just long enough to catch my breath, before bringing my hands to her breasts, and-

[Alim, Mika, is now a good time?]　

Both Mika and I were stunned in the darkness. The king had picked the worst timing for his message…  

_Gaaaaaaaaaaaaaaah! Even though we’ve just started[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-523-visitor-from-another-country/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-101314)!_

For now, I hurriedly made eye contact with Mika to take stock of the situation. As for the result of our deliberation of priorities merely via our gazes… we’d listen to what the king had to say for the time being. He was among the most important people of the country and disregarding him would only cost us… _sniffle_.

[It… it is, Your Majesty,]　  

[S-S-Same for me!]　

My reply was somewhat grumpy, and Mika added hers after hurriedly putting her top back on. No, it wasn’t a good time, not at all.

[I see, that’s good. There is something I’d like to inform you about in advance… You do know about Uruto and Parasuna’s wedding, don’t you? From what they told me, you are preparing various things for it, Alim.]　  

[Yes, it’s just as they say.]　

The king took his time to move on to the main topic.  

_I already know plenty about that wedding._

[That should make this quick. Foreign royalty and nobles will be arriving under various pretexts, but… a king from another country, who wasn’t able to attend Alim’s hero proclamation, did arrive today, as a matter of fact. He says he absolutely wants to meet you, Alim, Mika… Could you come to the castle at 11 am tomorrow?]　

_So, that’s how it is. Well, I don’t have any plans for tomorrow other than my normal work, so we can come meet this foreign king._

When I looked at Mika for confirmation, she nodded.

[Understood, Your Majesty! Then we shall be visiting tomorrow!]　  

[Yes, please do! See you tomorrow, then. Make sure to be here at 11 am!]　  

[We will!]　

The king cut off the telepathic connection.

For now, we had to organize our thoughts, considering said man was a dignitary of a foreign nation. And right now…

“What do we do?”  

“Start over from the beginning,” Mika replied bashfully.

It looked like we had the same idea.

“Let’s do that.”

I pushed her down on the bed once more…

______  

____  

__

The next day, Mika and I put on stylish clothes while grooming our hair a bit.

“I wonder what kind of guy he is, this foreign king who came to visit.”  

“I’m pretty sure he’ll turn out a nice person. That’s what my intuition tells me.”

Her gut was usually spot on. So, chances were high that he really was a nice guy.

We linked hands and made our way to the castle. The guards let us in after recognizing us and we were warmly welcomed by several maids and butlers. And then…

“Welcome, Alim, Mika!” Karua came rushing towards us in apparent joy.

Come to think of it, we didn’t stay at the castle last week, so it’s natural for her to be so happy.

“Uhm, sorry for not visiting. We were busy.”  

“It is fine!”  

“By the way, where’s that guest of yours?”  

“He is currently in the throne room.”

_Then he’s likely discussing something with the king. Just what kind of person is he? I’m so curious._  

The moment that thought crossed my mind, the doors to the throne room flew open.

#### Footnotes:

1. What, would he have preferred it right before reaching climax?

+++

# 524 – King Rama

“Oh! Alim, Mika, you’ve come.”

From how vigorously he had opened the doors, the king seemed to be in high spirits. Next to him stood a handsome young man with the appearance of a ruler.

“Oh… to think the day would come when We see those two in the flesh…”

This was likely the foreign ruler the king had told us about yesterday. Either way, he seemed to be one of your fans. That made me a bit happy.

“Alim, Mika, for now, come here. The rest of you, go back to your work or do what you normally would.”

After giving that order, the king retreated back into the throne room. Mika and I raced up the stairs and entered the room, as he had asked us to. In there, we found the king, the foreign ruler, the knight commander and… someone who was likely the foreign ruler’s guard.

“You’ve come. Now, let’s do some introductions first. This gentleman is His Majesty King Rishna Rama of Bufura[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-524-king-rama/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-101317).”

_So, he really is a king… I’ll refer to him as King Rama mentally._

“How do you do? We[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-524-king-rama/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-101317) are Rishna Rama, and We serve as the ruler of Bufara.”  

“It’s a pleasure to meet you! I am Alim Nariwei!”  

“I’m happy to make your acquaintance! My name is Mika Magarigi!”

King Rama gave us a perfect gentlemanly bow, to which we did our best to respond in kind. He made quite the good impression to me.

“Indeed, We know much about the two of you. We have subscribed to all the magazines in which you are featured.  

“That’s… thank you very much!”

_I think that’s quite a few magazine publishers at this point. There are few people who read all the reports about us._

“As a matter of fact, A-… Miss Alim…”

The king tried to continue but seemed to have some trouble speaking. Especially with how to address Mika and me. I had the impression that he wanted to address us without any honorifics, as was common among our fans[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-524-king-rama/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-101317).

“Oh, you may address us however you prefer, Your Majesty Rama!”  

“We can…? In that case, may We call you just Alim and Mika?”  

“Please.”

It was as I had assumed. That was usually the default for us to be addressed. Definitely.

“We are getting sidetracked, let us continue. Originally, We wanted to attend Alim’s Hero Proclamation. Back then should have been our first meeting, but… it was not to be. The distance between Mephilad and Bufura is not small by any means.”

_Huh… but if he had come back then, we couldn’t have talked in peace like now. Delaying it was probably the right call._

“On that note, Our country, the Bufura Kingdom, is the same distance from here as it is to Yggdrasil, the country of the Holy Tree.”

_Really, so does that mean those three countries form a triangle? How curious._

“Plus, several business affairs had accumulated… so it was a good opportunity to visit this country. Our main reason is to attend Lastman and Parasuna’s wedding.”

_This might be a rude way to put it, but… the genuine ruler of a country came here just to attend a wedding between SSS-Rankers? Does that mean SSS-Rankers are more important than they appear?_

“Are you acquainted with Lastman, Your Majesty Rama?” asked Mika, who was likely wondering the same.  

“You are correct, Mika. Either way, those two SSS-Rankers abolished slavery… Our country has a caste system similar to slavery, so I was asking them for their opinion about how to get rid of it. We are also close in age. In the first place, a wedding between two fellow SS-Rankers is all the reason needed to rush here… In any case, We are also at SSS-Rank.”

_I see, on top of such weddings being rare, he is friends with them._  

_…Hang on, that wasn’t all, was it? What did he say again right at the end? He himself is an SSS-Ranker, too? Huh… that’s incredible._

“I quit working as an adventurer to learn how to rule as a king, but he is an active SSS-Ranker.”  

“It is true. Well, We were lucky enough to obtain the ‘Great Master[4](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-524-king-rama/#easy-footnote-bottom-4-101317)‘ skill.”

_He has a Master skill on top of that?_

We helped Seinforce, Karua, and Tuhl to level up and you could say that they now had a general grasp of the concept of level concerning people in this world, but to both serve as ruler and SSS-Ranker sounded incredible.

“King Rama, you told me that you wished to meet Alim and Mika, so I called them here, but what are your thoughts after the fact?  

“…To state my honest feelings, they are magnificently lovely. The pictures cannot compare to reality in the slightest.”

_Hearing it like that makes me a bit bashful._  

I was currently a girl, so having my looks complimented did make me happy.

“Still, Our apologies for deliberately summoning you here, Alim, Mika.”  

“Not at all, our mansion is just around the corner, so it was no trouble. We are practically neighbors.”  

“Ah, so you built your mansion close to the castle…? How curious! It’s very… ha-ha-ha-ha!”

For some reason, he started laughing mid-sentence. Was it weird to have a house next to the castle?

#### Footnotes:

1. The originals are リシュナ (rishuna), ラーマ (raama), and ブフーラ (bufuura). With the general tone and the caste system later mentioned in the chapter, this is most likely fantasy India. “Bufura” might be intended to be something else, it doesn’t really sound like an Indian name.

2. He uses the 余 (yo) personal pronoun, which seems to be an archaic, dignified, elevated form of “I”. I translated it with the majestic plural.

3. It’s addressing them with the -chan suffix in the original

4. The original is グレートマスター (gureeto masutaa). This might also be “Grate Master”. It’s pretty much a placeholder until we see what his skill does, and then I might change it to something more appropriate. For now, it sounds like some martial arts skill.

+++

# 525 – The Bufura Kingdom

“Come to think of it, you defeated two evil gods, Alim, didn’t you?” King Rama asked after laughing for a while.  

“Yes, I did.”  

“…This is no mean feat. To think you brought down two godlike beings who caused issues for this world. It seems you are no longer living in the same realm as us.”

He really seemed interested in that topic. It felt a bit embarrassing.

“On that note, Our country also has an evil god.”  

“Wha-…”  

“Please wait, no need to be so displeased. Though it does look adorable… We do not wish for you to vanquish it.”

_This is bad, I ended up showing just how fed up I am with fighting evil gods in front of the king and all the other higher ups. What does he mean by “not wanting me to beat it”?_

“To be more precise, the evil god in Our country no longer exists. On top of being sealed, it was destroyed in the past, so We can no longer say for sure what its whereabouts are. What We mean to say is that it no longer is in Anazumu.”

_What’s that supposed to mean?_

I had no idea, since, although I did peruse this world’s historic records, I didn’t investigate them this thoroughly[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-525-the-bufura-kingdom/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-102017).  

_There are just so many… On second thought, I better study up properly on history soon._

“However… as one of the Rama lineage, I still have the ‘power to choose the guide’, who is necessary to defeat said evil god.”

_The Mephilad Kingdom has the power to find the hero by seeing status screens and… what was it again? Right, Yggdrasil, the country of the holy tree, had the ability to summon sages from another world. It sounds similar to those._

From what he said, the Rama family’s ability apparently was to freely nominate anyone apart from themselves.

“Well, there are some people We could nominate, but this feels like a waste,” King Rama continued. “If given the choice, wouldn’t you give such a privilege to a legendary figure?”

_Oh no… I can see where this is going…_

“So, Alim, how about you become the guide? We haven’t nominated anyone for generations, but-”  

“I respectfully decline,” I replied before he could even finish his sentence.  

“Why?” King Rama, who’d likely assumed I’d accept, looked stunned.  

“If I accepted, that evil god who should’ve been destroyed would be revived and cause trouble… that’s the feeling I get. In any case, I wish to live in peace…”

_In this world, things come back to life in the strangest of ways! Rir, who had been burned to ash could be revived, so it wouldn’t be weird if some evil god who was sealed and then destroyed would come back._

“…Hrm, certainly. It is possible Our predecessors feared this and didn’t nominate a guide for that reason. We understand your reasoning.”

This man listened to my argument and didn’t seem to mind even if I chose words that might’ve been seen as somewhat impolite. He really was a nice guy.

“…The time has already come for lunch,” King Mephilad, who likely saw this as a good stopping point, announced after looking at the clock.

He was right, it was that time.  

_…But what is the point of deliberately mentioning that in front of me?_

“…My apologies, Alim, I will compensate you for it at a later day, but couldn’t you cook lunch for us?  

“What…? A meal made by Alim herself!?” the foreign king interrupted, his eyes wide open.

His earlier gentlemanly atmosphere was gone without a trace. Even his guard seemed clearly shocked.

“I can do that,” I replied.  

“I-Is this real!?”  

“Please be assured… Alim’s cooking is the best in all Anazumu, I can attest to that.”

I actually had a title saying that.  

Still, King Rama seemed happy about something different from the flavor…

“I am curious about the taste, too, but… oh… as the special honorary chairman of the ‘Association of Alimika Adorers[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-525-the-bufura-kingdom/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-102017)‘, there could be no greater bliss.”

_Oh, so he’s part of that group, huh?_  

Even though we were trying to reduce our workload little by little over the days, the number of people in that association kept going up.

“I-I would love to taste it!”  

“Are you truly fine with that, Alim?” King Mephilad tried to confirm.  

“Yes, it doesn’t bother me, Your Majesty.”

When it came to cooking, I could make as much as needed. I liked to cook, and it gave me an opportunity to use some of my excessive material stores.

“Why not wait in the dining hall, then? Gordes, show the two of them the way.”  

“As you wish.”

The knight commander left the throne room with King Rama and his guard. King Mephilad then got up from his throne and closed in on us.

“My apologies for causing you trouble.”  

“Not at all, I don’t mind.”  

“We have been on friendly terms with that country since ages past, but you never know what the future may bring, so we want to deepen our friendship. Fortunately, King Rama seems to be a big fan of the two of you… Couldn’t you indulge him and converse with him today?”

To be blunt, I didn’t know anything about diplomacy and politics. But since he was our fan and this was the best way to improve relations, I would help. Moreover, from what I could glimpse, he didn’t seem to be part of Mika’s faction, but mine instead.

“Understood, you can count on me!”  

“Once more, you have my apologies.”

Mika and I calmed the apologetically bowing king and then went to the dining hall’s kitchen, so we wouldn’t leave King Rama waiting.

#### Footnotes:

1. Maybe the first step in avoiding a potential enemy should be to learn everything you can about them?

2. Sounds like they changed their name to something shorter.

+++

# 526 – A Meal with King Rama

“Sorry to keep you waiting!”

Mika and I brought in the finished food. It seemed like the dining hall was just for entertaining these guests right now, with Karua and most of this country’s higher ups missing, and merely the two kings, the foreign ruler’s guard, the knight commander, and finally Tuhl present.

It looked like there were also seats for Mika and me. Though they were right next to King Rama.

“For the appetizer… we prepared olives!” I explained, while the food was placed in front of everyone.

On that note, our job only went so far as to bring the food here, so while I did give the explanation, it was the maids who distributed it.

“Oh~… This looks truly delicious!” King Rama exclaimed.  

“It really does… let us begin,” King Mephilad agreed.  

“Hrm. Our thanks for the food.”

King Rama tried the appetizer. He then dropped his fork with a clatter.

“My King!?”

His guard, who hadn’t tried the food yet, rushed to the king in a panic. For some reason, King Rama seemed to be trembling.

“…It’s.”  

“It’s?”  

“It’s way too good… Is this something out of this world[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-526-a-meal-with-king-rama/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-102020)!?”

King Rama got up with such force from his chair, he almost blew away his guard who had come to his side.  

_I’m glad if that was only because it tastes so good._

“L-L-L-Let Us be blunt, Alim… We thought there was nothing past True Cooking, no matter what you did. While it is usually quite good, the cooking made by high-class chefs and adventurers with left-over skill points generally tastes similar. Even We have that skill… Still, what is this? Is this food intended for the gods?”

_Huh… and that was only the appetizer. Is he so enraptured with my cooking that he won’t be able to eat anything else? I mean, is that just my imagination, or is the guy genuinely crying?_

“Originally… originally, We’d have been fully satisfied merely by being able to eat your cooking, Alim…!”

His fists were clenched, and he was shaking.  

_Is this guy alright?_

“U-Uhm… there are more courses, so… could we talk about this after the dessert…?”  

“Hah… y-you’re right. Our apologies… you may go back to your seat and try the food, too, Hanuman[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-526-a-meal-with-king-rama/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-102020).”  

“I shall do so, My King.”

_So, the guard is called Hanuman. Somehow, this name fits his face to a T[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-526-a-meal-with-king-rama/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-102020)._

Right after eating some of the appetizers I had made, the guard also started trembling and then broke into tears.

“Well… Item Master is on a completely different level.”  

“That should be clear at this point,” Mika replied to my whisper, as if that was the most obvious thing.

After the appetizers came salad, soup, and bread, then fish and meat dishes… and finally dessert. The somewhat lavish meal was over. Seeing the two guests tremble from beginning to the end had been somewhat fun.

Incidentally, I had splurged a bit on the main meat dish and made dragon steak. Though it wasn’t Rose Dragon, just normal Child Dragon. But the sobbing likely meant that it was satisfactory.

“That was… truly delicious. As a trueborn royal, We assumed We had tasted the delicacies this world has to offer, but… We clearly felt why King Mephilad called Alim the best chef in Anazumu.”

_Eh-heh-heh, he’s going to make me blush. Well, I’ll be using more expensive ingredients for the wedding to clear out most of my stock._

“…King Mephilad, could We borrow this place for a short time?” King Rama asked, looking both rather happy and determined.  

“…? I’m not sure what your intentions are, but… as long as you don’t use it for anything untoward.”

It looked like King Mephilad didn’t know either what the foreign ruler was planning. Even the guard Hanuman looked as if he had a question mark floating over his head.

“You have Our thanks.”

Right after giving King Mephilad his gratitude, King Rama stood up, grabbed the chair he had been sitting on, and then brought it to a place a few meters away before returning to us. Then, he stood right behind me.

_Eh, what’s going on?_

“Alim… no, Alim Nariwei, could you turn your chair Our way?”  

“Hah… that’s fine, but…”

As he had asked, I turned my chair, so it faced the other way. Seeing him again from close up, he gave off the air off a handsome ruler, and I could feel youthfulness and power overflow from him.

“…Hah…” King Rama was taking deep breaths.

_What’s this about?_

At any rate, it felt like I had experienced that atmosphere before. How should I put it… he was exuding a kind of nervous excitement… something Mika and I had experienced on Earth to the point where we started to loathe it. For example, on Valentine’s Day, behind the school, when suddenly-

“Alright.”

Likely having made up his mind, Kind Rama looked at me seriously, as I was still sitting there. Finally… he went down on one knee, so his line of sight was level with mine, held out one hand, and spoke.

“Alim Nariwei, won’t you marry Us[4](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-526-a-meal-with-king-rama/#easy-footnote-bottom-4-102020)?”

#### Footnotes:

1. Alim’s cooking claims another victim.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-526-a-meal-with-king-rama/#easy-footnote-1-102020)

2. The original is ハヌマーン (hanumaan). [Hanuman] is a deity in Hinduism, further driving home the point that Bufura is supposed to be fantasy India.

3. Does that mean he looks like a monkey?

4. The original is closer to “won’t you start a relationship with the intention of getting married?” While this seems to be a common expression in Japanese (I’ve seen it in other LNs), it does **not** sound like what a king would say.

+++

# 527 – King Rama’s Affection

“Phew…”

Indeed, it was a confession. I had this indescribable feeling, which gave me a hunch, but it still came as a surprise.

I went rigid for a full hour… at least that was how it felt. In reality, it was around five seconds.

“Oh, Our apologies. You are likely speechless since it was so sudden.”

_Yes, I was certainly surprised._

“We were strongly captivated by your beauty from the beginning, Alim. It was like magic. Before We knew it, we had joined your fan-club.”

_I-I see._  

_Beauty, huh…? I’m only interested in Mika, so I merely perceive myself as cute, but assuming he sees the same divine beauty in me that I see when I look at Mika… then that happens._

“And now… having eaten your cooking. The taste was undoubtedly divine… Leaving aside all those stuffy formalities, let Us simply tell you that We fell in love with you. Your captivation and Our affection for you… they intermingled, causing the feelings for you We had from the start to erupt…”

He kept talking, still in the same posture.  

_Is this how nobles and royalty confess to others? Hm~, that doesn’t fit with the image Mr. Ruin and Mr. Orgo give me, so it might just be him._

“I understand. There is about a ten-year gap between you and me, Alim… You’re likely also anxious.”

_Now that he mentions it, he did say that he’s the same age as Mr. Uruto. In other words, between 22 and 23… And I’m 13._

For the public, this would undoubtedly scream ‘pedophile’! Well, with Mika’s and my popularity, this would describe many people in this world.

“Furthermore, while W may not marry you before you reach the age of 16, we could get engaged at your current age-”

_16, huh…? Once I’m 16 in this world, I’ll marry Mika. I’m already happy with that. We can have kids once we’re in the middle of our twenties. Until that point, we’ll just enjoy our love-live, like we do now._

“-What are We saying? It is too early for such feelings… I-In any case, Alim Nariwei, We love you. What say you… won’t you accept Our proposal?”

_Ah, I ended up thinking about Mika while he was confessing to me, and I completely missed what he was saying._

_To begin with, I’m originally a boy, so I would never accept the confession of another man… As Alim, I may think that Shuu and others are handsome, but that’s as far as it goes._

_I’ll refuse._

“Uhm… I’m sorry.” I told King Rama, who was looking at me full of anticipation. I did feel sorry.  

“…We did not want to tempt you with physical things and neither did We want to appear haughty, but as Our wife, money, social standing, power, and fame would be yours. You would be a queen.”
