He added that to his preface, and he had proven himself to be a nice guy, but… I could only shake my head.

“W-We see… you have these things already. As We feared… it was a poor idea to confess during our first meeting. It would appear we overreached…”

He looked rather disappointed. He had been serious, after all.

“Uhm… I’m really sorry.”  

“No, it is fine. We should be the one to apologize for springing this on you so sudden. We wouldn’t mind giving it another try at some point. Sometime.”

_Looks like he still hasn’t given up, so he leaves me no choice. I need to tell him how things really are… apart from the fact I’m male, obviously._

“Yes… but… this will be hard, as my heart already belongs to someone.”  

“What!? There is someone else!?” King Rama shouted in surprise.

It wasn’t just him, Hanuman looked the same. On that note, King Mephilad and Tuhl also seemed startled for a moment, but after looking at Mika, they appeared to understand.

“Yes. Someone I’ve loved for a long time… someone who loves me, too.”  

“To think there was someone like that… Could it be Prince Tuhl? Or maybe Prince Ruin…?”

Tuhl seemed surprised for an instant when his name came up[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-527-king-ramas-affection/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-102024).

I made eye contact with Mika. She nodded in agreement.

“Hm? Is something wrong, Mika? For you to suddenly leave your chair…” King Rama wondered.

Without giving him a reply, she came to my side. Then, I also stood up. The moment I was standing, she kissed me on my cheek.  

_…I didn’t intend it to go that far. Oh, well._

“Huh?”

It looked like the visitors from another country couldn’t make heads or tails of this. They seemed dumbfounded.

“Ah… well, that’s how it is.”

While scratching my cheek automatically, I put my hand on Mika’s shoulder. Ignoring said hand, she instead pulled me into an embrace.  

_…Did she get jealous from that conversation just now? How cute._

“I see… so, that’s how it is… Ha-ha-ha, ha-ha-ha-ha, ha-ha-ha-ha-ha-ha-ha!”

King Rama suddenly roared with laughter. It somehow felt like the laughter of a villain when they had lost.

“…Hah. In that case…”

_Wh-What now? The atmosphere suddenly turned scary…!_

#### Footnotes:

1. The original has another sentence after this that doesn’t seem to make sense: まあ…男の人ではないよね -> “well, is not man, right?”. This might be an error and be intended as something like “well, if I wasn’t male, then…” or it means something that I can’t see

+++

# 528 – No One Loses Out

“That’s good,” the foreign king suddenly said, his serious expression returning.

_What does he mean by “good”? Does he think that, since my lover is a woman, there’s still hope for him?_

“What do you mean by that…?”  

“Well, it made Us recall some things. It seems We were so overjoyed to meet you and Mika in person, it completely slipped Our mind… First, Our heartfelt apology.”

_Hang on, doesn’t this kind of self-reflection usually only happen when you get persuaded by either someone with ample life-experience or some self-styled protagonist?_  

_Why did he realize that on his own? King Rama… is a scary guy._

“I understand it even less now, but…”  

“Oh, well… In the ‘Association of Alimika Adorers[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-528-no-one-loses-out/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-102945)‘ there are occasionally people who oppose the relationship of you two, Alim, Mika. In such cases, there are usually discussions about how to pressure those people into changing their mind.”

_That sounds scary, like, genuinely terrifying. The atmosphere King Rama gave off earlier was scary, but what these weird fans of us get up to is just as frightening._  

_They might try to kill Shuu if they see him come out of our mansion too often. Not good, I need to give him something to turn invisible._

“Well… if We stole the march on them, We could no longer fulfill Our duties as ruler! Ha-ha-ha-ha!”

_So, these people are crazy enough to even oust a king, I mean, they totally would do that… They might be like fanatic idol fans back on Earth who cause large riots. Well, seeing they focus on us in contrast to the rest of Anazumu, their power is unfathomable. If Anazumu’s people were to oppose us, it might result in extreme destruction._

“Besides, Our opponent is not a man… Even assuming you are having a homosexual relationship, she isn’t a stranger… Mika is someone close to you, so there is no room for Us to complain. We fully support that… Still, do you truly love each other?”

_So, in other words, from his perspective its better if the two of us are together compared to being with some stranger? That would be a way to work this out peacefully._

_Somehow, this went in a weird direction._  

As far as I knew, homosexual relationships weren’t common in this world. Was this the right interpretation or was it something weirder?

“We do. We are in love!” Mika announced, as she brought her lips close to mine.

_…That’s bold of her. But we’ve been rather affectionate since the amusement park date and there aren’t that many people here, so it isn’t that embarrassing._

I let it happen and our lips met.

“Oh… oh, oh~~!” The foreign king seemed happy. “Hey, Hanuman! Once We get home, We shall erect a spire in commemoration of this moment! What a marvelous sight to see!” King Rama suddenly declared.  

“As you wish, my king!”  

“P-Please don’t.”

_I wish the taciturn Hanuman hadn’t reacted this excitedly to it, either._

“We were half joking! Well… We feel wonderful, despite just receiving splendid rejection!”

_Half joking, he says… Does that mean he’ll build half of a spire?_  

_Not good… our fans are scary…_

“K-King Rama… it is getting late…”  

“Hrm, you are not wrong, King Mephilad.”

The other king came to our rescue after checking the time. King Rama didn’t object, likely since they had some matter to take care of.

Come to think of it, King Mephilad did mention during the message yesterday about wanting to continue the good relations with said country. He had likely summoned us to improve the visitor’s mood. I should lighten his spirits a bit more.

“Your Majesty Rama!”

I had asked Mika in a whisper to give me some space and then got really close to the foreign king. He smelled of high-class perfume.

“Wh-What is it?”  

“…Uhm, I love Mika from the bottom of my heart, so I had to reject your proposal, but it made me very happy! Thank you so much for your kind words!”

When giving those words of thanks in a flirtatious voice while looking up at him, I grasped one of his hands with both of mine.

“Wa… wawa… wa… No, there is no need to thank Us… Our apologies for the trouble We caused you. We are also happy to hear you say that. Farewell, then.”

He said these words with a kind smile, before turning away and walking to King Mephilad’s side… While holding his nose, which was dripping with red blood[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-528-no-one-loses-out/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-102945).

_____  

___  

_

“Somehow, that got tough,” Tuhl commented after the two kings and their respective guards were gone and we left the dining hall.  

“Ah-ha-ha… We need to act with a bit more moderation during our activities,” I laughed. “Or things like that will keep happening.”  

“Well, if it’s you and your friends, Alim, you could probably just suppress such issues, so you’d be fine even if you continued like this,” the prince replied with a grin.

His face looked as handsome as always.  

_I guess royalty needs to have those kinds of looks[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-528-no-one-loses-out/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-102945)._

“…So, once you turn 16, you’ll get married? You can, thanks to that skill, right?”

Tuhl had seen my status screen. In other words, he knew of my Gender Conversion skill[4](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-528-no-one-loses-out/#easy-footnote-bottom-4-102945).

I decided to answer honestly.

“Yes, that’s the plan! Right, Mika!”  

“Yeah.”

She hugged me happily.

“Well, once that time comes, the whole country will have a large celebration. Oh, that’s right, you’re going to pay Karua visit, won’t you?”  

“Yes.”  

“She’s eagerly awaiting you in her room.”

Thus, Mika and I parted with Tuhl and then went to Karua’s room to play.

#### Footnotes:

2. The original is 赤い血が滴る花を抑えながら. Thanks to Kemm for pointing out that 花 (flower) is a homophone of 鼻 (nose). This was likely a typo.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-528-no-one-loses-out/#easy-footnote-2-102945)

4. So, he knew from the start but probably assumed that Alim started out as a girl.

# 529 – Before the Wedding

It was four days before the ceremony would take place. I had finished planning everything.

At this point, there was more talk about the upcoming wedding between two fellow SSS-Rankers than Mika and me. In any case, this was apparently the first time such a wedding happened since the establishment of the adventurer system[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-529-before-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-102948).

The way the public saw the union between Lastman and Parasuna was rather varied. First, Parasuna herself was a beauty, which was fine in itself. The problems were on Uruto’s side. People were honestly doubting whether a marriage between Parasuna and the inhuman seeming Lastman was possible.

Even though they were perfectly suited for each other, as long as he was in his real appearance. Also, there weren’t many people who knew that the two of them were in such a relationship. Which was obvious, since they had kept it hidden to avoid causing a ruckus.

Because it was such a rare occasion and of a variety of other reasons, there were numerous foreign visitors like King Rama. Some of them had likely been at my hero proclamation. An especially high percentage was made up by foreign SSS- and SS-Rankers, and officials from the adventurer guild.

For all these reasons, the city was currently bustling. Although this country had been one of the more prosperous ones from the start, which only became more pronounced due to the wealth gained from the war with the demons, this would now be reinforced further due to all those visitors eager to part with their money.

Incidentally, Mika and I were currently enjoying the final quiet day we had with each other. We spent yesterday playing with Karua… and tomorrow, the wedding preparations would start for real.

Well, if I made full use of my equipment and items, I’d be done in an instant, but… I felt like I shouldn’t do it at the last minute, plus the fine adjustments would likely take time.

“Eh-heh-heh~, Ayumu~.”

So, with that being said, I was putting all my efforts into spoiling Mika. She looked awfully cute.

“Ayumu! Hug me!”  

“Alright, hug it is!”

We embraced each other tightly. That moment, it happened. Someone pressed the intercom (people kept bothering us, so I came up with a way that it could only be activated by those who actually had business with us).

The scene outside was displayed on a nearby Tozumaho. In front of the gate to our residence stood a bearded, muscular, middle-aged man, and an old man with a friendly expression, who was carrying a staff.

_…What could they be here for? At least they aren’t acquaintances of Mika and me._

“…I’ll go check.”  

“…Alright,” Mika, who had cuddled up close to me, replied with both a disappointed tone of voice and expression.

I wanted to comfort her right away, but guests came first. We might be madly in love, but that didn’t mean we lost any common sense[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-529-before-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-102948). I exited the mansion and went through the garden to the gate.

“Greetings, is there something I can do for you?”

Looking at him from close up, the muscular man with blond hair was huge. He gave off a sense of pressure.

“O-Oh~! Could you be Alyum Nasuwei?”  

“You got the name wrong, Thor… She’s called Alim Nariwei.”

_D-Did that guy just get my name wrong? I guess there are actually people who do._

“Sorry for the sudden visit… and for mispronouncing your name! I’m Thor! Also called the ‘God of Thunder’, one of Yggdrasil’s esteemed SSS-Rankers! Gah-ha-ha-ha-ha-ha!” the blond middle-aged man introduced himself.  

“I am called Heimdall, and I am another SSS-Ranker from the same country.”

_Huh, they’re from Yggdrasil, the country of the holy tree? The place that treated my brother, sister-in-law, and best friend so harshly?_

_…That said, it was the king and his close advisor who were responsible for that, so those two men might be unrelated. For some reason, they feel like nice people, I should ask them why they’re here. Though they’ve probably come to visit Kanata and the others._

“Uhm… does that mean…”  

“Yes, we’ve come to meet Nakata, Sakura, and Juu[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-529-before-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-102948),” the man called Thor replied.  

“I also heard that an acquaintance of mine lives nearby… we were planning to show our faces while we’re here for the wedding between two fellow SSS-Rankers,” the man called Heimdal added.  

“Gah-ha-ha-ha-ha-ha! In any case, Nakata and Sakura also used to be our pupils.”

_I see, my hunch was correct. I’m curious about that acquaintance the old man mentioned, but… considering his age, it might be someone close to the king._

_In any case, I should call those four. I don’t want to barge in while they’re doing something lewd, so let’s ask them via message for now._

[Kanata, Sakura, Shuu, Rir! Is now a good time?]　  

[What’s up, Big Bro?]　  

[I guess? Did somethin’ happen?]　  

[Two SSS-Rankers called Thor and Heimdal have come to visit.]　  

[Oh!? We’re on our way!]　  

[Same here, Sakura and I will be there in a moment!]　

Shortly later, the four of them were here. They didn’t seem displeased, so those two men likely had helped them.

“Gah-ha-ha-ha-ha-ha! Long time no see!” Thor guffawed.  

“Indeed!”  

“Thank you once more for back then.”

Kanata’s reply was lively, while Shuu also gave a light bow together with his thanks.

“Erm, let’s not talk while standing, please come inside.”

Everyone seemed to agree with my proposal, so I led them into the mansion.

That actually makes sense, since it usually takes a long time to reach SSS-Rank, so people would marry before they reach it, and even if both are adventurers, they likely wouldn’t both reach the rank.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-529-before-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-1-102948)

2. Could’ve fooled me.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-529-before-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-2-102948)

# 530 – The Future of the Country of the Holy Tree (Shuu)

“Well, it’s been about two months. Right, Nakata?”  

“It’s Kanata.”

Apparently, there would be a wedding between two SSS-Rankers in this country soon, so big shots and famous high-rank adventurers from other countries were coming here. The bride- and groom-to-be were people who seemed to have helped Ayumu for a while when he came to this city, so he was preparing the wedding decorations, clothes, cake, and such.

Lately, he’d been working hard at school, even outside classes, and this was likely the reason (just like me, he no longer had to study for classes). Well, he was the kind of person to diligently accomplish a request he agreed to, so I wasn’t worried.

Still, I didn’t expect Thor and Heimdal to suddenly pay us a visit… Did them showing up like this mean that Yggdrasil was now stable? Even though it had only been a few months since the king died?

“In any case, it’s great that we could come here for that wedding! Gah-ha-ha-ha-ha-ha! You guys look well, much better than when you were over there.”  

“That’s because we are happy here… What happened over there after we left?” Kanata asked Thor and Heimdal.  

“Hrm.”

It looked like he wondered the same as I.

“I’m not sure if I should be blunt… well, the man is dead, so it’s not like he can complain… Wow, this stuff tastes great!?” Heimdal continued after taking a sip of the tea made by Ayumu. “To be completely honest, it is going far better than while the king was alive. Things can be done without spending money on weird affairs, and the excessively harsh treatment of slaves, that started three generations ago, has eased up. Moreover, the country is still able to operate as usual.”

“Even assuming the king being gone was beneficial… didn’t that cause issues?”

_I mean, the guy was the king, after all. The country pretty much used to be a dictatorship, so why would it be so easy to-_

“That fool king barely did any proper governing, it was mostly those around him,” Thor interrupted my train of thought. “That’s why it’s going fine. Also, with the only one gone, who was always opposed to improving things, such plans are now advancing smoothly.”

_H-He called him a “fool king”… Though guess it’s fine with the guy gone…_

“I mean, the family that was the symbol of the country may be gone, but that bloodline existed to oppose Yggdrasil’s evil god in the first place. Nalim Nasuwei, Juu, and Nakata made sure that this evil god is now gone for good, so it’s not like we need that lineage anymore.”

_I-I see. Guess that king wasn’t much liked by those around him… He tried to get Rir killed, and I didn’t like him either, but not to the point where I’d be happy he’s dead._

“D-Does that mean there aren’t any problems over there?”  

“That’s right. No issues except for the cruel slavery system.”

It wasn’t easy to get rid of slavery. Or rather, it was tough to abolish customs that had been established in the past.

“It would appear as if the politicians realized that the current system of government works well enough, so they will continue managing the country in this manner,” Heimdal explained. “That is also why we plan to consult with Lastman and King Mephilad on how to improve the slavery situation.”

I felt a bit bad for just thinking about my own happiness and up and leaving the country, but it sounded like they were moving in a good direction. From how they said it, it was only a question of time until slavery was gone there.

“At any rate, it feels weird. To be made an envoy to another country just by virtue of being an SSS-Ranker, you know? I was born a peasant,” Thor mused.  

“They probably had no choice, with the current shortage of able statesmen. They likely want to inspire at least some confidence in the populace.”

_Come to think of it, Lastman, one of the two who’ll get married soon, is apparently rather influential, too. Or rather… he’s said to be the one who got rid of slavery in this country. And there’s Alim and Mika who get summoned by the king on a regular basis and often spend time with the princess. Bein’ an SSS-Ranker is plenty meaningful._

_Well, the four of us are still SS-Rank… Plus, we’re unknowns and don’t have much influence. From what I see with Ayumu, that might be more enjoyable._

“That reminds me, Juu, Nakata, Sakura, Rir, there’s something we need to talk with you about,” Thor said, suddenly switching to serious mode.  

“What might that be?”

_Wh-What’s goin’ on? Don’t tell me we gotta return to that country? No way, I like it here more…_

While I was pondering that, Heimdal took out something from his magic bag. When he put it on the table, it turned out to be something like certificates. Four of them.

“…What is that?”  

“SSS-Rank certificates. From today on, the four of you are SSS-Rankers.”

_…What?_

# 531 – New SSS-Rankers (Shuu & ?)

“What is that supposed to mean?” Kanata asked with a serious look.  

“Well, it’s simple. You guys originally registered over there, didn’t you? Since you became adventurers there, the decision lays with our country, not the Mephalad Kingdom. So, the politicians discussed it with the adventurer guild and decided to formally promote you to SSS-Rank. It was decided by the country, so they treat it like a ‘royal appointment’.”

_H-How could that happen. Bein’ SSS-Rank probably comes with tons of headaches. And right after I thought ’bout it._

“Hold on a moment, Sakura and I never… oh.”  

“You remember? You temporarily registered as a party. So you could share experience points.”

Indeed, you needed to register as an adventurer to be able to share exp[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-531-new-sss-rankers-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-108510). Unless you used the item Alim had created. There was no other way.

“But don’t worry. They only promoted you, so you’d be counted among the strong,” Thor explained. “That doesn’t mean you need to go back to Yggdrasil.”  

“You can think of it as a simple title… Well, I suppose it is possible that the king of this country will make requests of you,” Heimdal added.

If we didn’t have to return to that country, I could accept it. It sounded like we’d get the rank but no obligation to act in that function. That was rather cushy. Not what I expected.

“Well, that’s about it…” Thor concluded. “Being SSS-Rank shouldn’t be a detriment to you.”  

“Indeed,” Heimdal agreed. “There are several unknown SSS-Rankers, so you don’t need to worry about public appearances.”

_…So, from now on, we’re also SSS-Rankers. I mean, looks like it’s pretty much like getting’ a degree. I gotta check later. There might be a title for bein’ SSS-Rank._

“In any case, the Mephalad Kingdom sure has many SSS-Rankers,” Thor mused.  

“Is that so?” Kanata asked.  

“Yes, there’s Gilmars, Uruto and Parasuna, Alim and Mika… and now you guys. Oh, come to think of it, the king is also a former SSS-Ranker.”

_Dang, sounds like a huge power imbalance. To think this country is this strong… I had no idea. Seems like this place has a lot of leeway._

“Gah-ha-ha-ha-ha! Well, having many strong people is a good thing!”  

“You’re right,” Heimdal agreed. “With Alim being involved in the fights with both evil gods, this country likely needs a certain amount of power.”

_Thinkin’ ’bout it like this, Ayumu does have it hard. And because of all that, they treat him like some holy woman… even though he’s male. For others he just looks like this incredibly beautiful girl who fights for the sake of the world._

“Hm… oh, it’s already been an hour.” After shooting a glance at the clock, Thor stood up. “Sorry, but I should head back. Thanks for the hospitality and see you guys again.”  

“In that case, I suppose I should take my leave, too.” Heimdal also rose.

It was nice to meet these two again who’d done so much for us in the past.

“I’ll go see you off.”  

“Sorry for the trouble, Nakata.”  

“It’s Kanata.”

Kanata brought our two guests to the porch to see them off.

_…Now that we’re SSS-Rank, we can go to that wedding, can’t we? I mean, Ayumu organized it, we gotta see that._

________  

_____  

__

“It’ll be soon.”  

“I’m so excited.”

The rabbitkin and the innkeeper were cuddled close, showing expressions of joy.

“It looks like Alim is almost done with the preparations.”  

“Right… as expected of her. I wonder how it will look.”  

“All she told me was that it’ll be ‘lavish but romantic’.”

Uruto caressed Parasuna’s head. Her white ears were twitching.

“I can’t wait to see you in your dress.”  

“Hm… it’s incredibly pretty. You won’t be disappointed.”

For them, the upcoming wedding was an extraordinary event. They had weathered many hardships, and this signified both the finish line and a new beginning.

“…After the wedding, will we be going on a honeymoon?”  

“We will… we have the leeway for it. We’ll pause our adventuring activities and close the inn for a few months. We’ll be able to relax, at least for some time.”  

“Well, we’ve been busy for a while now, so that won’t be a bad thing. Besides, after the wedding, everyone will know your true identity, so there’ll probably be tons of people coming to the inn… Closing it down for a few months sounds like a wise decision.”

Parasuna was gazing at Uruto. He looked back into her red eyes.

“By the way… uhm, what’s your stance on having children?” she asked.  

“I want to have some. We’re already 22, so I don’t see any issue.”  

“Right. So, during that honeymoon…”  

“Hm, that should work.”

He pulled her into an embrace. She showed a joyful smile while blushing.

“I know you can transform into any form you like, but please don’t make it weird, alright[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-531-new-sss-rankers-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-108510)? Like a goblin.”  

“Did I ever do that?”  

“I-I’m just talking hypotheticals. You don’t have to change anything.”  

“Ha-ha, alright.”

# Side Story 15 – Rir’s Sleep-Talk (Shuu)

This happened during a certain night after Rir joined the club.

---

“Mh… _yawn_.”

I ended up waking up in the middle of the night. It wasn’t even that I had to go to the restroom.

Rir was still sleeping soundly next to me, so I just shot a glance at the clock so I wouldn’t wake her. It was 6:05 am… I usually slept a bit longer, but today I apparently woke early.

I disentangled myself from Rir, who was as close to me as humanly possible, and went to the bathroom. When I came back… I decided to sleep a bit longer, as anyone having that chance likely would. I crawled back into the bed.

There was some light in the room from the morning sun. I took a good look at Rir’s face, who was so close, our bodies were touching.

We were currently in Anazumu, but if the people on Earth found out that I was sharing a bed with her, they’d probably shun me. In fact, looking at her so calmly, I started to feel awkward.

“Mhh… Shuu… Eh-heh-heh.”

She even called my name in her sleep. Far from waking up, she hugged me again instead.  

She told me before that she kept her body slender for my sake, so it felt very pleasant to hold her in an embrace. Even so, I often realized just how cute she was.

Deep asleep as she was right now, she probably wouldn’t notice if I stroked her head and poked her cheeks. I freed one of my hands from her embrace and brought a finger to her cheek. It felt silky soft, as if it would swallow it. She seemed healthy, which made me happy.

“Mrr… Master… Shuu… My apologies.”

She started saying something. What was she sorry about? I started to wonder what had happened in her dream.

“Woof… I’m sorry, Shuu… For me… for me to turn into such a macho…”

It sounded as if she was dreaming about turning into a beefcake.

“I had so much fun training with you, Shuu… and now… my muscles became so bulky… I look like some male pro-wrestler…”

Just how much had she trained? I honestly didn’t want to imagine it. Rir, with her face so cute you couldn’t help thinking of it as a remainder of her lost childhood, now trained up to the level of a body builder… Ugh.

“Ah, Shuu… please don’t! Don’t give up on me! Stop looking at the boobs of other girls. Mine are still the same.”

Did she think that I only stayed with her because of her rack? I mean, it was true that they were my favorite part of her.

“Woof, in that case… you can grope them as you always do. They’re… they’re still the same!”

I didn’t “always” grope them… only during special times when the mood was right… definitely.

Then, maybe since she was moving in her dream, she strengthened her hug. I didn’t know if the “me” in her dream thought the same, but… it didn’t feel bad. It was nice.

“How is that even possible? For you yourself to turn into a ball of muscles, Shuu… you didn’t need to do that for me. Wow, your muscles are swelling up…!”

What in the world happened to me in her dream? For even her, with her muscle fetish, to be shocked. I must’ve reached a point beyond even a bodybuilder with a severe case of steroids. That was rather concerning.

“…I-Incredible… you’re over two meters tall now… Your skeletal structure must’ve changed because of your swelling muscles… Besides, I can’t see body fat anywhere…!”

Now it sounded as if I had turned into a monster. What a strange dream.

“Oh… Shuu! If you hug me now, you’ll crush me. Though it was always my dream to die in your arms.”

How unsettling. In the first place, she was currently the one who hugged me.

“Get… g-g-g-get married!? Are you serious, Shuu?”

Now it sounded as if I had proposed to her in her dream. In the future, I’d probably do that for real.

“T-True enough, in Anazumu we’re just old enough to get married, but… are you sure? Am I good enough for you?”

I didn’t have any regrets. I was happy to be with her, or rather, I had not a single complaint. I could no longer imagine my life without her at this point.

“Woof… the wedding. How do you like my wedding dress?”

She had jumped straight to the wedding.  

_…I definitely want to see her in her wedding dress._

“Awoo~, no… noooo! My muscles ripped the dress and- woof?”

Her eyes, which had turned slightly moist, opened. Right as she dreamed of her muscles tearing the wedding dress, apparently.

“Good morning, Rir.”  

“Woof! You’re awake, Shuu. Morning.”

As she woke from her dream, a new day began.

---

**TL notes:**  

It’s another weird side story since the author, and I quote, “ran out of material and ideas”.
