# 532 – The Day of the Wedding – 1

“My… it’s marvelous,” Archbishop Chris, Myuri’s father, who’d do the ceremony, commented.

Today was the day of Uruto and Parasuna’s wedding. Since the day before yesterday, I had continuously prepared without sleeping (at least that was how it probably looked, but in reality, I had slept in the magic room) and finally finished last evening.

With my own and the bride and groom’s sensibilities in mind, I kept the decorations simple but gorgeous. I wanted people to marvel the moment the stepped into the church, like Chris right now. Though I hadn’t used any special enchantments.

It was also designed so people would gradually get used to it mentally. That was to prevent them from just admiring the decorations and not paying any attention to the bride and groom, who were supposed to be the stars.

As for who would be at the wedding venue… it was mainly close friends of Uruto and Parasuna and colleagues from work. Then, there were dozens of dignitaries from other countries and adventurers at SS-Rank or higher.

Adventurers at S-Rank and lower, who had no personal connection to the bride and groom and didn’t get a direct invitation, wouldn’t attend the ceremony. They could only see them in the afternoon when there’d be a parade around the city. It wasn’t Uruto and Parasuna who came up with that idea but the king and his close aides. It would surely be crowded with people.

Also, due to the events the other day, my younger brother and the other three now fulfilled the requirements to attend the wedding, so they’d be there, too. They just barely made it on the guest list.

Quite the lavish lunch was planned for the wedding. Well, I cooked it, so that part was obvious. I came up with recipes to get rid of more than 10% of my stock of cooking ingredients, and since they had been harvested from dungeon monsters, they were commonly seen as high-class ingredients. I was lucky in that regard.

Also, I prepared the whole program of what would be featured during the wedding. As their friend, Gilmars would hold a speech at some point. Then, there would be special events using pictures and fireworks.

To be honest, I had a lot of concerns at the start, but as “Alim Nariwei” going all out, I couldn’t let anyone leave unsatisfied.

“I would love such wonderful decorations at my daughter’s wedding, too.”  

“You mean when Miss Myuri and Mr. Orgo get married?”  

“Indeed… As archbishop, I have attended many weddings, but the decorations here are by far the best. I suppose this was to be expected with you holding Item Master.”  

“Eh-heh-heh.”

_Hearing him say that tells me that it is good enough. Great, this should calm my anxiety a bit._

“Hey! Alim!”  

“Oh, Mr. Gilmars!”

Although it was still rather early, Gilmars had come, wearing a stylish suit. It was still two hours before the bride and groom would arrive at the church.

On that note, it was currently 6 am. At 8 am, Uruto and Parasuna would arrive, and from 9 am on the guests. The ceremony itself would begin at 10 am.

“Isn’t it still a bit early?”  

“Well, you’re not wrong. Look, I’m going to hold a speech in front of everyone, right? I mean, I memorized it a bit. Or rather, I should know it by heart now, but I never did that in front of so many people.”  

“I’m surprised that would happen to someone as experienced as you, Mr. Gilmars.”  

“It happens. I’m only human. Besides, there will be tons of people attending.”

So, even someone who was seen as supreme commander among SSS-Rankers (not including those who acted in special roles, like me as the hero) could get this nervous? Well, from how he talked earlier, he didn’t seem _that_ tense, so maybe he simply decided to come early.

“Well, I’m sure Uruto and Parasuna will also arrive early,” he mused.  

“You might be right.”

No matter how you looked at it, most top rankers had intense personalities.

“Hey there, Alim!”  

“Oh, Mr. Bacchus!”

The winemaker had also come. As representative of the bride and groom’s mutual friends, his job would apparently be to tell anecdotes. Also, all the alcohol that would be served came from his company. That part was a foregone conclusion.

“Wow… it looks super fancy… but also calming.”  

“Eh-heh-heh, thank you for saying that!”  

“Yep, with all this, I’m sure those two will never forget this day,” Bacchus, who was likely the one who knew the bride and groom best, commented earnestly. “I know just how hard those two worked… this makes me as happy as if it was my own wedding.”

“I see.”  

“Yes, they really had to go through a lot of hardship. And they’re only 22,” he said with a laugh.

It felt like he was truly happy about their marriage.

“In any case, we gotta make this the best wedding possible.”  

“We will!”

Still, right now, we could only wait until it started.  

…Four more hours until the ceremony.

+++

# 533 – The Day of the Wedding – 2

“Ha-ha-ha, you want something to drink, Alim?” he asked while taking out something that looked like wine, then pouring it into a tankard, which he then handed to me.  

“Bacchus, you’re not trying to tempt Alim, who is still too young for alcohol, in front of a clergyman, are you?”  

“That’s grape juice, y’know.”

Sure enough, it didn’t smell like alcohol, so he probably wasn’t lying. His company also made juice, after all.

“Bottoms up.”

The tankard was a bit big, but I was thirsty, so I decided to take him up on it. Gilmars kept staring at me as I gulped down the juice.

“Is something wrong? Do I have something on my face?”  

“No, I just thought about your fans in my party… They’d probably have a field day if they saw you sipping grape juice from a tankard big enough to hold with both hands.”  

“Ah-ha-ha-ha.”

_Did I ever drink something in a flirtatious manner? As a boy, you’d call it gulping down, but… I guess I’ve been a girl for quite some time._  

_Well, being able to captivate men isn’t a bad thing, surely. At least from the perspective of my fans… and I’m happy, too._

“Bacchus, could I have some, too?”  

“You’ll be going with wine, I assume, Gilmars.”  

“Yep, I’ll-”

When Gilmars was about to take a bottle of wine from Bacchus, the door to the avenue opened. This time, the stars of the show appeared.

“We’re here way too early.”  

“I just couldn’t sit and wait.”

Gilmars’ prediction had come true. Even though it was still three and a half hours until the ceremony would begin.

“You’re here already. Congratulations to your big day, both of you,” the archbishop greeted them.  

“Th-Thank you so much, Mr. Chris.”

Being greeted in this manner by a clergyman made it appear as if their turn on the stage was already imminent.

“I can’t wait to see your wedding dress, Parasuna.”  

“…Oh, Gilmars! Yes, Alim made it for me.”

Girls adored wedding dresses. Once she had it on, she’d surely captivate everyone.

“Hey there, Uruto, Parasuna. Gratulations. Well… I’ve watched your relationship for a long time… and it finally happens.”  

“Thank you, Bacchus. You’re right… we aren’t that old yet, but it feels like we made it,” Uruto replied to Bacchus’ greeting while holding Parasuna’s shoulder.

Her face was slightly flushed. There were many female adventurers looking up to her, but if they saw her face now, their cool image of her would be shattered. She looked rather adorable.

Then it was my turn for greetings.

“For today… I wish you all the best!”  

“Yes, thank you so much, Alim!” Uruto replied. “…At any rate, these decorations are amazing.”  

“I’ve never seen anything so dazzling and mystical,” Parasuna added.

They were looking around the church interior, seemingly burning the sights into their minds.

“I did work hard.”  

“It seems we made the right choice leaving it to you. I’m looking forward to Parasuna’s dress and the cake.”  

“You won’t be disappointed!”

The two of them went back to looking at the interior design. As they did that, Gilmars closed in on me.

“Say, Alim, I also think those decorations are marvelous… You must’ve spent a lot of time on them.”  

“Yes, I studied up tons for today.”  

“I see,” he replied while patting my head. After just two pats, he seemed to realize something and removed his hand. “Sorry, I did that on impulse.”  

“Ah-ha-ha, it’s fine, I don’t mind.”  

“You sure? I’ll boast about it to the others later, then.”

_This man does things at his own pace. Oh, well._

On that note, we each brought congratulatory gifts. This custom existed in this world, too. Money was a given.

Bacchus, being who he was, likely brought some ultra-high-class alcohol on the level of treasure grade. Gilmars probably had something related to adventurers.

Given who the attendees were, I assumed no one brought dried bonito, seaweed[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-533-the-day-of-the-wedding-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-109376), or tableware. Well, it’s possible someone brought the latter. I obviously had prepared what I just mentioned. Needless to say, I didn’t use their payment on that.

_Heh-heh-heh… I’ve prepared something of legend grade to tie those two together._

“What do you think? There is still ample time to put on the wedding dress, but… should we move to the waiting room already?”  

“No… we can wait some more.”

It looked like they wanted to soak in the afterglow a bit longer.  

During these days, I’d seen several times just how close Uruto and Parasuna were. Well, back during the war, he did mention that he loved her. Those two really seemed happy.

_Well then, three more hours until the show starts. I’ll also have to do my very best._

#### Footnotes:

1. Typical gifts during Japanese weddings are apparently katsuobushi (dried bonito), which symbolizes a strong marriage, and konbu (seaweed), which represents joy and prosperity.

+++

# 534 – Wedding Dress – 1

“The two of you were slated to arrive about an hour from now. Will you be putting on the dress and suit already?” I asked Uruto and Parasuna, while shooting a glance at the church’s clock.  

“Right, I guess it’s about time.”  

“We’ll be in your care, Alim.”

Incidentally, I’d be the one to help Parasuna in the dress and apply her makeup. As for if it was fine for a boy to do that… I didn’t let that question bother me. In the end, I was a girl in this world.

Also, Bacchus would apparently help Uruto put on the suit, so I left that part to him.

“We’ll call you once we’re done putting on the dress.”  

“That will be the first time I’m seeing Parasuna in her wedding dress. Alright.”

Parasuna and I moved to a room specifically for putting on the wedding dress (the so-called bride’s room). I closed the door.

“Then… if you would,” she said.  

“Of course.”

I took out the dress from my magic bag. It was an article into I had put all my diligence into. This one dress would likely sell for as much as two legend grade weapons.

“First, please change into these bridal undergarments. I will leave the room during that time, so call me once you’re done.”  

“Bridal undergarments…? You mean underwear made to go with the dress? Alright.”

I left the room. Even as a girl, it wouldn’t fly to see her naked. That only worked in a relationship like the one Mika and I had.

A few minutes later, she called me back in.

“I’ll be starting to put on the dress, then.”  

“Please do.”

First, I had to make sure the interior and exterior were proper. After doing that, I asked her to stand over it.

“That’ll take just a moment.”  

“Hm.”

I raised the inner dress (a pannier that would cause the skirt to billow out), which was worn like a normal pair of pants, and secured it to her waist with a button on the back.

_…She has quite the good figure. She said she’s 22, right? That would be too young to be called a “mature woman” on Earth, but that’s the atmosphere she’s giving off. That obviously doesn’t mean she looks old._

“Next will be this part.”

I raised the outer dress (The one with a long hem called a train. The part that was usually held up by children during weddings, so it wouldn’t get dirty) until it covered her chest. On that note, dresses in this world for women with voluptuous breasts had distinct cleavages. This wasn’t seen as bold.

Once I secured it at the back with buttons and string, I’d be done. Though it would take some time to do that.

“Yeah… the dress is as wonderful as expected,” Parasuna commented as I was affixing things.  

“Eh-heh-heh, thank you for saying that.”

It was something I had put my all into (though I kept it at legend grade), so I was genuinely happy to receive praise for it.

And I was done.

“Next will be make-up.”  

“Yes.”

I asked her to sit in a chair and went to work. I had learned a lot about make-up used for weddings when I studied up on it. Maybe one day I could put it on use with Mika, too.

Well… my girlfriend looked fine with natural make-up, or none at all. She would probably only use it on such an occasion. For the same reason, I didn’t seem to need to put on much make-up myself in this world.

_Oh, self-praise is no praise at all… whatever._

“I’ll also be fixing your hair a bit.”  

“Alright.”

Applying make-up, which usually would have taken quite a bit of time, was done rather fast due to my quickness stat. Next, I put her hair into a bob, which would make wearing the veil easier. It also served to make sure her rabbit ears wouldn’t look unnatural.

“Once you’ve put on the shoes and gloves, we’re mostly done. We’ll be affixing the veil later.”  

“Yeah, thank you,” she replied while putting on the shoes.

Maybe I did have some talent for working at weddings.

“What do you think?”  

“This is me?”  

“Yes, it is.”

Parasuna kept looking into the mirror as she stood up. She was incredibly pretty. So pretty, Mika would likely say something like “let’s get married soon, too” once she saw her. With this, the attention should be on the bride, rather than the venue decorations.

“So pretty… Thank you, Alim.”  

“You’re welcome.”  

“For a former slave like me to wear such a thing[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-534-wedding-dress-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-109378)… I wonder what Uruto will say when he sees it… Heh-heh-heh-heh.”

_She’s a former slave!? I mean, I shouldn’t be that surprised, with Rir living with us. Something probably happened a long time ago with Mr. Uruto._

“I’ll be calling Mr. Uruto, then. He should be done putting on the suit.”  

“Right.”

On that note, I had also properly designed said tuxedo and made it by hand. I mean, it was part of the request.

I sent Bacchus a message, telling him that Parasuna was done putting on the dress, so he should bring the groom here.

#### Footnotes:

1. I guess this makes it probable that she was the slave that caused Uruto to start his crusade against the underworld slave trade in Mephilad

+++

# 535 – Wedding Dress – 2

For Uruto to see her in the dress for the first time, I asked Parasuna to put on the veil and gloves, and then hide behind a partition.

“I brought him, Alim.”

Just as asked in the message, Bacchus came together with Uruto. The latter looked good in the tuxedo.

“Y-You said it’s time for me to…”  

“We’ll show you right away… Miss Parasuna, please come out.”  

“Y-Yeah…”

While holding up the dress’ hem by herself, she stepped out from behind the partition. She was wearing the veil, and her rabbit ears were visible. How did her appearance, which should captivate anyone, look to him?

“Pa… rasuna…”  

“D-Do you like it?”

With her cheeks tinged red and slightly making her skirt flutter, she looked at Uruto, waiting for an answer. He just kept staring at her, spellbound, his mouth open, without saying anything.

“…Uruto?”  

“Won’t you say anything, man?”  

“Wha-…!? I-I was just so captivated… You’re incredibly pretty, Parasuna.”

He bashfully scratched his cheek after telling her his honest feelings.

“Heh-heh, thank you. I knew getting married was the right decision. My heart is beating so fast.”  

“S-Same here.”

They gazed at each other.  

There must’ve been some grand hardship for those two. I had Mika, so I could tell. Other than love, there was a sense of accomplishment.

“Heh-heh, Uruto… you look so handsome.”  

“You think so?”  

“I do. You always look good, but especially now. My dear husband.”  

“E-Enough already.”  

“Eh-heh-heh, I’m just messing with you.”

It looked as if they were reminiscing about something. Bacchus and I looked at each other, making eye-contact.

“There’s still a lot of time, so you two please enjoy yourselves,” I told them. “If you need to go to the toilet, there’s one right outside the room. In such a case, just enter the small fitting room, which will temporarily change what you’re wearing.”  

“Understood. Thanks again, Alim.”  

“Thank you too, Bacchus.”  

“It’s fine. Relax some, you guys.”

Bacchus and I left the waiting room. Those two would likely take some time to calm down.

“Alim, who of the two do you think was the one to propose?” he asked me, as he poured me some juice after we had returned to a waiting room for guests.  

“I expect it was Mr. Uruto.”  

“You’re right. And one of the reasons he proposed to her was related to you, Alim. He himself told me so.”  

“Really!? He said that?”

_Wh-What could that be? Something related to me._

“…During the war with the demons, we all died, regardless of how strong we were. And you brought us back to life, Alim.”  

“Th-That’s true. But Mr. Uruto also survived…”  

“Yep. His Creature Master skill allows him to change his form freely and recreate the appearance and powers of magic beasts. I think he endured it by transforming into a monster with special invulnerability.”

_Huh. What kind of magic beast would that be!? Does that mean it’s possible for him to turn into an SSS-Rank monster? Though I never encountered any SSS-Rank magic beasts in the wild so far. But I’m sure he can turn into something like a dragon._

_Now I want to know more…_

“Parasuna, on the other hand, has Magic Master, which increases the power of all basic elemental spells. Well, because of a skill called God of Water or something, not all her elements are equally strong[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-535-wedding-dress-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-109380)… Anyway, that’s the reason she didn’t survive like him.”

He then added with a chuckle, that all he himself had was Alcohol Magic and abilities that raised his firepower, so he died, too.

“So, once the war was over, you brought all of us back, right? Back then, it apparently made Uruto realize just how important she was to him.”  

“He took the plunge and proposed…?”  

“Exactly. Though if you ask me, he should’ve done that two years ago.”

_Does that make me their cupid? No, that doesn’t really fit. They were already in love at that point._

“They themselves said so, so it must be true. Well, she’s been in a relationship with him for a long time, but I didn’t expect his slave from back then to end up like this… Oh, by the way, I grew up in the house next to Uruto’s inn, y’know.”  

“R-Really!?”  

“Yep.”

However, he said that he thought it better to live closer to the factory where he made alcohol, so he moved there when he was 16.

“Well, it’s exactly because I know them so well that want them to be happy.”  

“I’m sure they are.”  

“Ah-ha-ha, you’re right.” He stretched a bit and then continued. “I also want a girlfriend already. I mean, it’s not like I didn’t have any before. Lahand has Margo and there’s apparently someone making advances towards Gabaina recently.”  

“Seriously!?”

_Wh-What, did spring finally come for those two? Even though they look like super rugged middle-aged men (although they actually aren’t that old, yet)._

“I’m not pulling your leg. I’m the only one without any romance prospects in our group. I’m going to drown my sorrows.”  

“Please don’t get drunk before the ceremony starts.”  

“I’ll be fine, I never get drunk!”

He brought out a bottle of wine from who-knows-where and started drinking.

#### Footnotes:

1. This may be wrong. The original is 『水神』とかよりはそれぞれの属性は弱い (“each element is weak(er) due to ‘Water God’ or something”). My translation is based on prior knowledge about those skills, which shouldn’t weaken other elements.

+++

# 536 – Assembly at the Venue – 1

“Alim~!”

Ten minutes after Parasuna had changed into her wedding dress, Mika arrived. She pulled me into a hug in front of quite a few acquaintances.

“Huh? Don’t tell me you don’t need my help with anything?”  

“Yep.”  

“I see… I thought I could lend you a hand, so I came early.”

She hung her head dejectedly. It looked cute, so I patted her head to cheer her up.

“Eh-heh-heh… I see Mr. Gilmars and Mr. Bacchus are here already,” she commented as she saw them milling about. “Does that mean the bride and groom are here, too?”  

“They are. I just finished helping Parasuna get dressed.”  

“You did? So, those two are on their own right now?”  

“Exactly. It’s just them in the waiting room. I’m pretty sure they’re currently reminiscing about the past.”

They probably needed some time on their own to think back on things and make this ceremony more memorable for them.

“In any case… how did you come up with the design for those decorations? You must’ve wracked your brain like crazy both on Earth and here,” she praised my work, as her gaze wandered around the church interior.

Then, her cheeks suddenly flushed, as if she thought about something embarrassing.

“I-I hope we’ll have an ambience like this when it comes to our wedding.”  

“Well, I’m sure I’ll manage something…”  

“When we get married on Earth… I wonder what your job will be, Ayumu. Will you design things like this?”

_Becoming a designer on Earth… huh? That never crossed my mind, but it might not be such a bad idea. Shuu mentioned that he’s planning to study statecraft on the university and then start a career as a policeman, and Mika would become my wife. Right, she also wanted to open a café._

_I’m the only one without any dreams for the future. Becoming a designer might work._

“You’re right… that might not be so bad!”  

“You think so? Well, with your talents, I’m sure you could do anything.”

With her at my side, that might be true. In any case, I’d have to work hard, on Earth, that is. In Anazumu, I was already successful enough.

“…Did we come here too early, after all?”  

“Hm? We ain’t. Bacchus, Gilmars, Alim, and Mika are here already, y’see?”

As the door to the church opened, I could hear voices.

“Woah… This is awesome! It’s so pretty…!”  

“…True, this is incredible…”

Four people, three men and one woman, entered. First were Gabaina and Lahand. Then the latter’s friends, Margo and Gog.

I called out to them.

“Mr. Gabaina, Mr. Lahand, it’s been a while!”  

“Long time no see, Alim. You’ve gone places since back then,” Gabaina replied.  

“You seem different from that affair with that Faust jackass[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-536-assembly-at-the-venue-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-109801),” Lahand added.

The two of them spoke seriously. There had never been a good opportunity to meet up, so it really had been a long time. They also never visited us at our house.

“So much happened since we last saw each other…”  

“I’m sure you’re at the point where you could defeat a Thunderbird in the blink of an eye now, right?”  

“Ha-ha… yes, I can.”

At this point, a wink might blast away such a monster, and a mere kiss could be enough to kill it. Okay, that was an exaggeration. But I was sure that I could defeat it with my pinky when it came to close combat, or, on the magical front, just by unleashing my magic power. You could think of it as having grown into one’s own.

“Oh… M-Mika!”

Margo, who had noticed Mika, was hiding a bit behind Lahand. The way she looked at her was completely different from back then.

“Oy, what’s wrong?”  

“I’m a bit nervous… after all, Mika is so different…”

True enough, from Margo’s perspective, she had gone from the lost girl back then to a famous top-ranker.

“Miss Margo! It’s been forever!”  

“Y-Yes, it has!”

When Mika called out to her, she flinched and straightened her back. The girl’s voice turned weirdly shrill, likely due to her nervousness.

“M-M-M-Mika, y-y-y-you’re so much stronger than back then.”  

“Eh-heh-heh… It’s all because I found Alim. That changed my life.”  

“Y-You changed so much, simply by being with Alim…?”

Mika’s reply was probably rather accurate. By meeting me, Karua changed a lot, too.  

_Am I the incredible one?_

“…Mr. Gog, why are you looking so grumpy?”  

“Oh, he told us he broke up with his girlfriend the other day,” Lahand explained. “And right after that happened, we get invited to a wedding…”  

“Huh, I see.”

_Poor Gog._  

Maybe due to what was just said, his expression turned even gloomier.

“Well, none of us got any marriage prospects, ain’t that right?”  

“…True.”

The two men who looked closer to middle aged despite being in the latter half of their twenties, chatted. It didn’t sound like Bacchus’ expectations[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-536-assembly-at-the-venue-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-109801) would come true for the time being.

“But Mr. Gabaina, isn’t there someone showing interest in you recently.”  

“Where did you hear that? All I did is talk a few times to a beastfolk girl with whom I’ve worked once.”

Still, from how Bacchus told it, maybe said girl was making an effort. Well, it was possible that the one she was trying to woo was simply too dense.

“How mean to say that, with Miss Margo telling you again and again that she is interested,” Mika delved deeper into the topic.  

“I-It’s true…” Margo stammered.  

“Didn’t I tell you before!? She’s like a younger sister or a daughter to me.”  

“B-But… ugh…” Margo hung her head in dejection.

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is メフィスト (mephisto). I can only assume that’s an error and he means Faust, since I don’t think Lahand ever met Mephistophales.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-536-assembly-at-the-venue-1/#easy-footnote-1-109801)

2. The verb used in the original is 報われる (“to be repaid/rewarded”). This seems weird in context and doesn’t appear to have a homophone, so I’m not sure if I’m misunderstanding something

+++

# 537 – Assembly at the Venue – 2

“Geez, these guys are lost causes,” Mika whispered to me, leaving Margo, who hung her head like her twin brother, to her own devices.

Still, just a short time ago, I was also such a lost cause who never managed to confess. Oh, well.

“Hey, there are people without a better half.”  

“Exactly.”

They better made sure Bacchus didn’t hear what they just said. That wouldn’t end well.

“…Whatever. We’ll go look around. See ya!” Lahand shouted.  

“I’ll also go say hi to Lastman… or rather, Uruto,” Gabaina added.

The four of them disappeared into the direction of the waiting room.

I got the feeling that people would now gather rapidly… and I was proven correct when members from Gilmars’ group arrived one after the other. All the top members of the Peace of Hercules had apparently been invited. Though the only one among them I was close to was Gilmars himself.

“It’s gradually starting to get lively.”  

“So many people. As expected, since it’s about those two.”

_Well, that’s the reason I made so much food. Not that I’m worried about that part._  

_It’s getting noisier and noisier! Though I’m happy to hear them praise my decorations._

“I wonder who’s arriving now.”

As Mika and I were shaking hands with someone who told us they were part of our fan club, a loud noise came from the church entrance.

That moment, it felt as if the air froze. All commotion came to a halt. On the other side of the door, I could see a group of dozens of people. And at the head of the procession stood the king. It seemed everyone had fallen silent when they saw him arrive.

“They’re here, a bit early,” Archbishop Chris muttered, before hastily making his way to the group.

Incidentally, this church had a seating section for those with political influence. Guided by the clergyman, the king’s group took their seats in the part for royals and nobles.

“Alim, Mika!” someone called our names.

Obviously, it was Karua. Mika and I went to her seat.

It looked as if to one side of her, the queen was seated, while on the other was Tuhl. The king sat next to the latter. Ruin and his friends stuck together as usual and sat next to each other. It was the same for the minister and knight commander. Furthermore, close to the minister sat the hero Herrell and the former princess Elle[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-537-assembly-at-the-venue-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-109803). The remainder were nobles I was only acquainted with in passing.

“Alim, these decorations are wonderful! I never expected any less of you!”  

“Truly. we never saw anything like it during our time as adventurers.”  

“They are rather marvelous.”

Karua, the king, and the queen praised my work.  

_Tee-hee. To get rave reviews even from those used to luxury. All that hard work paid off!_

“You really are amazing, Alim. We’ll never measure up to you.”  

“Hey, it’s only thanks to her that we got this strong.”

Ruin and Lilo also gave their comments. Orgo and Myuri had similar impressions,

“In that case, I’ll organize your weddings, too!”  

“”””!?””””

The four of them gaped in shock. It was the fate of those in relationships to be teased about it by their close friends.

“We… we aren’t thinking about getting married, yet.”  

“R-Right? We’re still young.”  

“A-As they say, Alim.”  

“Oh, but I cannot help longing for it.”

_I get it, those four took forever to even confess to each other. So, they probably won’t get married any time soon. Mika and I might beat them to it. I can’t imagine them kissing… much less doing the deed. All I can do is encourage them._

“Heh-heh-heh, it reminds me of back then.”  

“What do you mean?”  

“The day of our wedding.”

The queen, on the other hand, seemed to be reminiscing about the past.

“Ours should be soon, too…”  

“Indeed… I’m dreaming of it, even now.”

Herrell and Elle also seemed to be discussing something. Weddings did have a big effect on people. These two might rely on me for theirs, too.

While chatting with the king’s group for some time, lots of other guests arrived. As we were released when our talk reached a good stopping point, Mika and I spied our housemates. All four were wearing the dresses and tuxedos I custom made for them.

_Hrm, they suit them well, if I may say so. I guess I’ll ask them what they think of it later._

With everything going on, the time for the guests to arrive passed before I knew it, and all that remained was to hold the ceremony. All that talking made the time pass quickly.

“Alright, Mika, I’ll go make the final check on the bride and groom.”  

“Oh, okay!”

After giving Mika a head’s up, I made my way to stars of the show in the waiting room.

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is ノア (noa). I can only assume the author either forgot her name or mixed it up with another character. It’s obvious this is meant to be Elle.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-537-assembly-at-the-venue-2/#easy-footnote-1-109803)

+++

# 538 – Onwards to the Wedding

“Rir, are you ready?”  

“Woof, I am!”

We had decided to go to the wedding, since Ayumu set up the venue. All the SSS-Rankers could apparently attend. In any case, I was super curious how it turned out, after Ayumu put so much effort into it.

“Shuu, does it suit me?”

Rir was wearing the perfect dress for going to a wedding, which my best friend had prepared. And with him as the crafter, there was no way it wouldn’t suit her. He said he made it while paying attention to details like not leaving the shoulders open or using white, which was reserved for the wedding dress. My tuxedo was the same.

“It looks good.”  

“Eh-heh-heh… I’m never wearing dresses, so this feels new,” she commented, as she held the garment’s hem and made it flutter. Calling her cute… would be an understatement. “Nonetheless, this is my first time attending a wedding.”  

“I’ve been at a few.”  

“Woof, how were they?”

_That’s hard to answer. I mean, they were how weddings are._

“Well, everythin’ looked super fancy… and the bride and groom made their debut, I guess.”  

“They kiss and exchange rings, right? And if it was a Japanese wedding, there would be a big celebration.”  

“Yup. The former happens durin’ the ceremony and the latter’s the celebration afterwards. I heard this one will have one of those, too.”

_A celebration organized by Ayumu. I wonder how that’ll turn out._

“It sounds like a lot of work.”  

“Sure does.”  

“Still, weddings have a certain allure. Wearing the white dress… exchanging rings and kissing… I wonder how it feels to tie the know with your lover.”

_For her, this “lover” should be me. Well, if it ain’t, I’m gonna cry some manly tears._

“Well, just a question of time until it’s our turn.”  

“Huh?”

_Damn. I went and said stuff that’s still far out. She didn’t show a promising reaction either. This was lame. Sayin’ it’s “just a question of time” makes it sound like it’s already sttled that we get married. Feels way too early to decide that, seein’ we’ve only been together for a couple of months._

“Ah… sorry ’bout that.”  

“…Shuu… was this meant as a proposal?”  

“Nah, it just slipped out. The real one will be better thought out.”  

“I see… alright!”

Rir’s ears stood up straight and her tail under the dress went wild.  

_Does that mean she’s happy? I hope it does._

“We should be going, Shuu,” she commented after glancing at the clock.

She then hugged my arm with a radiant smile.

+++++

“H-How does it look?”

Sakura was showing to Kanata how she looked in her dress.

“It suits you well.”  

“I… I guess.”

The two kids were each wearing the dress and tuxedo Alim had prepared for them.

“How many years has it been since we were at a wedding?”  

“Hm~, I only remember one when we were in pre-school and some mutual acquaintances had theirs. I think that was the only one.”

Kanata’s memory was accurate in that regard. Pondering for a few seconds if there had been any other weddings, Sakura came the conclusion that the boy was correct.

“Might be… Weddings, huh. Big Sis and Ayu-nii will probably be the first among the three couples living here to tie the knot, right?”  

“I’m not so sure… If the two of us wanted, we could get married in this world in two years.”

Sakura only shrugged at Kanata’s comment.

“Let’s not get married this early, alright? There should be time to get our feeling in order.”  

“Ah-ha-ha-ha, I guess so.”

Likely since they both thought the same, they laughed in agreement. Neither of them had realized that, in their minds, their future wedding was already an unchangeable fact.

“Leaving that aside, this wedding is between SSS-Rankers of this country, isn’t it?” she asked.  

“It is. It’s the first ever wedding between two of them.”  

“Huh…”

While changing the topic somewhat, they did their remaining preparations.

“Alright, shall we be off?”  

“Don’t we still have a lot of time left?”  

“It feels as if it would be better in several way if we leave now. SSS-Rankers probably have tons of acquaintances, so we should get there before there’s a huge crowd. I also want to take my time to look at Big Bro’s handiwork.”  

“If that’s what you think, then let’s do so.”

Fully prepared, the two kids left the mansion and made their way to the venue.

“…Wow. So many people. It’s good that we came here early as you said, Kanata.”

Sakura seemed shocked by the throng of people surrounding the venue.

“Well, the ones out here probably won’t go into the church… We are on the guest list, so no need to worry.”  

“Yeah, you probably enter at the counter over there.”

The kids pushed through the crowed and entered the church after settling things at the counter.

+++

# 539 – Just Before the Ceremony

“You should get ready, it’s about time for you to go out there!” I told the two occupants, as I rushed into the waiting room.  

“I see… it’s already this late, is it?”  

“For some reason, my heart won’t stop racing.”

It felt like this was the first time I saw those two nervous. Normally, the bride and groom would meet their families during the preparation time, but neither of them had any relatives left, so that part was omitted.

“What were you talking about earlier?”  

“Stories from our past.”  

“Exactly, like what I always loved about Parasuna…”  

“Hang on… Uruto…”

_I see, so they had more than enough time to flirt and make out. Precisely how two people about to be married should be._

“But the truth is, the two of us have worked so hard for so long… this wedding feels like a ‘we finally made it’ moment.”  

“He’s right.”

I only heard pieces about how their romance started. I knew they went through hardship and Bacchus told me that Parasuna was originally Uruto’s slave, and that she was the reason he went and erased the concept of slavery from this country.

“A lot of it is thanks to you, Alim,” Uruto said.  

“Precisely. You brought us back to life, and now you keep the public busy, so we can take a break.”

True enough, little old me[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-539-just-before-the-ceremony/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-110070) went and took their jobs… but from their perspective, this was apparently a good thing. In exchange, I got busy… though I did manage to schedule things well, so it wasn’t a huge issue.

“That’s the reason you had a large influence on us getting to the point of marriage.”

Hearing that felt a bit awkward. Mika and me starting our relationship was also thanks to someone else – Lord Jizou in our case – so that was probably a commonality we had.

_This should be a good time to ask about their proposal._

“Which of you did propose again?”  

“It was me,” Uruto replied.  

“Heh-heh… how did you do it?”

Uruto and Parasuna looked at each other bashfully. It felt as if her red eyes turned even redder.

“We were on a date. And at the end of it, when we had dinner in the city’s highest-class restaurant, I proposed to her.”  

“That day was also the anniversary of when we first met. On that very day, more than 10 years ago, I arrived at Uruto’s home[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-539-just-before-the-ceremony/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-110070).”

_Huh, so he proposed on an anniversary? I might do that too when I pop the question with Mika. I guess in this world, this would the day we reunited, and on Earth, the one we returned._

“The two of you went on a date? Somehow, I can’t imagine that,” I said honestly.

Truthfully, it was hard for me to picture a scene with them flirting. It was generally difficult to imagine the daily lives of celebrities.

“Why, just so you know it, we were quite lovey-dovey on the day he proposed. We watched a play, and while we did that, he kept petting my head… and we kissed during the kiss scene. Doing the latter was a huge fad at the time.”  

“Hang on… Parasuna…”

Caressing someone’s head for a long time and kissing while watching a play did sound like what Mika and I did. I only heard that from Shuu, but Rir apparently also liked it when he patted her head. Maybe being fond of having one’s head caressed by the one you cared about, was a common trait among beastfolk.

_Hang on, Mika is human. I should try it with Rose the next time she visits._

“That sounds nice…”  

“Doesn’t it? And once we were back home, after dispelling the illusion so my real ears were back, he-” Parasuna continued excitedly.  

“L-Let’s leave it at that, alright…?” Uruto stopped her, while scratching his cheek in apparent embarrassment.

I was curious what he did with her ears, but he likely just gently caressed them like Shuu did with Rir’s, so I didn’t pursue it further.

“…As Uruto said, let’s leave it at that.”  

“Phew.”  

“Stop worrying, it’s not like I told her how we took a bath together.”  

“Whaaaaaaaaaaa-!?”

This time, Uruto’s face turned red.

_Taking a bath together… do all couples do that? Kanata and Sakura probably haven’t gone that far yet. And Ruin and his friends neither._

“You’re cute in that regard, Uruto.”  

“He sure is.”  

“Hah…”

It was funny how timidly they acted when their secrets were exposed. I was sure they went further… though I kept that part to myself.

“In any case, Uruto and I do plenty of flirting.”  

“Ha-ha-ha… yes, we do. That’s how it is.”

It was a bit cringy to see a couple act this intimate, but it did put a smile on my face, so I had no complaints.

_Oh… we’re genuinely running out of time now._

“It is time now, so I’ll return to the hall.”  

“You’re right. Thank you for everything.”  

“It’s your big moment! Make it memorable!”  

“Yes!”

I left the room. The moment I did, I spied the two sharing a tight embrace. They looked truly happy.

_Now… I’ll need to give it my all, too. Well, to be honest, everything is ready, so I shouldn’t have much to do._

#### Footnotes:

1. In the original Alim uses the フシ personal pronoun, which is normally used by old people. This might be intentional or an error, it’s always so hard to tell with the author. Here, I translated it as if it was intentional.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-539-just-before-the-ceremony/#easy-footnote-1-110070)

2. So, they were 12 or younger when they met, and she was already slave back then. Talk about dark…

+++

# 540 – The Ceremony – 1

“Phew… finally made it here.”  

“You had it tough.”

I managed to dodge the waves of nobles and ultra-high rank adventurers, all while keeping a smile on my face. Though it was nice how everyone commented how cute I looked when they saw me.

At this point, most eyes seemed to be glued to the decorations or Mika and me… which came as a bit of a surprise. Queen Karuna used to act as something like an idol before our time, then there was Sakura… and there were also some nobles from other countries present, who were said to be beautiful.

“You probably also had a hard time with all the greetings, Mika.”  

“Yeah, a bit.”

She boasted indescribable beauty, so it was unavoidable. Her dress was also rather lovely.

“Come to think of it, when will the food be served?”  

“Before the wedding celebration. After the vows and the kiss, but before the performances start.”  

“I see.”

At a normal wedding, the bride and groom wouldn’t have time to enjoy the food in peace. Therefore, I installed a device that sped up time[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-540-the-ceremony-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-110073) just in an area centered around them while they were eating.

“Oh, it’s time,” muttered Shuu, who’d arrived close to us unnoticed.

As if arranged in advance, all the people who were chatting, striking deals, or even pursuing their occupations here, fell silent and turned their attention to the altar. Archbishop Chris was already standing there.

A sacred atmosphere started to fill the venue. Well, I had tinkered a bit with things in advance.

“Today, I welcome all of you who’ve come from all over the world-” the archbishop started to greet the attendees.  

“-Thus, may the groom enter.” After talking for a few minutes, which included giving a few short words of thanks to the gods, Chris first called Uruto.

Two church sisters opened the large door. The next moment, Uruto, looking dapper wearing the tuxedo in his Lastman appearance, walked down the wedding aisle[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-540-the-ceremony-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-110073). His friend Bacchus served as best man.

At this point, I had added a few things to the arrangement.

First, the music… Normally, an orchestra would play, but I did away with that and instead let background music play. I had changed it under the assumption that a live performance of an orchestra would capture too much of the audience’s attention. Well, the fact that many people started to wonder where the music was coming from turned out to be a flaw in my plan, but they ultimately did turn their gazes on the groom.

Next, the lighting was dimmed, with only Uruto and Bacchus being illuminated, so they’d stand out. That said, it wasn’t like a spotlight, instead it created a mysterious effect, as if natural light somehow concentrated there. It turned out pretty good.

The two of them came to a halt in front of Chris.

“Next, may the bride enter.”

At these words, the natural-seeming spotlight hit Parasuna, who’d been waiting on stand-by. The role of her father… was played by Gilmars, to everyone’s surprise. I mean, I knew about it, and I even I couldn’t help being startled. They linked arms and walked down the aisle. With Gilmars’ nature, he’d normally break into a grin when he was this close to a woman, but this time, his expression stayed serious… or rather, soft.

The rabbit ears weren’t yet visible on Parasuna’s head. That would come later. It wouldn’t be long until both Uruto and Parasuna revealed their true identities.

The main actors were now all gathered in front of the archbishop.

Uruto gave Gilmars a bow, which the latter returned. With this, the handover of the bride by the (stand-in in of the) father to the groom was complete.

“Let us sing.”

At Chris’ words, everyone stood up. The people of this world all knew the sacred hymns, so no song lyrics had been distributed. I had provided our four housemates with them before they came to the venue.

To be honest, I also never sang sacred songs. In the first place, I never came in contact with the religious customs of this world (though it seemed they were fundamentally similar to those on Earth), so I didn’t know much about them. I still sang the songs.

“Let us pray-”

After the song was over, everyone sat down in unison without any word or signal, as if it had been arranged in advance. The fact that their actions were so aligned despite the absence of practice or anything, spoke of how uniform religion was in this world. I ended up feeling embarrassed since I was a beat late.

The archbishop opened the holy scriptures started to read prayers. It was apparently customary to read parts of the scriptures. Just as I had done in my former world during funerals and weddings, I let the words pass from one ear to the other[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-540-the-ceremony-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-110073).

Now, now now now, there finally came the part of the bride and groom’s vows. The part, where the two of them planned to reveal their true identities. Usually the main event of a wedding, and from the couple’s perspective, the most important part shaping their futures.

Uruto and Parasuna looked resolved… and they further seemed excited about their future life together.

#### Footnotes:

1. Slowed down, in the original, which would give them even less time to enjoy the food.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-540-the-ceremony-1/#easy-footnote-1-110073)

2. Can I just say how hilarious it is that Japan’s wasei word for “wedding aisle” is “virgin road”?[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-540-the-ceremony-1/#easy-footnote-2-110073)

3. I don’t think I ever related this much to Alim before.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-540-the-ceremony-1/#easy-footnote-3-110073)

+++

# 541 – The Ceremony – 2

A moment later, the archbishop finally spoke. Honestly, the pause was chosen well. Or rather, perfectly.

“-Then… Uruto Lastman, do you vow to take Parasuna Nervan as your wife, in sickness and in health, until death do you part[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-541-the-ceremony-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-110076)?”

_Finally, that’s the moment. Come on…!_

“YES… Yes, I vow!”

With these words, Uruto turned back from his Lastman appearance to looking like a pleasant young man. Those who already knew his secret gazed at him with expressions of satisfaction.

On the other hand, those who came from other countries, those unfamiliar with Uruto, or those who were invited on the virtue of being nobles, seemed shocked and grew uproarious. They unreservedly voiced their thoughts, which included things like “I always thought he was magic beast that had somehow turned human”, “Who is this handsome hunk?”, and “If this is who was in the Lastman costume, it was worth the wait”.

_Well, looks like Mr. Uruto’s debut went well. Miss Parasuna will be the problem. Since she’s originally from a country where slavery still hasn’t been abolished._  

_How will it go?_

“-Parasuna Nervan, do you vow to take Uruto Lastman as your husband, in sickness and in health, until death do you part?”  

“I vow.”

This wasn’t the moment where she would reveal her true identity. At this point, she likely enraptured everyone at the venue with her own charm and her wedding dress, boasting of a beauty that would cause anyone to fall silent. So much, that it even stopped Mika from whispering her impressions of the dress to me.

The audience turned even quieter at her words “I vow.”

“You may now exchange the ring,” Chris’ voice echoed through the silence.

Parasuna entrusted the gloves she was wearing and bouquet she’d been holding to Gilmars. After confirming that, the archbishop handed the ring to Uruto.

The bride and groom gazed at each other. Just what had happened to them in the past? I only heard about it in broad strokes and didn’t know the details.

What were they thinking, as they stood here, and what hardships had they overcome to finally tie the knot? How did they encourage each other in painful times, harsh time… sad times, and happy times? No one but them knew that weight and reality.

It felt like some time had passed. As Parasuna smiled through her veil with red, melancholic eyes, Uruto smiled back and took her left hand. He gently put the ring on it.

Either because of my arrangement or since the bride and groom exuded an air of repeated struggles, an atmosphere of what could only be called indescribable affection filled the venue.

“You may now seal your vows with a kiss.”

It was finally time for the kiss. On that note, no directions other than making it look mystical to draw the guest’s attention had been given for this part[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-541-the-ceremony-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-110076). Still, the two of them looked beautiful.

_Weddings are nice… that’s what I’ve come to think after setting one up myself._

“Yep.”  

“Let’s do it.”

They nodded at each other, seemingly having resolved themselves, and Uruto lifted Parasuna’s veil.

That moment, her body transformed. White ears, typical of a rabbitkin, appeared on her head and a slight protrusion on her behind could be seen, indicating a round tail.

To this, anyone in the venue, other than those already in the know, reacted with bafflement. It was on an entirely different level than during Uruto’s reveal.

“(…I love you.)”  

“(…I love you, too.)”

After muttering in small voices what could only be heard by a scant few people… the bride and groom’s lips met. Although it wasn’t intended to be a passionate and long kiss, it lasted for several minutes and looked sensuous and deep.

When he saw that they had finished, Chris clasped his hands in prayer.

“Gods, grant the birth of a new married couple-”

After muttering a few words in addition to that, he handed the couple a sheet of paper and an expensive looking pen. It was the marriage certificate. The bride and groom signed it without any hesitation.

“Let us sing.”

After receiving a lock of hair of the bride and groom, the archbishop raised his voice loudly. The guests, who’d been caught up in the atmosphere, staggered to their feet, as if they had just woken up.

I didn’t know whether it was due to the surprise concerning Parasuna’s true identity, or due to being enchanted by her dress, but everyone seemed emotionally drained. This was probably my fault.

Still, the song ended without incident like earlier. I had no idea what the words were, but I still did my best to sing. I had to give credit where it was due.

“The bride and groom may now leave the venue.”

At the archbishop’s words, Parasuna slightly skipped and linked arms with Uruto.

That moment, a single person started to clap. The one who did… was the king. As he broke the silence and clapped sincerely, others around him joined in… until it turned into a big applause with not a single person keeping still.

Amidst that, the bride and groom happily made their way down the wedding aisle and left the hall.

#### Footnotes:

1. In the original, the last part is “support each other for the rest of your life”. Since almost everything here seems to be based on a Christian wedding, I decided to go with the more traditional ending.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-541-the-ceremony-2/#easy-footnote-1-110076)

2. One word in this sentence, the さつまき in the ちなみにさつまきから神秘的に見せる part doesn’t seem to make sense. さつま is either a former province or a sweet potato, so I can only assume this is a typo of some sort. While I did find something rather close in たつまき (竜巻), this means “whirlwind” and doesn’t make any more sense.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-541-the-ceremony-2/#easy-footnote-2-110076)

+++

# Side Story 16 – The Wolf’s Gratitude

A long time ago, there lived a man, boasting both strength and good looks. His name was Shuu, and he was a gentle soul, unable to ignore those in need, and powerful enough to defeat barehandedly even a hundred armed warriors or samurais, if saving the one he wanted to save required it.

One day, when he entered the forest to create a strengthening serum (protein extract) from nature’s bounty, he encountered a wolf. Its white fur held an enchanting beauty.

“Woah!?”

Assuming it would attack him, the man immediately took a fighting stance, but the animal showed no hint of doing so. On the contrary, it didn’t seem to possess the energy to move.

“What’s wrong?”

When he looked at the wolf’s feet, he saw that its leg was caught in a foothold trap, which must’ve been set up by someone hunting tanuki or rabbits. Looking closer, he realized that its body was covered in wounds. In addition, one of its ears was missing.

“Woah, seriously…? Guess it can’t be helped.”

Shuu, mentally reasoning that the wolf was neither rabbit nor tanuki, so whoever set the trap wouldn’t mind, released the animal.

The wolf stared at the man’s face.

“What now? You hungry? Do your wounds hurt? For now, eat this.”

The man took some rabbit jerky from his pocket and held it out to the wolf. The animal’s nose moved, carefully sniffing the treat, before giving it a lick and finally nibbling on a small piece.

“…You like it?”

After staring at the man’s face for some time again, the animal devoured the rest of the meat.

“Gotcha, guess you were hungry… What ’bout your wounds?”

This might come as no surprise, but the wolf didn’t reply.

“Well, with all those injuries, I better carry you-”

Shuu was about to simply pick up the animal, when it nimbly licked his face. A moment later, it quickly stepped back, as if planning to flee.

“Wha-…? You fine already? If that was enough to bring you back to speed, guess you’ll manage…”

・・・

“I should go to sleep.”

Shuu was about to sink into his futon, when there was a knock on the door.

“Comin’, who is it?”

He opened the door. On the other side stood a woman wearing a bamboo hat, who seemed to be his age.

“Woof… U-Uhm… I got lost in the streets, so might I stay the night here, Sir…?”  

“‘Course, that’s fine! Come on in.”  

“Thank you! Thank you so much!”

She beamed in joy as she stepped into Shuu’s house.

“Did you eat already? I can make somethin’.”  

“I-I couldn’t impose on you! I will be-”

A growl came from the woman’s stomach.

“Ha-ha-ha, it’ll take just a moment.”  

“My apologies…”

Shortly later, Shuu brought her a simple meal. She ate it as if it was a genuine delicacy.

“It’s… good…”  

“I see, glad to hear that.”  

“Thank you so much…!” The woman prostrated herself on the floor.  

“Oy, no need for that. It was no big thing.”  

“I-I was just so overjoyed…”  

“Oh, well. For now, let’s go to sleep. Say, what’s your name?”  

“I… I am called Rir, Sir.”  

“Rir, huh? You look my age so… you talkin’ all polite feels weird. Anyway, good night.”  

“Understood… I wish you a good night.”

・・・

When the man woke up the next morning, Rir was gone.

“Left already, huh?”

“I’m back…!”

That moment, the door opened. The woman had returned. In her hand, she was clutching a pheasant’s wing.

“Woah!? What’s with that?”  

“This is… as thanks…”  

“There was no need to go that far…!”  

“Woof, I caught it with my own hands. This is what I am good at,” Rir proudly declared as she puffed her chest out proudly.  

“Guess it’s fine then, but… what’s with those wounds?” Shuu asked, trying to tear his eyes from her breasts.  

“I… I had those before…”  

“You gotta take it easy.”

Shuu patted her head. Surprised by his own boldness, he hurriedly pulled his hand back.”

“S-Sorry.”  

“I don’t mind… say, I have a favor to ask for. Might I stay here for a bit longer?”  

“S-Sure thing.”  

“Alright… In that case, I should properly show you my gratitude. My apologies, but could you close your eyes? Whatever happens, don’t open them.”  

“Huh?”

For now, he did what she said and closed his eyes. When he did, he could hear the rustling of fabric and not a moment later, he could feel her breath from close. She suddenly took his right hand and brought it somewhere. In the palm of his hand, there was a soft sensation.

That moment, Shuu, having realized what was going on, hurriedly pulled his hand back. Then, he impulsively opened his eyes.

“Y-You, what are you thinkin’!?”

In front of him, the woman from earlier was no more. From her head, a doglike ear was growing, there was a tail on her behind, her upper body was bare, and her cheeks were tinged red.

“Woof, I told you not to look…”  

“I mean, sorry ’bout that, but what were you doin’ just now…?”  

“I-I was showing you my gratitude…”

She was scratching her cheek bashfully.

“Also, what’s with that tail and your ears?”  

“Huh… ah!?”  

“Besides, that missin’ ear… no way, are you that wolf from back then!?”

When he pointed this out, her eyes went round like those of a startled dog, and they started to tear up.

“I am sorry… so sorry! I-I… that was the first time someone showed such kindness to me… I-If only it had ended then, but for whatever reason, I turned human afterwards… so… uhm, I used my nose to find your home… and…!”  

“Calm down and tell me what happened,” Shuu encouraged her to tell her story, as he gently rubbed her back.  

“I don’t understand it myself! Both why I found myself in human shape and my feelings towards you…! I am a monster, so I can’t be with you…!”  

“I don’t mind that, y’know.”  

“Huh?”  

“I mean, I don’t get it either, but… it might just be fate.”

Afterwards, there were rumors of the man having taken someone in marriage.

---

**TL notes:**  

The Author ran out of material. Again.
