# 542 – Wedding Meal

“We will now take a break to eat before we move on to the celebration.”

Archbishop Chris, who acted as host, chose the perfect moment for the break.

Speaking of hosts, the man who acted as commentator back when I participated in the fighting tournament (and who later became part of the upper echelon of my fan-club) was also present at the venue, but it looked like he was invited as a normal guest and wouldn’t act as commentator. Though he’d apparently do a performance during the celebration later.

“For that, I’d ask you all to please stay seated where you are. We will now serve the first course… cooked by Alim Nariwei.”

The moment my name was mentioned, the guests grew noisy. The atmosphere came to a boil.

“Squee~!”  

“No way~~!”  

“Alim’s home cooking!!”  

“Woo-hoo~!!”

Even those who looked calm and collected were caught up in the mood.  

_Hah… to excite people to such an extent… what a bad girl I am. Heh-heh._

“The bride and groom will also come back when the food is served, so please use this time to pay them your regards,” Chris announced amidst the uproar that still hadn’t abated.

To think people were this excited about my cooking… even those who had never tasted it. It being made by me was probably enough for them.  

_Just you wait, it’s so tasty, it will make your jaws drop!_

Shortly later, Uruto and Parasuna, who now both shared the family name “Lastman” entered arm in arm.  

_Hang on, wouldn’t it be Lastwoman for her…? Well, that doesn’t matter now._

She had taken off her gloves and the parts of the dress that might get in the way while eating, and seemed ready to devour the food.

Once both of them were seated, the doors to the venue opened and a great number of church sisters hauled in carts with appetizers for everyone. On that note, hidden among these women, there were several androids created by me. There weren’t enough people for the number of guests, so it had to be done.

“Ahem, I’d like to thank give my deepest gratitude to everyone for attending our wedding today.”

Uruto started speaking. Incidentally, he would only use this overly formal style of speaking at the start. That was at my instruction.

“At our chef’s behest, I will cut this part short without spending too much time on flowery words and merely tell you to enjoy the food. Let us eat.”

Normally, you’d expect someone to complain that tradition should be followed, but there were no objections to Uruto’s suggestion, as everyone’s attention seemed glued to the food.

“You have the word, Archbishop…”  

“Indeed. Let us give thanks to the gods for the meal in which we are to partake.”

Thus, the lunch consisting of several courses I cooked was distributed to everyone.  

_I think we gave it some fancy name on the menu, but I can’t remember it. Not like it matters as long as it gets eaten. Almost everything was made from ingredients I had on hand._

Everyone, including those from other countries, took the same prayer pose, said grace, and then elegantly speared their appetizers with their forks. They brought it to their mouths.

“Yeah, today’s meal is so good, it melts on the tongue. As usual.”  

“Eh-heh-heh, thank you for saying that.”

Mika ate my cooking every day, so her reaction wasn’t that different. But what about the others?

“Oh my…”  

“Wa-wa-wa…”  

“Delicious! Truly delicious! I have never eaten anything this good!”  

“I though I already experienced all the luxuries this world has to offer, but… this… this is heavenly.”

_Woo-hoo! Rave reviews! Both nobles and foreign royalty are being awed and enchanted by the food._

_Then, how are the reactions of people who weren’t born in the lap of luxury? Let’s take Mr. Lahand and his friends as an example…_

“…”  

“…”  

“Amazin’, Alim… this stuff’s crazy!”

While Lahand managed to hold on to his sanity, both Margo and Gog seemed completely out of it. From an outside perspective, the food might look like a dangerous drug, but it absolutely wasn’t. On that note, it seemed the dishes I made had an addictive effect to them, causing people to become unable to stop eating them and developing a craving.

_Quite dangerous._

So, I put in some measures to get rid of that effect. Now you could eat them without worry.

Everyone had wolfed down the appetizers. The soup, which was brought in next, also disappeared instantly, same for the beverages… the fish dish was also gone within seconds. We hadn’t even reached the main course yet, and everyone was fully focused on eating. It made me glad[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-542-wedding-meal/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-111196).

Then came the main dish. It was dragon steak (though not Golden Rose Queen Dragon). The moment it was carried in, several people looked as if they might faint, just from the smell. The church sisters now mostly relied on the androids. It had become impossible for them to work normally.

Someone started and ate a bite of the steak… It looked as if their consciousness was blown away. Well, they snapped out of it almost immediately. I didn’t anticipate it being enrapturing enough so they wouldn’t be able to eat the other dishes, but if it turned out that way, I could only apologize.

#### Footnotes:

1. I guess all his research failed to teach him that eating in such a setting is also about socializing.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-542-wedding-meal/#easy-footnote-1-111196)

+++

# 543 – The Celebration – 1

All the food had been served. This might be coming from me, but I thought it turned out quite tasty. The majority of guests had lost all their energy.

When I looked at the clock, it was the planned time. Time to start the celebration.

Chris stood up.

“Did you enjoy the lunch prepared by our nation’s hero, Alim Nariwei? Now the time has come for the bride and groom and all the guests to move on to the wedding celebration.”

Almost everyone clapped. At the celebration, there would be various performances and the wedding cake I had made would be cut. Oh, I made it in a way so it wouldn’t spoil, so that wasn’t the main reason to move to that part on time.

Then, at 3 pm, the bride and groom would start driving around the city in a carriage. In Japan, people in high places and celebrities would drive around in a car with tin cans tied to it When they did that, the two of them would apparently make their true identities known to everyone. In that regard, this wedding had a deeper meaning than just two people getting married.

“We’ll start by cutting the cake.”

With those words, the cake I had made was wheeled out. There were Ohs and Ahs from various places in the crowd. I had paid a lot of attention to its appearance (and its taste obviously, too).

“The one who both designed and made the cake is Alim Nariwei.”  

“”Oh~~!””

Chris kept bringing up my name, even though I never asked him to do that. Though it was possible the king asked him for it, to spread information about the creations I – the nation’s hero – made.

“Then, will the Bride and Groom cut the cake?”

Uruto and Parasuna received a large knife specifically to cut cakes from a church sister (a real one). It was a little funny to see both of them support the knife together, which should weight barely anything from their point of view. Well, it was part of the ceremony.

The blade hit the cake’s peak. Now, they only had to press it down.  

_Right, I should take a picture. That way, there’ll be something to remember it by._

The two of them stared at the wedding cake, as if to bore holes into it. You had to properly judge where exactly to cut it. After a minute or two, they looked at each other, nodded, and then put force into the knife. The cake was split in two.

“Now, for the first bite.”

The so-called first bite would be shared between the bride and groom before the cake was served to the other guests.

Using a fork that had been provided along with the cake knife, Parasuna scooped up a bite-sized portion close to where the initial cut had been made. She brought it to the mouth of her husband. The cake disappeared in Uruto’s mouth.

Just as she had done for him, he then also brough a bite of cake to her mouth, feeding it to her.

_How heartwarming. Feeding each other is nice. It might look different from an outside perspective, but it has a different meaning if it is with someone you love. I would know._

“…This cake will later be served to everyone together with Dionysus Wine. Next, we shall move on to the performances.”

Many guests looked pleased at the prospect of wine and cake being served. Most of them were on the level of royals, so you’d expect them to take offense at eating someone else’s leftovers, but… maybe it was because I made it.

In any case, I was curious about the performances. I knew that mine was the last, excluding the trip around the city, but I had no idea what others had been planned.

“We shall be first,” King Rama announced, as he stood up together with his guard Hanuman and several retainers.

Among them were likely also top-rank adventurers from his country. The group from the Bufura Kingdom climbed onto a separate stage than the one the bride and groom were sitting on.

“Now, for what We have planned; it shall be an ardent dance, for which Our country is known. We are thinking of having everyone in this group, including Us, partake.”

I had never heard of these famous dances But it looked like our group of people from Earth were the only ones who hadn’t.

The king’s announcement of participating himself had the venue quite excited.

Although two of them were SSS-Rankers[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-543-the-celebration-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-111198), who were so much stronger than the former commoners they had started out as, which showed just how high the status of SSS-Rankers was in this world. Mephilad’s king was also a former SSS-Ranker and the two from Yggdrasil were likely also entrusted with some of the country’s affairs.

“Start the music!”

At those words, two of King Rama’s followers brought out instruments; one used a wind instrument, and the other drums. Bodies started to move. Everyone on the stage, other than the musicians, started to dance nimbly.

It wasn’t anything like a flamenco[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-543-the-celebration-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-111198), ballet, or a dance fitting a pop song. This was… right, it reminded me of a dance I’d seen in an Indian movie I watched on a streaming site.  

_Exactly, an Indian dance._

It turned out to be quite the spectacle and I ended up enjoying it a lot.

#### Footnotes:

1. The original just talks about two SSS-Rankers, it’s unclear who they are. I assume he means they’re part of King Rama’s group, but it’s rather ambivalent.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-543-the-celebration-1/#easy-footnote-1-111198)

2. The original is フラメンゴ (flamengo). I assume this is a typo and the author meant flamenco, a Spanish art genre including dances.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-543-the-celebration-1/#easy-footnote-2-111198)

+++

# 544 – The Celebration – 2

There was thundering applause.

We had been treated to five minutes of intense, passionate dancing. Though I was concerned about the glances King Rama kept shooting me during the dance. Honestly, the dancing itself was just as good as I remembered from that Indian film. It made me excited to see more performances on this level later.

Well, not all of them would be this good, but that was a result of most of the other nations showing performances being less developed or wealthy than the one hosting the event.

“Next will be a display from —. You have the stage.”

It was the turn of a country that didn’t have much influence.  

_Was someone from there at my hero proclamation? Not sure, I can’t seem to remember._

The performance of this small country was called “Teleporting without using skills”. It looked like teleportation skills were super rare, and it was probably an incredible feat to manage it without utilizing those, but… in essence, it was just a magic trick. Moreover, it was a rather clichéd one. The venue seemed excited about it, but it wasn’t that enjoyable for us earthlings.

The performance of the next country was about drawings, demonstrating a realistic depiction of the bride and groom. It was both fast and good enough to meet the standards of everyone, including the couple and the king, who knew that my skills were better. The one who drew the picture was apparently that country’s king, and he likely had a title like the master chef at Mephilad castle, which gave a boost to his skills.

_What I can do is still better, though. Heh-heh!_

“Next will be Mr. Heimdal, an SSS-Ranker from Yggdrasil, the country of the holy tree.”

It was the old man who helped Kanata and the others and visited our house the other day. He had a white beard and was carrying a hunting horn[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-544-the-celebration-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-111606).

_Let me think, I’m pretty sure his specialty is summoning magic._  

Different from King Mephilad, who could call one or two overwhelmingly powerful beings, this man could apparently summon tens of thousands somewhat strong minions.

“In that case, Sir Chris, could you do the honors?”  

“Of course.”

Heimdal had asked Chris for something. The archbishop took a device from his pocket that I recognized.

When I went over the venue over the course of my preparations, I was commissioned by the country to enlarge the stage, so it could be used for big performances. From how it sounded, they wanted to keep using it for large events even after the wedding was over. It now had the option to widen considerably on the press of a button.

This switch was now pushed.

“Ho-ho… Alim Nariwei is no ordinary person, after all,” Heimdal muttered, as he ascended to the stage.

“Then… let me show you the true power of the One-Man Army!” he announced when it had opened fully, and countless magic circles appeared behind him on the stage. There were so many, it felt like an exercise in futility to even try to count them.

“Come out, my underlings!” he shouted in a loud, dignified voice, before blowing his horn.

The sound echoed through the venue, seemingly resonating in the spectators’ very souls. Likely serving as the key to activate his invocations, I could see all the magic circles lighting up and something being summoned.

They were humanoid, somewhere between dolls and warriors. Their numbers seemed endless.

“An army needs the be united, doesn’t it? Take a good look.”

There was a bang, as the humanoid beings slammed the butts of their spears on the stage. A controlled movement that happened momentarily.

They started performing actions that could only be described as befitting an army. I was an SSS-Ranker too, so I could tell. Moving countless humanoid summons by yourself in such a precise manner was an incredibly difficult feat. Calling it amazing would be an understatement.

_…I mean, I could probably do it if I tried, but it would take a ton of practice, or I’d have to use some kind of AI created by Item Master to make it look as if I was the one controlling them._

Put in Earth terms, it was like a group of countless people performing coordinated gymnastics. And any free moment was used congratulate the bride and groom.

_This old man is strong._

Relying on few but supremely powerful individuals… I had always been an adherent of that creed, so this display came as a bit of a shock. With such leadership over this many fighters, he could likely fell even SSS-Rank magic beasts. Though he’d probably struggle against an evil god.

A short time later, the gymnastics performance came to a close. At the end, Heimdal delivered a light bow.  

I clapped a lot.

“Then, next will be-”

To be blunt, none of the performances afterwards topped what Heimdal had shown us. Some among them were disappointing, and I ended up spending my time by looking at the decorations. Still… people certainly had fun.

“Finally, it is time for Alim Nariwei’s performance!”

It was my turn at last. I was worried that there hadn’t been any other performances from the Mephilad Kingdom thus far[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-544-the-celebration-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-111606), but it was possible they wanted my part to represent the country.

_In that case, I have to give it my all!_

I climbed onto the stage.

#### Footnotes:

1. This is a bit weird in the original; 白いひげの角笛ホルン (“hunting horn of white beard”) makes it sound as if the horn itself is bearded. I could imagine it having a small white part at the bottom, making it look as if it had a beard.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-544-the-celebration-2/#easy-footnote-1-111606)

2. I guess the author forgot about that commentator from the fighting tournament doing a performance.

+++

# 545 – The Celebration – 3

“It is my turn, then, to congratulate our couple, Uruto Lastman and Parasuna Nervan… I mean, Parasuna Lastman!”

I activated the innocent-little-girl mode I had cultivated ever since coming to this world. While lightly putting my index finger to my cheek and winking, I stumbled slightly forward… quickly stabilizing myself on one leg. Kanata seemed to regard me with cold looks, but I didn’t let that bother me. Incidentally, getting Parasuna’s family name wrong was on purpose.

The two of them, especially her, smiled awkwardly.

“Oh~!”  

“You’re so cute~, Alim!!”  

“Just seeing you is enough!”  

“Marry me!”

I could hear such comments from the nobles and adventurers, who seemed to be the type to get rambunctious at celebrations. Waving at the audience like an idol, I crossed my index fingers in front my face and cutely replied “No~” whenever I heard things like “Marry me!” or “Let me hug you!”.

This way, everyone would, once again, be captivated by me.

“It’s about to begin, so could I ask for some silence?”  

“””Yes~!”””

Just these words were enough to turn the venue quiet.  

_Hrm… I need to be more careful what I say in front of large crowds. Words have power. Though in this case, I probably just put everyone in the mood._

“Then…!”

_Time for the ace in my sleeve!_  

I had wracked my brain for a full month to come up with this performance. It was mostly for Uruto and Parasuna, but I hoped it would bring everyone joy.

I snapped my fingers. That moment, everything around the church – the venue – except for the floor, turned into particles. Normally, if the church’s walls and roof were gone, what you’d see outside was the city. But that wasn’t the case now.

“Bwuh!?”  

“Eh, wha-!?”

While the adventurers also seemed surprised, the reactions of the nobles, unused to combat, were more interesting. With the nothing separating the church from the outside, what could be seen was a whole new world… well, that would be an exaggeration. It was a plain, a simple field.

I felt bad for everyone’s bafflement, but I continued my performance. Forming a ring with my thumb and index finger, I put my lips against it and blew through it. With that as a trigger, countless fireworks rose over the plain.

You obviously couldn’t see any launch tubes. Those were unnecessary in this world ruled by skills.

“Incredible… ha-ha! This is amazing!” someone shouted in awe.

Innumerable fireworks rose into the blue sky in succession. Particles seemed to rise from the ground, enveloping (what used to be) the church, creating an even more fantastic atmosphere.

“This isn’t Illusion Magic?”  

“No, it doesn’t seem to be!”  

“Huh! You’re SSS-Rank, so it must be true.”

It sounded like one of the SSS-Rankers in attendance had verified that my performance wasn’t Illusion Magic. He probably stepped outside and touched one of the fireworks, finding that they caused damage. They were powerful enough to instantly kill a C-Rank magic beast.

“To think she’d change the whole environment for this performance…”  

“Just what kind of skill is that? Or did she use copious amounts of magic power, launching multiple spells in succession!?”

The investigation team was hard at work.

Spoiler: it was all Item Master. I used a device to move everyone to this fake church interior we were in right now. It was within a field-type magic room I had created Once we were in the magic room, I had free reign on what would happen. In other words, anything was possible.

“I-It’s turning to night!”

In that manner, I could also switch between day and night.

“L-Look! A meteor shower…!? I-Is that a meteorite!?”  

“It… it will crash…”  

“Please be assured, you are perfectly safe here,” I calmed them down, when the guests started to think they were in danger.

I was the one who created this space, so they would likely trust my words.

“Incredible… in addition to the countless fireworks, there’s now a meteor shower…!”  

“The moon also looks pretty!”  

“Amazing, so amazing!”

_Well, I’m glad people seem to enjoy it… I’ll end it in another two or so minutes._  

It would ramp up more and more.

“A… a dragon!”  

“No, look closely, it’s fireworks shaped like a dragon!”  

“It looks like it’s dancing… now there’s three of them!”

Now, I introduced fireworks that moved like living beings. It was about to end, so it grew more and more splendid. A bit like using CGI in movies.

“A swarm of fireworks shaped like bird monsters!?”  

“I’m lost… it’s too fantastical… too beautiful.”

_Alright, let’s end it here!_

I snapped my fingers again. That moment, the fireworks and magic beasts made of fireworks disappeared little by little, and the particles also sank back to the ground.

“…Is it over?” someone mumbled, when almost everything was gone.

The same moment, I blew through my fingers again. Then, large letters spelling “Congratulations on your marriage” appeared in the night sky.

“I wish you two all the best!” I said, as I gave Uruto and Parasuna a bow.

Then, particles surrounded the church, gradually restoring it. With this, my performance was over.

I raised my head to claps and cheers.

+++

# 546 – The End of the Celebration

_Heh-heh-heh, that was nice. It looks like my part was a huge success! Only I could pull off teleporting a whole church to a different location and giving a performance there!_  

_Well, Kanata might._

“That was Alim Nariwei. To close, some words of gratitude from the bride and groom.”

Since my performance was the last, this wrapped up the celebration in the church. Urged by the archbishop, Uruto and Parasuna rose.

“I want to take this chance to sincerely thank everyone who came here from near and far to bear witness to our wedding,” Uruto said, as he bowed his head quite deeply.

Any guests who stayed at his inn before knew that this was quite different from usual. You might attribute it to nervousness.

“In the same vein, we are profoundly grateful to the representatives from the many countries who came to congratulate us. While this was not our intention, we also received the honor of forming the ‘first marriage between two fellow SSS-Rankers in Anazumu'”.

I assumed that Mika and I would be the next such couple. Most likely. Almost certainly.

Uruto took the waiting megaphone with one hand and turned back into his Lastman outfit.

“I USUALLY… work in this appearance. Today, many of you likely saw how I look under the costume for the first time, and just as many learned here that Parasuna is a rabbitkin.”

As a matter of fact, I kept wondering whether there would be a representative of a country whose bearing would change completely once she revealed her true race. But that never happened.

On second thought, Lastman was known for being the foremost liberator of slaves. So, someone supporting slavery likely wouldn’t have shown their face at this wedding. In other words, almost everyone at the venue was at least somewhat considering how to do away with slavery.

“The reason I declared the liberation of all slaves two years ago… was entirely for Parasuna’s sake. Many think I did it out of righteousness, but it was all for her,” Uruto raised his voice as he spoke into the megaphone and continued talking about his past. “To deal with the former SSS-Rank adventurer turned slaver, Parasuna and I grew stronger side by side, until we reached SSS-Rank. Then, we gained the support of many and made our dearest wish a reality.”

Either since she reminisced too, as she stood next to him, or since she felt embarrassed by his story, Parasuna’s cheeks were tinged red. Indeed, it was the face of someone in love.

“And today, another of our wishes came true. This also was possible thanks to the support of many. I truly… sincerely thank you all.”

Uruto gave another deep bow. It wasn’t just on the physical side, you could feel his sincerity in your heart. He made it look as if he could deal with anything… In fact, he was an SSS-Ranker, managed an inn, and even shrugged off the skill of an evil god which killed anyone else… Such a man was he. And even he only managed to attain happiness through hardship and the support of many others.

It somehow felt as if I resonated with him. As for hardship… I couldn’t pretend there had been much, but I was the same in being supported by many.

“Finally… all the people who joined us here, everyone, I truly thank you!”  

“Thank you ever so much!”

The two of them… especially Uruto, thanked everyone for the umpteenth time. Applause rained down on them. It was probably thanks to who they were that people celebrated their marriage to this extent.

“May the two of you find perpetual happiness… The bride and groom shall now leave the venue. Afterwards, they will take part in a parade. A parade around Mephilad’s royal capital.

Together with the archbishop’s announcement, I started the background music I had prepared. Uruto, the groom, and Parasuna, the bride, linked arms and walked down the wedding aisle, showered by thundering applause.

_The last Parade was held by the Mephilad Kingdom. In the end, most of the things now were organized by me, not the country, which is kinda incredible, too._

When the couple was about to exit the venue, they stopped in front of the door to look back to the guests, bowing once more before leaving. The door to the church, which had served as the venue[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-546-the-end-of-the-celebration/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-111610), slowly closed.

“With this, the wedding and celebration have come to an end.”

This meant the ceremony was over. The next moment, all the guests stood up and got ready to head home… or rather, they probably got ready to watch the parade.

“What do you think?” I asked Mika.

Whether it was about the decorations or my performance, I’d be happy to hear her impressions.

“Hm? Yeah, I want to get married… those are my thoughts.”  

“Well, that wish will probably come true less than ten years from now.”

I also wanted to get married. And I obviously knew to whom. That would only be a question of time.

“Then, what did you think about the stuff I prepared here?”  

“It was wonderful! I also want to have a wedding like this… Oh, come on, won’t the parade start any moment? I heard they’ll throw the bouquet before they board the carriage, so we gotta get there fast!”  

“You’re right.”

Mika and I plus the other two couples from our household left the venue.

#### Footnotes:

1. I kept wondering if I had missed something or the author forgot to put on the transition from having the wedding in the church to the meal and celebration somewhere else, preferably outside with lots of room, but no. Apparently everything, even the performance where someone casually summoned tens of thousands of human-sized minions, happened in the church itself.

+++

# 547 – After the Wedding

“Miss Margo managed to catch the bouquet.”  

“She did. She might end up marrying Mr. Lahand.”

A few minutes before the parade with the bride and groom started, Parasuna had thrown the bouquet. All the preparations for said parade, with the streets cleared so the citizens and travelers could watch, were done well, seeing it had been performed in the name of the king.

On that note, Uruto was wearing his Lastman costume halfway on both his face and body, so people would recognize him. Parasuna wasn’t much different from usual, except for her rabbit ears and tail being on display.

“Still… it lost out to your performance, Alim. We were planning to use this to demonstrate the might of our country, but… both Item Master and your designs proved superior.”  

“Eh-heh-heh…! Thank you for your kind words, Your Majesty!”

I ended up receiving some words of praise from the king who had joined us unnoticed. I did work hard, so I was glad to hear that.

“This isn’t mere flattery. At this point, I absolutely want you to organize my son’s and his friends’ weddings,” he commented, while shooting a glance at the two couples some distance away.

He likely wanted them to tie the knot soon.

“Once that time comes, you can count on me.”

_Though when will that be? From how it looks, those four haven’t even kissed. Marriage and having kids are likely still far away. Worst case, Mika and I might have our ceremony first._

“Incidentally, I have something important to tell you… Let’s change location… is what I would like to say, but here should work fine. Only the two of us know about this. Just for the sake of caution, we should have our exchange via messages.”  

“Understood… Mika, please give us a moment.”  

“Alright.”

_What could be so important at this point?_

The king and I opened a message conversation just between the two of us.

[…It concerns Mephistophales.]　  

[Huh, him!?]　

It felt like it had been forever since I heard that name. Mephistophales, or Mr. Mitsuo Aijou.

He was a man originally from Earth like us, who brought the demon god Samaeyl back to life, to try to return there. It had apparently taken him hundreds of years, but ultimately his plan failed (largely due to me) and he was then rendered powerless and captured by this country. You could say that he was used by Samaeyl.

Furthermore, the reason that he was originally summoned to this world was seemingly for some deity’s amusement. He was a deeply tragic figure. Still, he did bring an evil god back to life, who then went after people dear to me like Mika and Karua… and Parasuna, from Uruto’s perspective. Except for Uruto and me, she killed everyone in and around the city. It was completely unforgivable.

By the way, Mephistophales had apparently been the leader of a circus troupe on Earth. Mika and I had been there before.

[What about him? Did he escape?]　  

[No, the restraints made by you are marvelous indeed. There was no hint of any escape attempt being made… What I am talking about, is that the time is near.]　  

[Uhm, what do you mean…?]　

At my reply, the king gave a grim look.

[You are strong, Alim. At this point, you are indispensable to this country, no, all of Anazumu. But you are still a young girl, the same age as Karua[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-547-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-113206). I am loath to paint a needlessly graphic picture, but that time I am talking about-]　

His message stopped at this point, and he mimed striking his neck with his hand.  

_Oh, so that’s what this is about._

They would finally execute him. It had been several months. Meaning, I could send him back to Earth at last.

[You will execute him?]　  

[Even though some went out of their way to speak up for him… it was unavoidable. Originally, I wouldn’t have informed you about it, but you are deeply connected to the affair, Alim.]　  

[Did you squeeze out all the information from him that you could?]　  

[Yes, we did. Thanks to your help…]　

Seeing he tried to keep this a secret even from me, it might be a good idea to sneak into the castle jail and take one of the man’s fingers while I still could. If they threw him into a volcano, reviving him afterwards would be a pain.

In any case, with Mephistophales’ fate being decided, what would happen to the former hero Herrell, who was also used by Samaeyl?

[I understand, Your Majesty. On that note, what about Mr. Herrell?]　  

[He might be the former hero, but his stats and skills are those of an active one. According to Tuhl, no new hero was found in this country since Herrell was alive. He needs to be placed under our supervision, so he will remain confined to this country. Normally, he’d be executed for treason, but he is the hero and hasn’t caused harm to anyone other than Gilmars.]　

So, Herrell would get to keep enjoying his life with Elle in the castle. Those two weren’t a great fit appearance-wise, but it was obvious how much in love they were.

“I will keep what you told me in mind, Your Majesty.”  

“Hrm. My apologies for staining this joyous celebration with such a ghastly topic… I shall count on your help in the future.”  

“Yes!”

The king showed a slight smile and then left Mika and me.

#### Footnotes:

1. Shouldn’t the king know Alim was older on Earth? Though maybe he argues that, with Anuzumu’s years being longer, their age is roughly the same.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-547-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-1-113206)

+++

# 548 – Two Days after the Wedding

Two days after the wedding, I was called to Uruto’s inn. Incidentally, it was currently closed.

It was because Lastman’s true identity had been disclosed. Quite a few curious people apparently came to the inn today and yesterday, but they all left after seeing the letters “temporarily closed for business”.

“We’re really grateful,” Uruto said.  

“We thank you from the bottom of our hearts, Alim,” Parasuna added.

The two of them were currently thanking me without pause. It seemed they were as happy as expected after the wedding succeeded that well.

“We didn’t think it would be this grand, you know,” Uruto said.  

“Well, I’m mostly glad you’re happy with the outcome.”

_True, I did work hard, so it’s nice that it was worth it. Anyway, you could say this was the first time I went all out since defeating the Black God Surtr._

“Then, here are the promised 55 million bells[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-113209). Please take them.”  

“Alright.”

They handed me a magic bag that was on the smaller side. There were no banks in this world[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-113209), so large transactions were done in this manner. Handing money over in person did feel more cordial than just transferring it from one account to the other.

For now, I checked the amount as formality dictated. It was exactly 55 million bells.

“I confirm the transfer.”  

“Well, I don’t think it makes up for that gift you gave us…” Uruto mumbled.

_But everyone would expect a gift from me to be legend grade at default._

“Exactly, the king and Gilmars also gave us a lot,” Parasuna agreed.  

“They gave us way too much…”

_Just what did those two gift them, so they’d mention it in the same vein with my legend grade article? They probably had more to go about, since they were around to personally see what happened two years ago._

“In any case, you two seem quite affectionate. Though I assume that’s normal on the third day of married life.”  

“Huh, you think so? It doesn’t feel any different.”  

“Right?”

_Nope, there definitely is something different._  

Parasuna was snuggled up to Uruto, nuzzling her ears against him, while he was stroking her. It was similar to what Mika and I did, but from an outside perspective, it did look sweet.

“I have one more thing for you two lovebirds.”  

“L-Lovebirds, you say… Didn’t you already give us a gift?”  

“Oh, this one is included in the 55 million[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-113209) fee you paid me.”

It was something I probably shouldn’t give natives from Anazumu. Still, I would do it either way. It would surely make them happy.

“Here you go.”

I handed them a device with a screen. It was a modern convenience from Earth.

“What is this, a board?”  

“It’s a device. For now, could you press the button on the upper left?”  

“This one?”

Uruto pressed the button I had pointed out. The screen lit up.

_“Today, I welcome all of you who’ve-“_  

“Th-That’s the archbishop’s voice!?”  

“A voice is coming from this device…!”  

“Well, just watch it, it’s about 10 minutes long.”

The device I’d given them displayed the events of their wedding. It worked like a tablet on which the ceremony had been recorded, like both a camera and a small TV screen[4](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-4-113209).

“I-Incredible. What is this?”  

“It works on the principle that many still images in succession make it appear as if the picture is moving, and consists of several tens of thousands of pictures that I took during the wedding. I also recorded the sounds in the venue. This is a combination of both.”  

“H-Hah~.”

_I see, so that’s how people who see a recording for the first time react._  

The two of them, who were adults for all intents and purposes, were in open-mouthed shock.

“That’s not the only function is has.”  

“What do you mean?”  

“Please press the button on the upper right this time.”

Same as before, Uruto obediently pressed the upper right button.

“For some reason, the device is now showing our feet…”  

“Then lift it up… like that, now please aim it at Miss Parasuna as if you’d be using a telescope.”  

“…Like this?”

I went around and looked at the display from Uruto’s side, where I could see Parasuna being shown.

“Now press the upper right button one more time!”  

“A-Alright!”

The moment he did, the screen went dark, and a sheet of paper came out of the device. It was a photograph.

“A… a realistic drawing!? Moreover, it’s incredibly detailed…”  

“It’s a function that lets you make pictures anywhere! While the size may be limited, it can instantly reproduce anything you see on the screen!”  

“Wh-Wha-… is this an artifact[5](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-5-113209)…?”

It was funny to see them panic. It took some time for them to calm down, before I could continue.

“In any case, you can use this to have records of how your kids grow up.”  

“K-Kids… You’re right. Anyway, thank you.”

The two of them thanked me intently once more. From my point of view, it wasn’t that much, so I felt a bit awkward. Well, as long as they were happy.

“So what, we’ll use this again once our children are born?”  

“Y-Yeah…”  

“You got it. Anyway, if there isn’t anything else…”

I stood up.  

_I’ve already been here for an hour, so let’s head home so they can enjoy their honeymoon._

“Best of luck to you!”  

“…Thank you, Alim!”  

“Really, we can’t thank you enough!”

After the newlyweds saw me off from the inn with waves, I made my way back to the home where my fiancée was waiting… Though before that, I had to make another stop, or rather, do some infiltration.

#### Footnotes:

1. 50 million in the original. I used the 55 from chapter 494 for consistency.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-1-113209)

2. For all the worldbuilding, this seems one of the most unrealistic that isn’t caused by it being a fantasy setting. With their tools and clear international relations, there would be no way they wouldn’t have some sort of banking.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-2-113209)

3. 500 million in the original. Maybe it was meant to be internal monologue and him thinking in Yen.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-3-113209)

4. The original doesn’t call it a tablet, I added that since it sounds like one. Maybe they weren’t called that in Japan back in 2016.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-4-113209)

5. I wonder if this is a hint of Anazumu being a post-apocalypse world or just Japanese using the word “Artifact” in a weird way.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-two-days-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-5-113209)

# 548.5 – The Hero and the Rabbit – 2

“She’s gone.” Parasuna had been waving until Alim was out of view.  

“…Phew, it really was the right decision to leave it to her.” Uruto earnestly thought that.  

“I’ll never forget it for the rest of my life. She even gave us such a thing.”

The two of them peered at the device Alim had handed them. No matter how you looked at it, it wasn’t something that could be created with the technology of this world. A thing of marvel, capable of leaving records of their wedding and the family they would nurture.

“And it can instantly create realistic depictions, huh?”  

“It seems so.”  

“Let’s take a picture of you as a test, Parasuna.”

Uruto pressed the upper right button to switch the device from video replay to photo mode.

“Of me?”  

“Yep, just as an experiment… Give me a smile.”

Doing like Alim had shown him, he pointed the device at Parasuna. She seemed embarrassed by it.

“S-Stop. You’re making me blush.”  

“But all I want is a detailed picture of the wife I love from the bottom of my heart…”  

“B-Bwuh!?”

Her face flushed red for an instant, and the same moment, she broke into a grin. Uruto didn’t miss that moment. A piece of paper dropped from the device.

“Yep, it’s adorable.”  

“Ugh…”  

“Don’t be so grumpy. It will ruin your cute looks.”  

“Grr…!”

As she puffed out her cheeks with a defiant gaze, a look she wouldn’t show anyone other than him, he gently caressed her head, including her ears.

“That feels nice… more please.”  

“That’s quite the change of attitude.”  

“In the end, I enjoy being petted.”  

“I know that.”

In accordance with her demand, Uruto continued patting her head. Feeling warmth in her heart, she nuzzled up closer to him with her eyes narrowed happily.

“…Kiss me.”  

“Alright. Now in you’re in the spirit of being newly wed.”  

“Even… even if we weren’t, I’d want you to kiss me…”  

“I get it.”

Their lips met. It wasn’t for the purpose of lovemaking, so their tongues didn’t entwine, but it was an intense kiss.

“Phew, this is bad. I can’t let all those people who admire me see me like this.”  

“Why’s that?”  

“Look, they think I’m all cool and composed. It would shatter their illusion.”

He impulsively smiled at her strange concern.

“Well, it’s not like they can see us here.”  

“Who knows, you might suddenly hug me when we’re outside.”  

“We’re married now, no one would think it weird if we did that.”

She buried her head in his chest at the thought of him embracing her outside as he did right now.

“I love you.”  

“I know.” He patted his wife’s back. “Oh, that’s right. Alim mentioned it earlier, what should we do about having children?”  

“Children… as for me…” Parasuna thought for a bit. “We can have as many as you want… I guess? One… or three… or even five or ten[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-5-the-hero-and-the-rabbit-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-113211)!” she told him with upturned eyes, as she counted with her fingers.

He smiled at her, as she mentioned the number ten with a serious look.

“W-Well… we could have ten.”  

“Right? I think we could raise that many.”  

“We could, but it might be hard on you. Three should be enough, let’s keep it at that.”  

“If you say so.” She easily backed down. “S-So, Uruto… uhm… when should we have children? Anytime works for me.”  

“Same here, I guess.”  

“So… right now?” she proposed as her cheeks turned bright red.  

“Right now!?”  

“W-We’re already 22, having kids at that age is normal, isn’t it? So…”

She hugged him again. He returned the embrace with a somewhat perplexed look.

“That’s true… I guess we’re old enough.”  

“R-Right?”  

“Yep.”

He gazed at her eyes.

“Wh-What is it?”  

“Well… I was just wondering if today would work.”  

“Huh? You mean… I guess it would,” she replied, understanding his meaning as the blush on her cheeks intensified.

He made a fist-pump in triumph.

“…Well, it’s the middle of the day, so let’s wait until evening. Oh, right. Should I make us lunch?”  

“You’d do that for me? Or I could do the cooking.”  

“I’ll leave it to you, then[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-5-the-hero-and-the-rabbit-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-113211).”  

“Heh-heh, you can count on me.”

The two of them separated and she disappeared into the kitchen. Shortly later, she returned with the finished meal.

“Here you go, enjoy!”  

“Thank you… it looks great. What’s with the heart shape, though?”  

“It symbolizes my heart for you, Uruto. I love you.”  

“I know. I love you, too… Now, shall we eat?”  

“Yeah.”

#### Footnotes:

1. Sounds like those rabbit genes are making themselves known.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-548-5-the-hero-and-the-rabbit-2/#easy-footnote-1-113211)

2. You’d think with him running the inn and doing all the cooking, he’d be a more experienced chef and she’d far prefer his cooking to her own.

# 549 – The Other Couples after the Wedding

“…Woof.”

“Somethin’ wrong, Rir?”

She was looking at me.

Yesterday, the wedding of two celebrities of this country had happened. The one where Ayumu went and showed off his outstanding designs. It was awesome. But since it was over, Rir kept shooting me these bitter looks.

“…Woof~.”  

“H-Hey, what’s goin’ on… just tell me.”

It was clear that she wasn’t in a bad mood, but unfortunately, I had no idea what was going on with her.

“Shuu, can I ask something selfish?”  

“Wh-What, at this point? I don’t mind.”

She probably wasn’t aiming at that, but how she looked at me with upturned eyes made me choke up.

“Thank you. Then, can we get married?”  

“…Come again?”  

“Woof, I was half joking,” she replied, changing her expression to a grin.

_That “half joking” startled me._

“…I was surprised that the SSS-Ranker Parasuna is a rabbitkin.”  

“T-True. I haven’t been in this world for long, so it didn’t seem so for me, but from how others reacted it’s pretty unusual, huh?”  

“It is,” she confirmed as she sat next to me and rested her head on my shoulder. “…I understand the pain Parasuna must’ve felt. Surely… she was so happy she could’ve died.”  

“What do you mean?”  

“Woof, it’s simple. She might’ve been raised[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-549-the-other-couples-after-the-wedding/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116206) in this country, but she was still treated like a slave… Even if she had it better than others, there must’ve been discrimination. That was the society back then. And now, to be united in marriage with the one who supported her through all that…”

At this point, she stopped talking and kept gazing at me again.  

_I get it. Her own situation resembles that a bit. Parasuna and Uruto… are like Rir and me. At least from her perspective._

“Well, if we put it in terms of a fairy tale, then Parasuna and I would be Cindrella, and Uruto and you the prince.”  

“A-Ain’t that a bit much?”  

“It’s not.”

_She sees me as her prince? I mean, I get it with some handsome guy like Uruto, but me with my muscles…? But if she thinks so, then I guess that’s how it is._

“I guess. Rir, I promised that before… but I hope to have such a weddin’ with you someday. No, we’ll have it together, I mean.”  

“Woof! Yeah, lets! Wearing a wedding dress has been a longing of mine for some time. I’d be happy to have you put one on me!”  

“That’s for sure.”

Normally, I’d have replied that we didn’t know what might happen a few years down the line. But then I saw how excited about marrying me she was, although we’d only been together for a few months, and I couldn’t imagine spending the rest of my life with someone other than her, either. Talking in occult terms, we might be fated for each other.

“And I want to have kids with you, Shuu.”  

“Been some time since you brought that up.”

I could clearly imagine her rubbing her pregnant belly while smiling. A happy thought.

“Woof. Still, I’m thinking differently now. I do want children, but only after we spent enough time together! If we had kids, it would get harder to do something by ourselves. And we could no longer get frisky.”  

“Frisky, you say… I guess so. I’ll keep you to it.”

At my reply, there was a look of relief on her face, as she happily pulled me into an embrace.

____  

__  

_

“What did you think? About the wedding, I mean.”  

“It was so pretty…”

Kanata and Sakura were talking in their room.

“If it comes to mine, I’d like one just as extravagant.,” she stated. “But I’d only invite family and friends.”  

“That’s true. Having so many people attend would be way too much trouble.”

From their perspective as 14-year-olds, this was still far off, but they had started to yearn for it.

“Wearing a wedding dress…”  

“I’m sure your dress will be the absolute prettiest, Sakura.”  

“You think so? Eh-heh-heh,” she giggled happily.

He gave her a heartwarming look.

“But that’s in the future, and the one who’ll get to see you in your wedding dress from up closest-”  

“Huh, i-isn’t that obvious?” Sakura asked impatiently, as the boy let his words taper of maliciously.  

“Yep. I assume it’ll be me.”  

“…R-Right. I-It can’t be anyone but you, Kanata. Y-You made sure I’m fully dependent on you, so don’t you dare leave me!” she told the boy her true feelings with a slightly flushed face.

He smiled at her happily.

“I also depend a lot on you, Sakura.”  

“R-Right? You’d be in trouble without me.”  

“Yep, I wouldn’t be alive,” he replied, as he patted her head while feeling satisfaction at how his words had made her blush even more, and then bit into one of the donuts they’d made together.

#### Footnotes:

1. She says “born and raised” in the original, but from what Alim mentioned a few chapters ago, she was born in another country that still has slavery

# 550 – The Clown’s Finger

“Hello.”

After parting with Uruto and Parasuna, I made full use of my items to sneak into the castle’s jail, where I called out to a strange-looking man occupying one of the cells. So many things had happened to him in this world, that he was completely unrecognizable as a human.

“Miss Alim?”  

“The very same, Mr. Mitsuo. It’s been a while.”

He looked worn-out, but still calmly raised his head from within his restraints (which had been made by me) and met my gaze.

“This doesn’t seem to cause you as much trouble as I expected.”  

“Well… what are a few months compared to waiting for hundreds of years?”

He had been stuck in this world for centuries due to some sort of divine prank. Though he actually spent most of that time sleeping.

“The reason I’ve come is that the time of your departure is near.”  

“I understand.”  

“For that, there are some things we need to do first.”

I brought out the Jizou statue and placed it on the cold, dark floor.

“Huh… I think I remember that one… Isn’t that Genten Jizou?”  

“Well, it resembles that specific statue in shape. Please place you hand on it.”

I used several tools made by Item Master to remove his restraints and also twisted the prison’s metal bats (likely made of ultimetal) out of the way.

“You are still just as incomprehensibly powerful…”  

“I’ll have to put these restraints back on after we’re done. For now, please put your hand on the statue.”

Never showing any signs of doubting me, he did as I told him.

“Now, first close your eyes and some sort of menu should appear, from which you then select the option ‘World Transfer’… or something like that.”  

“A-Alright.”

Likely going through the steps I had told him, he closed his eyes for some time before reopening them, apparently having finished his task.

“Uhm, it says that it’s possible for me to travel to another world[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-550-the-clowns-finger/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116210)…”  

“Alright. That was what I wanted to confirm. I’ll take the statue back.”

With the snap of a finger, I forcibly separated the statue from the clown and returned it to my side.

“Then, for your return to be successful, I will need a part of your body, Mr. Mitsuo… To be specific, some of your flesh. Could I take one of your fingers? I will heal you right afterwards,” I explained as I put away the statue.

Well, a bundle of hair and teeth like Rir’s might’ve worked too, but it felt like having a finger would be more reliable for the Amritas’ resurrection effect to work.

“T-To say something so horrifying with such a cute expression… If it is for the sake of my return to Earth… I accept…”

He held his left hand through the wrenched-open bars and extended his pinky. I cut it off quickly so it wouldn’t hurt too much, and then dripped a drop of Amrita I’d prepared in advance on the wound. I wrapped the cut-off pinky into a piece of cloth, which I then placed into a magic bag I made specifically for that.

“These Amritas never cease to amaze. So… what is going to happen now?”  

“You will have to wait for the right time.”  

“S-So, you’re saying I’ll have to let them execute me?”  

“Yes,” I replied in so cold a manner, I couldn’t believe it myself.

It shocked me, but I wasn’t about to take back my words.

“Because of you, the one most dear to me died. All my friends and the people who took care of me did too. That they came back to life doesn’t change that fact. This is to get even.”  

“…You’re right. I understand…”

“Right after you have been executed, I will revive you with this finger and send you back to Earth. However…” I was staring into his eyes. “How can I believe that you won’t turn to crime on Earth after murdering people in this world[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-550-the-clowns-finger/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116210)?”  

“About that…”  

“That’s my worry.”

Well, I could alter his mind before sending him back[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-550-the-clowns-finger/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-116210). But I couldn’t send a criminal to another world, so leaving him dead after the execution might be for the best. Showing mercy wouldn’t cut it here.

“…It will be fine.”  

“Will it really? I can send you back to this world by force.”  

“…Yes.”

I actually had no way of doing that. Well, I might at some point.

“In that case, I shall believe you… Let’s meet again when it is time to send you home.”

I put him back into his restraints, fixed the jail bars, and then escaped from the Mephilad castle prison.

If he safely made it back to the point where he originally left Earth and made a comeback as the leader of the Love Long circus troupe, I should pay him a visit with Mika. I might bring Kanata, Sakura, Shuu, and Rir too. When they performed close to where we lived, that is.

_Now, I should really return home to my loving fiancée._

---

**TL notes:**  

There were some changes to the site which affected the backend and made standard rectangular brackets that aren’t used for code cause weird things with the layout. The methods I previously used to deal with these issues no longer seem to work, so I’ll change the brackets for denoting message conversations to something else to remove this issue.

Other things also no longer work like they used to, though they aren’t as egregious in their effects. Ultimately, I’ll fix the older chapters, though it will take time, with how many there are. Don’t get me wrong, I’m not blaming anyone other than myself for this situation. The methods I used to deal with these issues were haphazard in the first place, and such effects were bound to pop up at some point.

1. I guess this disproves the “privilege is lost after a certain time” theory.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-550-the-clowns-finger/#easy-footnote-1-116210)

2. I wonder if this is here because the author themselves realized it or due to people’s comments concerning the initial version where he was sent back at the end of volume 7.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-550-the-clowns-finger/#easy-footnote-2-116210)

3. It’s unclear who would do the mind altering/brainwashing here. It’s possible he means that the transfer will include a personality adjustment.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-550-the-clowns-finger/#easy-footnote-3-116210)

# 552 – Trying to Relax

There is no chapter 551.

---

“Ayumu~! You must’ve worked hard!”

Mika jumped and hugged me right after I came home.

“The big work is over now.”  

“Yeah, we can finally take a breather.”

She hugged me even stronger and then placed her lips onto mine.

At this point, I’d been constantly busy, though before that matter started, I’d had too much free time in my hands. Whenever a big job like this one ended, I wanted to take it slow for a while.

“I also want to get married! Wear a wedding dress!” she exclaimed.  

“It will be at least three years until we can do that in this world… four and a half if we include the time spent on Earth. You’ll have to be patient.”  

“Hmph.” She puffed out her cheeks.

I gently pressed onto those cute cheeks with both my hands.

“Mph-”  

“We don’t have any photoshoots today, so… what should we do?”  

“Let’s play games together.”  

“Alright.”

That said, there wasn’t much else we could do. Reading manga and studying was possible, but those were things you mostly did on your own. At best, you could sit close together while doing them. In such cases, Mika got lonely, so we ended up watching a movie together or playing video games made for multiplayer.

In Anazumu, we no longer had to earn money and mostly pursued our hobbies and did some work on demand. That was how we could spend our time together constantly, but… there were more means of recreation on Earth and more free time.

Those were roughly my thoughts. On second thought, we were living in luxury.

“Let’s play a fighting game today! And each match, the loser has to take something off.”  

“Seriously? I’m terrible at those.”  

“If you don’t want to, we don’t have to. But if you win often enough… I’ll be completely…”

“…I’ll do it,” I ultimately replied after thinking for a while.

There wasn’t any real choice. I’d end up buck naked either way.

“Heh-heh-heh, oh, Ayumu! If we’re going so far to take even underwear off, could you turn into Alim?”  

“Why?”  

“This stuff is more fun if all participants are the same gender. It’s not interesting if a boy takes his clothes off. I mean… if you want me to keep looking at your…” she commented as her cheeks turned red.

She must’ve been frustrated by me focusing solely on work for days. Well, I couldn’t say for sure.

“Alrighty! Let’s start!” she exclaimed.  

“Y-You’re on!”

_____  

___  

_

_Why did it turn out like this?_

“A-Ayumu~… u-uhm, which one will it be?” Mika asked me with her face bright red.

She was only wearing a single piece of underwear each on her upper and lower body part, and once she took one of them off, she’d be fully exposed in that region.

“E-Erm, I just had a thought.”  

“Wh-What now?”  

“Did you lose on purpose?”

Indeed, it was straight up unthinkable for me to win this many matches against her in a fighting game. That said, I had also been reduced to panties, shirt, and shoes.

“T-To be honest… up to the point where you took my blouse, pants, and shoes, I was going easy on you, avoiding inescapable grabs[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-552-trying-to-relax/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116212) and combos, even throwing in some useless moves.”

_Why, you little…_

“B-But at that point, I started playing properly, alright!?”  

“Are you serious!?”  

“It’s true!”

From what I could tell, she wasn’t lying. In other words, I’d scored two legit wins against her, as she was going all out.

“To think after giving it my all… I’m now at your mercy…”  

“Leaving aside the fact that I won at the game, you should know I wouldn’t do that.”  

“Yeah, I do.”

She smiled, although she still seemed embarrassed. It was cute, but I had to do something about this situation.

“Well, you don’t have to take it off.”  

“Huh?”  

“What, you want to?”

She was giving me a blank look. My own expression was probably similar.

“I-It’s fine, you know? You can have me take off what you want and then stare and touch as much as you want…”  

“The top, then.”  

“Alright… eh-heh-heh.”

I managed to grasp her plan. Though she wouldn’t have had to go through all that trouble to get me to undress her. Well, it served as a way to pass the time.

“…H-Here you go.”

She looked at me with upturned eyes after doing what I asked her to.

“So, can I touch them?”  

“Y-Yeah, as much as you want.”

She showed no resistance, not even trying to hide them.

I picked her up. Then, I changed my hold to a princess carry.  

“…There was no need to use such a roundabout way.”  

“I mean, the normal way would’ve been boring, right? Eh-heh-heh, I love how you turn red, no matter of often you see me like this.”  

“Says the one who looks like an overripe tomato.”

I gently set her down on the bed. Then, I crawled in next to her. Obviously, I removed all the fabric between us.

“Alright… then-”

It happened after I swallowed and was about to perform the act we had done quite often at this point.

[Alim, Mika, it is Us! We would like to ask you something!]　

We were contacted by King Rama. This was the second time we’d been interrupted by royalty[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-552-trying-to-relax/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116212). The worst kind of déjà vu.

_…God damn it._

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is ハメ技. According to Google, this seems to be game terminology for (often inescapable) grabs/holds in fighting games.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-552-trying-to-relax/#easy-footnote-1-116212)

2. In the original, it says “again by King Rama”, but the first time was by King Mephilad (though he did contact them because of King Rama).

# 553 – Seeing King Rama Off

“Oh, you’re here. Alim, Mika, Our apologies for calling you.”

King Rama and his retainers were at the designated location. Said location was in Mephilad castle.

“Not at all, it was no trouble,” I replied.  

“Yes, we weren’t busy with anything…” Mika added.

All lies.  

At this point, the two of us should have been indulging ourselves in fleshly pleasures. Inwardly, I felt nothing but dissatisfaction. But this man was the king of another country, so I couldn’t show my anger. Mika seemed to feel the same.

“I see, that’s good. To put it simple, We shall be returning to our country today, so We wanted to see the two of you one final time.”  

“That makes sense.”  

“Indeed, and while We are at it, We would love for you to treat us to lunch.”

He likely got a taste for my food and yearned for one more chance to enjoy it. True enough, it was noon and if talk had switched to food, I’d have offered to treat everyone here. It couldn’t be helped.

_No comment about Mika and me planning to engage in such acts even before noon._

“That’s fine with me! Please go to the dining hall ahead of me then, everyone.”  

“Understood!”

A 23-year-old man getting excited at the prospect of a 13-year-old girl… this probably didn’t look good from an outside perspective. Although I was used to it.

King Rama’s group, seemingly overjoyed, disappeared in the direction of the dining hall.

_____  

___  

_

“Is something wrong?”

The food had been devoured in no time at all by King Rama, his retainers, and the usual people from Mephilad castle who had joined us. Either way, I was happy to see that they enjoyed it.

“Oh, this dish was so delicious, it brought Us to tears!”  

“That’s good to hear!”

The plates were sparkling. They hadn’t licked them clean, so how in the world did they get them so pristine? It was a mystery.

“Oh… it is finally time for Us to part, Alim…”  

“Your country is far away, so will it hard for us to meet again?”  

“Unfortunately,” the foreign king replied with a sad, lonesome look.

I wasn’t sure how to react to that.

And at that moment…  

“Say, won’t you become my wife, after all?”  

…He repeated his proposal.

“Mrr… didn’t I mention before that there is someone I hold dear, even if she is the same gender?”  

“Hrm, you did.” King Rama shot Mika a glance. “How will this work… together with Mika? If it may serve as a reason to come to the Bufura Kingdom[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-553-seeing-king-rama-off/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116270), a man there can have two or more women and-”  

“…No, we should leave it at this, Your Majesty. In the first place, there is no telling what my fans would do if we did this.”  

“You’re right, that is a valid concern.”

We had no idea what horrors my fans might unleash if someone tried to monopolize me. For an instant, there was a look of dread on King Rama’s face.

“…King Rama, Alim and Mika aren’t planning to leave this country in the first place.”  

“Oh dear, that would be another issue… Hah.”

The foreign king dropped his shoulders dejectedly at King Mephilad rubbing salt into his wounds. From King Rama’s perspective, this must’ve seemed like his last chance.

“Alim… are We allowed to stay your fan, as We were?”  

“Why wouldn’t you? I don’t see the issue…”  

“I see, then We shall keep rooting for you,” he replied, seemingly having regained his spirit a tiny bit.

I didn’t know why he even had to ask that. Well, he probably felt interacting with me would become harder after I rejected his proposal.

“…Also, if you don’t mind, We have a personal… no, this request concerns Our whole country. King Mephilad should hear this, too.”

He had seemingly realized something after Hanuman whispered to him, drawing the attention of everyone in the room. If King Mephilad had to hear it too, then it was likely crucial.

“Understood.”  

“Hrm, so… Alim, assuming Our country’s evil god were to resurrect, would you assist Us in vanquishing it?”

He made this request while holding my gaze, exuding a completely different air than just earlier.  

_But isn’t that a strange request?_

“Hasn’t your evil god… already been destroyed?”  

“It certainly has. But evil gods have come back to life one after the other within less than a year. These affairs haven’t become large issues due to them being sealed away promptly without causing many casualties, but… it is concerning, nonetheless. What might have happened if you hadn’t been there, Alim?”

He had a point. It was weird how two evil gods, who’d been sealed for centuries, came back one after the other. And I was conveniently there to take care of them… It was easy to assume that this hadn’t been the end of it. Though on second thought, it simply boiled down to sealing them once they appeared.

“Understood. Should your evil god appear, I will assist you in dealing with the issue! Is that fine for you too, Your Majesty King Mephilad?”  

“This would’ve been my request, too. You are able to deal with evil gods, so I see no reason not to send you. This concerns all of Anazumu, not a single country.”  

“As he says…”

The king had also sent me to Yggdrasil, when Surtr appeared there.

“Our apologies, King Mephilad, Alim… The chance of that happening should be miniscule.”

After apologizing to us and dropping a line that most definitely raised a flag, King Rama took his entourage and left towards his homeland while waving at me frantically.

_…Now that he’s gone, Mika and can finally go back to being intimate in peace. Well, before that, we should pay Karua a visit, seeing we’re at the castle already. We can probably continue where we left off tomorrow… Phew._

#### Footnotes:

1. Rama Country in the original. An error, I assume.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/chapter-553-seeing-king-rama-off/#easy-footnote-1-116270)

# Side Story 17 – The Ants and the Squirrel of the Bent Tree – 2

It’s the continuance of side story 4. If you thought the first one was weird, it’s going to get really crazy.

**Author’s note:**  

You may want to read this story from the perspective of how insect swarm societies work.

---

This is a story from a world different than Anazumu.

“Miss Squi-… Mika!”  

“Alim!”

A squirrel of the bent tree and an ant were intimately embracing each other.

“Thank you for safely birthing our children!”  

“You ants have so many children!”

Due to certain circumstances, the squirrel had married a group of ants and was now delivering their children one after the other. In this world, squirrels of the bent tree could give birth to ants. Vice versa, it was possible for an ant to give birth to a squirrel.

“Uhm, how many makes this?”  

“Our group increased by roughly 20%.”  

“If we include the squirrels, it would be 30%.”  

“What!? Are you alright, Mika?”

The other ants crowded in concern around the squirrel who was lying on the bed in the embrace of a single ant. But she seemed in high spirits.

“I still have a lot of energy!”  

“Is that so?”  

“Please don’t force yourself, alright?”

The ants rubbed the squirrel’s head and belly. The squirrel smiled happily, but then suddenly had a thought she decided to bring up with the ants.

“Come to think of it, how are we with food?”  

“Oh, no problems at all on that front. We have a magic storehouse with unlimited space where food won’t spoil… At our current pace, we should be fine for another ten years or so.”  

“That sounds incredible!”  

“It’s an ant skill!”

The ants made merry.

“Right… then let’s have many more children.”  

“We’ll increase our family! Woo-hoo!”

The squirrel, who seemed a bit exhausted after all, took the hand of the ant at her side. She signaled that she would sleep for a bit.

“Everyone, Miss Squirrel is going to sleep!”  

“Alright, then let’s keep quiet.”  

“Shush!”  

“In that case, everyone except for the ant who’s with her currently, disperse!”

As requested, the ants left the room where the squirrel was sleeping. In exchange, they went where their several dozens of kids were.

“Everyone! We’ve come to play!”  

“Oh, Mama!”  

“Mommy!”

When the adult ants entered the room where just few of them had been before, the young ants and squirrels there demanded they play with them.

“Mama, where’s Mother?”  

“Your mother is currently super tired, so she’s resting.”  

“Boo! Wanted to play with her!”  

“But your mother has a hard job, so it can’t be helped!”  

“Mrr… Can’t be helped, then.”

The ant children were dejected. One of the squirrel children hugged an ant child.

“Wh-What?”  

“Heh-heh… I hug you.”  

“Hm… then I hug you back!”

The ant child, who’d been hugged by the squirrel child, returned the embrace. The adult ants started to whisper as they saw that.

“They already have such a relationship at that age?”  

“When were those two born again?”  

“One at noon two days ago, and the other at 9 pm of the same day.”  

“Huh, so they were born on the same day.”  

“Right, now that you mention it, Mika had to work super hard on that day.”

The adult ants smiled in satisfaction as they looked at the young ants, who seemed no different from them in appearance other than age. They then each joined in groups of two or three and sang songs, drew pictures, had matches, acted as if they were celebrities, or started projects to support the next generation.

“Ugh! Our children are so cute, I could eat them up!”  

“Right?”  

“Huh, Mika and I are cute?”

At the child ant’s question, all the adults nodded. They didn’t realize that they were practically praising themselves, seeing their appearance was the same as their children.

“I-In that case, give me hug!”  

“Ah, m-me too!”

The children with their insufficient size jumped up and down, demanding hugs from their parents.  

The adult ants picked them up with joyful faces.

“Heh-heh-heh, hug!”  

“Hug! More!”

Time passed joyfully. But then it happened.

“I-It’s terrible!”

A single ant, still completely naked, barged into the room. It was the one who stayed with the squirrel mother earlier.”

“Woah, what’s wrong!?”  

“P-Put some clothes on, first! There are children present!”  

“I don’t see the issue, there are no male ants or squirrels here.”

There were only female ants and squirrels of the bent tree, but for some reason, they could still reproduce[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/side-story-17-the-ants-and-the-squirrel-of-the-bent-tree-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116272). The still-naked ant hurriedly continued to tell them what happened.

“M-Miss Squ-… Mika stopped breathing!”  

“””What~~!?”””

The ants rushed to the squirrel’s side.

“M-Mika!?”  

“Are you alright!?”

One ant checked her pulse and breathing. She shook her head.

“This happened because she worked too hard lately…”  

“Gah… if only we had taken better care of her…! Uhg… _sob_…”

The ants blamed themselves for this. Some of them cried, some collapsed in shock, some blanched mentally. The ant who performed the examination on the squirrel took out a bottle.

“In that case, we’ll need to use Amrita.”

Amrita was the very best medicine the ants could make. It would heal any living being, no matter what illnesses or wounds it had, even bringing them back from the dead.

“Phew… Next time, you need to make sure you don’t strain yourself so much!”  

“If you do, you’ll go ‘poof’!”  

“But first you should get enough sleep!”

__________  

_____  

_

“…Wha-!?”

Mika had experienced another strange dream.

“…Somehow, it feels as if I had one like this before. In any case, our children were so cute… heh-heh. Well, I better go back to sleep.”

She hugged Alim again and closed her eyes.

#### Footnotes:

1. If they reproduce asexually, that would explain why they all look the same.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-18/side-story-17-the-ants-and-the-squirrel-of-the-bent-tree-2/#easy-footnote-1-116272)
