# 554 – Death of a Clown

“Ayumu, can you kiss me?”  

“Hm? Sure.”

It was morning and I was drinking coffee while reading manga. Mika, who was sitting next to me, pestered me with her demands to be spoiled. Our lips soon met, and our tongues had their back and forth.

“Pfft. That was one bitter kiss.”  

“That’s because I was drinking coffee.”

Such was our lovestruck everyday life. From an outside perspective, it might’ve looked unusual (like two newlyweds having their honeymoon), but for us it was perfectly normal.

“Ayumu~, let’s do something~.”

Mika seemed to be in a mood to be spoiled today… it was adorable. She made that request while looking up at me from within a hug, which was quite the feat since we currently had the same height. Honestly, it was so cute, I could die.

“Hm, and what would that be?”  

“Maybe go on a date outside? Or we could do a cosplay convention?”

Cosplay. When we did that, Mika always wore the suggestive outfit of some manga character at the end. A very suggestive one. She’d say stuff like “It’s to make you happy”… and then turn bright red, even though there was no real reason to be embarrassed with me. And then, we’d usually move on to adult fun.

But I wasn’t in the mood for that today. I wanted to enjoy my time without getting frisky, so going on a date sounded like the better option.

“Shall we go on a date, then?”  

“Alright! Date it is!” she happily agreed.

Hm… so where should I take her? When we were on a date, she seemed happy no matter what we did. While that was cute, I couldn’t help feeling as if being pampered by me lowered her IQ. Maybe having too much fun was doing strange things to her mind?

“Let’s go, then.”  

“Yeah.”

We changed into outside clothes, held hands, equipped disguise items that made us look like completely different people (so no one would try to talk to us or send messages), and finally stepped outside. This might come as no surprise, but we walked around with arms linked so closely, it was practically a hug.

“Where are we going?”  

“I haven’t decided.”  

“Alright! Then let’s choose something while we’re on the date.”

I needed to settle on a spot. Going at it without a plan like a certain beefcake wouldn’t fly. Though Rir seemed happy with it.

“…In the end, there are more options for recreation on Earth.”  

“I guess. But this place has other merits… though there definitely are few date spots.”

We were walking around while sharing our complaints. At times, we stopped to look at birds or kiss each other on the cheek.

“Should we eat our boxed lunch already?”  

“Huh? We didn’t make any lunch boxes, you know?”  

“I’m making some with Item Master right now… Here you go.”  

“Thank you.”

We sat down on a bench in a park, stuffed our cheeks with sandwiches, and fed each other potato garnish. Mika deliberately licked all my fingers.

“That was yummy!”  

“My fingers?”  

“Those too. So, what will we do?”

No good idea had come to me, yet. Ultimately, I was just as bad as Shuu. Well, it wasn’t the same, definitely.

“Th-Then, how about visiting an art gallery?”  

“Eh-heh-heh… You know, I’ll follow you wherever you go, Ayumu.”

She was adorable. It felt like I kept calling her nothing but “adorable” and “cute”, but it was true.

“Alright, let’s do-”

⟦…Alim, my apologies for suddenly contacting you.⟧  

⟦Uhm, yes!?⟧

I was contacted by the king. His timing was just awful. Though at least it wasn’t when we were about to get intimate, like last time.

“What’s wrong?”  

“Sorry, Mika, I just got a message. Could you wait for a moment?”  

“Alright.”

Right after replying so, she hugged me from behind. This was apparently how she’d spend the wait.

In any case.

⟦…My apologies for keeping you waiting, Your Majesty, what do you need?⟧  

⟦Mephistophales’ execution has concluded… I merely wanted to inform you about the fact.⟧

_I see, so it’s over._  

It had been three days since Mr. Mitsuo had entrusted me with his pinky. The time to send him back to Earth had finally come. Well, we were on a date right now, so it would have to wait until tomorrow.

⟦Understood. Thank you for telling me, Your Majesty.⟧  

⟦Of course, ’til another time.⟧

The king cut off the transmission.

Thinking of the execution made me remember how Mika’s face had looked after she died because of Mephistophales. It made me uncomfortable, giving me the impulse to voice my grievances. For the time being, I erased the mental image by indulging in her cuteness.

“Oh, Mika! Come on, let’s kiss!”  

“Uhm, sure? Eh-heh-heh, you’re a kissing fiend, after all.”

We shared our second intense kiss of the day. This time, it tasted sweet all the way.

“Phew. Alright, shall we go to the art gallery?”  

“Let’s!”

We linked arms again. And then we did our best to enjoy the rest of our date.

---

**TL notes:**  

And that’s the end of volume 18, the longest and (at least in my opinion) most boring one so far. The dates went on for a full 15 chapters and were mostly filler, and the wedding wasn’t that exciting either.

Hopefully, the next volume, which seems to be focused on the guide, the Bufura Kingdom’s variation of the hero/sage, will be more interesting again.

# 555 – The Clown’s Return Home

In a certain room of the mansion.

Indeed, it was a good thing I made this place in the basement to use things that might be… dangerous. Well, I ended up barely utilizing it and considered repurposing it for risky activities with Mika. In that regard, the room could now finally fulfill its purpose.

For now, I threw Mr. Mitsuo’s pinky in an area fenced off by iron bars. I took the lives of thousands of magic beasts, but I couldn’t get used to human remains.

Next, I prepared some Amrita. It was thanks to this marvelous substance that we were here right now, so I did consider it something truly divine… which reminded me that I had yet to supply Kanata and co. with divine grade equipment.

We’d be in trouble if an enemy on par with an evil god appeared, which they had to face… and they then ended up dead because their weapons were too weak, so I should make equipment for those four sometime tomorrow.

I threw an Amrita bottle into the jail. Its contents hit the cut-off finger without incident, and the resurrection started.

Something rapidly grew from the digit’s cross-section. It was messy… well, not exactly graphic, but for someone who rarely read gory and grotesque manga, it was repulsive. Anyway, that description didn’t really do reality justice.

_…I wonder if it looked like that with Rir. Should I apologize for asking Mika and Sakura to take care of that part?_

Still, seeing a girl naked as a man was a total no-go. Back then, I had no idea how gruesome it would look[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-555-the-clowns-return-home/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116534), so letting Shuu – Rir’s boyfriend – watch the spectacle might have been a mistake.

Mr. Mitsuo’s resurrection was over fairly quickly. I was prepared for it, but he came back naked, as feared. Luckily, I managed to avoid looking at his member… For the time being, I put some clothes on him with Dark Matter Creation.

_Yep, the only person I want to be around naked is Mika._  

I had no desire to see others unclothed… Well, looking at someone as perfect as Shuu from an artistic standpoint was another story.

“Good morning,” I called out somewhat loudly.

The middle-aged dandy in the latter half of his forties opened his eyes.

“A-Ah, where am I?”  

“In the basement of my house.”  

“I see… I was executed, wasn’t I?” he mumbled dejectedly while scanning his surroundings.

_Did it feel bad to come back to life after being put to death?_

“I owe you my thanks, Miss Alim.”  

“Not at all, it was a promise. I understand very well how much you want to return to Earth.”

Mr. Mitsuo was rubbing his neck. Could it be they decapitated him? A frightening thought.

“So, do you wish to return right away, or would you like to eat Anazumu’s cuisine one final time before you leave?”  

“…You’re correct, I’d like to return quickly, but eating food from this world one last time would be nice. Could I ask you for that?”  

“Of course.”

Cooking each part normally would take too long, so I created everything, including tableware and beverages, with Item Master and brought it out.

“Is this steak made from dragon meat?”  

“Yes, the salad is also made from a plant-type monster. And there’s more.”

First, the dragon steak was something you’d never be able to eat on Earth… though the taste was probably close to crocodile meat.  

_Hang on, crocodile is supposed to taste like chicken, so that comparison won’t work._

“It is rather delicious…”  

“That’s good to hear.”

That was a rather curt reaction. Though it was likely unavoidable, given his situation. Mr. Mitsuo ate all the meat (apart from dragon, there were other magic beasts I used as ingredients, too) and vegetable dishes in the blink of an eye and put down the tableware with a “thank you for this delicious meal”.

“Any last things on your mind?”  

“Nothing that I could… no, there is one,” he replied, apparently having recalled something.  

“What is it?”  

“My skills… it won’t be possible for me to keep both ‘Contract Domain’ and ‘Vaporization’, will it? I was wondering… will my skills be lost once I return to Earth?”  

“Yes, they will disappear[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-555-the-clowns-return-home/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116534).”

He was likely talking about Forced Contract and what allowed him to turn into smoke. Those hadn’t been perks of becoming a demon.

“Since your power concerns items, Miss Alim, uhm… this isn’t meant as an apology, but if there is a way to extract those skills, which should be situated among or above the stronger SS-Rank skills, with an item, would you take them?”

Forced Contract certainly was in a completely different league than lower-end SS-Rank skills. Even I could make good use of it. Should I turn it into a skill card?

“Understood. In that case… use these items to turn the skills into cards. After I hand them to you, put them against your forehead and transfer both skills to them.”  

“So, it is possible… Alright.”

He took the empty cards from me and then extracted his skills like I told him. After he gave the two fresh skill cards back to me and I verified the contents, the contained skills were indeed named as he had mentioned earlier.

“I confirm that the skills have been extracted.”  

“…Then I have nothing left. Will you let me return home?”  

“Yes.”

I brought out the Jizou statue and had Mr. Mitsuo touch it like last time.

“So… apparently, I will be sent home in a few seconds. If… if all goes well, could you come visit the Love Long circus troupe? If our tent is close to where you live, that is…”

Indeed, this man used to be the leader of one of Japan’s leading circus troupes.  

_If they are performing nearby, let’s pay them a visit._

“I will come together with people dear to me. I can’t exactly put it into writing… but I promise. If I see you, Mr. Mitsuo, I’ll shout ‘How did it go in Anazumu?'”  

“Ah-ha-ha, that’s fine. So, I will keep the memories of what happened here?”  

“Yes.”

His body started to disappear. It looked like the transfer went off without a hitch. He never raised his Reincarnation count, so he could no longer return to Anazumu… probably.

“One last thing, could you tell me your name on Earth?”  

“I am called Joujou Ayumu.”  

“Joujou Ayumu… I see. I won’t forget it. Then… goodbye.”

With one last smile, he disappeared completely. Only the dark iron bars and the Jizou statue remained.

_Let’s go back to my room and make out with Mika._

---

**TL notes:**  

We’re starting volume 19 by finally, after not seeing the man for around 380 chapters, sending the clown back to Earth. It will be interesting to see if he arrives back when he disappeared originally (around two months before the start of the story, if I remember correctly), or at the point where Alim & the other’s Earth-selves are currently.

Now, I said that volume 19 will focus on the guide, but judging from the chapter titles, this will only be in the last third of its 43 chapters and 8 side stories. I’d like to say that the preceding two thirds won’t be the same filler we enjoyed in volume 18, but the titles don’t give me much hope. My motivation to translate this has been on its all-time low for a few weeks now, so the possibility of a hiatus has sadly increased.

There was never anything mentioned about skills disappearing.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-555-the-clowns-return-home/#easy-footnote-2-116534)

# 556 – Free Day (Shuu)

Today was a day we didn’t have anything special to do.

The ways to kill time in this world were limited, so it was easy to get bored on days like these. I already did my strength training alongside Rir’s body toning exercises and we didn’t have any work to do, so I was seriously at a loss at how to spend my time. This was a problem.

Thus, I was reading manga. I got them from a machine Ayumu made for us. This thing was crazy; it could make whatever you wanted, even stuff from Earth.

“Woof.”

Contrasting me, Rir was merely nuzzled up close to me. The warmth of her skin and the softness of her chest were transmitted to my arm. This was apparently her way to kill time. It kept puzzling me.

“Rir, you’re not goin’ to do anything? Ain’t you bored?”  

“Woof, being close to you, Shuu, calms me down the most,” she replied while resting her head on my shoulder.

When I put my arm around her and started stroking her head, she seemed happy. As always. Still… not having anything I could do with her always made me a bit uncomfortable. As her boyfriend.

_There ain’t no way it’s just me gettin’ bored here. Makes me worry I’ll end up like Ayumu._

“Rir, isn’t there anything you’d like to do?” I asked as I put down the manga and continued caressing her head.

She could ask for anything today. I was usually reluctant in these matters, but today I was planning to go along if she asked to take a bath together or do the deed. I had no idea how often she had tried to tempt me with it… and how often I had refused (though we did it once or twice per week).

“You mean it?”  

“Yep, anything is fine.”

Though if she had some other request, that would be fine, too…

“Then I want to hug you right here.”  

“Alright.”

She moved onto my lap and put her arms around me. She felt soft despite looking so dainty… but also firm in some places. This might make me sound like some deviant, but she was as outstanding as always. Still, it felt like she was hugging me all the time. I had no idea if girls went out of their way to ask for this. She was probably just in the mood for it today.

“Woof, how long can I stay like this?”  

“As long as you want today. Well, let me fix my posture.”  

“It’s perfect that way, I feel like getting excessively spoiled today.”

She put more strength into her embrace. True enough, there had been times when she seemed desperate for attention. Today was probably such a day.  

My own mood and hers seemed well-aligned. Though I always indulged her when she wanted to be spoiled.

“Come to think of it, just earlier, you said ‘anything’, didn’t you?”  

“Yep, I did.”  

“In that case, can we take a bath together?”  

“…Alright.”  

“Awoo!”

Her tail was wagging happily. We usually didn’t use bath towels when we took a bath together, so it inevitable led to sex.  

_Gah, but she looks super cute when she’s happy… If it makes her this happy, guess I can put up with it on a daily basis._

“Hm…”

We embraced each other quietly. On top of the warmth and softness, this silence felt nice. However, someone then ruined the mood.

⟦Shuu! Rir!⟧

It was Ayumu… or to be more precise, he was currently Alim. Rir, who’d closed her eyes to enjoy the embrace, opened them, apparently concentrating on the message, too.

⟦What now, did somethin’ happen?⟧  

⟦You seem in a bad mood. Were you in the middle of something?⟧  

⟦Not sure what you’re implyin’ with that, but yes, we were.⟧  

⟦Sorry~. Well, I had the idea of making new weapons for everyone, so I wanted to inform you about this like I did with Kanata and Sakura… If you have weapons around legend grade, could you bring them to me? I’ll upgrade them to divine grade!⟧

_That’s one really sudden idea._

⟦Rir’s axe is created by a skill… Could you make an axe from scratch that can be infused with skill weapons like my Lævateinn?⟧  

⟦Woof, if you were to make one, that would be nice.⟧

She afterwards added a mumbled “so I’ll match with Shuu”. I impulsively stroked her head at that.

⟦Okay, I can do that! Sorry for it being so sudden. Please bring me yours sometime today, Shuu.⟧  

⟦Will do.⟧  

⟦See you later.⟧

The connection was cut.

I thought there wasn’t much meaning in strengthening our weapons at this point, but this was probably a hint that Ayumu didn’t have anything to do, either.  

_I know what bein’ bored feels like, so I’ll help him out._

“A weapon, huh… We haven’t touched on that topic in some time.”  

“That’s true.”  

“In exchange, I’m touching you all the time, Shuu.”  

“Same here.”

_Though I won’t tell where exactly we’re touchin’…_

I was enjoying my time flirting with my weaponless girlfriend.

“You wanna keep doin’ this until noon?”  

“Woof, let’s. Keep spoiling me today, will you?”  

“Alright, I’ll keep it up as long as you want.”  

“Awoo~!”

She started to kiss me. Afterwards, she hugged me again. And after hugging each other… we went to Ayumu.

+++

# 557 – Crafting Again After a Long Time – 1

“Now that you mention it, you still haven’t crafted equipment for everyone.”

After secretly sending off Mr. Mitsuo, I discussed my idea of improving everyone’s equipment with Mika.

“Well, we were busy with all kinds of stuff, so I simply forgot.”  

“You said you would be free until noon, didn’t you? But you’re right, it sounds like a good idea.”

With Mika also in agreement, I thought about starting right away. First, I called my brother and his girlfriend.

⟦Kanata, Sakura, do you have a moment?⟧  

⟦Hm? Is something wrong, Big Bro?⟧  

⟦I’m not taking you away from anything?⟧  

⟦No, you’re not, Ayu-nii.⟧  

⟦Right now is perfect, we just finished watching a movie.⟧

Those two apparently spent their free day by enjoying a film. They probably watched it in the mansion’s cinema.

⟦That’s great! Could the two of you come to Mika’s and my room?⟧  

⟦Sure? We’re there right away.⟧

When I received that message, Kanata and Sakura were already standing in front of us. They used teleportation.  

Well, I wasn’t about to complain.

“What do you need us for?”  

“Well, I realized I still haven’t made divine grade weapons for all of you, so I was thinking of rectifying that.”  

“So that’s what this is about.”

Kanata seemed to understand. Same for Sakura.

“Could you take out any equipment you’re using regularly? I’ll recraft and modify it.”  

“Huh, alright.”  

“U-Uhm, Ayu-nii, can I have a word?” Sakura asked timidly.

She seemed to be embarrassed about something.

“That’s fine.”  

“E-Erm, it’s about this thing,” she said, as she presented the extremely pretty necklace she was often wearing.

If I remembered correctly, it was called Brisingamen.

“What would you like to do with it?”  

“I-It should look as close as possible to how it does right now. Uhm… the thing is…”

She beckoned me closer and whispered into my ear.

“(It was the reason I started dating Kanata, so I want to treasure it. If possible, I’d like to keep it as it is, but…)”

She was a tsundere. And she cared a great deal for Kanata.

“(In that case, I’ll just perform maintenance and strengthen it by adding enchantments. That alone should bring it to divine grade.)”  

“(R-Really? Could you do that?)”  

“(Sure thing!)”

We were whispering, but I was sure Kanata overheard everything with his sharp ears. In fact, he looked quite happy right now.

“Could you give me your equipment, then?”  

“Alright, this one, too.”

She handed me a sword. I was relatively sure that it was a weapon that could attack automatically.

“For me, it’s these… and also…”

Kanata handed me an eyepatch, a black spear, and a golden bracelet. He then got close to me and whispered just as Sakura had done before.

“(First, the spear.)”  

“(Sure, what would you like me to do with it?)”  

“(I’d like to refrain from using Gungnir, so could you simply strengthen it? It already looks cool enough, don’t you think? At least from my point of view.)”  

“(You can put your trust in me.)”

Kanata nodded.

Even getting a girlfriend hadn’t cured his eight grader’s syndrome. Nothing probably would, it was in his nature.

“(Also, if you can set the name, I’d like you to call it something like ‘Gáe Bolgnir’.)”  

“(Isn’t that just Gáe Bolg and Gungnir combined?)”

Both were legendary weapons. And both probably existed in this world[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-557-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-1/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116552).

“(I knew you’d understand, Big Bro.)”  

“(I also went through that phase… So, what about the eyepatch?)”

He had been clutching it as if it was important to him. No matter how you looked at it, he must’ve gotten it from Sakura.

“(Sakura made it for me, so I want to treasure it. Could you to do the same with it as what Sakura requested earlier?)”  

“(That’s completely fine!)”  

“(Please do that, then.)”

So, he did hear it, after all. I saw joy in his expression, and with how similar our faces were, I could tell just how happy he was.

“Alright, I’ll finish them until evening! Are you fine leaving the decision of what abilities to add to me? I’ll mostly just strengthen what they already have.”  

“That’s fine, I’ll leave it to you.”  

“We’ll come get them tonight, Ayu-nii.”

The two of them teleported back into their room.

Next would be Shuu and Rir. There was a high chance at least one of them had an item with important memories attached to it. Rir’s red hood, for example.

But would this be a good time to message them? I wouldn’t catch them in the act, right? Well, it was the middle of the day, so they surely weren’t doing that. They obviously weren’t like Mika and me.

Thus, I contacted them.

#### Footnotes:

1. As a matter of fact, Gilmars used a weapon called “Gáe Bolg” back in chapter 163

+++

# 558 – Crafting Again After a Long Time – 2

“Sorry, sorry.”  

“Woof, it took us a bit longer.”

Around 10 minutes after I had called them, Shuu and Rir arrived.  

_Don’t tell me they really were doing the unspeakable in the middle of the day? Maybe they hurriedly put on some clothes after getting messaged by me. In that case, I need to apologize to them._

There had been two instances where we were contacted due to King Rama (though he was the caller on only one of those occasions) when Mika and I were just getting in the mood. I knew exactly how unpleasant this felt.

“Sorry, I did contact you while you were in the middle of something delicate, didn’t I?”  

“Y-You ain’t! It absolutely wasn’t what you think. We were just a bit tied up, so it took some time for us to come here.”

Shuu’s overly panicked reaction told me everything.  

_…Seriously. Rir is also averting her eyes. Oh, whatever. I choose to believe what my best friend told me._

“Gotcha! Then, could you bring out the equipment you’d like me to strengthen?”  

“It’s just Lævateinn for me.”  

“Woof, I have this bracelet…”

Both held out one legend grade item each.

“Are you fine with how your red hood is currently, Rir? Just adding some enchantments would make a huge difference.”  

“I got it from Shuu and want to treasure it, so I’m not wearing it during fights… But if you have cards that keep it from degrading and getting dirty, I’d like those.”  

“Alright, here you go.” I handed her several magic cards.  

“Woof, thank you, Alim.”

What I would make for them were improved versions of Lævateinn and the bracelet that looked closer to a chain, plus an axe with similar abilities to the aforementioned sword.

“Can we go back, then?” Shuu asked.  

“Sure, come get your stuff in the evening.”  

“Right!”  

“Woof, see you!”

They happily went back to their room.  

_Maybe it was a mistake to call them during daytime, after all… oh, well._

“Ayumu, you’ll lock yourself into your workroom, right? Before you do that, give me a hug and kiss me.”  

“Of course.”

I pressed a kiss on her lips while embracing her. After spending a few minutes like that, I entered my workshop.

_________

I was done. Everything was finished.  

_If I may say so myself, my ability to focus is frightening._

The equipment I crafted and strengthened this time turned out as follows. First, Sakura’s sword, which could attack by itself:

Then came Kanata’s bracelet. The one that could multiply. Strangely enough, my attempt to raise said multiplication limit from 8 to 100 ended in failure. It could happen.

|   |

|**“Draupnir, Golden Bracelet of Divine Affection”**  <br>-Status → Best  <br>-Quality → Highest  <br>-Value → Divine  <br>Materials: Adamant, several kinds of golden materials, Enchanted  <br>-Type → Divine Bracelet  <br>　  <br>Description:  <br>-Defense and Magic +6000  <br>-Miraculous boost to performance when used as a bracelet[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-558-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116616) (10 times multiplier to durability and effects)  <br>-This bracelet can create up to eight copies of itself if desired. Said copies will disappear 24 hours to one year later, at the owner’s discretion.  <br>-Miraculous increase to the effects of support magic cast on the wearer.  <br>-The owner receives a miraculous (10x) boost to all stats other than HP and MP  <br>-Adapts its size to the wearer’s arm.  <br>-Feels moderately light  <br>-Indestructible  <br>-Constantly maintains the best condition|

I’d go over my brother’s new weapon at the end, so next was Rir’s chain-like bracelet. Well, it was only in appearance now, it was no longer different from a normal bracelet. Having it clamped around your arm looked painful.

Then there was Shuu’s prided weapon, Lævateinn. It had been powerful from the beginning. To be honest, I was considering adding similar abilities to my own sword.

Next was Rir’s axe, which had practically the same abilities. I merely changed the elemental attributes to what I assumed was her specialty. Only, it ended up looking eerie.

Then there was Kanata’s eyepatch. To that, I had only added the usual “Feels moderately light”, “Indestructible”, “Constantly maintains the best condition”, and the 10 times boost to all stats. It still had all its original enchantments.

Finally, I was holding Kanata’s weapon. To be honest, it was the one I was most proud of. I gave it the best abilities of my and Shuu’s swords.

|“Gáe Bolgnir, Black Divine Spear of the Champion[4](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-558-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-2/#easy-footnote-bottom-4-116616)”  <br>-Status → Best  <br>-Quality → Highest  <br>-Value → Divine  <br>-Materials: Adamant, S- and SS-Rank magic beast materials (details omitted), Enchanted  <br>-Type → Divine Magic Spear  <br>　  <br>Description:  <br>-Attack Power +6000  <br>-Miraculous boost to performance when used as a spear (10 times multiplier to piercing ability, durability, and attack power)  <br>-Miraculous increase to the effects of darkness and wind magic and skills. Well, that was about it. It also looked perfect, my chuuni brother would be completely satisfied for sure.

I was finished checking the equipment. Once I delivered it, it would be over.  

_Oh, it’s been forever since I had so much fun crafting._

---

**TL notes:**  

Wow, it’s been such a long time since we had any equipment stats in this series (the last one should have been in chapter 309), and now there are seven of them at once! Ironically, while more than half of this chapter was just copy-pasting from other chapters, it still took forever since I always had to make sure there either were no changes or implement said changes in my version. Plus all the usual errors the author made, as you can see with the plethora of footnotes.

Also, this stuff is OP as hell (compare it to the versions in chapter 302 and 309 if you’re curious). Here’s hoping that for the next evil god, everyone will contribute, and it won’t just be Alim stealing the show.

#### Footnotes:

1. This is “Spell Necklace” in the original. Everything else is “divine”, so I assume that’s an error.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-558-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-2/#easy-footnote-1-116616)

2. “Necklace” in the original. Likely copy-pasted from above and then not changed to “bracelet”.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-558-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-2/#easy-footnote-2-116616)

3. This is “various kinds of magic beast materials” in the original. I used the version from earlier to keep things consistent. The same change was made for all following instances of this descriptor.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-558-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-2/#easy-footnote-3-116616)

4. The original is 英雄 (“hero”). I used “champion” to differentiate from the Hero’s Sword since different words are use in Japanese (勇者 for the latter).[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-558-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-2/#easy-footnote-4-116616)

5. Sharpness in the original. Likely an error since it earlier increases specifically piercing and not sharpness.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-558-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-2/#easy-footnote-5-116616)

6. Not sure about this part. The original is 刺突して部位より、魔法を放ちやすくなる。 (“makes shooting magic easier than piercing and slicing”). It’s possible there’s a typo and it’s supposed to make all three aspects easier.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-558-crafting-again-after-a-long-time-2/#easy-footnote-6-116616)

# 559 – Consultation at School (Mika

It had been two days since Ayumu’s sudden impulse to improve everyone’s equipment. From what Rir told me, they hadn’t had a chance to test it out so far[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-559-consultation-at-school-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116638). Mostly since we didn’t have to work in Anazumu.

On that note, we were currently on Earth. We’d been busy with various things, so the last two weeks felt more like three or four months. Maybe that was just me?

“Can anyone answer this question?”  

“Here!”

We had math class. And Rir acted like a model student, as usual. On top of having good looks, her physique was nice, so she seemed to be popular with the boys. Well, not like anything could separate her from Shuu. Just as I deeply adored Ayumu, she seemed completely fixated on our friend.

In any case, the question was way too easy. It was the fault of us going along with it when Kanata started to cram in Anazumu. When I tried the past exam question collection of a certain university as a test, I easily reached a passing mark.

My personal dream, other than becoming Ayumu’s wife, had been to run either a café or a flower shop. But with my options broadened like this, I might shoot for a different profession. One that enabled me to spend as much time with Ayumu as possible.

_Heh-heh, somehow, I’m looking forward to it. Will others see this as too calculating of me?_  

But it was something I attained through hard work, so I didn’t feel guilty.

“Yes, a perfect answer, as usual.”

After writing the answer on the blackboard without any hesitation, Rir turned around and went back to her place (which was next to Shuu’s). From how she appeared here, Rir probably came over as “cute but level-headed”, as was her reputation at school. Still, her deformed, barely legible letters were adorable.

“It’s incredible, it has only been a month since you came to Japan, Fún, and you can both read Japanese and solve problems without issue. And that isn’t all, you have been improving dramatically like the Joujou married couple and the harem king. Could it be that something caused you to do that? Normal students would be satisfied if they were both good-looking and able to follow the coursework.”

Laughter echoed through the classroom. This teacher often made jokes like this. Ayumu and I weren’t married yet… though it would happen at some point. But his interpretation of Rir advancing so quickly because she studied relentlessly, wasn’t that far off the mark.

“Well, time is up. The ones on school duty today, please make sure to do your jobs.”

Class was over. Next was lunchbreak, and consequently lunch. Today, I felt like eating with the girls’ group rather than Ayumu.

“Ayumu~. I’ll be joining the other girls today.”  

“Alright. Then I’ll eat with Shuu,” he replied before making his way to the boys’ group.

“Ayumu is coming over here~!”  

“Sit down here, Ayumu[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-559-consultation-at-school-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116638)!”  

“My! You’re not eating with your esteemed bride today?”  

“I’ll be eating with you guys.”

For some reason, they always treated him like a princess. Well, it was the same for me.

“Rir!”  

“Mika!”

Today, Rir also mingled with the girls rather than eat with Shuu. I joined the group.

“The two of you are eating with us today, huh?”  

“Yes, I felt like it.”  

“Yeah, same for me.”

They seemed to consider me joining them as unusual. Maybe I spent too much time with Ayumu.

“Woah… that’s one amazing boxed lunch!” one of the girls exclaimed.  

“Thank you for saying that.”

Rir’s lunch box was extremely lavish. Well, it wasn’t in quantity, but you could tell the quality on a single glance.

“Y-Yours is as amazing as usual, Mika,” the girl added. “You know, your cooking suddenly became so good, it’s like you’re no longer human.  

“Eh-heh-heh, you think so? Maybe it’s because of all the love for Ayumu I’m putting in there?”

That probably had nothing to do with it. Excessively gushing over my love life was bound to cause them to look at me in scorn, so I was planning to restrain myself, but it just slipped out.

“Oh, could I visit you at home today, Mika?” Rir asked.  

“Huh? I mean, that’s fine.”

She suddenly made that request in a manner so the others wouldn’t overhear us. This was rare… no, it was practically the first time she asked for such a thing.  

_I wonder what she’s going for._

“Woof, I have some things I’d like to talk about in female company.”  

“My, don’t tell me there are problems with Shuu? Alright, will you come to my house, then?”  

“Yeah, I will! Visiting a friend at their home was something I always wanted to do.”

She never had been able to make these experiences, so she seemed happy as she said that. We lived under the same roof in Anazumu, so she could’ve visited me there all the time, but… that probably wasn’t the same. Walking to a friend’s home was part of the fun.

“In that case… I’ll invite Sakura too and we can have fun by the three of us who all know about Anazumu.”  

“Yeah! I’m already getting excited! Here, you can have some of my Karaage.”  

“Thank you.”

Rir, who loved meat some much, offered me some of hers. She must’ve been overjoyed.

That aside… for some reason, I could hear the boys blabbing about Shuu’s harem… In any case, I ignored them and enjoyed Rir’s cooking. It was way too good.

# 560 – Girls’ Meeting – 1 (Mika)

“Pardon the intrusion!”  

“Come on in!”

Rir had come to my home. On Earth, I barely every saw her in anything other than her school uniform or training attire, so her casual outfit felt fresh. She usually wore cute clothes.

“Woof! So, this is where you and Sakura live…?”  

“It is! Should we go to my room? Sakura is waiting there.”  

“Alright.”

I showed her to my room. Our girls’ meeting, during which we’d talk about our respective partners in detail, would now begin.  

Quite exhaustive detail, at that. Since the men in question weren’t present.

“Hey Rir, come in!”  

“Hello, Sakura!”

Normally, you’d talk more politely to someone older than you, whom you’d only known for a few months… but for some reason Sakura used casual speech with Rir[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-560-girls-meeting-1-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116640).

“We got lots of sweets, too.”  

“Hang on, you started eating them already, Sakura?”  

“You thought I’d just sit still[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-560-girls-meeting-1-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116640) with milk chocolate and Konpeitou[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-560-girls-meeting-1-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-116640) in front of me, Sis?”

My sister, who’d usually just stare at the treats with drool hanging from her mouth while waiting, when other girls came to visit, had started before us. How disrespectful!

“Whatever. Have a seat, Rir.”  

“Alright, woof… so this is your room on Earth, Mika? If I had to describe it, I guess I’d use the words ‘girly and neat’.”

The way she judged my room was not how Japanese people normally would put it. Did she understand the concept of neatness? Though I myself wasn’t sure whether I did.  

Still, people often said that my room looked neat.

“Can you see Alim’s room from here?”  

“You can, I mean, you can even open his window if you stretch out your arm.”  

“Huh…”

But right now, the curtains were closed. This was a girls’ only meeting, so even Ayumu, who was male on Earth, wouldn’t be allowed to peek.

“By the way, Sis. You never told me why we gathered here. Only that Rir would come to visit.”  

“Huh? We have a rare opportunity today, so I was thinking of having an intense talk about some things. Things that aren’t for the boys’ ears.”

Sakura, who was still more like a child and hadn’t had an intense kiss with Kanata so far, gulped.  

_Heh-heh-heh, let’s see if she can keep up with this conversation._

“Woof, this salami is so good.”  

“I prepared it, assuming you’d like it, Rir.”  

“Thank you, Sakura.”

_Oh, looks like I lost Rir somewhere along the way, too._

We didn’t have such an opportunity every day, so I wanted to talk about all kinds of things, not just eat snacks.

“Incidentally, we discussed quite some time ago why we started dating our respective boyfriends, didn’t we?”  

“Woof, we did.”  

“You also told us that you already had your first time, Sis.”

_Why does she remember exactly that part? Let’s tease her a bit._

“I remember… But it’s quite different now compared to how it had been back then.”  

“It is?”  

“Yes. Oh, but no telling others, alright?”  

“Woof, I won’t.”

The three of us got close together in the center of the room. It would be embarrassing if, though unlikely, anyone outside overheard us.

“So, what is different, Sis?”  

“How often we did it.”  

“How… often…!”

My sister, still quite pure, made big eyes. Rir instead, likely experienced herself at this point, looked calm.

“Woof, I’ve also slept quite a few times with Shuu since then, but… how many are you talking about, Mika?”  

“Quite… quite a few times!?” Sakura gasped.  

“As for that…” I trailed off and then used a ballpoint pen to write down a number in a nearby notebook. It was higher than you could count with your fingers and toes. I had already resolved myself to be frank today. In all aspects.

“Eek… Are you this debauched, Big Sis!?”  

“Don’t call it that! I’m simply heads over heels in love!”  

“Woof, judging from the number, you do it once every two days.”  

“You’re correct.”

It was exactly as she had guessed. She was always quick at calculations. That aside, I didn’t expect my younger sister to brand me a debauched woman.

“Sakura, you are aware that the day will come when you do the deed too, aren’t you?”  

“I-I guess.”  

“It’s natural. I love Ayumu from the bottom of my heart. You think that way about Kanata too, don’t you?”  

“W-Well…”

I might as well tell them the other part, too. These two… Sakura was a given, but I wouldn’t have told her this much, if I didn’t trust Rir.

“Also… I did it on this side, too.”  

“B-Bwuh!?”  

“Woof! Good for you!”

Their reactions were quite different.

“I-In that case, Sis, did you get pregnant!?”  

“…We obviously used birth control!”

“Where did you do it?” Rir asked, sounding quite interested.

This topic seemed to have tickled her fancy, after all. I’d be in trouble if the other girls in class heard about this. Absolutely.

“In a love hotel.”  

“Woof~… I tried to get Shuu to go to one of those with me too, but he refused.”  

“He did!?”

_Why in the world would he do that? Was Rir’s charm not enough for this beefcake?_

1. I know it’s a cultural thing, and Japan is still tame compared to South Korea, but as someone from a place where no kid would ever talk to another kid politely, regardless which one is older, and where people usually decide within days of meeting whether they are going to talk to each other politely or casually, this feels incredibly alien to me.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-560-girls-meeting-1-mika/#easy-footnote-1-116640)

The original is 猫にマタタビだって思わなかったの？. 猫にマタタビ might be related to 猫に木天蓼お女郎に小判 (“everyone has their favorite”, or “pick the right thing to please someone”), but this doesn’t really suit the context. # 561 – Girls’ Meeting – 2 (Mika)

“Why would he refuse?”

_Just what was Shuu thinking? I mean, it had been an offer from his girlfriend from the beginning… Well, with Ayumu, it’s also about 70% me who is the one to initiate._

“Woof, it’s apparently forbidden to stay at these hotels if you’re underage… He said it would cause issues if anyone saw us, since his father works at the police.”  

“Oh, that makes sense.”

_It probably can’t be helped, but was the law really the reason he refused? I can’t help thinking there are some personal issues involved. Well… it isn’t my place to comment on that._

“Then why not seduce him at home? On a day when his parents aren’t there.”  

“When his parents are gone… and it’s just the two of you…!” Sakura mumbled.  

“Woof, it might work… I’ll try it when I have the chance.”

Putting aside Sakura who was trembling at this point, Rir should be successful soon. If he turned her down again, there was something wrong with Shuu.

“Still… the thought of him refusing worries me.”  

“Does he do that so often?”  

“Woof, I try to get him to have sex once every two days, like you and Alim apparently do, Mika. But… I only manage to get him to do it once or twice per week.”

_So, he refuses two out of three times? Well… Shuu’s sense of virtue is strong, so she might have a hard time._

From a societal viewpoint, once per week was probably normal, but we had lots of free time in Anazumu, which, in my opinion, should increase the frequency.

“Once… per week…! S-So often…”  

“Did you ask him why he refuses?”  

“Yes, first he said it’s exhausting to do it two days in a row. So, I asked him once every two days, but now… he says he isn’t in the mood most of the time.”

_Not in the mood… if he isn’t up for it, there’s not much she can do. We don’t force it if one of us doesn’t want to either… Though if Ayumu tried to force me… I might go along with it._  

_I-I’m probably an exception to that rule!_

“Well, not much do be done about that.”  

“Woof, both partners need to consent! Though if he asked, I’d be up for it anytime.”

It was adorable how her cheeks turned slightly red as she said that. As for Sakura, she already looked like a tomato.

“So? What are you and Shuu doing?”  

“Woof… what we always do, I guess? Or do you mean… during sex?”  

“That should be obvious from the conversation.”

_I want to know. How does that beefcake do it?_

These topics were the best part of gossiping among only girls, if you asked me. Well, you could only bring it up with people you got along well enough.

“…N-Normal stuff? But…”  

“”But?””  

“H-He fondles my breasts and… he often d-does stuff with my chest…”

_So, Ayumu was right when he told me that Shuu likes them big._

As far as I could see in the bath, hers were about as big as mine. Maybe slightly bigger. In British units, they would be DD-cup…[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-561-girls-meeting-2-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116642)! It had been some time since then, and there was the chance they’d get even bigger.

“H-He fondles… your breasts…!”  

“What stuff?”  

“A-All kinds! I won’t tell you any more!”

_I wonder what exactly they’re doing, for her to blush that much. Well, delving deeper into this won’t do any good, so I guess I’ll change the topic._

“Even so, your breasts are pretty big, Rir.”  

“Woof, they are… Moreover, they recently started hurting for some reason…”  

“Huh, they hurt?”  

“Yeah, they seem to tighten up…”

In that case, they really might be getting bigger as I hypothesized earlier.

“Did you measure them?”  

“No, I only tried to measure them once since coming to Earth.”  

“Right now, the bra you’re wearing is the same size as mine, right?”  

“I think so.”

_…Well._

“Can I touch them?”  

“B-Big Sis…!?”  

“Yes, if it’s you, Mika, I don’t mind.”  

“Rir!?”

After getting her permission, I grabbed her breasts.

“Ah… ngh… woof.”

_Hrm… I clearly need to open my hands more compared to when I touch my own._  

When I put one of my hands to my own chest for reference, the different was striking. In other words…

“Rir, you’ve gone up by one cup-size.”  

“Woof, really?”

In any case, hers felt very soft. They were different from Sakura’s and mine. And Alim’s, obviously.

“I wonder why they got bigger.”  

“…Must’ve been because of Shuu.”  

“W-Woof! We still haven’t done it on this side!”  

“Things that happen on the other side might have an effect here… All that studying we did, for example.”

Well, there was a difference between body and mind, but I left it at that for now[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-561-girls-meeting-2-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116642). It was fun to see her blush.

“…I guess.”  

“Yes, I’m sure of it.”  

“…Woof, now it’s your turn, Mika. What do you guys do?”

_Ah, I was hoping switching the topic to our breasts would make her forget that part._

Earlier, she gave an answer, so I had to do the same.

“Normal stuff, completely normal. In the first place, we’re younger there than even Sakura, so we’re limited in what we can do.”  

“Really?”  

“R-Really!”

# 562 – Boys’ Meeting – 1

“Sorry for calling you here.”  

“It’s fine. Rir is at Mika’s place today, so ain’t like I got anythin’ to do.”

Shuu had come to my home. I didn’t know how long it had been since he was here the last time. Though until a few months ago, he visited once per week.

“So, what am I here for?”  

“For a boys’ meeting.”  

“A boys’ meetin’?”  

“Exactly.”

After putting away his shoes rather carefully and mumbling the customary “sorry for the intrusion”, Shuu steeped from entryway into the house.

“Look, right now, Mika and the other girls have gathered, likely to have some girls’ meeting. The whole Anazumu crew.”  

“Right, so they’ll ask Rir stuff.”  

“Well, it’s been while since you came here, so let’s have a boys’ meeting while we have the time.”

After entering my room, Shuu sat down in his usual spot (on a sitting cushion he brough here a long time ago). I opened one of my closet’s drawers and brought out some modest snacks.

“You say ‘boys’ meetin”, but it’s just the two of us.”  

“It can’t be helped. Kanata is currently busy with stock market investment. And I wanted to limit it to people who know about Anazumu.”

From what my brother told me, Monday was an especially busy day. He even put off visiting Sakura.

“…Kanata, huh? Just how much money has he made at this point? I hear he’s constantly playin’ the market…”  

“It’s not just that, he apparently also started to trade in foreign currency. To begin with, he developed quite a few products on his own and licensed them…”

I wasn’t sure how much money he had earned so far. He didn’t talk about it much, but I once overheard him tell Dad that he had “enough to buy a house”.

“At the end of the day, the guy is a super-genius… What was his IQ again?”  

“I forgot.”

But it was bound to be extremely high. He was so bright, even some international corporations had their eyes on him. Though one of those was the institute where they tried to find out how Sakura’s eyes had been healed, which wasn’t a bad place.

He was still a middle schooler, and thus limited in what he could do, but the thought of what he’d accomplish as an adult made me shiver. If they hadn’t been summoned to Anazumu, he’d probably have devoted his life to researching a method for restoring Sakura’s eyesight.

“Well, today isn’t about my brother, it’s our boys’ meeting, so let’s talk about things that are normal at those times.”  

“Stuff you talk ’bout on a boys’ meetin’? You mean who’s the cutest girl and what video games are the most fun?”

That certainly were typical topics among male middle and high schoolers.

“I mean, you keep callin’ it ‘boys’ meetin”, but are you even a boy?”  

“Huh? I am! On this side, at least!”  

“I ain’t so sure. Just what are you wearin’ today?” He stared at me intently. The bottom, the top, then the bottom again. Finally, he snorted. “Hot pants? Ain’t it a bit too chilly for those?”  

“Eh, it’s fine, they’re easy to move in. Why, don’t tell me my tights got you excited, Shuu?”  

“They might if I didn’t know your real gender.”

_Grr, but it’s nice that he’s being honest. Others just stare silently! Assuming I’m a girl._

“Well, if I really were a girl, I might have confessed to you.”  

“Nope, I already got an awesome girlfriend in Rir.”

I didn’t know how often we had this kind of banter.  

_It’s not like we’re gay… there’s a difference._

“So, what are we goin’ to talk about today, then? If you got nothin’, let’s play video games. I brought one just in case.”  

“No, today is our boys’ meeting, so I want to talk about things with _enthusiasm_, like girls do in their meetings.”

At my words, Shuu came to sudden stop. Then he spoke with a look of revulsion.

“You serious? That’s awful!”

_It should work… I’ll get him on board with this._

“I am serious!”  

“What, you’re actually serious ’bout this? That’s hilarious!”  

“…”  

“…”

“”…Hah.””

Both of us sighed simultaneously.

“Damn fool. You actually think Mika and Rir have this kinda talk?”  

“You’ve been at boys’ meetings, so…”  

“That don’t mean we gotta talk in this creepy way. Ah-ha-ha-ha-ha-ha!”  

“Heh-heh-ha-ha-ha-ha!”

_Not good, I can’t stop laughing. This is way too funny…!_

“Hah… well, there is something I want to talk about today. What we think about our girlfriends.”  

“Phew… true, girls often talk how they feel ’bout their boyfriends.”  

“Exactly, let’s do that.”

He rested his chin on his hand and started thinking.  

_Does he have something he wants to talk about, too?_

“I guess, should I start, then? With my thoughts ’bout Rir.”  

“Is there anything about her that you’re unsatisfied with?”  

“…We’re both human. No matter how much you love each other, there’ll be stuff you’re unhappy ’bout.”  

“I guess that’s true.”

Even though you could say that Mika and I had feelings for each other since a long time ago, I couldn’t deny there were unpleasant parts (Mika’s dislike of my gaming habits, for example).

“So? What are you unsatisfied about?”  

“…Guess I can tell you.”

He crossed his arms and took a deep breath. Just what was this mood? Was his dissatisfaction with her this big?

He finally spoke. And what he said…

“…Rir is way too cute.”

# 563 – Boys’ Meeting – 2

“You’re dissatisfied by her being _too cute_?”  

“I am… well, guess it’s more insecure than unsatisfied.”

That didn’t make sense. Wasn’t your girlfriend being cute a good thing?

From what Hunkydorky – our handsome otaku dork – told me, Rir didn’t compare unfavorably when she stood next to us. And when I asked him “so, would the other girls look bad if they stood next to Mika and me?” he replied “why yes, they very much would” without hesitation.

“What are you insecure about?”  

“Well… I feel like I can no longer stop myself if we keep goin’ like this.”  

“Oh…”

Shuu was an adolescent boy. I mean, looking at him, you couldn’t see him as anything else. In addition to that, he was already in a relationship with Rir, where they had sex, so having insecurities wasn’t strange.

“How often do you do it currently?”  

“Once per week in Anazumu. On this side… we’ve only kissed and napped side by side. That’s ’bout it.”  

“So, when you say you’re scared you’ll lose yourself, what kind of frequency are you talking about?”  

“Daily… or once every two days.”  

“…”

_Not good, Mika and I do it once every two days._  

It was usually her who initiated, but there were also times when I asked her. With that combined, we ended up doing it every other day.

“Shuu, that’s awfully hard to say, but…”  

“What now?”  

“Mika and I have sex every other day.”  

“You… you serious?”  

“I am.”

His eyes popped open in shock. It was unavoidable.

“Uhm… are you guys alright?”  

“We use proper preparations, so yes, we’re doing fine. Do you think that’s bad?”  

“N-Nah…”

Shuu ate one of the spread-out rice crackers. But I could see the trembling in his face.

“Gotcha… so, could it be you also did it on this side…?”  

“Yep. Mika and I have graduated from being children.”  

“N-No way…”

I still remembered that day. Mika’s grown-up body… it was a world of difference compared to Anazumu.

“What do I do…?”  

“How does Rir think about it? Is she fine with once per week?”  

“Nah, she asks me to do it once every two days.”  

“Don’t tell me you turn her down?”  

“…Guess I messed up, after all.”

He seemed uncharacteristically weak. Though it explained why he felt so insecure.

“Why do you refuse? If it’s because you’re worried you won’t be able to stop yourself, you should explain that to her.”  

“N-Nah… that ain’t all. Somehow… I don’t want to.”  

“Is it because of her?”  

“That ain’t it! I love Rir!!”

Untypically for him, he kept getting louder and louder. Just how big was her influence on him? In any case, I could guess what he was thinking.

“Shh… Rir is in the neighboring building…”  

“Ah… you think she heard me?”  

“Even if she did, I don’t think she’d be bothered by you saying you love her. Calm down.”  

“I-I guess.”

The somewhat agitated ball of muscles sat back down.

“So, you love her. What exactly makes you not want to do it?”  

“… I said it before, it feels like I’m losin’ myself… that’s what I don’t like.”  

“You think you won’t be able to stop yourself, huh? She’s exactly your type, isn’t she?”  

“Yup.”

He replied easily, not even trying to deny it. He probably saw no reason to hide it, since we all knew what kind of person Rir was.

“Maybe ’cause she knows that too, Rir-”  

“Eh?”

He whispered into my ear. What he told me was a bit shocking.

“Seriously?”  

“Yep.”  

“…But Mika did that for me too, you know?”  

“Really?”

Still, it sounded like Rir was quite bold herself. She probably acted that way since, in her mind, “making Shuu happy” was the highest priority.

“So, were you even once the one to initiate?”  

“Nah.”  

“…You’re joking.”  

“I ain’t.”

He replied as if it was the most normal thing ever. Did he actually think that it was fine to leave things like this?

“Are you happy with that?”  

“I-I think it’s awful. That’s another part I’m anxious ’bout.”

_Ah, at least he is aware. Still._

“…You’re a wuss, dude.”  

“Yep, I realized that only recently.”

I never thought he could be that much of a weakling. It had to be frustrating for Rir.

_Hrm…_

“So, on top of refusing her advances, you never make any yourself… If this was Mika, she’d glare at me in dissatisfaction.”  

“I know… I’m seriously anxious ’bout that part.”

It made sense; his dissatisfaction with Rir was that she was so cute he had to fight his desires, causing him anxiety, which wasn’t that strange.

“…Dude, isn’t it more that you’re dissatisfied with yourself rather than her?”  

“You really are my closest friend. You understand me so well.”

The dejection on his face was even clearer than before. This was what happened when a boy who’d (convinced himself that he’d) never been in love, got a girlfriend.

“What are you going to do, Shuu?”  

“…Apologize to her, obviously. And be the one who initiates on this side… Though we can’t go to a love hotel, it’s against the law.”

_Th-That’s it. I got through to him, but will it work?_  

_…It has to!_

“-I’ll ask her at home, the next time my parents are gone for the day.”

He seemed to have made up his mind… his face looked the same as last year, right before he left for the intra scholastic tournament. When he declared something this boldly, he appeared quite manly. The day for Rir’s dissatisfactions to disappear might be close.

“That’s good to hear. Do your best!”  

“Right!”

It would be perfect if his courage to ask her would cure him of his worries of losing himself. Though it would also be fine, if it happened on the day he was thinking of.

# 564 – Girls’ Meeting – 3 (Mika)

“W-Woof…” In a rare case for her, Rir glared at me scornfully.

_B-But it really is just normal stuff! All I can do is act like the people in such scenes in manga._

“Oh, well. In any case, what should I do? Would it be better to stop my advances?”  

“Are you fine with that?”  

“Woof… I love Shuu, so I desire his warmth, but it seems there is no other way. If pushing doesn’t work, I might as well try putting off.”  

“It’s ‘if pushing doesn’t work, I might as well try pulling[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-564-girls-meeting-3-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116763)‘, Rir…”

True enough, Shuu wasn’t as easy to understand as Ayumu, who was always sticking to me, and Kanata, who jealously watched over Sakura.

“Woof, what does he think of my body, and this verbal tick of mine.”  

“Oh, so you realized that yourself, Rir?”  

“Yeah, but only after coming to this world. I used to be a wolf, so it’s not something I can fix[3](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-564-girls-meeting-3-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-3-116763).”

No one ever brought it up at school. Maybe that changed once people were somewhere private.

“Hm~, I’m always with him, does he think I’m too clingy…? I hug him all the time.”  

“Isn’t that fine?”  

“Woof?”

He clearly had feelings for her, at least, so I couldn’t imagine him not being happy to be embraced by a girl with such a nice body.

“Woof~… I want to ask him what he really thinks. But if I keep pestering him, he might no longer want to spend time with me and-”  

“I think you should ask him when you get home. You could whisper it to him while you hug him. With his personality, I’m sure he’ll give you a reply.”  

“You might be right…”

_I wonder if this will really be enough to solve the issue._

_Geez… she’s way too much in the springtime of her life! That certainly doesn’t make it easier for Shuu to understand her feelings. But I’ve known him since we were little, so I know how he ticks. Once he has romantic feelings for a girl, he’ll love her as long as she stays with him. So, all her worries should be resolved already._

_After all, just like it won’t happen with Ayumu and me, and Kanata and Sakura, there’s no way Rir will ever stop having feelings for Shuu[4](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-564-girls-meeting-3-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-4-116763)._

**“-I love Rir!!”**

“Woof?”

We could hear Shuu’s voice from the neighboring building. If he was saying that, he was probably talking with Ayumu. There was something before and after, so it probably wasn’t intentional, but the timing was perfect.

“Rir, I’m pretty sure Shuu is talking with Ayumu right now, and we heard some of that.”  

“W-Woof… he said, he loves me…”  

“I’m confident they didn’t hear our talk, so this must be his true feelings!”

Even Sakura who’d been whimpering and trembling was back with us. Rir’s eyes were moist, and she seemed quite happy.

“Awoo… I love you too, Shuu…”

With all that considered, Rir’s plan was bound to succeed. Though it was still possible Shuu would refuse if he was too embarrassed. But I had the feeling she’d get there, if she took him by surprise and pushed through.

“Once you get home, hug him while you tell him that you heard it.”  

“Woof, I’ll do that…”

Her eyes were those of a maiden in love.

_I’m getting jealous, what do I do? I also want to make out with Ayumu! I’ll go to his room later._  

_…Oh, and I’ll also try that stuff Rir mumbled about doing with Shuu at home._

“Did that clear up your worries?”  

“Woof, it did!”  

“That’s good to hear! Then let’s enjoy the rest of the day. It’s not just our girls’ meeting, the best part of going to someone’s home is to have fun and play games!”  

“Awoo!”

#### Footnotes:

1. In the original, Rir confuses ドン引き (“being put off (by someone’s words, behavior, etc.)”) with 引く (“to pull”). I’m not happy with that localization, but I couldn’t think of anything better.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-564-girls-meeting-3-mika/#easy-footnote-1-116763)

2. The verb in the original is 愛想を突かれた (“affection being poked/stabbed”). This sounds weird, and there’s a similar verb 愛想を尽かす, meaning “fall out of love”, which would make more sense here. Not sure if that’s correct, though.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-564-girls-meeting-3-mika/#easy-footnote-2-116763)

3. I’m genuinely surprised it was even brought up.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-564-girls-meeting-3-mika/#easy-footnote-3-116763)

4. That sounds overly optimistic.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-564-girls-meeting-3-mika/#easy-footnote-4-116763)

# 565 – Destructive Introduction

A certain man opened his eyes. Then he looked left and right.

“Guardrails…”

The man, someone who’d come from another world, showed an expression of relief as he saw the guardrails painted white along the road.

“Did I finally return?”

Traveling a different world for what amounted to hundreds of years had been harsh on him. His only wish had been to “return to his hometown”, but he ended up turning the whole of humanity against himself and was almost annihilated, almost destroying himself… but with the help of a girl from his own world, he nevertheless somehow managed to return.

“In any case, where am I?”

He didn’t have a map on hand. However, there were a few things in his suit – likely the clothing he’d been wearing before he was sent[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-565-destructive-introduction/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116766) to another world.

“There it is… my smartphone.”

He hadn’t touched the shining flat device in centuries. However, possibly since it was so ingrained in him, he still somewhat remembered how to use it. Though he wasn’t fast at it by any means.

He opened an app that happened to be installed, which could display his current location on a map.

“Over there, such a device would absolutely be legend grade…” While he pondered that, a map of his surroundings appeared. “Hm…? It looks like I’m not that far away.”

From his ancient memories, he compared the place where he used to live, before being spirited away, with his current location. Ancient memories… or they should have been. The man didn’t notice that said memories were rapidly restored due to his return to Earth.

“In any case, it’s dark… looks like it’s… around 9 pm. What about the date!?”

Even assuming he had returned, there was the crucial question if several decades had passed since his departure, like with Urashima Taro. Realizing this only now, the man immediately checked the device’s calendar.

“The day after… Looks like today is the day after it happened.”

He once more looked deeply relieved.

“My wallet is also where it should be, and my money too… I should head home for now.”

He first walked towards a metro station, from which he could reach his destination a few stops away. As he walked, he thought about various things.

_-Once I’m home, let’s eat something, maybe Katsudon. But before that, I should have a nice drink._  

_-The next circus performance should still be in its preparatory stage, so let’s take tomorrow off._  

_-I need to give my thanks to this “Joujou Ayumu” before long. The family name sounds unusual, so I should find her soon if I use a detective agency._  

_-I wonder what a good way to thank her would be. The best I could give her as circus manager, would be a lifetime VIP pass._  

_-It also sounded like she has friends she cares about a great deal, so let’s make that three to five passes._

Deep in thought, his eyes suddenly fell on two houses. It was quite dark, so he couldn’t read the name plates. But for some strange reason, the houses caught his interest.

“Well, today was lotsa fun! See ya!”

A rather healthy and fit looking boy exited one of the houses while waving his hand.

“Woof, thank you for today! Let’s have another girls’ meeting at some point.”

And from the other house, a girl with ashen, nearly white hair emerged. She was surprisingly good-looking. Though it didn’t reach the level of Alim Nariwei.

More than that, what surprised the man was that she had something that screamed “Anazumu” about her. She looked as if she had come from there to this world. The man pinched his own cheek. The hypothesis that this was yet another world, different from both Earth and Anazumu, came to his mind. Still, when he checked his phone, it clearly showed the area where he’d grown up.

Pondering this felt like a chore, so he decided not to let it bother him, instead assuming the girl was an exchange student somewhat fluent in Japanese.

“Sh-Shuu!”  

“Rir…”

The two people who had exited the houses seemed acquainted and called out their names, as they saw each other. But when he immediately saw them walk away harmoniously, though somewhat distantly, with linked arms, he changed his assumption to them being more than friends.

“Oops, this isn’t the time for that.”

He started walking again, feeling young and vigorous himself. But then he stopped in his tracks once more. His eyes fell on someone… or rather, a statue.

“Is this…?”

It felt as if he had seen this statue before. It looked rather unusual. He used the light on his smartphone to see it better.

“…!?”

It was as he’d thought. He remembered seeing it. It looked like the transfer device Alim Nariwei had brought out just a short time ago (from the man’s perspective). And memories from much longer ago also arose.

It made him wonder, once more, whether this was Earth, after all. As these thoughts echoed in his mind, a stranger’s whisper joined them.

⟦Offer a prayer, Jester and Guide.⟧

“Wha-…!”

Before he knew it, the man took the characteristic pose to pray to the gods in Anazumu. The next moment, his consciousness fled.

---

**TL notes:**  

Well, that’s not ominous at all…

You may have noticed a big incongruity here. Namely the date of Mehpistophales’ departure and return. To make sure, I went back to chapter 177 to check if I made a mistake there, but no, it 100% says that he was spirited away one month _before_ Alim died. And this chapter’s events clearly happen after chapter 564, so this point should be 1.5 to 2 months _after_ Alim’s original time of death.

Either something messed with his memories on return, or the Author made a big retcon. Only time will tell.

#### Footnotes:

1. The original is 転載 (“reprinting”). It doesn’t seem to have a homophone with something meaning “sending/transferring”, but I can only assume it’s an error

+++

# 566 – The Circus is Coming!?

“Good morning.”  

“Morning, Rir!”

At school, Rir and Mika greeted each other like good friends.  

_Come to think of it, I wonder what they talked about when they met yesterday. I’m curious… but it’s probably safe to say that some was about us._

“So… how did it go afterwards?”  

“Woof, still no change. Though I managed to get him to let me sleep next to him in his bed at night.  

“Well, over there, you’re sleeping in the same bed all the time, so you can’t exactly call this progress…”  

“Woof.”

It sounded like Shuu had featured heavily in their talk yesterday. He was currently talking with Yamagami, so he probably didn’t hear what they just said.

“What did you talk about yesterday?

I decided to just nonchalantly ask them. But Mika merely puffed out her cheeks as she often did, when she was unhappy with me. Meaning, she wouldn’t tell me anything.

“Please don’t puff out your cheeks,” I told her, before poking them, forcing her to expel the air.  

“Mph…”

At school… or rather, in front of others, we regularly acted like this, so people saw us as a sickeningly sweet couple, though I didn’t mind that.

Rir gave an amused chuckle at the sight and then continued.

“Woof~! As a matter of fact, he promised to go on another date with me this week.”

Now that she mentioned it, they were on a date last week. It completely slipped my mind, but it was only the day before yesterday in this world, when Mika and I became adults here. Shocking. It felt like more than two weeks had passed since then… which wasn’t exactly wrong.

“Where will you go?” Mika asked her.  

“To a game arcade.”  

“A game arcade…?”

You’d think there would be other, more standard date spots in the area. Like the amusement park, the aquarium, or the zoo. Well, rather than that, there was one thing I was curious about.

“Does that work for Shuu? Isn’t the intra scholastic tournament in a few weeks?”  

“I asked him the same question, but he replied, ‘I have three times as much time as a normal person, so it’ll work out’.”

True enough, he could train in Anazumu. He could also use the item creation machine I gave him to make something like a robot to serve as a training partner. Additionally, we had magic rooms that sped up time, so it wasn’t just three times as much.

“That makes sense, I hope you’ll have fun.”  

“I will! Oh… Mika.”  

“What is it?”

Rir beckoned Mika over and whispered something into her ear. A short time later, Mika replied with a “That’s great! Keep at it seducing him.” I had no idea what this was about, but it sounded like things were going fine.

“Oh, Ali, Mika, Rir, there you are!”  

“Huh? Did something happen, Sana?” Mika asked.

Sanada, our resident news specialist, came over to us. Usually when she approached us like this, she either had a scoop or was trying to confirm a piece of gossip.  

_I wonder which one it is today._

“I just got my hand on some great news!”  

“What happened?”  

“Y-You won’t believe it! In two weeks, the Love Long Circus will be coming to town and perform!”  

“Really!?”

_Is that actually such great news? I expected it would take years until my reunion with Mr. Mitsuo. Didn’t this happen way too fast[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-566-the-circus-is-coming/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116768)?_

“It’s true! Right now, they’re in the middle of setting up the tent in the adjacent town!”  

“The Love Long Circus, huh…?”  

“You know about it, Rir?”  

“Only from my memories… Since it’s one of the four biggest circuses in the world[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-566-the-circus-is-coming/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116768).”

To think she had even been provided with such details. Did that circus also hold performances in Norway?

“You three are the very first people I told, you know? Though I am planning to tell everyone else soon. I mean, you guys make up this school’s best-known couples… Going there would be perfect for a date, wouldn’t it?”  

“Woof…! Thank you so much for telling us!”  

“Thank you~!”

It was nice that she thought about us.

This was the third time the Love Long Circus came to this town. The first time had been before I was born. The second, when Mika and I had been seven or eight years old. And the third time was now.

“According to past performances, tickets will be 2800 yen if you book in advance, and 3200 on the day of the performance.”  

“That should be something Ayumu and I can afford.”  

“Yeah, it should work for Shuu and me, too. I’ll ask him later.”

A 2800-yen entry fee… well, that was normal enough.

Assuming we went there, Saturday or Sunday would work best. If Kanata and Sakura joined us, we’d be a group of six… though it was also possible to go there separately as three groups of two. It was a rare occasion, so going there with the six of us might be better.

“How nice… I wish I also had a boyfriend. Someone to go with me to watch the circus… Hah, guess I’ll have to go there with my family.”  

“You’ll be fine, Sana, you’re cute.”  

“…That’s not much consolation coming from you, Mika.”

Well, if you asked me, she was among the better-looking girls. But saying that might come back to bite me, so I kept my mouth shut.

“Oh, whatever! I’ve got people to inform!”

With regained enthusiasm, Sanada charged off toward where the rest of our classmates were chatting.

_In any case, it was good information. I look forward to reuniting with Mr. Mitsuo. Heh-heh-heh._

#### Footnotes:

1. If Mephistophales had actually arrived more than two months before this point, that would have been ample time to find Alim on Earth and shift the performance schedule to facilitate a meeting.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-566-the-circus-is-coming/#easy-footnote-1-116768)

2. Now it suddenly went from “somewhat well known” to “one of the four biggest in the world”? In that case, how was the disappearance of the manager not a big thing in the news?[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-566-the-circus-is-coming/#easy-footnote-2-116768)
