# 567 – How to Relationship – 1 (Shuu)

It was Saturday. With the intra scholastic tournament drawing near, our club activities had increased. Well, Sunday was still off.

In a rare occasion for her, Mom who usually acted as the housewife, would be gone from Sunday to Monday. That happened a few times per month. Well, she was a self-defense instructor for women.

Pops would be at work as usual, so once we came back from our date on Sunday, it would just be the two of us. When that time came… it was my turn to seduce Rir. On second thought, I had never been the one to directly initiate.

Usually, Rir either wore something suggestive, invited me to take a bath with her, or straight up asked if I wanted to have sex. And I’d usually decline. Since I didn’t feel like it.

Even on Earth, I had already declined her advances once. No matter how you looked at it, she must have been unsatisfied. But she never made a mention of it, even though I’d told her she could come with anything to me.

_She’s probably still puttin’ up with it. And even knowin’ she’s the type to hold it in, idiot that I am never realized._

Calling me a wuss was probably obvious at this point. Though only Ayumu had done that.

_…I hope I won’t be too nervous._  

I had to bring it up in a cool, or rather, nonchalant way.

Ayumu also told me that my date idea sucked. He straight up asked me, “Why are you taking her to a game arcade? Aren’t you planning to seduce her on the same day? In that case, the amusement park or the zoo would be better!”

He was completely right. No matter how much fun Rir had at the arcade, it was a poor choice for a date. I had discussed it with Ayumu during our boys’ meeting. She might even leave me if I kept being such a useless boyfriend. No more planless dates.

She seemed to have fun no matter what we did… so if I picked something that was fun for normal girls, she’d probably be overjoyed. You could say that one of the goals was to appear like a proper boyfriend to others[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-567-how-to-relationship-1-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116771).

Also, on Saturday next week, we’d go to the circus as a group of six. I needed to inform our club instructor that we’d take that day off.

“Yaaaaaah!”

My body was lightly lifted up a tiny bit. It happened together with Rir’s adorable shout.  

_Right, looks like I’m ’bout to be thrown. Come to think of it, we’re in the middle of sparrin’ right now._

“Too bad for you.”

I immediately reacted by sweeping her legs, strongly but in way that wouldn’t hurt. That alone was enough to break her balance, regain my own stance, and then lightly throw her instead.

“I thought I finally scored a point against you, Shuu…”  

“Nah, that was great. You actually managed to lift me.”  

“…I-I guess.”

I really thought so. While her arms did have a healthy amount of meat now, they were still slender. And despite that, she was strong enough to throw a man like me.

“That was incredible, Fún.”  

“Oh, thank you for saying that, Gorilla Sensei!”

Our instructor ended up praising her. He had likely watched the whole thing from beginning to the end.

“Shuu, on the other hand, are your thoughts somewhere else?”  

“Gah… was it that obvious?”

Well, he often noticed such things.

After almost scoring a point, failing, and then learning that it only happened since I wasn’t paying attention, Rir seemed even more frustrated. It looked adorable, so I lightly patted her head, which made her perk up again with a smile.

_I wanna hug her right now, but I gotta put that off ’til we’re in a place without so many jealous eyes._

“Will you really be fine for the tournament? Well, I’d like to ask that, but I’m not really worried about you, Shuu. As for you, Fún, I’m thinking of having you participate next year.”  

“Are you serious, Teacher?” Gouda, the vice club head asked in apparent shock.

He was in the class next to ours, so he knew how much time I spent flirting with Rir and probably thought I didn’t do any training on my own.

“Do you want to give it a try, then?”  

“N-No, I’m good.”  

“Hrm, besides, I said that before, but there’s a world of difference in the sharpness of your moves, Shuu. To put it bluntly… it’s like you’re no longer human… as if you were planning to take on a tank.”

_A tank, huh…?_

I fought my fair share of stronger enemies than that. Maybe Gorilla Sensei could see the actual fighting experience I had accumulated. It was probably that.

“I guess… I never was a match for Hino from the start, and now he got even better. It’s as you say, Gorilla Sensei, we’ll probably be fine at the intra scholastic tournament.”

_Yep, I’m not plannin’ to cut any corners there. I’m goin’ to give it my all. I’ll use all that fightin’ experience I brought from over there… though, lots of that was with magic against monsters._

“Rather than that, I’m super jealous of you.”  

“Huh? You are?”  

“Yes, I am. It’s like you got everything. Your judo skills have become even better and then you have a girlfriend who’s both cute and smart…”  

“Th-Thanks…”  

“And that isn’t all. I also keep hearing how you became one of the top students of our academic year, and improved abnormally in arts, music, and sports other than judo.”

It probably looked like that from an outside perspective. It sounded awesome, but I couldn’t exactly tell him the reason.

“W-Well… I’m not sure either how it happened.”  

“Hmph… whatever. Let’s go back to training.

We started sparring again.

#### Footnotes:

1. No, the point of a date is to have fun together and possibly progress the relationship. Why care about how others see you?[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-567-how-to-relationship-1-shuu/#easy-footnote-1-116771)

# 568 – How to Relationship – 2 (Shuu)

“I’m tired.”  

“You worked hard.”

It was after 3 pm on Saturday, after club activities had ended. At this point, Rir and I were dripping with sweat, so we wanted to get home and take a shower as quickly as possible. Our school also had showers, but weirdly enough, no one ever used them.

“You stopped hugging me after club, Rir.”  

“I… I’m drenched in sweat. I don’t want to force that smell on you.”  

“I see.”

As a girl, she must’ve been more concerned than I as a boy. I obviously wasn’t enough of a degenerate to forcibly sniff her after she said that she didn’t want me to.

“Come to think of it, Shuu, have you heard? What happened to that Jizou statue, I mean.”  

“Hm? Yep, I did.”

Apparently, the statue’s head had been removed. I heard that it wasn’t Ayumu and Mika who fixed it this time, but some random passerby. It must’ve happened on Monday, but Ayumu only told me about it today. The reason it was found out this late was because said passerby had fixed it right after the head had been removed.

Well Sanada probably still would’ve found out the day after.

It was only the direct area around it that held the statue in such high regard. It was apparently famous for mysterious events occurring close to it.

“Why would someone remove the head?”  

“Might’ve been the same as with you, Rir…”  

“Oh, you mean they were controlled by something? So, someone other than me has fallen victim to it?”

_Did someone go through the same stuff she did? Or was it just some prank…?_

Considering you needed to do an Anazuman prayer to start the strange chain of events, it probably was the latter. If so, said prank might result in being haunted.

Lord Jizou was real, not just a statue, so you couldn’t treat him rudely. Though it was just us who knew that, no one else.

“What’s more important now is our date tomorrow! You’ll be taking me to the game arcade again, right?” Rir asked with a joyful look.

She looked awfully cute, but this time would be different. Would she still be happy with my new proposal?  

_…Alright._

“Nah, I was thinkin’ of goin’ somewhere else.”  

“Woof? Somewhere else? Where will you be taking me, then?”

I’d been pondering both the zoo and the amusement park. Of those two choices, the zoo sounded like the better one. But then I remembered her keen sense of smell. Consequently, going to the zoo might cause her some distress.

With that being said.

“To the amusement park.”  

“Woof! The Amusement park? Really!?”  

“Yep, I’m serious.”  

“Wow~!”

She jumped up and down like a little kid, almost dancing. The way her large, sweat-covered breasts bounced was- Nope, not going there.

“This is my first time going to an amusement park! Well, according to my Earth memories, I visited one in the past, but this will be the first time for real!”  

“I see. Well, the other day, I was talkin’ with Ayumu ’bout date spots and told him we just walked through department stores.”  

“Oh, you mean last Monday? When you shouted that you love me?” she bashfully asked right to my face.

_I wonder what kinda expression she made when she heard that. Did it make her happy?_

“Alright~, I can’t wait!”  

“You’re lookin’ forward to it that much?”  

“Yeah! I probably won’t be able to fall asleep today.”

_Unable to fall asleep… huh. Might be the same for me today. Since I gotta be the one to bring up sex tomorrow. And not as impulsively as durin’ our first time in Anazumu._  

_I-I gotta practice, if possible. Practice how to ask her. What do I do if she refuses…? I better stop thinkin’ ’bout that. To begin with, would be weird for her to refuse._

“I-If you have trouble sleepin’ you could stay in my room tonight, too.”  

“Woof!?”

She stopped moving and her already wide eyes opened even more.

“Wh-What do you think?”  

“I’d love to!”  

“Gotcha.”

_Great. If she refused, I wouldn’t have brought it up again. And while we’re at it._

“Also, once we’re back home and done showerin’, it’ll probably be ’round 4 pm, right? We could take a long walk afterwards.”  

“What’s going on with you today, Shuu? I’d be happy if we did!”

There was this hallucination again. I could see her tail and dog-ears move happily. It kept appearing.

“Shuu…! Oh.”

She was about to hug me but stopped herself. She sniffed her own armpits before hanging her head. If you asked me, she was too hard on herself. Well, she used to be a wolf, so it probably was something she couldn’t change.

“Rir, I don’t think you smell much of sweat. It was never somethin’ that bothered me from the start… and right now, there ain’t no other people around…”  

“…Woof… Awoo…”

She threw herself at me, as if her body had acted on its own. Her breasts, damp with sweat and better visible than usually, looked- Nope, still not going there.

I rubbed her back.

# 569 – Amusement Park Date (Shuu)

“Woof, we’re here!”  

“Yep, we are.”

We had finally arrived at the amusement park. She had had her arms around mine all that time, and I could sense her heart racing… or at least it felt that way. All I did was change our date location from the department store to the amusement park, but we were still this excited.

_What’s goin’ on?_

Maybe the place made the difference. This was my first time coming to the amusement park since I got a girlfriend.

“In the end, I didn’t sleep very well yesterday…”  

“You didn’t?”  

“Woof. I was already so excited, and then you proposed sleeping next to you in the same bed. I couldn’t fall asleep.”

I mean, it felt like both of us slept rather soundly. We always were next to each other in Anazumu, so we were used to it at this point. Well, we were both excited, but not to the point where we couldn’t fall asleep.

“Does that mean the amusement park will be too much for you?”  

“…I-I managed to get about five hours of sleep, so I’ll be fine!”  

“Alright, let’s go in, then.”  

“Woof.”

It was common (according to Kanata) for the guy to pay the entry fee for the amusement park. So, I obviously paid for the one day passes that’d let us use all attractions. Or at least I tried to.

“Woof, you can’t!”

Well, I somewhat expected her to object.

“Just let me pay for it.”  

“No, I have my own money!”  

“That’s not how I mean it.”  

“Not how you mean it…? Oh!”

Maybe because she understood my aim, she took a step back from the counter. This was (once again, according to Kanata) the best point for a guy to show off. We managed to enter the park without further incident.

“Which one should we ride, Rir?”  

“Wh-Which one? How about the one where this girl called Mary makes her rounds?”  

“You mean the Merry-Go-Round[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-569-amusement-park-date-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-116776)? Sure thing.”

We boarded the ride she had suggested. I was already 17, so riding the carousel felt embarrassing… or it would have if I were on my own, but strangely enough, having my girlfriend with me made all the difference.

“You’re like a prince to me, Shuu, so you should take the white horse.”  

“S-Sure.”

_I’m like a prince to her, huh? She says that occasionally and it always feels a bit awkward. Though not in a bad way._

“Awoo! This was so~ much fun!” Rir called out excitedly after it was over. There was a dazzling smile on her face.  

“That’s good to hear.”

It looked like she enjoyed riding the attraction during her first time in an amusement park.

After savoring the thrill of go-kart driving, we had lunch at the food court. Though it was somewhat after noon, since we had prioritized the rides.

“But it was fun drinking cola while gazing at each other.”  

“I guess.”

Indeed, she looked very happy.

“Woof, this is so much fun.”

She leaned her head against me and hugged me, as if to spoil me.

“You’re right. I’m havin’ fun, too.”

“Yep, I do.”

Rather than just enjoying it… it was both calming and adorable to see her expressions switch all the time.

“Good to hear! What should we ride next, then?”  

“How ’bout the pirate ship?”  

“I heard about that. Thinking about it makes my tummy feel a bit weird[2](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-569-amusement-park-date-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-2-116776). Let’s ride it!”

_____  

___

“It’s already this late?”

It was a bit past half past five in the afternoon. It would take one hour to get home, and I was thinking of stopping to have dinner on the way, so the next ride would be the last.

“In that case, the last should be…”  

“The Ferris Wheel, right?”  

“Woof~! I heard the ride on Ferris Wheel here is quite long.”

Maybe Ayumu and Mika also took it as their last ride on their date last week. And if they did, they made out during the ride for sure.

“The line was a bit long, but we made it.”  

“Yep, we’re goin’ up.”

While sitting side by side in the cabin, we turned around and looked at the scenery. As she looked outside, I watched her face in profile. The light from the setting sun was illuminating her, giving her an atmosphere that seemed different from usual.

I hugged her.

“Woof… Shuu, eh-heh-heh.”  

“Rir… I love you.”  

“I love you, too. Always have.”

She returned the embrace. There was nothing different from our usual hugs, but it felt more intense, warmer.

“…I didn’t notice, but we’re already close to the peak.”  

“You’re right, we are.”  

“Shuu…”

She closed her eyes. I could guess what she wanted me to do, so I kissed her. The moment I did, she opened her eyes, and we were looking at each other. Not letting this bother us, our tongues entwined and had their back and forth while we were high up in the air, where no one could see us.

Coming to the amusement park had been the right idea. Well, I couldn’t exactly speak in absolutes here.

“…Heh-heh.”

Our lips parted and the evening sun shone on her again. It somehow made her look magical, as if she would disappear at any moment. Maybe that was because she came from another world, or because I had let her die once. I couldn’t say for sure, but I wouldn’t let go of her.

I hugged her again.

#### Footnotes:

1. In the original, Rir confuses メリーゴーランド (“merry-go-round”) with メリーさんのコーラランド (“Miss Mary’s Cola Land”). The problem here is that this is an English word and people from northern Europe tend to be very good at English, so it’s not a mistake that makes sense for her.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-569-amusement-park-date-shuu/#easy-footnote-1-116776)

2. In the original, Shuu proposes the バイキング (“Viking), which I assume would be something like the pirate ship attraction swinging back and forth. However, the word also means “all-you-can-eat buffet” in Japanese, so in the original, Rir says that it makes her hungry again.[](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-569-amusement-park-date-shuu/#easy-footnote-2-116776)

# 570 – Finally (Shuu)

“Today was so~ much fun!” Rir commented with a smile.

Just spending some time thinking about date spots caused her to show me this radiant smile. She was so cute. I was weirdly excited, too. Well, I did love her, so it was unavoidable.

We had fully enjoyed our time in the amusement park and then stopped for dinner on the way home. I obviously was the one to pay for the food. I had earned some money doing part-time jobs during summer break, so it wasn’t an issue. I normally didn’t spend much for myself, so I had saved up a good deal. It went without saying that Rir tried to stop me, but she backed down when I asked her to “please let me pay for it.”

“Woof, can we go on another date like this one?”  

“‘Course we can. Let’s have another when we got time.”  

“Eh-heh-heh.”

She was hugging my arm. I didn’t think she was pushing her breasts against it on purpose… they were soft and- Well, in any case, it felt nice.

“Once we’re home, it won’t be anyone but us, right?”  

“Yep, that’s true.”

She was right, I had so much fun, I’d completely forgotten that part. Today, there wouldn’t be anyone else at home, just the two of us. Which was a big opportunity.

As a matter of fact, yesterday I secretly cleaned my bed and room (though it hadn’t exactly been messy), and went to the drugstore to get some… uhm… things appropriate for the situation. In any case, I did my preparations.

In Anazumu, Rir took care of that stuff. That probably didn’t speak well of me as a man. Still… buying that stuff was crazy embarrassing. I thought I’d die of shame. But I had to get it[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-570-finally-shuu/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117183).

“W-Woof…”

She started fidgeting and her face turned red. If I let her suggest it first, my plan would be in shambles. It was embarrassing, but I had to be faster.

“H-Hey, Rir.”  

“Wh-Wh-What is it, Shuu…?”

I was staring at her, and she was staring right back. Her cheeks were crimson and there was melancholy in her blue eyes.

“O-Once we’re home, it’ll be just us.”  

“Yes, it will.”

_I just repeated what she said earlier. I’m super nervous… But I gotta do it. I’ll say it!_

“Rir… will you come to my room tonight?”  

“I will, I’ll come…!”

Her head bobbed up and down. Did she understand what I was trying to say? I didn’t want her to think we’d just be sleeping side-by-side as usual.

_Still… we’re outside right now, and it’ll probably work once she comes to my room for real… Guess I better put it a bit more clearly._

“Say, right before we go to bed, could you take a bath? But come early enough.”  

“…! I will,” she nodded, still hugging my arm.

______  

____  

__

“I-I’m here.”

One hour after we had gotten home, Rir arrived at my room in her pajamas. She was still fidgeting.

_From now on, it’s countin’._

“…Come sit next to me.”  

“Woof.”

She obediently sat down next to me on the bed. She brought her body close and rested her head on my shoulder. I was pretty sure we used the same shampoo… but she smelled really nice. Moreover, if she hugged me like this, I was sure she’d feel awfully soft…

“Today was fun.”  

“It was!”

_I ended up repeatin’ stuff we’d said before again. Get yourself together, me._

I had to keep talking. For now, I stroked her head resting on my shoulder. Her hair was silky smooth.

“Rir.”  

“What is it, Shuu?”  

“…I love you.”  

“Yeah.”

_Gah… can’t I say anythin’ new? I’m just repeatin’ myself! Calm down! I gotta tell her what I wanna say._

“Can I… kiss you?”  

“I’d love for you to.”

_Right, first I’ll kiss her._

I pressed my lips onto hers. When I tried moving my tongue right after, she welcomed it. This was our second French kiss today. No matter how often I experienced it, it tasted sweet.  

When I pulled away, judging the timing right to speak, there was a string of saliva between our mouths.

“…Your chest, can I touch it?”  

“…Yes.”

As I had said, I stretched out my hands towards her breasts. The twin mounds she often allowed me to caress over on the other side. Something I hadn’t experienced on Earth, yet.

Even through her pajamas, they felt soft and heavenly in my hands. Said hands were large, but incredibly enough, they weren’t large enough to fully grasp her breasts. They were soft but also had a tautness to it. Not that I had ever touched anyone else’s chest, so I had no comparison.

“…”  

“…”

We were both silent.  

I looked into her eyes. She nodded. Understanding my aim.

I started unbuttoning her pajamas. Now, she was only wearing a bra on her upper body. I couldn’t tear my eyes from it, which was probably unavoidable.  

_I can’t help it, alright?_

“Woof. Shuu… it appears that my beasts have gotten bigger.”  

“I-I see.”  

“Does that mean you’ll love me even more?”  

“Y-Your boobs got nothin’ to do with me lovin’ you.”

She fell silent when she heard that. Her face had already been bright red before that, so I couldn’t tell if it embarrassed her. It felt like her eyes were urging me to keep going quickly.

“I’ll continue, then.”  

“Woof, alright.”

# 571 – What Happened on Sunday (Mika)

“Good morning, Rir!”  

“Morning… Mika.”

It was Monday. We were all planning to got to the circus this Saturday, but before that… something important should’ve happened yesterday. Between Rir and Shuu.

They had come to school together as usual, but the moment she saw me, she jumped my way[1](https://re-library.com/translations/levelmaker/volume-19/chapter-571-what-happened-on-sunday-mika/#easy-footnote-bottom-1-117185).

“How did it go?”

That was the only thing I wanted to know. She fidgeted as if ashamed but still gave me a reply.

“Shuu… seduced me…”  

“That’s great, isn’t it?”

The goal was for him to accept her advances, but to think he’d be the one to initiate… you couldn’t call this anything but a huge success.

Maybe he realized by himself that it couldn’t go on like this. Or maybe Ayumu gave him some helpful advice. Either way, it sounded like a good thing.

Right. Even if you often spent the night together, there were times when both partners undressed and still didn’t go all the way, like Ayumu and I when we still were inexperienced. I guess I should ask her to clarify.

“So…”  

“So?”  

“Did you go all the way?”  

“Woof!”

In reply to my whisper, she nodded energetically.  

_Seems like they did it, after all._

“Does that mean you’re feeling sluggish today…?”  

“It’s not that bad, but I’m glad we don’t have PE.”

_Right, so she does feel tired._

After checking her surroundings, she plopped down in my table’s seat and rested her arms and head on the desk. Then, she pouted slightly.

“Woof~. I want to have children with Shuu, soon. But we’re still students, so that’s impossible.”  

“That would mean waiting a long time, you know? That also goes for getting married. You might be able to do so right away in Anazumu, but here, Shuu is going to be a police officer. And a career one at that.”

He was trying to follow in his father’s footsteps. You might call him more manly than Ayumu, who still hadn’t decided on what to do in the future. But there were still hardships waiting before Shuu’s dreams would become reality.

“I’m not sure about the details, but he’ll have to go to university, so marriage would be at 25 or older. So, even if you want kids, that would still be nine years off.”  

“Woof~… nine years. Of my 16 years, ten were spent in a harsh environment, so I guess another nine will pass relatively quickly.”  

“That’s one way to look at it.”

She gave a smile. If she showed Shuu such radiant smiles often enough, there was no way he’d never put his hands on another girl. Plus, she was way too cute.

“Woof! Besides, once we’re going to university, we can travel during the summer holiday as the two of us, which should give us lots of opportunities to do… uhm… stuff like what we did yesterday. I guess that’s not too bad.”  

“That’s true. I want to get married and have children quickly, but spending time together with your partner first is more important.”  

“Exactly!”

Whether Ayumu went the designer path due to the wedding’s influence or chose a more difficult profession, thanks to all the studying we did, I was planning to keep supporting him from the sidelines.

“Woof~, in any case, yesterday was a great day…”  

“That’s good to hear. If only I’d been able to do the same with Ayumu.”

Yes, if only. We still had some of the contraceptives left. So, if I managed to kick Sakura out by urging her to visit Kanata in his room, it would’ve just been the two of us. But the moment I had that idea, I remembered that Ayumu and Kanata would be out with their parents.

How could I forget this?

“Woof, why didn’t you?”  

“…I remembered that he wouldn’t be home on Sunday.”  

“Nothing to be done about that.”  

“On that note, Rir, you haven’t gone anywhere with the Hinos so far, have you? Is Shuu’s father too busy?”

That man always used work a lot. Shuu must’ve been lonely at times… well, thinking about it, he didn’t seem to be. On the contrary, he had great respect for his father. The man had been helping people for a long time, a genuine paragon of justice.

“It seems so. I’ve only been on dates with Shuu.”  

“I see.”  

“Don’t you go on outings with your Family, Mika?”  

“Of course I do!”

I wasn’t sure when the last time was. Back then, Sakura’s eyes hadn’t been healed yet. Yeah, there had been hardships, but also fun.

“Still, we haven’t gone anywhere for some time.”  

“I see… Oh right, speaking of outings, we’ll be out as the six of us this Saturday, won’t we?”  

“Yeah!”

Maybe my family would do something on Sunday together. Mom and Dad probably thought along the same lines as Kanata, and wanted to show sights to Sakura, after she’d been almost blind for so long.

Being able to see the circus alone was huge. Sakura was loved by quite a few people, which obviously included me.

“Oh, Rir, homeroom is about to start.”  

“Woof, you’re right! Talk to you later!”

She returned to her seat next to Shuu.
